pradhānapuruṣeśāya sargasthityantakāriṇe ।। hiraṇyagarbhe svarlīne hy avimukte mahālaye ।। vighneśvare ca kedāre tathā gomāyukeśvare ।। śukreśvare yathānyāyaṃ naimiṣaṃ prayayau muniḥ ।।
samabhyarcyāsanaṃ tasmai tadyogyaṃ samakalpayan ।। sampūjyamāno munibhiḥ sukhāsīno varāsane ।। etasminnevakāle tu sūtaḥ paurāṇikaḥ svayam ।। tasmai sāma ca pūjāṃ ca yathāvaccakrire tadā ।।
atha teṣāṃ purāṇasya śuśrūṣā samapadyata ।। apṛcchaṃśca tataḥ sūtam ṛṣiṃ sarve tapodhanāḥ ।। tvayā sūta mahābuddhe kṛṣṇadvaipāyano muniḥ ।। tasmādbhavantaṃ pṛcchāmaḥ sūta paurāṇikottamam ।।
nārado apyasya devasya rudrasya paramātmanaḥ ।। iha saṃnihitaḥ śrīmān nārado brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ ।। asyāgrato muneḥ puṇyaṃ purāṇaṃ vaktumarhasi ।। evamuktaḥ sa hṛṣṭātmā sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ ।।
naimiṣeyāṃśca puṇyātmā purāṇaṃ vyājahāra saḥ ।। munīśvaraṃ tathā vyāsaṃ vaktuṃ liṅgaṃ smarāmyaham ।। varṇāvayavam avyaktalakṣaṇaṃ bahudhā sthitam ।। oṅkārarūpam ṛgvaktraṃ samajihvāsamanvitam ।।
pradhānapuruṣātītaṃ pralayotpattivarjitam ।। sattvena sarvagaṃ viṣṇuṃ nirguṇatve maheśvaram ।। punaḥ ṣoḍaśadhā caiva ṣaḍviṃśakam ajodbhavam ।। praṇamya ca yathānyāyaṃ vakṣye liṅgodbhavaṃ śubham ।।
brahmaṇā kalpitaṃ pūrvaṃ purāṇaṃ laiṅgam uttamam ।। caturlakṣeṇa saṃkṣipte vyāsaiḥ sarvāntareṣu vai ।। liṅgamekādaśaṃ proktaṃ mayā vyāsācchrutaṃ ca tat ।। tasmātsaṃkṣepato vakṣye na śrutaṃ vistareṇa yat ।।
atraikādaśasāhasraiḥ kathito liṅgasambhavaḥ ।। aṇḍasyāsya ca sambhūtir aṇḍasyāvaraṇāṣṭakam ।। viṣṇutvaṃ kālarudratvaṃ śayanaṃ cāpsu tasya ca ।। brahmaṇaś ca divārātram āyuṣo gaṇanaṃ punaḥ ।।
divyaṃ ca mānuṣaṃ varṣam ārṣaṃ vai dhrauvyameva ca ।। avṛddhirjagato bhūyo devyāḥ śaktyudbhavastathā ।। ākhyāṣṭakaṃ hi rudrasya kathitaṃ rodanāntare ।। śilādasya tapaścaiva vṛtrārerdarśanaṃ tathā ।।
śilādaśakrasaṃvādaḥ padmayonitvameva ca ।। vyāsāvatārāś ca tathā kalpamanvantarāṇi ca ।। kalpeṣu kalpe vārāhe vārāhatvaṃ hares tathā ।। punarliṅgodbhavaścaiva ṛṣimadhye pinākinaḥ ।।
vārāṇasyāś ca māhātmyaṃ kṣetramāhātmyavarṇanam ।। antarikṣe tathāṇḍe asmin devāyatanavarṇanam ।। dakṣaśāpaś ca dakṣasya śāpamokṣastathaiva ca ।। caturyugapramāṇaṃ ca yugadharmaḥ suvistaraḥ ।।
śmaśānanilayaścaiva candrarekhāsamudbhavaḥ ।। maithunātiprasaṅgena vināśo jagatāṃ bhayam ।। śukrotsargastu rudrasya gāṅgeyodbhava eva ca ।। kṣubdhadhī ca vivādaś ca dadhīcopendrayos tathā ।।
pativratāyāścākhyānaṃ paśupāśavicāraṇā ।। vasiṣṭhatanayotpattir vāsiṣṭhānāṃ mahātmanām ।। daurātmyaṃ kauśikasyātha surabherbandhanaṃ tathā ।। snuṣāyāḥ preṣaṇaṃ caiva garbhasthasya vacas tathā ।।
vināśo rākṣasānāṃ ca kṛto vai śaktisūnunā ।। purāṇakaraṇaṃ caiva pulastyasyājñayā guroḥ ।। jīvacchrāddhavidhānaṃ ca śrāddhārhāḥ śrāddhameva ca ।। pañcayajñaprabhāvaś ca pañcayajñavidhis tathā ।।
maithunasya vidhiścaiva prativarṇamanukramāt ।। prāyaścittam aśeṣasya pratyekaṃ caiva vistarāt ।। svarginārakiṇāṃ puṃsāṃ cihnaṃ janmāntareṣu ca ।। kalpaṃ pañcākṣarasyātha rudramāhātmyameva ca ।।
śvetasya mṛtyoḥ saṃvādaḥ śvetārthe kālanāśanam ।। sudarśanasya cākhyānaṃ kramasaṃnyāsalakṣaṇam ।। madhunā kaiṭabhenaiva purā hṛtagatervibhoḥ ।। sarvāvasthāsu viṣṇoś ca jananaṃ līlayaiva tu ।।
manthānadhāraṇārthāya hareḥ kūrmatvamevaca ।। yadūnāṃ caiva sambhūtir yādavatvaṃ hareḥ svayam ।। bālabhāve hareḥ krīḍā putrārthaṃ śaṃkarārcanam ।। bhūbhāranigrahārthe tu rudrasyārādhanaṃ hareḥ ।।
devāsure purā labdho bhṛguśāpaś ca viṣṇunā ।। labdho hitāya śāpastu durvāsasyānanāddhareḥ ।। erakasya tathotpattis tomarasyodbhavas tathā ।। līlayā caiva kṛṣṇena svakulasya ca saṃhṛtiḥ ।।
brahmaṇaścaiva mokṣasya vijñānaṃ tu suvistaram ।। madanasyādidevasya brahmaṇaś cāmarāriṇām ।। jālaṃdharavadhaścaiva sudarśanasamudbhavaḥ ।। tathānyāni ca rudrasya caritāni sahasraśaḥ ।।
prabhāvānubhavaścaiva śivalokasya varṇanam ।। tapasāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ caiva dvijānāṃ vaibhavaṃ tathā ।। liṅge asminnānupūrvyeṇa vistareṇānukīrtyate ।। sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmalokaṃ sa gacchati ।।
aliṅgaḥ śiva ityukto liṅgaṃ śaivamiti smṛtam ।। gandhavarṇarasairhīnaṃ śabdasparśādivarjitam ।। gandhavarṇarasairyuktaṃ śabdasparśādilakṣaṇam ।। vigraho jagatāṃ liṅgam aliṅgād abhavatsvayam ।।
liṅgānyaliṅgasya tathā māyayā vitatāni tu ।। ekasmāttriṣvabhūdviśvam ekena parirakṣitam ।। aliṅgaṃ caiva liṅgaṃ ca liṅgāliṅgāni mūrtayaḥ ।। aliṅgī bhagavān bījī sa eva parameśvaraḥ ।।
bījayonipradhānānām ātmākhyā vartate tviha ।। viśuddho ayaṃ tathā rudraḥ purāṇe śiva ucyate ।। sargādau sā guṇairyuktā purāvyaktā svabhāvataḥ ।। viśvadhātrī tvajākhyā ca śaivī sā prakṛtiḥ smṛtā ।।
janitrīmanuśete sma juṣamāṇaḥ svarūpiṇīm ।। ajā janitrī jagatāṃ sājena samadhiṣṭhitā ।। ajājñayā pradhānasya sargakāle guṇais tribhiḥ ।। vyaktasṛṣṭiṃ vikurute cātmanādhiṣṭhito mahān ।।
mahatas triguṇas tasmād ahaṃkāro rajo adhikaḥ ।। mahato bhūtatanmātraṃ sargakṛdvai babhūva ca ।। saśabdamāvṛṇotpaścād ākāśaṃ śabdakāraṇam ।। sparśamātraṃ tathākāśāt tasmādvāyur mahānmune ।।
rasādāpaḥ śubhāstābhyo gandhamātraṃ dharā tataḥ ।। āvṛṇodrūpamātraṃ tu vāyurvāti kriyātmakaḥ ।। āvṛṇvānā gandhamātram āpaḥ sarvarasātmikāḥ ।। triguṇo bhagavānvahnir dviguṇaḥ sparśasambhavaḥ ।।
tanmātrādbhūtasargaś ca vijñeyaś ca parasparam ।। sargas tathāpyahaṃkārād evamatra prakīrtitaḥ ।। śabdādīnāmavāptyarthaṃ manaścaivobhayātmakam ।। jalabudbudavattasmād avatīrṇaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।।
tasminnaṇḍe tvime lokā antarviśvamidaṃ jagat ।। āpo daśaguṇenaiva tadbāhyastejasā vṛtāḥ ।। vāyurdaśaguṇenaiva bāhyato nabhasā vṛtaḥ ।। mahatā śabdaheturvai pradhānenāvṛtaḥ svayam ।।
koṭikoṭiyutānyatra cāṇḍāni kathitāni tu ।। sṛṣṭāḥ pradhānena tadā labdhvā śambhostu saṃnidhim ।। sargasya pratisargasya sthiteḥ kartā maheśvaraḥ ।। pratisarge tamodriktaḥ sa eva trividhaḥ kramāt ।।
tasmānmaheśvaro devo brahmaṇo adhipatiḥ śivaḥ ।। ekadaṇḍe tathā lokā ime kartā pitāmahaḥ ।। sargaś cābuddhipūrvastu dvijāḥ prāthamikaḥ śubhaḥ ।। sargasya tādṛśī rātriḥ prākṛtasya samāsataḥ ।।
aupacārikamasyaitad ahorātraṃ na vidyate ।। prajānāṃ patayaḥ sarve tiṣṭhantyanye maharṣayaḥ ।। ahastu tasya vaikalpo rātristādṛgvidhā smṛtā ।। catvāri tu sahasrāṇi vatsarāṇāṃ kṛtaṃ dvijāḥ ।।
triśatī dviśatī saṃdhyā tathā caikaśatī kramāt ।। tridvyekasāhasramito vinā saṃdhyāṃśakena tu ।। nimeṣapañcadaśakā kāṣṭhā svasthasya suvratāḥ ।। kalātriṃśatiko viprā muhūrta iti kalpitaḥ ।।
pitrye rātryahanī māsaḥ pravibhāgastayoḥ punaḥ ।। triṃśadye mānuṣā māsāḥ pitryo māsastu sa smṛtaḥ ।। pitryaḥ saṃvatsaro hyeṣa mānuṣeṇa vibhāvyate ।। pitṝṇāṃ trīṇi varṣāṇi saṃkhyātānīha tāni vai ।।
laukikenaiva mānena abdo yo mānuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। divye rātryahanī varṣaṃ pravibhāgastayoḥ punaḥ ।। ete rātryahanī divye prasaṃkhyāte viśeṣataḥ ।। mānuṣaṃ tu śataṃ viprā divyamāsāstrayastu te ।।
trīṇi varṣaśatānyeva ṣaṣṭivarṣāṇi yāni tu ।। trīṇi varṣasahasrāṇi mānuṣāṇi pramāṇataḥ ।। nava yāni sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu ।। ṣaṭtriṃśattu sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu ।।
trīṇyeva niyutānyāhur varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu ।। divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu prāhuḥ saṃkhyāvido janāḥ ।। pūrvaṃ kṛtayugaṃ nāma tatastretā vidhīyate ।। atha saṃvatsarā dṛṣṭā mānuṣeṇa pramāṇataḥ ।।
sahasrāṇāṃ śatānyāsaṃś caturdaśa ca saṃkhyayā ।। tathā daśasahasrāṇāṃ varṣāṇāṃ śatasaṃkhyayā ।। saptaiva niyutānyāhur varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu ।। tathā śatasahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ trīṇi saṃkhyayā ।।
evaṃ caturyugaḥ kāla ṛte saṃdhyāṃśakātsmṛtaḥ ।। catvāriṃśattathā trīṇi niyutānīha saṃkhyayā ।। evaṃ caturyugākhyānāṃ sādhikā hyekasaptatiḥ ।। manvantarasya saṃkhyā ca varṣāgreṇa prakīrtitā ।।
saptaṣaṣṭistathānyāni niyutānyadhikāni tu ।। manvantarasya saṃkhyaiṣā laiṅge asminkīrtitā dvijāḥ ।। caturyugasahasraṃ vai kalpaścaiko dvijottamāḥ ।। tatra vaimānikānāṃ tu aṣṭāviṃśatikoṭayaḥ ।।
trīṇi koṭiśatānyāsan koṭyo dvinavatis tathā ।। punastathāṣṭasāhasraṃ sarvatraiva samāsataḥ ।। maharlokāt prayāntyete janalokaṃ janāstataḥ ।। dviṣaṣṭiś ca tathā koṭyo niyutāni ca saptatiḥ ।।
kalpānāṃ vai sahasraṃ tu varṣamekamajasya tu ।। savanaṃ yugasāhasraṃ sarvadevodbhavasya tu ।। brahmaṇastu tathā proktaḥ kālaḥ kālātmanaḥ prabho ।। ṛturvahnirhavyavāhaḥ sāvitraḥ śuddha eva ca ।।
ṛṣabhaś ca tathā ṣaḍjo majjālīyaś ca madhyamaḥ ।। pañcamaścitrakaścaiva ākūtir jñāna eva ca ।। raktaś ca pītavāsāś ca asitaḥ sarvarūpakaḥ ।। koṭikoṭisahasrāṇi kalpānāṃ munisattamāḥ ।।
parānte vai vikārāṇi vikāraṃ yānti viśvataḥ ।। saṃhṛte tu vikāre ca pradhāne cātmani sthite ।। guṇānāṃ caiva vaiṣamye viprāḥ sṛṣṭiriti smṛtā ।। līlayā devadevena sargāstvīdṛgvidhāḥ kṛtāḥ ।।
asaṃkhyātāś ca kalpākhyā hy asaṃkhyātāḥ pitāmahāḥ ।। pradhānādipravṛttāni līlayā prākṛtāni tu ।। aprākṛtasya tasyādir madhyāntaṃ nāsti cātmanaḥ ।। divā sṛṣṭaṃ tu yatsarvaṃ niśi naśyati cāsya tat ।।
rātrau caikārṇave brahmā naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame ।। śarvaryante prabuddho vai dṛṣṭvā śūnyaṃ carācaram ।। udakairāplutāṃ kṣmāṃ tāṃ samādāya sanātanaḥ ।। nadīnadasamudrāṃś ca pūrvavaccākarotprabhuḥ ।।
dharāyāṃ so acinotsarvān girīn dagdhān purāgninā ।। sraṣṭuṃ ca bhagavāṃścakre tadā sraṣṭā punarmatim ।। dvijāś ca buddhipūrvaṃ tu brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।। avidyā pañcadhā hyeṣā prādurbhūtā svayambhuvaḥ ।।
asādhaka iti smṛtvā sargo mukhyaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। tridhā kaṇṭho munestasya dhyāyato vai hyavartata ।। ūrdhvasrotaḥ parastasya sāttvikaḥ sa iti smṛtaḥ ।। brahmaṇo mahatastvādyo dvitīyo bhautikas tathā ।।
tiryagyonyaḥ pañcamastu ṣaṣṭho daivika ucyate ।। navamaścaiva kaumāraḥ prākṛtā vaikṛtāstvime ।। sanātanaṃ muniśreṣṭhā naiṣkarmyeṇa gatāḥ param ।। dakṣamatriṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca so asṛjadyogavidyayā ।।
brahmavādina evaite brahmaṇaḥ sadṛśāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। dvādaśaiva prajāstvetā brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।। tāvūrdhvaretasau divyau cāgrajau brahmavādinau ।। vakṣye bhāryākulaṃ teṣāṃ munīnāmagrajanmanām ।।
śatarūpāṃ tu vai rājñīṃ virājamasṛjatprabhuḥ ।। lebhe putradvayaṃ puṇyā tathā kanyādvayaṃ ca sā ।। jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā tvākūtiḥ prasūtiścānujā smṛtā ।। prasūtiṃ bhagavāndakṣo lokadhātrīṃ ca yoginīm ।।
dakṣiṇā janayāmāsa divyā dvādaśa putrikāḥ ।। śraddhāṃ lakṣmīṃ dhṛtiṃ puṣṭiṃ tuṣṭiṃ medhāṃ kriyāṃ tathā ।। khyātiṃ śāntiṃ ca sambhūtiṃ smṛtiṃ prītiṃ kṣamāṃ tathā ।। svadhāṃ caiva mahābhāgāṃ pradadau ca yathākramam ।।
dharmaṃ prajāpatiṃ jagmuḥ patiṃ paramadurlabhāḥ ।। sambhūtiṃ ca marīcistu smṛtiṃ caivāṅgirā muniḥ ।। kratuś ca saṃnatiṃ dhīmān atristāṃ cānasūyakām ।। vibhāvasus tathā svāhāṃ svadhāṃ vai pitaras tathā ।।
dakṣeṇa jagatāṃ dhātrī rudramevāsthitā patim ।। vibhajasveti cāhādau yadā jātā tadābhavat ।। ekādaśāvidhā rudrās tasya cāṃśodbhavās tathā ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagavān brahmā dakṣamālokya suvratām ।।
punnāmno narakāttrāti iti putrītvihoktitaḥ ।। tasmāt putrī satī nāmnā tavaiṣā ca bhaviṣyati ।। labdhvā putrīṃ dadau sākṣāt satīṃ rudrāya sādaram ।। tāsu dharmaprajāṃ vakṣye yathākramamanuttamam ।।
śrutastu daṇḍaḥ samayo bodhaścaiva mahādyutiḥ ।। kṣemaṃ sukhaṃ yaśaścaiva dharmaputrāś ca tāsu vai ।। apramādas tathā bodho buddherdharmasya tau sutau ।। bhṛgupatnī ca suṣuve khyātirviṣṇoḥ priyāṃ śriyam ।।
prabhūtirnāma yā patnī marīceḥ suṣuve sutau ।। tuṣṭirjyeṣṭhā ca vai dṛṣṭiḥ kṛṣiścāpacitis tathā ।। kardamaṃ ca varīyāṃsaṃ sahiṣṇuṃ munisattamāḥ ।। prītyāṃ pulastyaś ca tathā janayāmāsa vai sutān ।।
putrāṇāṃ ṣaṣṭisāhasraṃ saṃnatiḥ suṣuve śubhā ।। sinīvālīṃ kuhūṃ caiva rākāṃ cānumatiṃ tathā ।। labdhānubhāvamagniṃ ca kīrtimantaṃ ca suvratā ।। tāsvekā kanyakā nāmnā śrutiḥ sā sūnupañcakam ।।
somaś ca vai śrutiḥ ṣaṣṭhī pañcātreyāstu sūnavaḥ ।। jyāyasī puṇḍarīkākṣān vāsiṣṭhān varalocanā ।। sutapāḥ śukra ityete munervai sapta sūnavaḥ ।। svāhā ca tasmātsuṣuve sutānāṃ trayaṃ trayāṇāṃ jagatāṃ hitāya ।।
nirmathyaḥ pavamānastu vaidyutaḥ pāvakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। putraiḥ pautraistvihaiteṣāṃ saṃkhyā saṃkṣepataḥ smṛtā ।। ityete vahnayaḥ proktāḥ praṇīyante adhvareṣu ca ।। prajānāṃ patayaḥ sarve sarve rudrātmakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
agniṣvāttāś ca yajvānaḥ śeṣā barhiṣadaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। agniṣvāttātmajā menā mānasī lokaviśrutā ।। gaṅgāṃ haimavatīṃ jajñe bhavāṅgāśleṣapāvanīm ।। svadhā sā merurājasya patnī padmasamānanā ।।
ṛṣīṇāṃ ca kulaṃ sarvaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ tatsuvistaram ।। dākṣāyaṇī satī yātā pārśvaṃ rudrasya pārvatī ।। tāṃ dhyātvā vyasṛjadrudrān anekānnīlalohitaḥ ।। yācito muniśārdūlā brahmaṇā prahasan kṣaṇāt ।।
tāndṛṣṭvā vividhān rudrān nirmalānnīlalohitān ।। namo astu vo mahādevās trinetrā nīlalohitāḥ ।। hiraṇyakeśā dṛṣṭighnā nityā buddhāś ca nirmalāḥ ।। pradakṣiṇīkṛtya tadā bhagavānkanakāṇḍajaḥ ।।
mṛtyuhīnā vibho sraṣṭuṃ mṛtyuyuktāḥ sṛja prabho ।। sa tvaṃ sṛja yathākāmaṃ mṛtyuyuktāḥ prajāḥ prabho ।। jarāmaraṇasaṃyuktaṃ jagadetaccarācaram ।। sthāṇutvaṃ tasya vai viprāḥ śaṃkarasya mahātmanaḥ ।।
śaṃ rudraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ karoti ghṛṇayā yataḥ ।। vairāgyasthaṃ viraktasya vimuktiryacchamucyate ।। vairāgyājjāyate puṃso virāgo darśanāntare ।। tasya cāsya ca saṃdhānaṃ prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ ।।
sa eva śaṃkaraḥ sākṣāt pinākī nīlalohitaḥ ।। na gacchantyeva narakaṃ pāpiṣṭhā api dāruṇam ।। māyāntāścaiva ghorādyā hy aṣṭaviṃśatireva ca ।। anāśritāḥ śivaṃ rudraṃ śaṃkaraṃ nīlalohitam ।।
puruṣaṃ paramātmānaṃ puruhūtaṃ puruṣṭutam ।। sattvena sarvagaṃ viṣṇuṃ nirguṇatve maheśvaram ।। karmaṇākarmaṇā vāpi śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। prabhāvaṃ śaṃkarasyādyaṃ saṃkṣepātsarvadarśinaḥ ।।
yoginaḥ sarvatattvajñāḥ paraṃ vairāgyamāsthitāḥ ।। prāṇāyāmādibhiścāṣṭasādhanaiḥ sahacāriṇaḥ ।। karmāṇi narakaṃ svargaṃ gacchantyeva svakarmaṇā ।। yogena jāyate muktiḥ prasādādakhilaṃ tataḥ ।।
divyaṃ māheśvaraṃ caiva yogaṃ yogavidāṃ vara ।। prasādaṃ yogamārgeṇa kasminkāle nṛṇāṃ vibhuḥ ।। śailādinā tu kathitaṃ śṛṇvantu brahmasūnave ।। yogācāryāvatārāṇi tathā tiṣye tu śūlinaḥ ।।
praśiṣyā bahavasteṣāṃ prasīdatyevamīśvaraḥ ।। vaiśyāntaṃ brāhmaṇādyaṃ hi ghṛṇayā cānurūpataḥ ।। kalpeṣu kasminkalpe no vaktumarhasi cātra tān ।। vyāsāṃś ca sāmprataṃ rudrāṃs tathā sarvāntareṣu vai ।।
yathākramaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvāvarteṣu sāmpratam ।। mṛtyuḥ śatakraturdhīmān vasiṣṭho munipuṃgavaḥ ।। śatatejāḥ svayaṃdharmo nārāyaṇa iti śrutaḥ ।। ṛtaṃjayo bharadvājo gautamaḥ kavisattamaḥ ।।
tṛṇabindur munī rūkṣaḥ śaktiḥ śākteya uttaraḥ ।। vyāsāstvete ca śṛṇvantu kalau yogeśvarān kramāt ।। kalau rudrāvatārāṇāṃ vyāsānāṃ kila gauravāt ।। avatārān pravakṣyāmi tathā sarvāntareṣu vai ।।
tathaiva cordhvakalpeṣu siddhānvaivasvatāntare ।। uttamastāmasaścaiva raivatāścākṣuṣas tathā ।। piśaṅgaścāpiśaṅgābhaḥ śabalo varṇakas tathā ।। śvetaḥ pāṇḍus tathā raktas tāmraḥ pītaśca kāpilaḥ ।।
apiśaṅgaḥ piśaṅgaś ca trivarṇaḥ śabalas tathā ।। nāmato varṇataścaiva varṇataḥ punareva ca ।। vaivasvata ṛkārastu manuḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sureśvaraḥ ।। samatīteṣu kalpeṣu tathā cānāgateṣu vai ।।
yogāvatārāṃś ca vibhoḥ śiṣyāṇāṃ saṃtatis tathā ।। ādye śvetaḥ kalau rudraḥ sutāro madanas tathā ।। jaigīṣavyo mahātejā bhagavān dadhivāhanaḥ ।। gautamaścātha bhagavān sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ ।।
jaṭāmālyaṭṭahāsaś ca dāruko lāṅgalī tathā ।। sahiṣṇuḥ somaśarmā ca nakulīśo jagadguruḥ ।। yogācāryāvatārā ye sarvāvarteṣu suvratāḥ ।। yogeśvarāṇāṃ catvāraḥ śiṣyāḥ pratyekamavyayāḥ ।।
dundubhiḥ śatarūpaś ca ṛcīkaḥ ketumāṃs tathā ।। sumukho durmukhaścaiva durdamo duratikramaḥ ।। ṛbhuḥ sanatkumāraś ca sudhāmā virajās tathā ।। suvāhano muniśreṣṭho meghavāho mahādyutiḥ ।।
vālkalaś ca mahāyogī dharmātmāno mahaujasaḥ ।। balabandhur nirāmitraḥ ketuśṛṅgastapodhanaḥ ।। sarvajñaḥ samabuddhiś ca sādhyaḥ sarvastathaiva ca ।। kuṇiś ca kuṇibāhuś ca kuśarīraḥ kunetrakaḥ ।।
utathyo vāmadevaś ca mahāyogo mahābalaḥ ।। hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyo logākṣiḥ kuthumis tathā ।। plakṣo dālbhyāyaṇiścaiva ketumān gopanas tathā ।। uśiko bṛhadaśvaś ca devalaḥ kavireva ca ।।
chagalaḥ kuṇḍakarṇaś ca kumbhaścaiva pravāhakaḥ ।। akṣapādaḥ kumāraś ca ulūko vatsa eva ca ।। śiṣyāstvete mahātmānaḥ sarvāvarteṣu yoginām ।। ete pāśupatāḥ siddhā bhasmoddhūlitavigrahāḥ ।।
prāpya pāśupataṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya saṃsthitāḥ ।। teṣāṃ patitvātsarveśo bhavaḥ paśupatiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। yogaḥ pāśupato jñeyaḥ parāvaravibhūtaye ।। kalpitāni śivenaiva hitāya jagatāṃ dvijāḥ ।।
yogasthānamadho nābher āvartaṃ madhyamaṃ bhruvoḥ ।। ekāgratā bhaveccaiva sarvadā tatprasādataḥ ।। vaktuṃ na śakyaṃ brahmādyaiḥ kramaśo jāyate nṛṇām ।। tasya heturṛṣerjñānaṃ jñānaṃ tasya prasādataḥ ।।
niruddhendriyavṛttestu yogasiddhirbhaviṣyati ।। sādhanānyaṣṭadhā cāsya kathitānīha siddhaye ।। tṛtīyamāsanaṃ proktaṃ prāṇāyāmastataḥ param ।। dhyānaṃ saptamamityuktaṃ samādhistvaṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
ahiṃsā prathamo hetur yamasya yamināṃ varāḥ ।। niyamasyāpi vai mūlaṃ yama eva na saṃśayaḥ ।। ahiṃsaiṣā samākhyātā yā cātmajñānasiddhidā ।। kathanaṃ satyamityuktaṃ parapīḍāvivarjitam ।।
paradoṣān parijñāya na vadediti cāparam ।। manasā karmaṇā vācā tadasteyaṃ samāsataḥ ।। brahmacaryamiti proktaṃ yatīnāṃ brahmacāriṇām ।। sadārāṇāṃ gṛhasthānaṃ tathaiva ca vadāmi vaḥ ।।
manasā karmaṇā vācā brahmacaryamiti smṛtam ।। evaṃ gṛhastho yuktātmā brahmacārī na saṃśayaḥ ।। vidhinā yādṛśī hiṃsā sā tvahiṃsā iti smṛtā ।। kuṇapeṣu yathā cittaṃ tathā kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ ।।
tathā kāryā ratau cāpi svadāre cānyataḥ kutaḥ ।। tasmānnārīṣu saṃsargaṃ dūrataḥ parivarjayet ।। tasmādvirāgaḥ kartavyo manasā karmaṇā girā ।। haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmeva bhūya evābhivardhate ।।
avirakto yato martyo nānāyoniṣu vartate ।। karmaṇā prajayā nāsti dravyeṇa dvijasattamāḥ ।। ṛtau ṛtau nivṛttistu brahmacaryamiti smṛtam ।। śaucamijyā tapo dānaṃ svādhyāyopasthanigrahaḥ ।।
niyamaḥ syādanīhā ca śaucaṃ tuṣṭistapas tathā ।। bāhyamābhyantaraṃ proktaṃ śaucamābhyantaraṃ varam ।। āgneyaṃ vāruṇaṃ brāhmaṃ kartavyaṃ śivapūjakaiḥ ।। ā dehāntaṃ mṛdālipya tīrthatoyeṣu sarvadā ।।
śaivalā jhaṣakā matsyāḥ sattvā matsyopajīvinaḥ ।। tasmādābhyantaraṃ śaucaṃ sadā kāryaṃ vidhānataḥ ।। suvairāgyamṛdā śuddhaḥ śaucamevaṃ prakīrtitam ।। nyāyenāgatayā vṛttyā saṃtuṣṭo yastu suvrataḥ ।।
cāndrāyaṇādinipuṇas tapāṃsi suśubhāni ca ।। vācikaścādhamo mukhya upāṃśuścottamottamaḥ ।। tathā śivapraṇīdhānaṃ manovākkāyakarmaṇā ।। nigraho hyapahṛtyāśu prasaktānīndriyāṇi ca ।।
cittasya dhāraṇā proktā sthānabandhaḥ samāsataḥ ।। tatraikacittatā dhyānaṃ pratyayāntaravarjitam ।। samādhiḥ sarvahetuś ca prāṇāyāma iti smṛtaḥ ।। tridhā dvijairyamaḥ prokto mando madhyottamas tathā ।।
prāṇāyāmasya mānaṃ tu mātrādvādaśakaṃ smṛtam ।। madhyamas tu dviruddhātaś caturviṃśatimātrakaḥ ।। prasvedakampanotthānajanakaśca yathākramam ।। romāñcadhvanisaṃviddhasvāṅgamoṭanakampanam ।।
tadottamottamaḥ proktaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ suśobhanaḥ ।। ibho vā śarabho vāpi durādharṣo atha kesarī ।। tathā samīraṇo asvastho durādharṣaś ca yoginām ।। yathaiva mṛgarāṅnāgaḥ śarabho vāpi durmadaḥ ।।
tathā paricayātsvāsthyaṃ samatvaṃ cādhigacchati ।। evamabhyasyamānastu muneḥ prāṇo vinirdahet ।। saṃyuktasya tathā samyak prāṇāyāmena dhīmataḥ ।। prāṇāyāmena sidhyanti divyāḥ śāntyādayaḥ kramāt ।।
ādau catuṣṭayasyeha proktā śāntiriha dvijāḥ ।। praśāntiḥ saṃyamaḥ samyag vacasāmiti saṃsmṛtā ।। sarvendriyaprasādastu buddhervai marutāmapi ।। prāṇo apānaḥ samānaś ca udāno vyāna eva ca ।।
eteṣāṃ yaḥ prasādastu marutāmiti saṃsmṛtaḥ ।। apānayatyapānastu āhārādīn krameṇa ca ।। udvejayati marmāṇi udāno ayaṃ prakīrtitaḥ ।। udgāre nāga ākhyātaḥ kūrma unmīlane tu saḥ ।।
dhanaṃjayo mahāghoṣaḥ sarvagaḥ sa mṛte api hi ।। prasādo asya turīyā tu saṃjñā viprāścatuṣṭaye ।। khyātiḥ saṃvittataḥ paścād īśvaro matireva ca ।। asyā buddheḥ prasādastu prāṇāyāmena sidhyati ।।
agrajaḥ sarvatattvānāṃ mahānyaḥ parimāṇataḥ ।। bṛhattvād bṛṃhaṇatvācca brahmā brahmavidāṃvarāḥ ।। smarate yatsmṛtiḥ sarvaṃ saṃvidvai vindate yataḥ ।। sarvatattvādhipaḥ sarvaṃ vijānāti yadīśvaraḥ ।।
arthaṃ bodhayate yacca budhyate buddhirucyate ।। doṣānvinirdahetsarvān prāṇāyāmādasau yamī ।। viṣayānviṣavaddhyātvā dhyānenānīśvarān guṇān ।। sthānaṃ labdhvaiva kurvīta yogāṣṭāṅgāni vai kramāt ।।
ādeśakāle yogasya darśanaṃ hi na vidyate ।। jantuvyāpte śmaśāne ca jīrṇagoṣṭhe catuṣpathe ।। aśubhe durjanākrānte maśakādisamanvite ।। sugupte tu śubhe ramye guhāyāṃ parvatasya tu ।।
gṛhe tu suśubhe deśe vijane jantuvarjite ।। darpaṇodarasaṃkāśe kṛṣṇāgarusudhūpite ।। phalapallavamūlāḍhye kuśapuṣpasamanvite ।। praṇipatya guruṃ paścād bhavaṃ devīṃ vināyakam ।।
āsanaṃ svastikaṃ baddhvā padmamardhāsanaṃ tu vā ।। samaṃ dṛḍhāsano bhūtvā saṃhṛtya caraṇāvubhau ।। pārṣṇibhyāṃ vṛṣaṇau rakṣaṃs tathā prajananaṃ punaḥ ।। samprekṣya nāsikāgraṃ svaṃ diśaścānavalokayan ।।
tataḥ sattvasthito bhūtvā śivadhyānaṃ samabhyaset ।। dhyāyedvai puṇḍarīkasya karṇikāyāṃ samāhitaḥ ।। tryaṅgule cāṣṭakoṇaṃ vā pañcakoṇamathāpi vā ।। sauraṃ saumya tathāgneyam atha vānukrameṇa tu ।।
agneradhaḥ prakalpyaivaṃ dharmādīnāṃ catuṣṭayam ।। sattvasthaṃ cintayedrudraṃ svaśaktyā parimaṇḍitam ।। lalāṭaphalikāyāṃ vā mūrdhni dhyānaṃ samācaret ।। daśāre vā ṣaḍasre vā caturasre smarecchivam ।।
dvādaśādityasaṃkāśe candrabimbasame api vā ।। agnivarṇe athavā vidyud valayābhe samāhitaḥ ।। nīlalohitabimbe vā yogī dhyānaṃ samabhyaset ।। candracūḍaṃ lalāṭe tu bhrūmadhye śaṃkaraṃ svayam ।।
nirmalaṃ niṣkalaṃ brahma suśāntaṃ jñānarūpiṇam ।। nirālambam atarkyaṃ ca vināśotpattivarjitam ।। amṛtaṃ cākṣaraṃ brahma hy apunarbhavam adbhutam ।। heyopādeyarahitaṃ sūkṣmātsūkṣmataraṃ śivam ।।
atīndriyam anābhāsaṃ paraṃ tattvaṃ parātparam ।। advayaṃ tamasaścaiva parastātsaṃsthitaṃ param ।। nābhau sadāśivaṃ cāpi sarvadevātmakaṃ vibhum ।। kanyasenaiva mārgeṇa codghātenāpi śaṃkaram ।।
uttamenāpi vai vidvān kumbhakena samabhyaset ।। recakaṃ pūrakaṃ tyaktvā kumbhakaṃ ca dvijottamāḥ ।। ekībhāvaṃ sametyaivaṃ tatra yadrasasambhavam ।। dhāraṇā dvādaśāyāmā dhyānaṃ dvādaśa dhāraṇam ।।
athavā jñānināṃ viprāḥ samparkādeva jāyate ।। yogāntarāyās tasyātha jāyante yuñjataḥ punaḥ ।। naśyanty abhyāsatas te api praṇidhānena vai guroḥ ।। pramādaḥ saṃśayasthāne cittasyehānavasthitiḥ ।।
daurmanasyamayogyeṣu viṣayeṣu ca yogyatā ।। ālasyaṃ cāpravṛttiś ca gurutvātkāyacittayoḥ ।। pramādastu samādhestu sādhanānām abhāvanam ।। anavasthitacittatvam apratiṣṭhā hi yoginaḥ ।।
aśraddhābhāvarahitā vṛttirvai sādhaneṣu ca ।। viparyayajñānamiti bhrāntidarśanam ucyate ।। duḥkhamādhyātmikaṃ proktaṃ tathā caivādhibhautikam ।। icchāvighātātsaṃkṣobhaś cetasastadudāhṛtam ।।
tamasā rajasā caiva saṃspṛṣṭaṃ durmanaḥ smṛtam ।। haṭhātsvīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā yogyāyogyavivekataḥ ।। antarāyā iti khyātā yogasyaite hi yoginām ।। pranaṣṭeṣvantarāyeṣu dvijāḥ paścāddhi yoginaḥ ।।
pratibhā prathamā siddhir dvitīyā śravaṇā smṛtā ।। āsvādā pañcamī proktā vedanā ṣaṣṭhikā smṛtā ।। pratibhā pratibhāvṛtiḥ pratibhāva iti sthitiḥ ।। sūkṣme vyavahite atīte viprakṛṣṭe tvanāgate ।।
śravaṇātsarvaśabdānām aprayatnena yoginaḥ ।। sparśasyādhigamo yas tu vedanā tūpapāditā ।। saṃviddivyarase tasminn āsvādo hyaprayatnataḥ ।। vindante yoginastasmād ābrahmabhuvanaṃ dvijāḥ ।।
aupasargikam eteṣu guṇeṣu guṇitaṃ dvijāḥ ।। paiśāce pārthivaṃ cāpyaṃ rākṣasānāṃ pure dvijāḥ ।। aindre vyomātmakaṃ sarvaṃ saumye caiva tu mānasam ।। ādye cāṣṭau dvitīye ca tathā ṣoḍaśarūpakam ।।
catvāriṃśat pañcame tu bhūtamātrātmakaṃ smṛtam ।। pratyekamaṣṭadhā siddhaṃ pañcame tacchatakratoḥ ।। catuḥṣaṣṭiguṇaṃ brāhmaṃ labhate dvijasattamāḥ ।। lokeṣvālokya yogena yogavitparamaṃ sukham ।।
nānājātisvarūpaṃ ca caturbhir dehadhāraṇam ।। etadaṣṭaguṇaṃ proktam aiśvaryaṃ pārthivaṃ mahat ।। icchecchaktaḥ svayaṃ pātuṃ samudramapi nāturaḥ ।। yadyadvastu samādāya bhoktumicchati kāmataḥ ।।
bhāṇḍaṃ vinātha hastena jalapiṇḍasya dhāraṇam ।। etat ṣoḍaśakaṃ proktam āpyamaiśvaryamuttamam ।। lokaṃ dagdhamapīhānyad adagdhaṃ svavidhānataḥ ।। agninigrahaṇaṃ haste smṛtimātreṇa cāgamaḥ ।।
dvābhyāṃ rūpaviniṣpattir vinā taistribhir ātmanaḥ ।। manogatitvaṃ bhūtānām antarnivasanaṃ tathā ।। laghutvaṃ ca gurutvaṃ ca pāṇibhyāṃ vāyudhāraṇam ।। ekena dehaniṣpattir vātaiśvaryaṃ smṛtaṃ budhaiḥ ।।
ākāśagamanaṃ nityam indriyārthaiḥ samanvitam ।। tanmātraliṅgagrahaṇaṃ sarvaprāṇinidarśanam ।। yathākāmopalabdhiś ca yathākāmavinirgamaḥ ।। kāmānurūpanirmāṇaṃ vaśitvaṃ priyadarśanam ।।
chedanaṃ tāḍanaṃ bandhaṃ saṃsāraparivartanam ।। prājāpatyamidaṃ proktam āhaṅkārikamuttamam ।। pralayaścādhikāraś ca lokavṛttapravartanam ।। saṃsārasya ca kartṛtvaṃ brāhmam etad anuttamam ।।
brahmaṇā tadguṇaṃ śakyaṃ vettumanyairna śakyate ।। asaṃkhyeyaguṇaṃ śuddhaṃ ko jānīyācchivātmakam ।। niroddhavyāḥ prayatnena vairāgyeṇa pareṇa tu ।। aśraddhayā tyajetsarvaṃ virakta iti kīrtitaḥ ।।
vairāgyeṇaiva saṃtyājyāḥ siddhayaścaupasargikāḥ ।। nirudhyaiva tyajetsarvaṃ prasīdati maheśvaraḥ ।। athavānugrahārthaṃ ca līlārthaṃ vā tadā muniḥ ।। kvacidbhūmiṃ parityajya hy ākāśe krīḍate śriyā ।।
kvacicchrute tadarthena ślokabandhaṃ karoti saḥ ।। mṛgapakṣisamūhasya rutajñānaṃ ca vindati ।। bahunātra kimuktena vijñānāni sahasraśaḥ ।। abhyāsenaiva vijñānaṃ viśuddhaṃ ca sthiraṃ bhavet ।।
devabimbānyanekāni vimānāni sahasraśaḥ ।। grahanakṣatratārāś ca bhuvanāni sahasraśaḥ ।। ātmavidyāpradīpena svasthenācalanena tu ।। tamo nihatya puruṣaḥ paśyati hyātmanīśvaram ।।
vairāgyamapavargaś ca nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। yoge pāśupate niṣṭhā sthātavyaṃ ca munīśvarāḥ ।। dharmajñānāṃ ca sādhūnām ācāryāṇāṃ śivātmanām ।। saṃnyāsināṃ viraktānāṃ jñānināṃ vaśagātmanām ।।
alubdhānāṃ sayogānāṃ śrutismṛtividāṃ dvijāḥ ।। saditi brahmaṇaḥ śabdas tadante ye labhantyuta ।। daśātmake ye viṣaye sādhane cāṣṭalakṣaṇe ।। sāmānyeṣu ca dravyeṣu tathā vaiśeṣikeṣu ca ।।
varṇāśrameṣu yuktasya svargādisukhakāriṇaḥ ।। vidyāyāḥ sādhanātsādhubrahmacārī gurorhitaḥ ।। sādhanāttapaso araṇye sādhurvaikhānasaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। evamāśramadharmāṇāṃ sādhanātsādhavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
dharmādharmāviha proktau śabdāvetau kriyātmakau ।। dhāraṇārthe mahān hy eṣa dharmaśabdaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। atreṣṭaprāpako dharma ācāryairupadiśyate ।। vṛddhāścālolupāścaiva ātmavanto hyadāmbhikāḥ ।।
svayamācarate yasmād ācāre sthāpayatyapi ।। vijñeyaṃ śravaṇācchrautaṃ smaraṇātsmārtamucyate ।। dṛṣṭvānurūpamarthaṃ yaḥ pṛṣṭo naivāpi gūhati ।। brahmacaryaṃ tathā maunaṃ nirāhāratvameva ca ।।
ātmavat sarvabhūteṣu yo hitāyāhitāya ca ।। yadyadiṣṭatamaṃ dravyaṃ nyāyenaivāgataṃ kramāt ।। dānaṃ trividhamityetat kaniṣṭhajyeṣṭhamadhyamam ।। śrutismṛtibhyāṃ vihito dharmo varṇāśramātmakaḥ ।।
māyākarmaphalatyāgī śivātmā parikīrtitaḥ ।। asakto bhayato yastu viṣayeṣu vicārya ca ।। ātmārthaṃ vā parārthaṃ vā indriyāṇīha yasya vai ।। anudvigno hyaniṣṭeṣu tatheṣṭānnābhinandati ।।
saṃnyāsaḥ karmaṇāṃ nyāsaḥ kṛtānāmakṛtaiḥ saha ।। avyaktādyaviśeṣānte vikāre asminnacetane ।। evaṃ tu jñānayuktasya śraddhāyuktasya śaṅkaraḥ ।। kiṃ tu guhyatamaṃ vakṣye sarvatra parameśvare ।।
ayogyasyāpi bhagavān bhaktasya parameśvaraḥ ।। jñānamadhyāpanaṃ homo dhyānaṃ yajñastapaḥ śrutam ।। cāndrāyaṇasahasraiś ca prājāpatyaśatais tathā ।। abhaktā bhagavatyasmiṃl loke giriguhāśaye ।।
bhaktānāṃ darśanādeva nṛṇāṃ svargādayo dvijāḥ ।। brahmaviṣṇusurendrāṇāṃ tathānyeṣāmapi sthitiḥ ।। bhavena ca tathā proktaṃ samprekṣyomāṃ pinākinā ।। avimukte samāsīnā rudreṇa paramātmanā ।।
kena vaśyo mahādeva pūjyo dṛśyastvamīśvaraḥ ।। niśamya vacanaṃ tasyās tathā hyālokya pārvatīm ।। smṛtvātha menayā patnyā girergāṃ kathitāṃ purā ।। devi labdhā purī ramyā tvayā yatpraṣṭumarhasi ।।
purā pitāmahenāpi pṛṣṭaḥ praśnavatāṃ vare ।। śvete śvetena varṇena dṛṣṭvā kalpe tu māṃ śubhe ।। pīte tatpuruṣaṃ pītam aghore kṛṣṇamīśvaram ।। īśānaṃ viśvarūpākhyo viśvarūpaṃ tadāha mām ।।
kena vaśyo mahādeva dhyeyaḥ kutra ghṛṇānidhe ।। avocaṃ śraddhayaiveti vaśyo vārijasaṃbhava ।। pūjyaḥ pañcāsyarūpeṇa pavitraiḥ pañcabhirdvijaiḥ ।। so api māmāha bhāvārthaṃ dattaṃ tasmai mayā purā ।।
tasmāttu śraddhayā vaśyo dṛśyaḥ śreṣṭhagireḥ sute ।। śraddhā dharmaḥ paraḥ sūkṣmaḥ śraddhā jñānaṃ hutaṃ tapaḥ ।। śraddhā svargaś ca mokṣaś ca dṛśyo ahaṃ śraddhayā sadā ।। vāmadevaṃ mahātmānaṃ purāṇapuruṣottamam ।।
ekonatriṃśakaḥ kalpo vijñeyaḥ śvetalohitaḥ ।। utpannastu śikhāyuktaḥ kumāraḥ śvetalohitaḥ ।। hṛdi kṛtvā mahātmānaṃ brahmarūpiṇamīśvaram ।। dhyānayogātparaṃ jñātvā vavande devamīśvaram ।।
tato asya pārśvataḥ śvetāḥ prādurbhūtā mahāyaśāḥ ।। śiṣyāste vai mahātmāno yaistadbrahma sadāvṛtam ।। vijajñe atha mahātejās tasmājjajñe harastvasau ।। prapannāḥ parayā bhaktyā gṛṇanto brahma śāśvatam ।।
prāṇāyāmaparā bhūtvā brahmatatparamānasāḥ ।। viṣṇulokamatikramya rudralokaṃ vrajanti te ।। brahmā yatra mahātejā raktavarṇamadhārayat ।। prādurbhūto mahātejāḥ kumāro raktabhūṣaṇaḥ ।।
sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā mahātmānaṃ kumāraṃ raktavāsasam ।। sa taṃ praṇamya bhagavān brahmā paramayantritaḥ ।। tathā stuto mahādevo brahmaṇā parameśvaraḥ ।। dhyāyatā putrakāmena yasmātte ahaṃ pitāmaha ।।
tasmāddhyānabalaṃ prāpya kalpe kalpe prayatnataḥ ।। tatastasya mahātmānaś catvāraste kumārakāḥ ।। virajāś ca vibāhuś ca viśoko viśvabhāvanaḥ ।। raktāṃbaradharāḥ sarve raktamālyānulepanāḥ ।।
tato varṣasahasrānte brahmatve adhyavasāyinaḥ ।। anugrahārthaṃ lokānāṃ śiṣyāṇāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। punareva mahādevaṃ praviṣṭā rudramavyayam ।। prapaśyanti mahādevaṃ tadbhaktās tatparāyaṇāḥ ।।
rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham ।। brahmā yatra mahābhāgaḥ pītavāsā babhūva ha ।। prādurbhūto mahātejāḥ kumāraḥ pītavastradhṛk ।। hemayajñopavītaś ca pītoṣṇīṣo mahābhujaḥ ।।
manasā lokadhātāraṃ prapede śaraṇaṃ vibhum ।। gāṃ viśvarūpāṃ dadṛśe maheśvaramukhāccyutām ।। caturnetrāṃ catuḥśṛṅgīṃ caturdaṃṣṭrāṃ caturmukhīm ।। sa tāṃ dṛṣṭvā mahātejā mahādevīṃ maheśvarīm ।।
matiḥ smṛtirbuddhiriti gāyamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।। viśvamāvṛtya yogena jagatsarvaṃ vaśīkuru ।। brāhmaṇānāṃ hitārthāya paramārthā bhaviṣyasi ।। pradadau devadeveśaḥ catuṣpādāṃ jagadguruḥ ।।
brahmā lokaguroḥ so atha pratipede maheśvarīm ।। ityetāṃ vaidikīṃ vidyāṃ raudrīṃ gāyatrīmīritām ।। prapannastu mahādevaṃ dhyānayuktena cetasā ।। aiśvaryaṃ jñānasaṃpattiṃ vairāgyaṃ ca dadau prabhuḥ ।।
pītamālyāṃbaradharāḥ pītasraganulepanāḥ ।। tato varṣasahasrānta uṣitvā vimalaujasaḥ ।। dharmayogabalopetā munīnāṃ dīrghasattriṇām ।। evametena vidhinā ye prapannā maheśvaram ।।
te sarve pāpamutsṛjya vimalā brahmavarcasaḥ ।। praviśanti mahādevaṃ rudraṃ te tvapunarbhavāḥ ।। punaranyaḥ pravṛttastu kalpo nāmnāsitastu saḥ ।। sraṣṭukāmaḥ prajā brahmā cintayāmāsa duḥkhitaḥ ।।
kṛṣṇaḥ samabhavadvarṇo dhyāyataḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ mahāvīryaṃ dīpyamānaṃ svatejasā ।। kṛṣṇena maulinā yuktaṃ kṛṣṇasraganulepanam ।। vavande devadeveśam adbhutaṃ kṛṣṇapiṅgalam ।।
manasā dhyānuyuktena prapannastu tamīśvaram ।। tathā vai dhyāyamānasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। athāsya pārśvataḥ kṛṣṇāḥ kṛṣṇasraganulepanāḥ ।। kṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇaśikhaścaiva kṛṣṇāsyaḥ kṛṣṇavastradhṛk ।।
upāsitvā mahāyogaṃ śiṣyebhyaḥ pradaduḥ punaḥ ।। amalaṃ nirguṇaṃ sthānaṃ praviṣṭā viśvamīśvaram ।। cintayanti mahādevaṃ gantāro rudramavyayam ।। tuṣṭāva devadeveśaṃ brahmā taṃ brahmarūpiṇam ।।
anenaiva tu rūpeṇa saṃharāmi na saṃśayaḥ ।। hīnāṃścaiva mahābhāga tathaiva vividhānyapi ।। mānasāni sutīkṣṇāni vācikāni pitāmaha ।। buddhipūrvaṃ kṛtānyeva sahajāgantukāni ca ।।
saṃharāmi na saṃdehaḥ sarvaṃ pātakajaṃ vibho ।। tadardhaṃ vācike vatsa tadardhaṃ mānase punaḥ ।। vīrahā lakṣamātreṇa bhrūṇahā koṭimabhyaset ।। goghnaścaiva kṛtaghnaś ca strīghnaḥ pāpayuto naraḥ ।।
surāpo lakṣamātreṇa buddhyābuddhyāpi vai prabho ।। asnātāśī sahasreṇa ajapī ca tathā dvijaḥ ।। brāhmaṇasvāpahartā ca svarṇasteyī narādhamaḥ ।। gurutalparato vāpi mātṛghno vā narādhamaḥ ।।
saṃparkātpāpināṃ pāpaṃ tatsamaṃ paribhāṣitam ।। saṃsargātpātakī lakṣaṃ japedvai mānasaṃ dhiyā ।। pātakādardhameva syād upapātakināṃ smṛtam ।। brahmahatyā surāpānaṃ suvarṇasteyameva ca ।।
rudragāyatriyā grāhyaṃ gomūtraṃ kāpilaṃ dvijāḥ ।। tejo asi śuktam ityājyaṃ kāpilaṃ saṃharedbudhaḥ ।। gavyaṃ dadhi navaṃ sākṣāt kāpilaṃ vai pitāmaha ।। ekasthaṃ hemapātre vā kṛtvāghoreṇa rājate ।।
sakūrcaṃ sarvaratnāḍhyaṃ kṣiptvā tatraiva kāñcanam ।। ghṛtena caruṇā caiva samidbhiś ca tilais tathā ।। pratyekaṃ saptavāraṃ tu dravyālābhe ghṛtena tu ।। aṣṭadroṇaghṛtenaiva snāpya paścādviśodhya ca ।।
brāhmaṃ brahmajapaṃ kuryād ācamya ca yathāvidhi ।। vīrahā gurughātī ca mitraviśvāsaghātakaḥ ।। madyapo vṛṣalīsaktaḥ paradāravidharṣakaḥ ।। devapracyāvakaścaiva liṅgapradhvaṃsakas tathā ।।
vācikāni tathānyāni kāyikāni sahasraśaḥ ।। etadrahasyaṃ kathitam aghoreśaprasaṃgataḥ ।। tasmājjapeddvijo nityaṃ sarvapāpaviśuddhaye ।। viśvarūpa iti khyāto nāmataḥ paramādbhutaḥ ।।
brahmaṇaḥ putrakāmasya dhyāyataḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। viśvamālyāṃbaradharā viśvayajñopavītinī ।। tathāvidhaṃ sa bhagavān īśānaṃ parameśvaram ।। atha taṃ manasā dhyātvā yuktātmā vai pitāmahaḥ ।।
omīśāna namaste astu mahādeva namo astu te ।। namo astu sarvabhūtānām īśāna vṛṣavāhana ।। namo brahmādhipataye śivaṃ me astu sadāśiva ।। prapadye tvāṃ prapanno asmi sadyojātāya vai namaḥ ।।
bhavodbhava bhaveśāna māṃ bhajasva mahādyute ।। namo rudrāya kālāya kalanāya namo namaḥ ।। balāya balināṃ nityaṃ sadā vikaraṇāya te ।। sarvabhūteśvareśāya bhūtānāṃ damanāya ca ।।
vāmadevāya vāmāya namastubhyaṃ mahātmane ।। kālahantre namastubhyaṃ namastubhyaṃ mahātmane ।। yaḥ paṭhet sakṛdeveha brahmalokaṃ gamiṣyati ।। evaṃ dhyānagataṃ tatra praṇamantaṃ pitāmaham ।।
tatastu praṇato bhūtvā vāgviśuddhaṃ maheśvaram ।। yadidaṃ viśvarūpaṃ te viśvagauḥ śreyasīśvarī ।। kaiṣā bhagavatī devī catuṣpādā caturmukhī ।। caturhastā caturnetrā viśvarūpā kathaṃ smṛtā ।।
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā devadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ ।। rahasyaṃ sarvamantrāṇāṃ pāvanaṃ puṣṭivardhanam ।। evaṃ yo vartate kalpo viśvarūpastvasau mataḥ ।। tvattaḥ parataraṃ deva viṣṇunā tatpadaṃ śubham ।।
tadāprabhṛti kalpaś ca trayastriṃśattamo hyayam ।। purastāttava deveśa tacchṛṇuṣva mahāmate ।। māṇḍavyagotrastapasā mama putratvamāgataḥ ।। ṛtaṃ satyaṃ dayā brahma ahiṃsā sanmatiḥ kṣamā ।।
kāntirnītiḥ prathā medhā lajjā dṛṣṭiḥ sarasvatī ।। dvātriṃśatsuguṇā hyeṣā dvātriṃśākṣarasaṃjñayā ।। viṣṇorbhagavataścāpi tathānyeṣāmapi prabho ।। caturmukhī jagadyoniḥ prakṛtir gauḥ pratiṣṭhitā ।।
pradhānaṃ prakṛtiścaiva yāmāhustattvacintakāḥ ।। ajo ahaṃ māṃ viddhi tāṃ viśvarūpaṃ gāyatrīṃ gāṃ viśvarūpāṃ hi buddhyā ।। tataś ca pārśvagā devyāḥ sarvarūpakumārakāḥ ।। tatastena yathoktena yogena sumahaujasaḥ ।।
dharmopadeśamakhilaṃ kṛtvā yogamayaṃ dṛḍham ।। śiṣṭāś ca niyatātmānaḥ praviṣṭā rudramīśvaram ।। yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā dvijottamān ।। kathaṃ liṅgamabhūlliṅge samabhyarcyaḥ sa śaṅkaraḥ ।।
evaṃ devāś ca ṛṣayaḥ praṇipatya pitāmaham ।। liṅge maheśvaro rudraḥ samabhyarcyaḥ kathaṃ tviti ।। pradhānaṃ liṅgamākhyātaṃ liṅgī ca parameśvaraḥ ।। vaimānike gate sarge janalokaṃ saharṣibhiḥ ।।
caturyugasahasrānte satyalokaṃ gate surāḥ ।। śuṣke ca sthāvare sarve tv anāvṛṣṭyā ca sarvaśaḥ ।। gandharvādyāḥ krameṇaiva nirdagdhā bhānubhānubhiḥ ।। suṣvāpāṃbhasi yogātmā nirmalo nirupaplavaḥ ।।
sahasrabāhuḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvadevabhavodbhavaḥ ।। sattvena sarvago viṣṇuḥ sarvātmatve maheśvaraḥ ।। nārāyaṇo mahābāhuḥ sarvātmā sadasanmayaḥ ।। māyayā mohitastasya tamavocamamarṣitaḥ ।।
tadā hastaprahāreṇa tīvreṇa sa dṛḍhena tu ।। dadarśa nidrāviklinnanīrajāmalalocanaḥ ।। āha cotthāya bhagavān hasanmāṃ madhuraṃ sakṛt ।। tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā smitapūrvaṃ surarṣabhāḥ ।।
bhāṣase vatsa vatseti sargasaṃhārakāraṇam ।। kartāraṃ jagatāṃ sākṣāt prakṛteś ca pravartakam ।। viśvātmānaṃ vidhātāraṃ dhātāraṃ paṅkajekṣaṇam ।। so api māmāha jagatāṃ kartāhamiti lokaya ।।
vismṛto asi jagannāthaṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam ।। viṣṇumacyutamīśānaṃ viśvasya prabhavodbhavam ।। śṛṇu satyaṃ caturvaktra sarvadeveśvaro hyayam ।। ahameva paraṃ brahma paraṃ tattvaṃ pitāmaha ।।
yadyaddṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ sarvaṃ jagatyasmiṃścarācaram ।। mayā sṛṣṭaṃ purāvyaktaṃ caturviṃśatikaṃ svayam ।। prasādāddhi bhavānaṇḍāny anekānīha līlayā ।। tanmātrāpañcakaṃ tasmān manaḥ ṣaṣṭhendriyāṇi ca ।।
ityuktavati tasmiṃś ca mayi cāpi vacas tathā ।। pralayārṇavamadhye tu rajasā baddhavairayoḥ ।। vivādaśamanārthaṃ hi prabodhārthaṃ ca bhāsvaram ।। kṣayavṛddhivinirmuktam ādimadhyāntavarjitam ।।
tasya jvālāsahasreṇa mohito bhagavān hariḥ ।। adhogamiṣyāmyanalastaṃbhasyānupamasya ca ।। evaṃ vyāhṛtya viśvātmā svarūpamakarottadā ।। tadāprabhṛti māmāhurh aṃsaṃ haṃso virāḍiti ।।
suśveto hyanalākṣaś ca viśvataḥ pakṣasaṃyutaḥ ।। nārāyaṇo api viśvātmā nīlāñjanacayopamam ।। meruparvatavarṣmāṇaṃ gauratīkṣṇāgradaṃṣṭriṇam ।। hrasvapādaṃ vicitrāṅgaṃ jaitraṃ dṛḍham anaupamam ।।
evaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu tvaranviṣṇuradhogataḥ ।। tāvatkālaṃ gato hyūrdhvam ahamapyarisūdanaḥ ।। śrānto hyadṛṣṭvā tasyāntam ahaṅkārādadhogataḥ ।। sarvadevabhavastūrṇam utthitaḥ saḥ mahāvapuḥ ।।
māyayā mohitaḥ śaṃbhos tasthau saṃvignamānasaḥ ।। praṇipatya mayā sārdhaṃ sasmāra kimidaṃ tviti ।। omomiti suraśreṣṭhāḥ suvyaktaḥ plutalakṣaṇaḥ ।। liṅgasya dakṣiṇe bhāge tadāpaśyatsanātanam ।।
makāraṃ madhyataścaiva nādāntaṃ tasya caumiti ।। uttare pāvakaprakhyam ukāraṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥ ।। tasyopari tadāpaśyac chuddhasphaṭikavat prabhum ।। nirdvandvaṃ kevalaṃ śūnyaṃ bāhyābhyantaravarjitam ।।
ādimadhyāntarahitam ānandasyāpi kāraṇam ।। ṛgyajuḥsāmavedā vai mātrārūpeṇa mādhavaḥ ।। tadābhavadṛṣirveda ṛṣeḥ sāratamaṃ śubham ।। cintayā rahito rudro vāco yanmanasā saha ।।
ekākṣareṇa tadvācyam ṛtaṃ paramakāraṇam ।। ekākṣarādakārākhyo bhagavānkanakāṇḍajaḥ ।। ekākṣarānmakārākhyo bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ ।। makārākhyas tayor nityam anugrahakaro abhavat ।।
ukārākhyo hariryoniḥ pradhānapuruṣeśvaraḥ ।। bījī vibhajya cātmānaṃ svecchayā tu vyavasthitaḥ ।। ukārayonau nikṣiptam avardhata samantataḥ ।। anekābdaṃ tathā cāpsu divyamaṇḍaṃ vyavasthitam ।।
aṇḍam apsu sthitaṃ sākṣād ādyākhyeneśvareṇa tu ।। jajñe yaddyaustadaparaṃ pṛthivī pañcalakṣaṇā ।। sa sraṣṭā sarvalokānāṃ sa eva trividhaḥ prabhuḥ ।। yajuṣāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā ṛcaḥ sāmāni sādaram ।।
tato vijñāya deveśaṃ yathāvacchrutisaṃbhavaiḥ ।। āvayoḥ stutisaṃtuṣṭo liṅge tasminnirañjanaḥ ।। akārastasya mūrdhā tu lalāṭaṃ dīrghamucyate ।। ukāro dakṣiṇaṃ śrotram ūkāro vāmamucyate ।।
vāmaṃ kapolam ṝkāro ḷ ḹ nāsāpuṭe ubhe ।। okāraś ca tathaukāro dantapaṅktidvayaṃ kramāt ।। kādipañcākṣarāṇyasya pañca hastāni dakṣiṇe ।। ṭādipañcākṣaraṃ pādas tādipañcākṣaraṃ tathā ।।
bakāro vāmapārśvaṃ vai bhakāraṃ skandhamasya tat ।। yakārādisakārāntaṃ vibhorvai sapta dhātavaḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā umayā sārdhaṃ bhagavantaṃ maheśvaram ।। oṅkāraprabhavaṃ mantraṃ kalāpañcakasaṃyutam ।।
medhākaram abhūdbhūyaḥ sarvadharmārthasādhakam ।। caturviṃśativarṇāḍhyaṃ catuṣkalamanuttamam ।। abhicārikamatyarthaṃ trayastriṃśacchubhākṣaram ।। kalāṣṭakasamāyuktaṃ suśvetaṃ śāntikaṃ tathā ।।
sāmodbhavaṃ jagatyādyaṃ vṛddhisaṃhārakāraṇam ।। pañca mantrāṃs tathā labdhvā jajāpa bhagavān hariḥ ।। īśānamīśamukuṭaṃ puruṣāsyaṃ purātanam ।। sadyaḥ pādaṃ mahādevaṃ mahābhogīndrabhūṣaṇam ।।
brahmaṇo adhipatiṃ sargasthitisaṃhārakāraṇam ।। tuṣṭāva punariṣṭābhir vāgbhir varadamīśvaram ।। ukārāyādidevāya vidyādehāya vai namaḥ ।। sūryāgnisomavarṇāya yajamānāya vai namaḥ ।।
śivāya śivamantrāya sadyojātāya vedhase ।। aghorāyātighorāya sadyojātāya raṃhase ।। namo astu śrutipādāya ūrdhvaliṅgāya liṅgine ।। śivāya śivaliṅgāya vyāpine vyomavyāpine ।।
tejase tejasāṃ bhartre namastejo adhivyāpine ।। pṛthivyai cāntarikṣāya pṛthivīvyāpine namaḥ ।। gaṇādhipataye tubhyaṃ guhyādguhyatamāya te ।। śāśvatāya variṣṭhāya vārigarbhāya yogine ।।
goptre hartre sadā kartre nidhanāyeśvarāya ca ।। arūpāya surūpāya anaṅgāyāṅgahāriṇe ।। śvetāya śvetavarṇāya tuhinādricarāya ca ।। śvetāsyāya mahāsyāya namaste śvetalohita ।।
śatarūpavirūpāya namaḥ ketumate sadā ।। vipāśāya supāśāya namaste pāśanāśine ।। sumukhāya suvaktrāya durdamāya damāya ca ।। sanakāya namastubhyaṃ sanātana sanandana ।।
lokākṣiṇe tridhāmāya namo virajase sadā ।। sārasvatāya meghāya meghavāhana te namaḥ ।। namaḥ śivāya rudrāya pradhānāya namonamaḥ ।। saṃsārāya namastubhyaṃ namaḥ saṃsārahetave ।।
ātmane ṛṣaye tubhyaṃ svāmine viṣṇave namaḥ ।। oṅkārāya namastubhyaṃ sarvajñāya namo namaḥ ।। namo hiraṇyagarbhāya ādidevāya te namaḥ ।। mahādevāya devānām īśvarāya namo namaḥ ।।
brahmaṇe caiva bhūtānāṃ sarvajñāya namo namaḥ ।। citaye citirūpāya smṛtirūpāya vai namaḥ ।। śikharāya namastubhyaṃ nīlakaṇṭhāya vai namaḥ ।। ekādaśavibhedāya sthāṇave te namaḥ sadā ।।
yaśaskarāya devāya śaṅkarāyeśvarāya ca ।। hiraṇyabāhave tubhyaṃ namaste hemaretase ।। kapardine namastubhyaṃ nāgāṅgābharaṇāya ca ।। vīrarāmātirāmāya rāmanāthāya te vibho ।।
namaḥ pālādhipataye pālāśākṛntate namaḥ ।। namaḥ śrīkaṇṭhanāthāya namo likucapāṇaye ।। sāraṅgāya namastubhyaṃ rājahaṃsāya te namaḥ ।। sarpakuṇḍalamālāya kaṭisūtrīkṛtāhine ।।
virarāmeti saṃstutvā brahmaṇā sahito hariḥ ।। yaḥ paṭhecchrāvayedvāpi brāhmaṇān vedapāragān ।। tasmājjapetpaṭhennityaṃ śrāvayedbrāhmaṇāñchubhān ।। sarvapāpaviśuddhyarthaṃ viṣṇunā paribhāṣitam ।।
paśyatāṃ māṃ mahādevaṃ bhayaṃ sarvaṃ vimucyatām ।। ayaṃ me dakṣiṇe pārśve brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।। prīto ahaṃ yuvayoḥ samyag varaṃ dadmi yathepsitam ।। pasparśa subhagābhyāṃ tu kṛpayā tu kṛpānidhiḥ ।।
prāha nārāyaṇo nāthaṃ liṅgasthaṃ liṅgavarjitam ।। bhaktirbhavatu nau nityaṃ tvayi cāvyabhicāriṇī ।। brahmaṇe viṣṇave caiva śraddhāṃ śītāṃśubhūṣaṇaḥ ।। praṇipatya ca viśveśaṃ prāha mandataraṃ vaśī ।।
ihāgato bhavān yasmād vivādaśamanāya nau ।। praṇipatya sthitaṃ mūrdhnā kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ smayan ।। vatsa vatsa hare viṣṇo pālayaitaccarācaram ।। sargarakṣālayaguṇair niṣkalaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।।
pādme bhaviṣyati sutaḥ kalpe tava pitāmahaḥ ।। evamuktvā sa bhagavāṃs tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। liṅgavedī mahādevī liṅgaṃ sākṣānmaheśvaraḥ ।। yastu laiṅgaṃ paṭhennityam ākhyānaṃ liṅgasannidhau ।।
sa yāti śivatāṃ vipro nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। bhavaṃ ca dṛṣṭavāṃstena brahmaṇā puruṣottamaḥ ।। āsīdekārṇavaṃ ghoram avibhāgaṃ tamomayam ।। jīmūtābho ambujākṣaś ca kirīṭī śrīpatirhariḥ ।।
aṣṭabāhurmahāvakṣā lokānāṃ yonirucyate ।। phaṇāsahasrakalitaṃ tamapratimavarcasam ।। tasminmahati paryaṅke śete caikārṇave prabhuḥ ।। ātmārāmeṇa krīḍārthaṃ līlayākliṣṭakarmaṇā ।।
vajradaṇḍaṃ mahotsedhaṃ nābhyāṃ sṛṣṭaṃ tu puṣkaram ।। hemagarbhāṇḍajo brahmā rukmavarṇo hyatīndriyaḥ ।। śriyā yuktena divyena suśubhena sugandhinā ।। savismayamathāgamya saumyasampannayā girā ।।
atha tasyācyutaḥ śrutvā brahmaṇastu śubhaṃ vacaḥ ।। pratyuvācottaraṃ caiva kalpe kalpe pratiśrayaḥ ।। dyaurantarikṣaṃ bhūścaiva paraṃ padamahaṃ bhuvaḥ ।। kastvaṃ khalu samāyātaḥ samīpaṃ bhagavānkutaḥ ।।
ko bhavān viśvamūrtirvai kartavyaṃ kiṃ ca te mayā ।। māyayā mohitaḥ śaṃbhor avijñāya janārdanam ।। yathā bhavāṃstathaivāham ādikartā prajāpatiḥ ।। anujñātaś ca te nātha vaikuṇṭho viśvasaṃbhavaḥ ।।
imānaṣṭādaśa dvīpān sasamudrān saparvatān ।। brahmaṇastambhaparyantaṃ saptalokān sanātanān ।। aho asya tapaso vīryam ityuktvā ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। tato varṣasahasrānte nāntaṃ hi dadṛśe yadā ।।
nārāyaṇo jagaddhātā pitāmahamathābravīt ।। nāhamantaṃ prapaśyāmi udarasya tavānagha ।। bhagavānevamevāhaṃ śāśvataṃ hi mamodaram ।। tataḥ prāhlādinīṃ vāṇīṃ śrutvā tasyābhinandya ca ।।
tāneva lokān garbhasthān apaśyat satyavikramaḥ ।। vibhurmanaḥ kartumiyeṣa cāśu sukhaṃ prasupto ahamiti pracintya ।। sūkṣmaṃ kṛtvātmano rūpaṃ nābhyāṃ dvāramavindata ।। ujjahārātmano rūpaṃ puṣkarāccaturānanaḥ ।।
brahmā svayaṃbhūrbhagavāñ jagadyoniḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। vartamāne tu saṃgharṣe madhye tasyārṇavasya tu ।। śūlapāṇirmahādevo hemavīrāṃbaracchadaḥ ।। śīghraṃ vikramatastasya padbhyām ākrāntapīḍitāḥ ।।
atyuṣṇaścātiśītaś ca vāyustatra vavau punaḥ ।। abbindavaś ca śītoṣṇāḥ kampayantyaṃbujaṃ bhṛśam ।। etadevaṃvidhaṃ vākyaṃ pitāmahamukhodgatam ।। kiṃ nu khalvatra me nābhyāṃ bhūtamanyatkṛtālayam ।।
ityevaṃ manasā dhyātvā pratyuvācedamuttaram ।। kiṃ mayā ca kṛtaṃ deva yanmāṃ priyamanuttamam ।। evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ deveśaṃ lokayātrānugaṃ tataḥ ।। yo asau tavodaraṃ pūrvaṃ praviṣṭo ahaṃ tvadicchayā ।।
tathaiva dṛṣṭāḥ kārtsnyena mayā lokāstavodare ।। tvayā matsarabhāvena māṃ vaśīkartumicchatā ।। tato mayā mahābhāga saṃcintya svena tejasā ।। mā bhūtte manaso alpo api vyāghāto ayaṃ kathaṃcana ।।
yanmayānantaraṃ kāryaṃ brūhi kiṃ karavāṇyaham ।। anavadyāṃ priyāmiṣṭāṃ śivāṃ vāṇīṃ pitāmahāt ।। na hyevamīdṛśaṃ kāryaṃ mayādhyavasitaṃ tava ।। āśu dvārāṇi sarvāṇi ghāṭitāni mayātmanaḥ ।।
sarvaṃ marṣaya kalyāṇa yanmayāpakṛtaṃ tava ।। nāhaṃ bhavantaṃ śaknomi soḍhuṃ tejomayaṃ gurum ।। putro bhava mamārighna mudaṃ prāpsyasi śobhanām ।। sa tvaṃ ca no mahāyogī tvamīḍyaḥ praṇavātmakaḥ ।।
padmayoniriti hyevaṃ khyāto nāmnā bhaviṣyasi ।। tataḥ sa bhagavāndevo varaṃ dattvā kirīṭine ।। pratyāsannam athāyāntaṃ bālārkābhaṃ mahānanam ।। aprameyo mahāvaktro daṃṣṭrī dhvastaśiroruhaḥ ।।
lokaprabhuḥ svayaṃ sākṣād vikṛto muñjamekhalī ।। kaḥ khalveṣa pumān viṣṇo tejorāśir mahādyutiḥ ।। tenaivamukto bhagavān viṣṇurbrahmāṇamabravīt ।। vegena mahatākāśe apyutthitāś ca jalaśayāḥ ।।
ghrāṇajena ca vātena kampyamānaṃ tvayā saha ।। samāgato bhavānīśo hy anādiścāntakṛtprabhuḥ ।। tataḥ kruddho ambujābhākṣaṃ brahmā provāca keśavam ।। brahmāṇaṃ lokakartāraṃ māṃ na vetsi sanātanam ।।
tasya tatkrodhajaṃ vākyaṃ śrutvā harirabhāṣata ।। mahāyogendhano dharmo durādharṣo varapradaḥ ।। bījī khalveṣa bījānāṃ jyotirekaḥ prakāśate ।। pradhānamavyayo yonir avyaktaṃ prakṛtistamaḥ ।।
yaḥ kaḥ sa iti duḥkhārtair dṛśyate yatibhiḥ śivaḥ ।। sa evamukto viśvātmā brahmā viṣṇumapṛcchata ।। etanme sūkṣmamavyaktaṃ saṃśayaṃ chettumarhasi ।। imaṃ paramasādṛśyaṃ praśnam abhyavadaddhariḥ ।।
mahataḥ paramaṃ dhāma śivam adhyātmināṃ padam ।। niṣkalastatra yo avyaktaḥ sakalaś ca maheśvaraḥ ।। purā liṅgodbhavaṃ bījaṃ prathamaṃ tvādisargikam ।। hiraṇmayamakūpāre yonyāmaṇḍamajāyata ।।
ante varṣasahasrasya vāyunā taddvidhā kṛtam ।। ulbaṃ tasya mahotsedho yo asau kanakaparvataḥ ।। hiraṇyagarbho bhagavāṃs tv abhijajñe caturmukhaḥ ।। ko ahamityapi ca dhyāte kumārāste abhavaṃstadā ।।
bhūyo varṣasahasrānte tata evātmajāstava ।। śrīmānsanatkumāraś ca ṛbhuścaivordhvaretasau ।। utpannāḥ samakālaṃ te buddhyātīndriyadarśanāḥ ।। nārapsyante ca karmāṇi tāpatrayavivarjitāḥ ।।
jīvanaṃ maraṇaṃ caiva saṃbhavaś ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। viditvā cāgamaṃ sarvam avaśyaṃ bhavitavyatām ।। trayastu trīn guṇān hitvā cātmajāḥ sanakādayaḥ ।। tatasteṣu pravṛtteṣu sanakādiṣu vai triṣu ।।
evaṃ kalpe tu vaivṛtte saṃjñā naśyati te anagha ।। sarveṣāṃ hyaiśvarī māyā jāgṛtiḥ samudāhṛtā ।। tasya cedaṃ hi māhātmyaṃ viddhi devavarasya ha ।। mahādevaṃ mahābhūtaṃ bhūtānāṃ varadaṃ prabhum ।।
tvāṃ ca māṃ caiva saṃkruddho niḥśvāsānnirdahedayam ।। ahaṃ tvāmagrataḥ kṛtvā stoṣyāmyanalasaprabham ।। atītaiś ca bhaviṣyaiś ca vartamānaistathaiva ca ।। namastubhyaṃ bhagavate suvratānantatejase ।।
sumeḍhrāyārcyameḍhrāya daṇḍine rūkṣaretase ।। namo mānyāya pūjyāya sadyojātāya vai namaḥ ।। namaste hyasmadādīnāṃ bhūtānāṃ prabhave namaḥ ।। prabhave karmadānānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ prabhave namaḥ ।।
namo dhruvanibaddhānām ṛṣīṇāṃ prabhave namaḥ ।। vaidyutāśanimeghānāṃ garjitaprabhave namaḥ ।। adrīṇāṃ prabhave caiva varṣāṇāṃ prabhave namaḥ ।। mahauṣadhīnāṃ prabhave vṛkṣāṇāṃ prabhave namaḥ ।।
prabhave ca parārdhasya parasya prabhave namaḥ ।। kṣaṇānāṃ prabhave caiva lavānāṃ prabhave namaḥ ।। ṛtūnāṃ prabhave tubhyaṃ saṃkhyāyāḥ prabhave namaḥ ।। namaḥ purāṇaprabhave sargāṇāṃ prabhave namaḥ ।।
caturvidhasya sargasya prabhave anantacakṣuṣe ।। namo viśvasya prabhave brahmādhipataye namaḥ ।। namo vratādhipataye vratānāṃ prabhave namaḥ ।। pitṝṇāṃ pataye caiva paśūnāṃ pataye namaḥ ।।
namaḥ paśūnāṃ pataye govṛṣendradhvajāya ca ।। daityadānavasaṃghānāṃ rakṣasāṃ pataye namaḥ ।। garuḍoragasarpāṇāṃ pakṣiṇāṃ pataye namaḥ ।। gokarṇāya ca goptre ca śaṅkukarṇāya vai namaḥ ।।
namaḥ surāṇāṃ pataye gaṇānāṃ pataye namaḥ ।। namo astu lakṣmīpataye śrīpāya kṣitipāya ca ।। dīptaśṛṅgaikaśṛṅgāya vṛṣabhāya kakudmine ।। atītāya bhaviṣyāya vartamānāya vai namaḥ ।।
varadāya vareṇyāya puruṣāya mahātmane ।। janāya ca namastubhyaṃ tapase varadāya ca ।। namo bandhāya mokṣāya svargāya narakāya ca ।। pratyudīrṇāya dīptāya tattvāyātiguṇāya ca ।।
hutāya upahūtāya prahutaprāśitāya ca ।। sadasyāya namaścaiva dakṣiṇāvabhṛthāya ca ।। namaḥ puṣṭipradānāya suśīlāya suśīline ।। suvarcase ca vīryāya śūrāya hyajitāya ca ।।
namo bhūtāya bhavyāya mahate cābhayāya ca ।। adhare mahate caiva namaḥ sastupatāya ca ।। viśvāya viśvarūpāya viśvataḥ śirase namaḥ ।। namo havyāya kavyāya havyavāhāya vai namaḥ ।।
suvīrāya sughorāya akṣobhyakṣobhaṇāya ca ।। namo buddhāya śuddhāya vistṛtāya matāya ca ।। varṣate jvalate caiva vāyave śiśirāya ca ।। namo namaḥ suvarṇāya tapanīyanibhāya ca ।।
vṛṣṭighnāya namaścaiva namaḥ saumyekṣaṇāya ca ।। piśitāya piśaṅgāya pītāya ca niṣaṅgiṇe ।। nama ījyāya pūjyāya upajīvyāya vai namaḥ ।। namo bhūtāya satyāya satyāsatyāya vai namaḥ ।।
namo gaurāya śyāmāya kadrave lohitāya ca ।। namaḥ kamalahastāya digvāsāya kapardine ।। namo rūpāya gandhāya śāśvatāyākṣatāya ca ।। durgamāya maheśāya krodhāya kapilāya ca ।।
sikatyāya pravāhyāya sthitāya prasṛtāya ca ।। citrāya citraveṣāya citravarṇāya medhase ।। namaḥ kṣāntāya dāntāya vajrasaṃhananāya ca ।। rakṣoghnāya viṣaghnāya śitikaṇṭhordhvamanyave ।।
lelihāya kṛtāntāya tigmāyudhadharāya ca ।। anāmayāya sarvāya mahākālāya vai namaḥ ।। mṛgavyādhāya dakṣāya dakṣayajñāntakāya ca ।। puraghnāya suśastrāya dhanvine atha paraśvadhe ।।
kāmadāya variṣṭhāya kāmāṅgadahanāya ca ।। daityānāmantakeśāya daityākrandakarāya ca ।। śmaśānaratinityāya namo astūlmukadhāriṇe ।। prahīṇaśokairvividhair bhūtaiḥ parivṛtāya ca ।।
jaṭine muṇḍine caiva vyālayajñopavītine ।। manyave gītaśīlāya munibhir gāyate namaḥ ।। vibhīṣaṇāya bhīṣmāya bhagapramathanāya ca ।। namo muktāṭṭahāsāya kṣveḍitāsphoṭitāya ca ।।
namo mṛḍāya śvasate dhāvate adhiṣṭhite namaḥ ।। valgate krīḍate caiva lambodaraśarīriṇe ।। nama unmattadehāya kiṅkiṇīkāya vai namaḥ ।। aprameyāya goptre ca dīptāyānirguṇāya ca ।।
namastokāya tanave guṇairapramitāya ca ।। lokadhātrī tviyaṃ bhūmiḥ pādau sajjanasevitau ।। madhye antarikṣaṃ vistīrṇaṃ tārāgaṇavibhūṣitam ।। diśo daśabhujāstubhyaṃ keyūrāṅgadabhūṣitāḥ ।।
kaṇṭhaste śobhate śrīmān hemasūtravibhūṣitaḥ ।। padmamālākṛtoṣṇīṣaṃ śiro dyauḥ śobhate adhikam ।। auṣṇyamagnau tathā śaityam apsu śabdo ambare tathā ।। japo japyo mahādevo mahāyogomaheśvaraḥ ।।
taponidhirguhagurur nandano nandavardhanaḥ ।। boddhavyo bodhitā netā durdharṣo duṣprakampanaḥ ।। ghaṇṭāpriyo dhvajī chattrī pinākī dhvajinīpatiḥ ।। aghasmaro anaghaḥ śūro devarājo arimardanaḥ ।।
agniḥ sadārṇavāṃbhastvaṃ pibannapi na tṛpyase ।। brahmacāri cāgādhaś ca brahmaṇyaḥ śiṣṭapūjitaḥ ।। prīte tvayi mahādeva vayaṃ prītā bhavāmahe ।। sāṃkhyāḥ prakṛteḥ paramaṃ tvāṃ viditvā kṣīṇadhyānāstvāmamṛtyuṃ viśanti ।।
ye cāpyanye tvāṃ prasannā viśuddhāḥ svakarmabhiste divyabhogā bhavanti ।। kīrtitaṃ tava māhātmyam apārasya mahātmanaḥ ।। ya idaṃ kīrtayedbhaktyā brahmanārāyaṇastavam ।। aśvamedhāyutaṃ kṛtvā yatphalaṃ tadavāpnuyāt ।।
japedvāpi vinirmukto brahmalokaṃ sa gacchati ।। kīrtayedvā satāṃ madhye sa yāti brahmaṇo antikam ।। prahṛṣṭavadano atyartham abhavatsatyakīrtanāt ।। pinākī khaṇḍaparaśuḥ suprītastu trilocanaḥ ।।
jānannapi mahādevaḥ krīḍāpūrvamathābravīt ।। sametāvaṃbujābhakṣāv asmin ghore mahāplave ।। bhagavān kiṃ tu yatte adya na vijñānaṃ tvayā vibho ।। tayostadvacanaṃ śrutvā abhinandyābhimānya ca ।।
bho bho hiraṇyagarbha tvāṃ tvāṃ ca kṛṣṇa bravīmyaham ।। bhavantau hṛdayasyāsya mama hṛdyatarāvubhau ।। athovāca mahābhāgo viṣṇurbhavamidaṃ vacaḥ ।। tvayi me supratiṣṭhā tu bhaktirbhavatu śaṅkaraḥ ।।
pradadau ca mahādevo bhaktiṃ nijapadāṃbuje ।। tadevaṃ svasti te vatsa gamiṣyāmyaṃbujekṣaṇa ।। anugṛhyāspṛśaddevo brahmāṇaṃ parameśvaraḥ ।। matsamastvaṃ na saṃdeho vatsa bhaktaś ca me bhavān ।।
evamuktvā tu bhagavāṃs tato antardhānamīśvaraḥ ।। avāpya saṃjñāṃ govindāt padmayoniḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। tasyaivaṃ tapyamānasya na kiṃcit samavartata ।। krodhāviṣṭasya netrābhyāṃ prāpatannaśrubindavaḥ ।।
mahābhāgā mahāsattvāḥ svastikairapyalaṃkṛtāḥ ।। sarpāṃstānagrajāndṛṣṭvā brahmātmānam anindayat ।। lokavaināśikī jajñe ādāveva prajā mama ।। mūrcchābhiparitāpena jahau prāṇānprajāpatiḥ ।।
athaikādaśa te rudrā rudanto abhyakramaṃs tathā ।। ye rudrāste khalu prāṇā ye prāṇāste tadātmakāḥ ।। atyugrasya mahattvasya sādhurācaritasya ca ।। labdhvāsūn bhagavānbrahma devadevamumāpatim ।।
sarvalokamayaṃ devaṃ dṛṣṭvā stutvā pitāmahaḥ ।। uvāca vacanaṃ śarvaṃ sadyāditvaṃ kathaṃ vibho ।। brahmarūpī prabodhārthaṃ brahmāṇaṃ prāha sasmitam ।। śvetoṣṇīṣaḥ śvetamālyaḥ śvetāṃbaradharaḥ sitaḥ ।।
tena nāmnā ca vikhyātaḥ śvetakalpastadā hyasau ।। śvetavarṇā tadā hyāsīd gāyatrī brahmasaṃjñitā ।। vijñātaḥ svena tapasā sadyojātatvamāgataḥ ।। tasmādguhyatvamāpannaṃ ye vetsyanti dvijātayaḥ ।।
yadā caiva punastvāsīl lohito nāma nāmataḥ ।। tadā lohitamāṃsāsthilohitakṣīrasaṃbhavā ।। tato asyā lohitatvena varṇasya ca viparyayāt ।। tatrāpi ca mahāsattva tvayāhaṃ niyatātmanā ।।
tataś ca vāmadeveti khyātiṃ yāto asmi bhūtale ।। rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham ।। matkṛtena ca nāmnā vai pītakalpo abhavattadā ।। pītavarṇā tadā hyāsīd gāyatrī brahmasaṃjñitā ।।
yasmādahaṃ tairvijñāto yogatatparamānasaiḥ ।। tasmāttatpuruṣatvaṃ vai mamaitatkanakāṇḍaja ।। vetsyanti tapasā yuktā vimalā brahmasaṃgatāḥ ।। yadāhaṃ punarevāsaṃ kṛṣṇavarṇo bhayānakaḥ ।।
tatrāhaṃ kālasaṃkāśaḥ kālo lokaprakālakaḥ ।। matprasūtā ca gāyatrī kṛṣṇāṅgī kṛṣṇalohitā ।। tasmād ghoratvamāpannaṃ ye māṃ vetsyanti bhūtale ।। punaś ca viśvarūpatvaṃ yadā brahmanmamābhavat ।।
viśvarūpā ca saṃvṛttā gāyatrī lokadhāriṇī ।। teṣāṃ śivaś ca saumyaś ca bhaviṣyāmi sadaiva hi ।। viśvarūpā tathā ceyaṃ sāvitrī samudāhṛtā ।। catvāraste mayā khyātāḥ putra vai lokasaṃmatāḥ ।।
sarvabhakṣā ca medhyā ca varṇataś ca bhaviṣyati ।। yasmādvedāś ca vedyaṃ ca caturdhā vai bhaviṣyati ।। dharmasya pādāścatvāraś catvāro mama putrakāḥ ।। caturdhāvasthitaścaiva catuṣpādo bhaviṣyati ।।
janastapaś ca satyaṃ ca viṣṇulokastataḥ param ।। bhūrbhuvaḥ svarmahaścaiva pādāścatvāra eva ca ।। svarloko vai tṛtīyaś ca caturthastu mahas tathā ।। satyaṃ tu saptamo loko hy apunarbhavagāminām ।।
skāndamaumaṃ tathā sthānaṃ sarvasiddhisamanvitam ।। nirmamā nirahaṅkārāḥ kāmakrodhavivarjitāḥ ।। yasmāccatuṣpadā hyeṣā tvayā dṛṣṭā sarasvatī ।। aumaṃ māheśvaraṃ caiva tasmāddṛṣṭā catuṣpadā ।।
tataścaiṣāṃ bhaviṣyanti catvāraste payodharāḥ ।। jīvaḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ brahman punaḥ pītastanāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। catuṣpādā bhaviṣyanti śvetatvaṃ cāsya tena tat ।। dṛṣṭā punastathaivaiṣā sāvitrī lokabhāvinī ।।
tasmācceyamajā bhūtvā sarvavarṇā maheśvarī ।। tasmācca viśvarūpatvaṃ prajānāṃ vai bhaviṣyati ।। amogharetāḥ sarvatra mukhe cāsya hutāśanaḥ ।। tapasā bhāvitātmāno ye māṃ drakṣyanti vai dvijāḥ ।।
rajastamobhyāṃ nirmuktās tyaktvā mānuṣyakaṃ vapuḥ ।। ityevamukto bhagavān brahmā rudreṇa vai dvijāḥ ।। ya evaṃ bhagavān vidvān gāyatryā vai maheśvaram ।। tasya dehi paraṃ sthānaṃ tathāstviti ca so abravīt ।।
sa yāti brahmasāyujyaṃ vacanād brahmaṇaḥ prabhoḥ ।। punaḥ praṇamya deveśaṃ rudramāha prajāpatiḥ ।। umādhava mahādeva namo lokābhivandita ।। yā imāste mahādeva tanavo lokavanditāḥ ।।
kena vā tapasā deva dhyānayogena kena vā ।। tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā śarvaḥ samprekṣya taṃ puraḥ ।। tapasā naiva vṛttena dānadharmaphalena ca ।। na vedādhyayanairvāpi na vittena na vedanaiḥ ।।
saptame caiva vārāhe tatastasminpitāmaha ।। manurvaivasvataścaiva tava pautro bhaviṣyati ।। anugrahārthaṃ lokānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ hitāya ca ।। yugapravṛttyā ca tadā tasmiṃś ca prathame yuge ।।
tadāhaṃ brāhmaṇārthāya kalau tasmin yugāntike ।। himavacchikhare ramye chāgale parvatottame ।। śvetaḥ śvetaśikhaścaiva śvetāsyaḥ śvetalohitaḥ ।। tataste brahmabhūyiṣṭhā dṛṣṭvā brahmagatiṃ parām ।।
tataḥ punaryadā brahman dvitīye dvāpare prabhuḥ ।। tadā lokahitārthāya sutāro nāma nāmataḥ ।। tatrāpi mama te śiṣyā nāmataḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। prāpya yogaṃ tathā dhyānaṃ sthāpya brahma ca bhūtale ।।
tṛtīye dvāpare caiva yadā vyāsastu bhārgavaḥ ।। tatrāpi ca bhaviṣyanti catvāro mama putrakāḥ ।। te api tenaiva mārgeṇa yogoktena mahaujasaḥ ।। caturthe dvāpare caiva yadā vyāso aṅgirāḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
tatrāpi mama te putrāś catvāro api tapodhanāḥ ।। sumukho durmukhaścaiva durdaro duratikramaḥ ।। te api tenaiva mārgeṇa yogayuktā mahaujasaḥ ।। pañcame dvāpare caiva vyāsastu savitā yadā ।।
anugrahārthaṃ lokānāṃ yogātmaikakalāgatiḥ ।। śiṣyā mama bhaviṣyanti yogātmāno dṛḍhavratāḥ ।। vibhuḥ sanatkumāraś ca nirmamā nirahaṃkṛtāḥ ।। parīvarte punaḥ ṣaṣṭhe mṛtyurvyāso yadā vibhuḥ ।।
tatrāpi mama te śiṣyā yogātmāno dṛḍhavratāḥ ।। sudhāmā virajāścaiva śaṅkhapādraja eva ca ।। te api tenaiva mārgeṇa dhyānayogasamanvitāḥ ।। saptame parivarte tu yadā vyāsaḥ śatakratuḥ ।।
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi kalau tasmin yugāntike ।। tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti yuge tathā ।। te api tenaiva mārgeṇa dhyānayogaparāyaṇāḥ ।। vasiṣṭhaścāṣṭame vyāsaḥ parīvarte bhaviṣyati ।।
tatrāpi mama te putrā yogātmāno dṛḍhavratāḥ ।। kapilaścāsuriścaiva tathā pañcaśikho muniḥ ।। prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ jñānino dagdhakilbiṣāḥ ।। parivarte tu navame vyāsaḥ sārasvato yadā ।।
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti mahaujasaḥ ।। bhaviṣyanti mahātmāno brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ ।। sarve tapobalotkṛṣṭāḥ śāpānugrahakovidāḥ ।। rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham ।।
yadā bhaviṣyate vipras tadāhaṃ bhavitā muniḥ ।। nāmnā bhṛgostu śikharaṃ prathitaṃ devapūjitam ।। balabandhurnirāmitraḥ ketuśṛṅgastapodhanaḥ ।। rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti tapasā dagdhakilbiṣāḥ ।।
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi gaṅgādvāre kalau tathā ।। tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti mahaujasaḥ ।। prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokaṃ gatā hi te ।। bhaviṣyati mahātejā vyāsastu kavisattamaḥ ।।
haitukaṃ vanamāsādya atrirnāmnā pariśrutaḥ ।। bhaviṣyanti mahāyogā rudralokaparāyaṇāḥ ।। prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokaṃ gatā hi te ।। dharmo nārāyaṇo nāma vyāsastu bhavitā yadā ।।
vālakhilyāśrame puṇye parvate gandhamādane ।। sudhāmā kāśyapaścaiva vāsiṣṭho virajāstathā ।। prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokaṃ gatā hi te ।। tatrāpi punarevāhaṃ bhaviṣyāmi yugāntike ।।
bhaviṣyati mahāpuṇyaṃ gautamaṃ nāma tadvanam ।। atrirdevasadaścaiva śravaṇo atha śraviṣṭhakaḥ ।। prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya te gatāḥ ।। traiyyāruṇiryadā vyāso dvāpare samapadyata ।।
tatra vedaśiro nāma astraṃ tatpārameśvaram ।। himavatpṛṣṭhamāsādya sarasvatyāṃ nagottame ।। kuṇiś ca kuṇibāhuś ca kuśarīraḥ kunetrakaḥ ।। prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya te gatāḥ ।।
tatra yogapradānāya bhaktānāṃ ca yatātmanām ।। bhaviṣyati supuṇyaṃ ca gokarṇaṃ nāma tadvanam ।। kāśyapo hyuśanāścaiva cyavano atha bṛhaspatiḥ ।। prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ gantāro rudrameva hi ।।
yadā bhaviṣyati vyāso nāmnā devakṛtañjayaḥ ।। himavacchikhare ramye mahottuṅge mahālaye ।। tatrāpi mama te putrā yogajñā brahmavādinaḥ ।। utathyo vāmadevaś ca mahāyogo mahābalaḥ ।।
bhaviṣyanti tadā kāle sarve te dhyānayuñjakāḥ ।। mahālaye padaṃ nyastaṃ dṛṣṭvā yānti śivaṃ padam ।। dhyāne manaḥ samādhāya vimalāḥ śuddhabuddhayaḥ ।। gatvā mahālayaṃ puṇyaṃ dṛṣṭvā māheśvaraṃ padam ।।
ātmānamekaviṃśaṃ tu tārayitvā mahālaye ।। tato aṣṭādaśame caiva parivarte yadā vibho ।। tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi śikhaṇḍī nāma nāmataḥ ।। himavacchikhare ramye śikhaṇḍī nāma parvataḥ ।।
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti tapodhanāḥ ।। yogātmāno mahātmānaḥ sarve te vedapāragāḥ ।। atha ekonaviṃśe tu parivarte kramāgate ।। tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi jaṭāmālī ca nāmataḥ ।।
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti mahaujasaḥ ।। īśvarā yogadharmāṇaḥ sarve te hyūrdhvaretasaḥ ।। tato viṃśatimaścaiva parivarto yadā tadā ।। tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi aṭṭahāsastu nāmataḥ ।।
tatraiva himavatpṛṣṭhe aṭṭahāso mahāgiriḥ ।। tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti mahaujasaḥ ।। sumanturbarbarī vidvān kabandhaḥ kuśikaṃdharaḥ ।। ekaviṃśe punaḥ prāpte parivarte kramāgate ।।
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi dāruko nāma nāmataḥ ।। tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti mahaujasaḥ ।। yogātmāno mahātmāno niyatā ūrdhvaretasaḥ ।। dvāviṃśe parivarte tu vyāsaḥ śuṣmāyaṇo yadā ।।
nāmnā vai lāṅgalī bhīmo yatra devāḥ savāsavāḥ ।। tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti sudhārmikāḥ ।। prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ te api dhyānaparāyaṇāḥ ।। parivarte trayoviṃśe tṛṇabinduryadā muniḥ ।।
śveto nāma mahākāyo muniputrastu dhārmikaḥ ।। tena kālañjaro nāma bhaviṣyati sa parvataḥ ।। uśiko bṛhadaśvaś ca devalaḥ kavireva ca ।। parivarte caturviṃśe vyāsa ṛkṣo yadā vibho ।।
śūlī nāma mahāyogī naimiṣe devavandite ।। śālihotro agniveśaś ca yuvanāśvaḥ śaradvasuḥ ।। pañcaviṃśe punaḥ prāpte parivarte kramāgate ।। tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi daṇḍī muṇḍīśvaraḥ prabhuḥ ।।
chagalaḥ kuṇḍakarṇaś ca kubhāṇḍaś ca pravāhakaḥ ।। ṣaḍviṃśe parivarte tu yadā vyāsaḥ parāśaraḥ ।। puraṃ bhadravaṭaṃ prāpya kalau tasmin yugāntike ।। ulūko vidyutaścaiva śaṃbūko hyāśvalāyanaḥ ।।
saptaviṃśe punaḥ prāpte parivarte kramāgate ।। tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi somaśarmā dvijottamaḥ ।। tatrāpi mama te śiṣyā bhaviṣyanti tapodhanāḥ ।। yogātmāno mahātmāno vimalāḥ śuddhabuddhayaḥ ।।
aṣṭāviṃśe punaḥ prāpte parivarte kramāgate ।। yadā bhaviṣyati vyāso nāmnā dvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ ।। vasudevādyaduśreṣṭho vāsudevo bhaviṣyati ।। lokavismayanārthāya brahmacāriśarīrakaḥ ।।
brāhmaṇānāṃ hitārthāya praviṣṭo yogamāyayā ।। bhaviṣyāmi tadā brahmaṃl lakulī nāma nāmataḥ ।। bhaviṣyati suvikhyātaṃ yāvad bhūmir dhariṣyati ।। kuśikaś caiva gargaś ca mitraḥ kauruṣya eva ca ।।
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ vimalā hyūrdhvaretasaḥ ।। ete pāśupatāḥ siddhā bhasmoddhūlitavigrahāḥ ।। bhaktyā mayi ca yogena dhyānaniṣṭhā jitendriyāḥ ।। svarūpajñānasiddhyarthaṃ yogaṃ pāśupataṃ mahat ।।
na nivṛttimupāyānti vinā pañcākṣarīṃ kvacit ।। tadā sa mukto mantavyaḥ pakvaṃ phalamiva sthitaḥ ।। na sāṃkhye pañcarātre vā na prāpnoti gatiṃ kadā ।। manvādikṛṣṇaparyantam aṣṭāviṃśad yugakramāt ।।
bhaviṣyati tadā kalpe kṛṣṇadvaipāyano yadā ।। rudrāvatāraṃ bhagavān praṇipatya maheśvaram ।। sarve viṣṇumayā devāḥ sarve viṣṇumayā gaṇāḥ ।। ityevaṃ satataṃ vedā gāyanti nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
tava praṇāmaparamaḥ kathaṃ devo hyabhūtprabhuḥ ।। prapibanniva cakṣurbhyāṃ prītastatpraśnagauravāt ।। bhavānnārāyaṇaścaiva śakraḥ sākṣātsurottamaḥ ।। svaṃsvaṃ padaṃ vibho prāptās tasmāt sampūjayanti te ।।
ātmano yajate nityaṃ śraddhayā bhagavānprabhuḥ ।। punaḥ samprekṣya deveśaṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। sraṣṭuṃ tvaśeṣaṃ bhagavāṃl labdhasaṃjñastu śaṅkarāt ।। vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ romaharṣaṇa sāṃpratam ।।
aṅkasthāmāha deveśo liṅgārcanavidhiṃ kramāt ।। śrutvākhilaṃ purā prāha brahmaputrāya suvratāḥ ।। tasmādvyāso mahātejāḥ śrutavāñchrutisaṃmitam ।। śrutavān tatpravakṣyāmi snānādyaṃ cārcanāvidhim ।।
sarvapāpaharaṃ sākṣāc chivena kathitaṃ purā ।। brahmakūrcaṃ ca pītvā tu sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। hitāya brāhmaṇādyānāṃ caturmukhasutottama ।। mantrasnānaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā pūjayetparameśvaram ।।
bhāvaśuddhaścarecchaucam anyathā na samācaret ।। snātvāpi bhāvaduṣṭaścen na śudhyati na saṃśayaḥ ।। prasuptaṃ tamasā jñānabhānorbhāsā tadā śuciḥ ।। ādāya tīre niḥkṣipya snānatīrthe kuśāni ca ।।
dravyaistu tīradeśasthais tataḥ snānaṃ samācaret ।। mṛdādāya tataścānyad vastraṃ snātvā hyanulbaṇam ।। kapilāgomayenaiva khasthenaiva tu lepayet ।। śuklavastraparīdhāno bhūtvā snānaṃ samācaret ।।
sampūjya manasā devaṃ dhyānayajñena vai bhavam ।। punarācamya vidhivad abhimantrya mahājalam ।। tattoye bhānusomāgnimaṇḍalaṃ ca smaredvaśī ।। praviśya tīrthamadhye tu punaḥ puṇyavivṛddhaye ।।
sakuśena sapuṣpeṇa jalenaivābhiṣecayet ।। taratsamandīvargādyais tathā śāntidvayena ca ।। tattanmantrādhidevānāṃ svarūpaṃ ca ṛṣīn smaran ।। dhyāyecca tryambakaṃ devaṃ hṛdi pañcāsyam īśvaram ।।
pavitrahastaḥ svāsīnaḥ śucau deśe yathāvidhi ।। pibetprakṣipya tristoyaṃ cakrī bhūtvā hyatandritaḥ ।। evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ snānācamanamuttamam ।। sarveṣāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ tu hitārthe dvijasattamāḥ ।।
āyātu varadā devīty anenaiva maheśvarīm ।। prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā samāsīnaḥ sthito api vā ।। gāyatrīṃ praṇavenaiva trividheṣvekamācaret ।। uttame śikhare devīty uktvodvāsya ca mātaram ।।
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā prārthayedbhāskaraṃ tathā ।। abhivandya punaḥ sūryaṃ brahmāṇaṃ ca vidhānataḥ ।। japtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ paścāt triḥ kṛtvā ca vibhāvasoḥ ।। abhivandya punaḥ sūryaṃ brahmāṇaṃ ca vibhāvasum ।।
sarvānāvāhayāmīti devānāvāhya sarvataḥ ।। dhyātvā svarūpaṃ tattattvam abhivandya yathākramam ।। pitṝṇāṃ tilatoyena gandhayuktena sarvataḥ ।। prācīnāvītī viprendra pitṝṇāṃ tarpayet kramāt ।।
ṛṣīn kaniṣṭhāṅgulinā śrotriyaḥ sarvasiddhaye ।। tathaivaṃ muniśārdūla brahmayajñaṃ yajed dvijaḥ ।। pitṛyajñaṃ ca pūtātmā yajñakarmaparāyaṇaḥ ।। agnau juhoti yaccānnaṃ devayajña iti smṛtaḥ ।।
bhūtayajña iti prokto bhūtidaḥ sarvadehinām ।। praṇamya tebhyo yaddattam annaṃ mānuṣa ucyate ।। evaṃ pañca mahāyajñān kuryāt sarvārthasiddhaye ।। brahmayajñarato martyo brahmaloke mahīyate ।।
brahmā ca bhagavānviṣṇuḥ śaṅkaro nīlalohitaḥ ।। grāmādbahirgato bhūtvā brāhmaṇo brahmayajñavit ।। prācyāmudīcyāṃ ca tathā prāgudīcyāmathāpi vā ।। prītyarthaṃ ca ṛcāṃ viprāḥ triḥ pītvā plāvya plāvya ca ।।
prītyarthaṃ sāmavedānām upaspṛśya ca mūrdhani ।। nāsike brāhmaṇo aṅgānāṃ kṣālya kṣālya ca vāriṇā ।। tathā copapurāṇānāṃ saurādīnāṃ yathākramam ।। śrotre spṛśeddhi tuṣṭyarthaṃ hṛddeśaṃ tu tataḥ spṛśet ।।
evamācamya cāstīrya darbhapiñjūlam ātmanaḥ ।। hemāṅgulīyasaṃyukto brahmabandhayuto api vā ।। akṛtvā ca muniḥ pañca mahāyajñāndvijottamaḥ ।। tasmātsarvaprayatnena kartavyāḥ śubhamicchatā ।।
tīrthaṃ saṃgṛhya vidhivat praviśecchibiraṃ vaśī ।। bhasmasnānaṃ tataḥ kuryād vidhivad dehaśuddhaye ।। jyotiḥ sūrya iti prātar juhuyādudite yataḥ ।। tasmāduditahomasthaṃ bhasitaṃ pāvanaṃ śubham ।।
īśānena śirodeśaṃ mukhaṃ tatpuruṣeṇa ca ।। sadyena pādau sarvāṅgaṃ praṇavenābhiṣecayet ।। vyapohya bhasma cādāya devadevamanusmaran ।। puṇyaiścaiva tathā mantrair ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃbhavaiḥ ।।
saṃkṣipya yaḥ sakṛtkuryāt sa yāti paramaṃ padam ।। vaktuṃ varṣaśatenāpi na śakyaṃ vistareṇa yat ।। prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā dhyāyeddevaṃ triyaṃbakam ।। sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ citrāṃbaravibhūṣitam ।।
śaivīṃ tanuṃ samāsthāya pūjayetparameśvaram ।। sarvatra praṇavenaiva brahmāṇi ca yathākramam ।। mantrāṇi sūkṣmarūpeṇa saṃsthitāni yatastataḥ ।। mahatyapi mahadbrahma saṃsthitaṃ sūkṣmavatsvayam ।।
dravyāṇi śodhayetpaścāt kṣālanaprokṣaṇādibhiḥ ।। prokṣaṇī cārghyapātraṃ ca pādyapātram anukramāt ।। sthāpayed vidhinā dhīmān avaguṇṭhya yathāvidhi ।। teṣu teṣvatha sarveṣu kṣipettoyaṃ suśītalam ।।
uśīraṃ candanaṃ caiva pādye tu parikalpayet ।। cūrṇayitvā yathānyāyaṃ kṣipedācamanīyake ।। karpūraṃ ca yathānyāyaṃ puṣpāṇi vividhāni ca ।। ājyasiddhārthapuṣpāṇi bhasitaṃ cārghyapātrake ।।
dāpayetprokṣaṇīpātre bhasitaṃ praṇavena ca ।। kevalaṃ praṇavaṃ vāpi vedasāramanuttamam ।। prokṣaṇīpātrasaṃsthena īśānādyaiś ca pañcabhiḥ ।। dīptānalāyutaprakhyaṃ trinetraṃ tridaśeśvaram ।।
puṣpamālādharaṃ saumyaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam ।। suyaśāṃ suvratāṃ cāmbāṃ pādamaṇḍanatatparām ।। dattvā puṣpāñjaliṃ bhaktyā pañcamūrdhasu pañcabhiḥ ।। skandaṃ vināyakaṃ devīṃ liṅgaśuddhiṃ ca kārayet ।।
kalpayedāsanaṃ paścāt padmākhyaṃ praṇavena tat ।। laghimā dakṣiṇaṃ caiva mahimā paścimaṃ tathā ।। īśitvaṃ nairṛtaṃ patraṃ vaśitvaṃ vāyugocare ।। somasyādhas tathā sūryas tasyādhaḥ pāvakaḥ svayam ।।
avyaktādicaturdikṣu somasyānte guṇatrayam ।। sadyojātaṃ prapadyāmīty āvāhya parameśvaram ।। sānnidhyaṃ rudragāyatryā aghoreṇa nirudhya ca ।। pādyamācamanīyaṃ ca vibhoścārghyaṃ pradāpayet ।।
pañcagavyavidhānena gṛhya pātre abhimantrya ca ।। ājyena madhunā caiva tathā cekṣurasena ca ।। jalabhāṇḍaiḥ pavitraistu mantraistoyaṃ kṣipettataḥ ।। kuśāpāmārgakarpūrajātipuṣpakacampakaiḥ ।।
āpūrya puṣpaiḥ suśubhaiḥ candanādyaiś ca tajjalam ।। suvarṇakalaśenātha tathā vai rājatena vā ।। śaṃkhena mṛnmayenātha śodhitena śubhena vā ।। mantrāṇi te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu sarvārthasiddhaye ।।
pavamānena mantrajñāḥ tathā vāmīyakena ca ।। rajanīsūktakenaiva camakena śubhena ca ।। śāntyā cātha punaḥ śāntyā bhāruṇḍenāruṇena ca ।। tathāntareṇa puṇyena sūktena puruṣeṇa ca ।।
āvosajeti sāmnā tu bṛhaccandreṇa viṣṇunā ।। pañcabrahmaiś ca sūtreṇa kevalapraṇavena ca ।। vastraṃ śivopavītaṃ ca tathā hyācamanīyakam ।। toyaṃ sugandhitaṃ caiva punarācamanīyakam ।।
dāpayetpraṇavenaiva mukhavāsādikāni ca ।। kāraṇaṃ sarvadevānāṃ sarvalokamayaṃ param ।। vedavidbhir hi vedāntais tv agocaramiti śrutiḥ ।। śivatattvamiti khyātaṃ śivaliṅge vyavasthitam ।।
stotraṃ japecca vidhinā namaskāraṃ pradakṣiṇam ।। praṇipatya ca deveśam ātmanyāropayecchivam ।। ābhyantaraṃ pravakṣyāmi liṅgārcanamihādya te ।। guṇatrayaṃ ca hṛdaye tathā cātmatrayaṃ kramāt ।।
kāntārdharūḍhadehaṃ ca pūjayeddhyānavidyayā ।। cintakasya tataścintā anyathā nopapadyate ।। smarettannānyathā jātu budhyate puruṣasya ha ।। yājyaṃ yajñena yajate yajamānastu sa smṛtaḥ ।।
pradhānapuruṣeśānaṃ yāthātathyaṃ prapadyate ।। caturviṃśakam avyaktaṃ mahadādyāstu sapta ca ।। karmendriyāṇi pañcaiva tathā buddhīndriyāṇi ca ।। sa eva bhartā kartā ca vidherapi maheśvaraḥ ।।
viśvādhikaś ca viśvātmā viśvarūpa iti smṛtaḥ ।। na jāyante tathā somaṃ vinā nāsti jagattrayam ।। tathā kārayitā caiva kurvato alpātmanas tathā ।। tvayokto muktidaḥ kiṃ vā niṣkalaścetkaroti kim ।।
niṣkalaṃ ca manaḥ sarvaṃ manyate so api niṣkalaḥ ।। kimatra devadevasya mūrtyaṣṭakamidaṃ jagat ।। tejasā vāriṇā caiva yajamānaṃ tathā vinā ।। vicāratastu rudrasya sthūlametaccarācaram ।।
yato vāco nivartante aprāpya manasā saha ।। na bhetavyaṃ tathā tasmāj jñātvānandaṃ pinākinaḥ ।। sarvaṃ rudra iti prāhur munayastattvadarśinaḥ ।। sarvaṃ tu khalvidaṃ brahma sarvo vai rudra īśvaraḥ ।।
evaṃ vibhurvinirdiṣṭo dhyānaṃ tatraiva cintanam ।। saṃsārahetuḥ saṃsāro mokṣahetuś ca nirvṛtiḥ ।। cintā bahuvidhā khyātā saikatra parameṣṭhinā ।। aindrī cendre tathā saumyā some nārāyaṇe tathā ।।
saivāhaṃ so ahamityevaṃ dvidhā saṃsthāpya bhāvataḥ ।। evaṃ brahmamayaṃ dhyāyet pūrvaṃ vipra carācaram ।। tyājyaṃ grāhyam alabhyaṃ ca kṛtyaṃ cākṛtyameva ca ।। ābhyantaraṃ samākhyātam evamabhyarcanaṃ kramāt ।।
virūpā vikṛtāścāpi na nindyā brahmavādinaḥ ।। nindakā eva duḥkhārtā bhaviṣyantyalpacetasaḥ ।। tasmātsevyā namaskāryāḥ sadā brahmavidas tathā ।। varṇāśramavinirmuktā varṇāśramaparāyaṇaiḥ ।।
pravṛttaṃ tadvanasthānāṃ tapasā bhāvitātmanām ।। vikṛtaṃ rūpamāsthāya cordhvaretā digambaraḥ ।। vaktumarhasi tattvena devadevasya ceṣṭitam ।। śilādasūnurbhagavān prāha kiṃcidbhavaṃ hasan ।।
tuṣṭyarthaṃ devadevasya sadāratanayāgnayaḥ ।। dhūrjaṭiḥ parameśāno bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ ।। parīkṣārthaṃ jagannāthaḥ śraddhayā krīḍayā ca saḥ ।। devadāruvanasthānāṃ pravṛttijñānacetasām ।।
mugdho dvihastaḥ kṛṣṇāṅgo divyaṃ dāruvanaṃ yayau ।। bhrūvilāsaṃ ca gānaṃ ca cakārātīva suṃdaraḥ ।। anaṅgavṛddhim akarod atīva madhurākṛtiḥ ।। striyaḥ pativratāścāpi tamevānvayurādarāt ।।
labdhvā smitaṃ tasya mukhāravindād drumālayasthās tam athānvayustāḥ ।। vilāsabāhyāstāścāpi bhrūvilāsaṃ pracakrire ।। kiṃcid visrastavasanāḥ srastakāñcīguṇā jaguḥ ।। svānsvānvicitrān valayānpravidhya madānvitā bandhujanāṃś ca jagmuḥ ।।
śākhāvicitrān viṭapānprasiddhān madānvitā bandhujanāṃstathānyāḥ ।। niṣedurgajavaccānyā provāca dvijapuṅgavāḥ ।। nirudhya mārgaṃ rudrasya naipuṇāni pracakrire ।। kutretyatha prasīdeti jajalpuḥ prītamānasāḥ ।।
pativratāḥ patīnāṃ tu saṃnidhau bhavamāyayā ।। śubhaṃ vāpyaśubhaṃ vāpi noktavānparameśvaraḥ ।। atīva paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ jajalpuste munīśvarāḥ ।। yathādityaprakāśena tārakā nabhasi sthitāḥ ।।
samṛddhaśreyasāṃ yonir yajñā vai nāśamāptavān ।। prādurbhāvāndaśa prāpto duḥkhitaś ca sadā kṛtaḥ ।। ṛṣiṇā gautamenorvyāṃ kruddhena vinipātitam ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ caiva śāpena nahuṣaḥ sarpatāṃ gataḥ ।।
dvitīyaścāmṛtādhāro hy apeyo brāhmaṇaiḥ kṛtaḥ ।। kṣīreṇa cābhiṣicyeśaṃ devadevaṃ triyaṃbakam ।। niṣiktena svayaṃ devaḥ kṣīreṇa madhusūdanaḥ ।। kṣīrodaṃ pūrvavaccakre nivāsaṃ cātmanaḥ prabhuḥ ।।
vṛṣṇayaścaiva kṛṣṇena durvāsādyairmahātmabhiḥ ।। śrīvatsaś ca muneḥ pāda patanāttasya dhīmataḥ ।। varjayitvā virūpākṣaṃ devadevamumāpatim ।। atyugravacanaṃ procuś cogro apyantaradhīyata ।।
pitāmahaṃ mahātmānam āsīnaṃ paramāsane ।। śubhe dāruvane tasmin munayaḥ kṣīṇacetasaḥ ।। teṣāṃ pravṛttamakhilaṃ puṇye dāruvane purā ।। uvāca satvaraṃ brahmā munīndāruvanālayān ।।
vṛthākṛtaṃ yato viprā yuṣmābhir bhāgyavarjitaiḥ ।। yuṣmābhir vikṛtākāraḥ sa eva parameśvaraḥ ।। virūpāś ca surūpāś ca malināścāpyapaṇḍitāḥ ।। purā bhūmau dvijāgryeṇa jito hyatithipūjayā ।।
tyaktvā cātithipūjāṃ tām ātmano bhuvi śodhanam ।। pratijñāmakarojjāyāṃ bhāryāmāha pativratām ।। tvayā vai nāvamantavyā gṛhe hyatithayaḥ sadā ।। tasmādatithaye dattvā ātmānamapi pūjaya ।।
patimāha rudantī ca kimuktaṃ bhavatā prabho ।। deyaṃ sarvaṃ śivāyārye śiva evātithiḥ svayam ।। evamuktā tadā bhartrā bhāryā tasya pativratā ।। parīkṣituṃ tathā śraddhāṃ tayoḥ sākṣād dvijottamāḥ ।।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā cārcayāmāsa sārghyādyairanaghā dvijam ।। bhadre kutaḥ patirdhīmāṃs tava bhartā sudarśanaḥ ।। sā ca lajjāvṛtā nārī smarantī kathitaṃ purā ।। kiṃcetyāha punastaṃ vai dharme cakre ca sā matim ।।
etasminnantare bhartā tasyā nāryāḥ sudarśanaḥ ।। ehyehi kva gatā bhadre tamuvācātithiḥ svayam ।। sudarśana mahābhāga kiṃ kartavyamihocyatām ।। sudarśanastataḥ prāha suprahṛṣṭo dvijottamaḥ ।।
hṛṣṭo atha darśayāmāsa svātmānaṃ dharmarāṭ svayam ।। eṣā na bhuktā viprendra manasāpi suśobhanā ।। jito vai yastvayā mṛtyur dharmeṇaikena suvrata ।। tasmāttathā pūjanīyāḥ sarve hyatithayaḥ sadā ।।
tameva śaraṇaṃ tūrṇaṃ gantumarhatha śaṅkaram ।। brahmāṇamabhivandyārtāḥ procurākulitekṣaṇāḥ ।। dṛṣṭo asmābhir mahādevo nindito yastvaninditaḥ ।। ajñānācchāpajā śaktiḥ kuṇṭhitāsyanirīkṣaṇāt ।।
draṣṭuṃ vai devadeveśam ugraṃ bhīmaṃ kapardinam ।। vicāryārthaṃ munerdharmān pratijñāya dvijottamāḥ ।। snātvāhṛtya ca dārānvai putrānutpādya suvratān ।। agniṣṭomādibhiśceṣṭvā yajñairyajñeśvaraṃ vibhum ।।
munirdvādaśavarṣaṃ vā varṣamātram athāpi vā ।। kṣīrabhuk saṃyutaḥ śāntaḥ sarvān sampūjayetsurān ।। apsu vai pārthivaṃ nyasya gurave taijasāni tu ।। praṇipatya guruṃ bhūmau viraktaḥ saṃnyasedyatiḥ ।।
pañcabhir juhuyād apsu bhūḥ svāheti vicakṣaṇaḥ ।। vratenānaśanenāpi toyavṛttyāpi vā punaḥ ।। evaṃ jīvanmṛto no cet ṣaṇmāsādvatsarāttu vā ।। śivasāyujyamāpnoti karmaṇāpyevamācaran ।।
sadyo api labhate muktiṃ bhaktiyukto dṛḍhavratāḥ ।। yajñaiś ca dānairvividhaiś ca homair labdhaiścaśāstrairvividhaiś ca vedaiḥ ।। vo astu bhaktirmahādeve śaṅkare paramātmani ।। śvetasya ca kathāṃ puṇyām apṛcchan paramarṣayaḥ ।।
sakto hyabhyarcya yadbhaktyā tuṣṭāva ca maheśvaram ।। tataḥ kālo mahātejāḥ kālaprāptaṃ dvijottamam ।। śveto api dṛṣṭvā taṃ kālaṃ kālaprāpto api śaṅkaram ।। triyaṃbakaṃ yajedevaṃ sugandhiṃ puṣṭivardhanam ।।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā sasmitaṃ prāha śvetaṃ lokabhayaṃkaraḥ ।। rudro vā bhagavān viṣṇur brahmā vā jagadīśvaraḥ ।। anena mama kiṃ vipra raudreṇa vidhinā prabhoḥ ।। yasmādgatāyustvaṃ tasmān mune netumihodyataḥ ।।
hā rudra rudra rudreti lalāpa munipuṅgavaḥ ।। netreṇa bāṣpamiśreṇa saṃbhrāntena samākulaḥ ।। liṅge asmin śaṅkaro rudraḥ sarvadevabhavodbhavaḥ ।। vidhinā kiṃ mahābāho gaccha gaccha yathāgatam ।।
śrutvā śvetasya tadvākyaṃ pāśahasto bhayāvahaḥ ।। babandha ca muniṃ kālaḥ kālaprāptaṃ tamāha ca ।। adya vai devadevena tava rudreṇa kiṃ kṛtam ।। kva cāhaṃ kva ca me bhītiḥ śveta baddho asi vai mayā ।।
niśceṣṭo asau mahādevaḥ kathaṃ pūjyo maheśvaraḥ ।। nihantumantakaṃ smayan smarāriyajñahā haraḥ ।। triyaṃbako ambayā samaṃ sanandinā gaṇeśvaraiḥ ।। papāta cāśu vai balī munestu saṃnidhau dvijāḥ ।।
nirīkṣaṇena vai mṛtaṃ bhavasya viprapuṅgavāḥ ।। praṇemuraṃbikāmumāṃ munīśvarāstu harṣitāḥ ।। suśobhanaṃ suśītalaṃ supuṣpavarṣamaṃbarāt ।। śilāśanātmajo avyayaṃ śivaṃ praṇamya śaṅkaram ।।
maheśvaraṃ maheśvara-sya cānugo gaṇeśvaraḥ ।। kṣaṇādgūḍhaśarīraṃ hi dhvastaṃ dṛṣṭvāntakaṃ kṣaṇāt ।। muktidaṃ bhuktidaṃ caiva sarveṣāmapi śaṅkaram ।। bhaktyā cāparayā tasmin viśokā vai bhaviṣyatha ।।
prasīda bhaktirdeveśe bhavedrudre pinākini ।। vratairvā bhagavadbhaktā bhaviṣyanti dvijātayaḥ ।। yajñair homair vratair vedair yogaśāstrair nirodhanaiḥ ।। atha tasya vacaḥ śrutvā sarve te paramarṣayaḥ ।।
tasmātpāśupatī bhaktir dharmakāmārthasiddhidā ।। dadhīcastu purā bhaktyā hariṃ jitvāmarairvibhum ।। mayāpi nirjito mṛtyur mahādevasya kīrtanāt ।। mahādevaprasādena jito mṛtyuryathā mayā ।।
prapannāḥ śaraṇaṃ devaṃ vaktumarhasi me prabho ।। devadāruvanasthāṃstu tapasā pāvakaprabhān ।। na tasmātparamaṃ kiṃcit padaṃ samadhigamyate ।। sahasrayugaparyante pralaye sarvadehinaḥ ।।
eṣa caiva prajāḥ sarvāḥ sṛjatyekaḥ svatejasā ।। yogī kṛtayuge caiva tretāyāṃ kratur ucyate ।। rudrasya mūrtayastvetā ye abhidhyāyanti paṇḍitāḥ ।। vṛttaṃ sudarśanaṃ yogyam evaṃ liṅgaṃ prapūjayet ।।
mūrtirekā sthitā cāsya mūrtayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। tasmāddhi devadeveśam īśānaṃ prabhumavyayam ।। liṅgaṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam ।। samanābhaṃ tathāṣṭāsraṃ ṣoḍaśāsram athāpi vā ।।
vedikā dviguṇā tasya samā vā sarvasaṃmatā ।। paṭṭikā ca samantādvai yavamātrā dvijottamāḥ ।। vedikāyāś ca vistāraṃ triguṇaṃ vai samantataḥ ।। samantānnirvraṇaṃ śubhraṃ lakṣaṇaistat sulakṣitam ।।
kalaśaṃ sthāpayettasya vedimadhye tathā dvijāḥ ।। secayecca tato liṅgaṃ pavitraiḥ pañcabhiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। samāhitāḥ pūjayadhvaṃ saputrāḥ saha bandhubhiḥ ।। tato drakṣyatha deveśaṃ durdarśamakṛtātmabhiḥ ।।
tataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā brahmāṇamamitaujasam ।। ārādhayitumārabdhā brahmaṇā kathitaṃ yathā ।। nadīnāṃ ca vivikteṣu pulineṣu śubheṣu ca ।। keciddarbhāvakāśāstu pādāṅguṣṭhāgradhiṣṭhitāḥ ।।
sthānavīrāsanāstvanye mṛgacaryāratāḥ pare ।। evaṃ saṃvatsare pūrṇe vasante samupasthite ।। devaḥ kṛtayuge tasmin girau himavataḥ śubhe ।। bhasmapāṃsūpadigdhāṅgo nagno vikṛtalakṣaṇaḥ ।।
kvacicca hasate raudraṃ kvacidgāyati vismitaḥ ।। āśrame hyaṭate bhaikṣyaṃ yācate ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। tataste munayaḥ sarve tuṣṭuvuś ca samāhitāḥ ।। sapatnīkā mahābhāgāḥ saputrāḥ saparicchadāḥ ।।
ajñānāddevadeveśa yadasmābhir anuṣṭhitam ।। caritāni vicitrāṇi guhyāni gahanāni ca ।। agatiṃ te na jānīmo gatiṃ naiva ca naiva ca ।। stuvanti tvāṃ mahātmāno devadevaṃ maheśvaram ।।
anantabalavīryāya bhūtānāṃ pataye namaḥ ।। gaṅgāsaliladhārāya ādhārāya guṇātmane ।। kandarpāya hutāśāya namo astu paramātmane ।। daṇḍahastāya kālāya pāśahastāya vai namaḥ ।।
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ ca yat ।। pāsi haṃsi ca bhadraṃ te prasīda bhagavaṃstataḥ ।। tatsarvaṃ bhagavāneva kurute yogamāyayā ।। yācanta tapasā yuktāḥ paśyāmastvāṃ yathāpurā ।।
rūpaṃ tryakṣaṃ ca saṃdraṣṭuṃ divyaṃ cakṣuradātprabhuḥ ।। punastuṣṭuvurīśānaṃ devadāruvanaukasaḥ ।। vikaṭāya karālāya karālavadanāya ca ।। kaṭaṅkaṭāya rudrāya svāhākārāya vai namaḥ ।।
nityaṃ nīlaśikhaṇḍāya śrīkaṇṭhāya namonamaḥ ।। tvaṃ brahmā sarvadevānāṃ rudrāṇāṃ nīlalohitaḥ ।। parvatānāṃ mahāmerur nakṣatrāṇāṃ ca candramāḥ ।। oṅkāraḥ sarvavedānāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sāma ca sāmasu ।।
grāmyāṇāmṛṣabhaścāsi bhagavāṃllokapūjitaḥ ।। tvāmeva tatra paśyāmo brahmaṇā kathitaṃ tathā ।। etad icchāmahe boddhuṃ prasīda parameśvara ।। karaṃ lalāṭe saṃvidhya vahnirutpāditastvayā ।।
tasmādagnisamā hyete bahavo vikṛtāgnayaḥ ।। yāni cānyāni bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca ।। asmākaṃ dahyamānānāṃ trātā bhava sureśvara ।। maheśvara mahābhāga prabho śubhanirīkṣaka ।।
bhūtakoṭisahasreṣu rūpakoṭiśateṣu ca ।। antaṃ gantuṃ na śaktāḥ sma devadeva namo astu te ।। stutiṃ śrutvā stutasteṣām idaṃ vacanamabravīt ।। śrāvayedvā dvijānvipro gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt ।।
strīliṅgamakhilaṃ devī prakṛtirmama dehajā ।। ubhābhyāmeva vai sṛṣṭir mama viprā na saṃśayaḥ ।। bālonmattaviceṣṭaṃ tu matparaṃ brahmavādinam ।। yathoktakāriṇo dāntā viprā dhyānaparāyaṇāḥ ।।
arcayanti mahādevaṃ vāṅmanaḥkāyasaṃyatāḥ ।। tasmādetadvrataṃ divyam avyaktaṃ vyaktaliṅginaḥ ।। na tānparivadedvidvān na caitānnābhilaṅghayet ।। yastānnindati mūḍhātmā mahādevaṃ sa nindati ।।
evameṣa mahādevo lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। evaṃ carata bhadraṃ vas tataḥ siddhimavāpsyatha ।। vyapagatabhavalobhamohacittāḥ praṇipatitāḥ sahasā śirobhir ugram ।। gandhodakaiḥ suśuddhaiś ca kuśapuṣpavimiśritaiḥ ।।
gāyanti vividhairguhyair huṃkāraiścāpi susvaraiḥ ।। ardhanārīśarīrāya sāṃkhyayogapravartine ।। kṛṣṇājinottarīyāya vyālayajñopavītine ।। mṛgapativaracarmavāsase ca prathitayaśase namo astu śaṅkarāya ।।
prīto asmi tapasā yuṣmān varaṃ vṛṇuta suvratāḥ ।। bhṛgvaṅgirā vasiṣṭhaś ca viśvāmitrastathaiva ca ।। marīciḥ kaśyapaḥ kaṇvaḥ saṃvartaś ca mahātapāḥ ।। bhasmasnānaṃ ca nagnatvaṃ vāmatvaṃ pratilomatā ।।
tatasteṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā bhagavānparameśvaraḥ ।। sasmitaṃ prāha samprekṣya sarvānmunivarāṃstadā ।। agnirhyahaṃ somakartā somaścāgnimupāśritaḥ ।। asakṛttvagninā dagdhaṃ jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam ।।
bhasmanā vīryamāsthāya bhūtāni pariṣiñcati ।। bhasmanā mama vīryeṇa mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ ।। bhakṣaṇāt sarvapāpānāṃ bhasmeti parikīrtitam ।। agnīṣomātmakaṃ sarvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṅgamam ।।
ahamagniś ca somaś ca prakṛtyā puruṣaḥ svayam ।। svavīryaṃ vapuṣā caiva dhārayāmīti vai sthitiḥ ।। bhasmanā kriyate rakṣā sūtikānāṃ gṛheṣu ca ।। matsamīpaṃ samāgamya na bhūyo vinivartate ।।
pūrvaṃ pāśupataṃ hyetan nirmitaṃ tadanuttamam ।। sṛṣṭireṣā mayā sṛṣṭā lajjāmohabhayātmikā ।। ye cānye mānavā loke sarve jāyantyavāsasaḥ ।। taireva saṃvṛtairgupto na vastraṃ kāraṇaṃ smṛtam ।।
tulyau mānāvamānau ca tadāvaraṇamuttamam ।। yadyakāryasahasrāṇi kṛtvā yaḥ snāti bhasmanā ।। tasmād yatnaparo bhūtvā trikālamapi yaḥ sadā ।। samāhṛtya kratūn sarvān gṛhītvā vratamuttamam ।।
uttareṇāryapanthānaṃ te amṛtatvamavāpnuyuḥ ।। aṇimā garimā caiva laghimā prāptireva ca ।। aṇimā garimā caiva laghimā prāptireva ca ।। aiśvaryaṃ paramaṃ prāpya sarve prathitatejasaḥ ।।
paribhavamidamuttamaṃ viditvā paśupatiyogaparo bhavetsadaiva ।। yaḥ paṭhecca śucirbhūtvā śraddadhāno jitendriyaḥ ।। te sarve munayaḥ śrutvā vasiṣṭhādyā dvijottamāḥ ।। rudralokāya kalpānte saṃsthitāḥ śivatejasā ।।
rūpānvitāś ca viprendrāḥ sadā yogīndraśaṅkayā ।। saṃpūjyāḥ sarvayatnena śivavannātra saṃśayaḥ ।। dadhīcastu yathā devadevaṃ jitvā vyavasthitaḥ ।। tasmātsarvaprayatnena bhasmadigdhatanūruhāḥ ।।
saṃpūjyāḥ śivavannityaṃ manasā karmaṇā girā ।। dadhīcaḥ samare jitvā devadevaṃ janārdanam ।। vaktumarhasi śailāde jito mṛtyustvayā yathā ।। abhūnmitro dadhīcasya munīndrasya janeśvaraḥ ।।
abhavat kṣatriyaśreṣṭho vipra eveti viśrutaḥ ।। tasmādindro hyayaṃ vahnir yamaś ca nirṛtis tathā ।। īśvaro ahaṃ na saṃdeho nāvamantavya eva ca ।। tasmāttvayā mahābhāga cyāvaneya sadā hyaham ।।
śrutvā tathā mataṃ tasya kṣupasya munisattamaḥ ।। cicheda vajreṇa ca taṃ dadhīcaṃ balavān kṣupaḥ ।। labdhaṃ vajraṃ ca kāryārthaṃ vajriṇā coditaḥ prabhuḥ ।। tasmādrājā sa viprendram ajayadvai mahābalaḥ ।।
papāta bhūmau nihato vajreṇa dvijapuṅgavaḥ ।। śukro api saṃdhayāmāsa tāḍitaṃ kuliśena tam ।। saṃdhāya pūrvavaddehaṃ dadhīcasyāha bhārgavaḥ ।। sampūjya pūjyaṃ brahmādyair devadevaṃ nirañjanam ।।
