mṛtasaṃjīvanaṃ tasmāl labdhametanmayā dvija ।। mṛtasaṃjīvanaṃ cāpi śaivamadya vadāmi te ।। trimaṇḍalasya pitaraṃ triguṇasya maheśvaram ।। trivedasya mahādevaṃ sugandhiṃ puṣṭivardhanam ।।
indriyeṣu tathānyeṣu deveṣu ca gaṇeṣu ca ।। puṣṭiś ca prakṛtiryasmāt puruṣasya dvijottama ।। viṣṇoḥ pitāmahasyāpi munīnāṃ ca mahāmune ।। taṃ devamamṛtaṃ rudraṃ karmaṇā tapasā tathā ।।
satyenānena mukṣīyān mṛtyupāśād bhavaḥ svayam ।। mṛtasaṃjīvano mantro mayā labdhastu śaṅkarāt ।। liṅgasya saṃnidhau dhyātvā nāsti mṛtyubhayaṃ dvija ।। vajrāsthitvam avadhyatvam adīnatvaṃ ca labdhavān ।।
prāpyāvadhyatvamanyaiś ca vajrāsthitvaṃ prayatnataḥ ।। kṣupo dadhīcaṃ vajreṇa jaghānorasi ca prabhuḥ ।। prabhāvātparameśasya vajrabaddhaśarīriṇaḥ ।। ārādhayāmāsa hariṃ mukundam indrānujaṃ prekṣya tadāṃbujākṣam ।।
śrībhūmisahitaḥ śrīmāñ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ ।। pītāṃbaraś ca bhagavān devairdaityaiś ca saṃvṛtaḥ ।। divyena darśanenaiva dṛṣṭvā devaṃ janārdanam ।। tvamādistvamanādiś ca prakṛtistvaṃ janārdanaḥ ।।
yo ayaṃ brahmāsi puruṣo viśvamūrtiḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। paramātmā paraṃ dhāma śrīpate bhūpate prabho ।। tvatprasādājjagaddhātā rajasā ca pitāmahaḥ ।। kālamūrte hare viṣṇo nārāyaṇa jaganmaya ।।
tvayaivādhiṣṭhitānyeva viśvamūrte maheśvara ।। prasīda devadeveśa prasīda parameśvara ।। vaikuṇṭha śaure sarvajña vāsudeva mahābhuja ।। aniruddha mahāviṣṇo sadā viṣṇo namo astu te ।।
sahasraphaṇasaṃyuktas tamomūrtirdharādharaḥ ।। aiśvaryamāsanasyāsya pādarūpeṇa suvrata ।। vāsāṃsi sāgarāḥ sapta diśaścaiva mahābhujāḥ ।। netre somaś ca sūryaś ca keśā vai puṣkarādayaḥ ।।
kathaṃ stoṣyāmi deveśaṃ pūjyaś ca puruṣottamaḥ ।। yadiṣṭaṃ tatkṣamasveśa nārāyaṇa namo astu te ।। yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi kṣupeṇa parikīrtitam ।। śrāvayedvā dvijān bhaktyā viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।।
vijñāpayāmāsa nirīkṣya bhaktyā janārdanāya praṇipatya mūrdhnā ।। dharmavettā vinītātmā sakhā mama purābhavat ।। sāvajñaṃ vāmapādena sa māṃ mūrdhni sadasyatha ।। uvāca ca madāviṣṭo na bibhemīti sarvataḥ ।।
yathā hitaṃ tathā kartuṃ tvamarhasi janārdana ।। sasmāra ca maheśasya prabhāvamatulaṃ hariḥ ।। viprāṇāṃ nāsti rājendra bhayametya maheśvaram ।। nīcānāmapi sarvatra dadhīcasyāsya kiṃ punaḥ ।।
duḥkhaṃ karomi viprasya śāpārthaṃ sasurasya me ।। vināśo mama rājendra punarutthānameva ca ।। karomi yatnaṃ rājendra dadhīcavijayāya te ।। bhagavānapi viprasya dadhīcasyāśramaṃ yayau ।।
dadhīcamāha brahmarṣim abhivandya jagadguruḥ ।। varamekaṃ vṛṇe tvattas taṃ bhavāndātumarhati ।। jñātaṃ tavepsitaṃ sarvaṃ na bibhemi tavāpyaham ।। bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ deveśa vartamānaṃ janārdana ।।
ārādhito asi deveśa kṣupeṇa madhusūdana ।। sthāne tavaiṣā bhagavan bhaktavātsalyatā hare ।। vaktumarhasi yatnena varadāṃbujalocana ।। na bibhemi jagatyasmin devadaityadvijādapi ।।
svarūpaṃ sasmitaṃ prāha saṃtyajya dvijatāṃ kṣaṇāt ।। bhavārcanarato yasmād bhavān sarvajña eva ca ।। niyogānmama viprendra kṣupaṃ prati sadasyatha ।। na bibhemīti taṃ prāha dadhīco devasattamam ।।
śarvasya śaṅkarasyāsya sarvajñasya mahāmuniḥ ।। cakramudyamya bhagavān didhakṣurmunisattamam ।। prabhāvāddhi dadhīcasya kṣupasyaiva hi saṃnidhau ।। dadhīcaḥ sasmitaṃ sākṣāt sadasadvyaktikāraṇam ।।
sudarśanamiti khyātaṃ cakraṃ viṣṇo prayatnataḥ ।। brahmāstrādyaistathānyairhi prayatnaṃ kartumarhasi ।। sasarja ca punastasmai sarvāstrāṇi samantataḥ ।। dvijenaikena yoddhuṃ hi pravṛttasya mahābalāḥ ।।
sasarja sarvadevebhyo vajrāsthiḥ sarvato vaśī ।। dagdhuṃ devānmatiṃ cakre yugāntāgnirivāparaḥ ।। āyudhāni samastāni praṇemus triśikhaṃ mune ।। sasarja bhagavān viṣṇuḥ svadehātpuruṣottamaḥ ।।
tāni sarvāṇi sahasā dadāha munisattamaḥ ।। tasya dehe hareḥ sākṣād apaśyaddvijasattamaḥ ।। rudrāṇāṃ koṭayaścaiva gaṇānāṃ koṭayastadā ।। dṛṣṭvaitadakhilaṃ tatra cyāvanir vismitaṃ tadā ।।
aṃbhasābhyukṣya taṃ viṣṇuṃ viśvarūpaṃ mahāmuniḥ ।। vijñānānāṃ sahasrāṇi durvijñeyāni mādhava ।। brahmāṇaṃ ca tathā rudraṃ divyāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ dadāmi te ।। taṃ prāha ca hariṃ devaṃ sarvadevabhavodbhavam ।।
vastuśaktyātha vā viṣṇo dhyānaśaktyātha vā punaḥ ।। evaṃ tasya vacaḥ śrutvā dṛṣṭvā māhātmyamadbhutam ।। vārayāmāsa niśceṣṭaṃ padmayonirjagadguruḥ ।। jagāma bhagavān viṣṇuḥ praṇipatya mahāmunim ।।
dadhīcamabhivandyāśu prārthayāmāsa viklavaḥ ।। viṣṇunā hi surairvāpi rudrabhaktasya kiṃ tava ।। bhaktirbhaktimatāṃ śreṣṭha madvidhaiḥ kṣatriyādhamaiḥ ।। rājānaṃ muniśārdūlaḥ śaśāpa ca surottamān ।।
dhvastā bhavantu devena viṣṇunā ca samanvitāḥ ।। evaṃ śaptvā kṣupaṃ prekṣya punarāha dvijottamaḥ ।। brāhmaṇā eva rājendra balinaḥ prabhaviṣṇavaḥ ।। dadhīcamabhivandyaiva jagāma svaṃ nṛpaḥ kṣayam ।।
sthāneśvaram anuprāpya śivasāyujyam āpnuyāt ।। prabhāvaś ca dadhīcasya bhavasya ca mahāmune ।। jitvāpamṛtyuṃ dehānte brahmalokaṃ prayāti saḥ ।। nāsti mṛtyubhayaṃ caiva vijayī ca bhaviṣyati ।।
śrotumicchāmi tatsarvaṃ vaktumarhasi me prabho ।। so apyandhaḥ suciraṃ kalaṃ tapastepe suduścaram ।। śilādamāha tuṣṭo asmi varayasva varāniti ।। provāca muniśārdūla kṛtāñjalipuṭo harim ।।
ayonijaṃ mṛtyuhīnaṃ putramicchāmi suvrata ।। anyathā te na dāsyāmi mṛtyuhīnā na santi vai ।। pitāmaho api bhagavān kimutānye mahāmune ।। yonijaś ca mahātejāś cāṇḍajaḥ padmasaṃbhavaḥ ।।
tasyāpyāyuḥ samākhyātaṃ parārdhadvayasaṃmitam ।। samatītāni kalpānāṃ tāvaccheṣāparatraye ।। parityajāśāṃ viprendra gṛhāṇātmasamaṃ sutam ।। śilāda iti puṇyātmā punaḥ prāha śacīpatim ।।
maheśvarāṅgayonitvaṃ śrutaṃ vai brahmaṇo mayā ।। nāradādvai mahābāho kathamatrāśu no vada ।। pautrīkanakagarbhasya kathaṃ tasyāḥ suto vibhuḥ ।। kalpe tatpuruṣe vṛttaṃ brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।।
janārdano jagannāthaḥ kalpe vai meghavāhane ।। nārāyaṇo mahādevaṃ bahumānena sādaram ।। pradadau tasya sakalaṃ sraṣṭuṃ vai brahmaṇā saha ।। hiraṇyagarbhastaṃ dṛṣṭvā tasya dehodbhavastadā ।।
tava vāmāṅgajo viṣṇur dakṣiṇāṅgabhavo hyaham ।। jaganmayo avahadyasmān megho bhūtvā divāniśam ।। nārāyaṇādapi vibho bhakto ahaṃ tava śaṅkara ।। tadātha labdhvā bhagavān bhavātsarvātmatāṃ kṣaṇāt ।।
ekārṇavālaye śubhre tv andhakāre sudāruṇe ।। duṣprāpye durjanaiḥ puṇyaiḥ sanakādyairagocare ।। anantabhogaśayyāyāṃ śāyinaṃ paṅkajekṣaṇam ।। sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ śaśimaṇḍalasannibham ।।
ramāmṛdukarāmbhojasparśaraktapadāmbujam ।। rajasā sarvalokānāṃ sargalīlāpravartakam ।। sarvātmānaṃ mahātmānaṃ paramātmānamīśvaram ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā prāha vai brahmā bhagavantaṃ janārdanam ।।
smayamānastu bhagavān pratibudhya pitāmaham ।। viveśa cāṇḍajaṃ taṃ tu grastastena mahātmanā ।। sṛṣṭastena hariḥ prekṣya sthitastasyātha saṃnidhau ।। vikṛtaṃ rūpamāsthāya purā dattavarastayoḥ ।।
prasādamatulaṃ kartuṃ brahmaṇaś ca hareḥ prabhuḥ ।। apaśyatāṃ bhavaṃ devaṃ kālāgnisadṛśaṃ prabhum ।। praṇematuś ca varadaṃ bahumānena dūrataḥ ।। janārdanaṃ jagannāthas tatraivāntaradhīyata ।।
praṇamya bhagavānprāha padmayonimajodbhavaḥ ।। āvayorakhilasyeśaḥ śaraṇaṃ ca maheśvaraḥ ।। bhavān bhavasya devasya dakṣiṇāṅgabhavaḥ svayam ।। avyaktamajamityevaṃ bhavantaṃ puruṣastviti ।।
īśaṃ sarvasya jagataḥ prabhumavyayamīśvaram ।। vareṇyaṃ varadaṃ rudram astuvatpraṇanāma ca ।। pūrvavatsthāpayāmāsa vārāhaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ ।। kṛtvā corvīṃ prayatnena nimnonnatavivarjitām ।।
bhūrādyāṃścaturo lokān kalpayāmāsa pūrvavat ।। mukhyaṃ ca tairyagyonyaṃ ca daivikaṃ mānuṣaṃ tathā ।। purastādasṛjaddevaḥ sanandaṃ sanakaṃ tathā ।। marīcibhṛgvaṅgirasaṃ pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum ।।
saṃkalpaṃ caiva dharmaṃ ca hy adharmaṃ bhagavānprabhuḥ ।। ṛbhuṃ sanatkumāraṃ ca sasarjādau sanātanaḥ ।। kumārau brahmaṇastulyau sarvajñau sarvabhāvinau ।। yugadharmānaśeṣāṃś ca kalpayāmāsa viśvasṛk ।।
punaḥ papraccha deveśaṃ praṇamya racitāñjaliḥ ।। śacīpate jagannātha sahasrākṣa maheśvara ।। vaktumarhasi me sarvaṃ sāṃprataṃ praṇatāya me ।। vyājahāra yathādṛṣṭaṃ yugadharmaṃ suvistaram ।।
dvāparaṃ tiṣyamityete catvārastu samāsataḥ ।। kalistamaś ca vijñeyaṃ yugavṛttiryugeṣu ca ।। bhajanaṃ dvāpare śuddhaṃ dānameva kalau yuge ।। tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaś ca tathāvidhaḥ ।।
āyuḥ kṛtayuge viddhi prajānāmiha suvrata ।। pādāvaśiṣṭo bhavati yugadharmastu sarvataḥ ।। kṛtārdhaṃ dvāparaṃ viddhi tadardhaṃ tiṣyamucyate ।। saṃdhyāṃśakaṃ tathāpyevaṃ kalpeṣvevaṃ yuge yuge ।।
tretāyuge tripādastu dvipādo dvāpare sthitaḥ ।। kṛte tu mithunotpattir vṛttiḥ sākṣādrasollasā ।। adhamottamatā tāsāṃ na viśeṣāḥ prajāḥ śubhāḥ ।। tāsāṃ prītirna ca dvandvaṃ na dveṣo nāsti ca klamaḥ ।।
viśokāḥ sattvabahulā ekāntabahulās tathā ।। apravṛttiḥ kṛtayuge karmaṇoḥ śubhapāpayoḥ ।। rasollāsaḥ kālayogāt tretākhye naśyate dvija ।। apāṃ saukṣmye pratigate tadā meghātmanā tu vai ।।
sakṛd eva tathā vṛṣṭyā saṃyukte pṛthivītale ।। sarvavṛttyupabhogastu tāsāṃ tebhyaḥ prajāyate ।। tataḥ kālena mahatā tāsāmeva viparyayāt ।। viparyayeṇa tāsāṃ tu tena tatkālabhāvinā ।।
tatasteṣu pranaṣṭeṣu vibhrāntā maithunodbhavāḥ ।। prādurbabhūvustāsāṃ tu vṛkṣāste gṛhasaṃjñitāḥ ।। teṣveva jāyate tāsāṃ gandhavarṇarasānvitam ।। tena tā vartayanti sma sukhamāyuḥ sadaiva hi ।।
tataḥ kālāntareṇaiva punarlobhāvṛtāstu tāḥ ।। tāsāṃ tenopacāreṇa punarlobhakṛtena vai ।। tasyāmevālpaśiṣṭāyāṃ siddhyāṃ kālavaśāttadā ।। śītavarṣātapaistīvrais tatastā duḥkhitā bhṛśam ।।
kṛtadvandvapratīghātāḥ ketanāni girau tataḥ ।। yathāyogaṃ yathāprīti niketeṣvavasanpunaḥ ।। naṣṭeṣu madhunā sārdhaṃ kalpavṛkṣeṣu vai tadā ।। tataḥ prādurbabhau tāsāṃ siddhistretāyuge punaḥ ।।
tāsāṃ vṛṣṭyudakādīni hy abhavannimnagāni tu ।। evaṃ nadyaḥ pravṛttāstu dvitīye vṛṣṭisarjane ।। apāṃ bhūmeś ca saṃyogād oṣadhyastāstadābhavan ।। ṛtupuṣpaphalāścaiva vṛkṣagulmāś ca jajñire ।।
tenauṣadhena vartante prajāstretāyuge tadā ।। avaśyaṃ bhāvinārthena tretāyugavaśena ca ।। vṛkṣagulmauṣadhīścaiva prasahya tu yathābalam ।। matvā dharāṃ praviṣṭāstā ityauṣadhyaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।।
tadāprabhṛti cauṣadhyaḥ phālakṛṣṭāstvitastataḥ ।। vārtā vṛttiḥ samākhyātā kṛṣikāmaprayatnataḥ ।। hastodbhavā hyapaścaiva bhavanti bahuśastadā ।। sutadāradhanādyāṃstu balādyugabalena tu ।।
sasarja kṣatriyāṃstrātuṃ kṣatātkamalasaṃbhavaḥ ।। vṛttena vṛttinā vṛttaṃ viśvātmā nirmame svayam ।। paśuyajñaṃ na sevante kecittatrāpi suvratāḥ ।। dvijāstadā praśaṃsanti tatastvāhiṃsakaṃ mune ।।
manasā karmaṇā vācā kṛcchrādvārtā prasidhyati ।। lobho bhṛtirvaṇigyuddhaṃ tattvānāmaviniścayaḥ ।। varṇāśramaparidhvaṃsaḥ kāmadveṣau tathaiva ca ।। vedo vyāsaiścaturdhā tu vyasyate dvāparādiṣu ।।
saṃkṣayādāyuṣaścaiva vyasyate dvāpareṣu saḥ ।। mantrabrāhmaṇavinyāsaiḥ svaravarṇaviparyayaiḥ ।। sāmānyā vaikṛtāścaiva draṣṭṛbhistaiḥ pṛthakpṛthak ।। anye tu prasthitāstānvai kecittānpratyavasthitāḥ ।।
brāhmaṃ pādmaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ ca śaivaṃ bhāgavataṃ tathā ।। āgneyaṃ brahmavaivartaṃ laiṅgaṃ vārāhameva ca ।। skāndaṃ tathā ca brahmāṇḍaṃ teṣāṃ bhedaḥ prakathyate ।। manvatriviṣṇuhārītayājñavalkyośano aṅgirāḥ ।।
parāśaravyāsaśaṅkhalikhitā dakṣagautamau ।। avṛṣṭirmaraṇaṃ caiva tathā vyādhyādyupadravāḥ ।। nirvedājjāyate teṣāṃ duḥkhamokṣavicāraṇā ।। doṣāṇāṃ darśanāccaiva dvāpare jñānasaṃbhavaḥ ।।
ādye kṛte tu dharmo asti sa tretāyāṃ pravartate ।। dvāpare vyākulībhūtvā praṇaśyati kalau yuge ।। sādhayanti narāstatra tamasā vyākulendriyāḥ ।। anāvṛṣṭibhayaṃ ghoraṃ deśānāṃ ca viparyayaḥ ।।
adhārmikāstvanācārā mahākopālpacetasaḥ ।। duriṣṭairduradhītaiś ca durācārairdurāgamaiḥ ।। nādhīyante tadā vedān na yajanti dvijātayaḥ ।। śūdrāṇāṃ mantrayogena saṃbandho brāhmaṇaiḥ saha ।।
rājānaḥ śūdrabhūyiṣṭhā brāhmaṇān bādhayanti te ।। śūdrāś ca brāhmaṇācārāḥ śūdrācārāś ca brāhmaṇāḥ ।। ekapatnyo na śiṣyanti vardhiṣyantyabhisārikāḥ ।। tadā svalpaphalā bhūmiḥ kvaciccāpi mahāphalā ।।
śūdrā vai jñāninaḥ sarve brāhmaṇairabhivanditāḥ ।। āsanasthā dvijāndṛṣṭvā na calantyalpabuddhayaḥ ।। āsye nidhāya vai hastaṃ karṇaṃ śūdrasya vai dvijāḥ ।। uccāsanasthān śūdrāṃś ca dvijamadhye dvijarṣabha ।।
puṣpaiś ca vāsitaiścaiva tathānyair maṅgalaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। na prekṣante garvitāś ca śūdrā dvijavarān dvija ।। vāhanasthān samāvṛtya śūdrāñśūdropajīvinaḥ ।। tapoyajñaphalānāṃ ca vikretāro dvijottamāḥ ।।
puruṣālpaṃ bahustrīkaṃ yugānte samupasthite ।। kalau devo mahādevaḥ śaṅkaro nīlalohitaḥ ।। ye taṃ viprā niṣevante yena kenāpi śaṅkaram ।। śvāpadaprabalatvaṃ ca gavāṃ caiva parikṣayaḥ ।।
tadā sūkṣmo mahodarko durlabho dānamūlavān ।। arakṣitāro hartāro balibhāgasya pārthivāḥ ।। aṭṭaśūlā janapadāḥ śivaśūlāścatuṣpathāḥ ।। citravarṣī tadā devo yadā prāhuryugakṣayam ।।
kuśīlacaryāḥ pāṣaṇḍair vṛthārūpaiḥ samāvṛtāḥ ।। nāvyāhṛtakrūravākyo nārjavī nānasūyakaḥ ।। nindakāścaiva patitā yugāntasya ca lakṣaṇam ।। maṇḍalāni bhaviṣyanti deśeṣu nagareṣu ca ।।
goptāraścāpyagoptāraḥ sambhaviṣyantyaśāsanāḥ ।। kāmātmāno durātmāno hy adhamāḥ sāhasapriyāḥ ।। janāḥ ṣoḍaśavarṣāś ca prajāyante yugakṣaye ।। śūdrā dharmaṃ cariṣyanti yugānte samupasthite ।।
caurāścorasvahartāro harturhartā tathāparaḥ ।। kīṭamūṣakasarpāś ca dharṣayiṣyanti mānavān ।। kauśikīṃ pratipatsyante deśānkṣudbhayapīḍitāḥ ।। dṛśyante na ca dṛśyante vedāḥ kaliyuge akhilāḥ ।।
kāṣāyiṇo apyanirgranthāḥ kāpālībahulāstviha ।। varṇāśramāṇāṃ ye cānye pāṣaṇḍāḥ paripanthinaḥ ।। adhīyante tadā vedāñ śūdrā dharmārthakovidāḥ ।। strībālagovadhaṃ kṛtvā hatvā caiva parasparam ।।
duḥkhaprabhūtamalpāyur dehotsādaḥ sarogatā ।। prajāsu brahmahatyādi tadā vai sampravartate ।। tadā tvalpena kālena siddhiṃ gacchanti mānavāḥ ।। śrutismṛtyuditaṃ dharmaṃ ye carantyanasūyakāḥ ।।
yathākleśaṃ caranprājñas tadahnā prāpnute kalau ।। yuge yuge ca hīyante trīṃstrīnpādāṃstu siddhayaḥ ।। saṃdhyāsvabhāvāḥ svāṃśeṣu pādaśaste pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।। teṣāṃ śāstā hyasādhūnāṃ bhūtānāṃ nidhanotthitaḥ ।।
mānavasya tu so aṃśena pūrvaṃ svāyaṃbhuve antare ।। anukarṣan sa vai senāṃ savājirathakuñjarām ।। sa tadā taiḥ parivṛto mlecchān hanti sahasraśaḥ ।। pākhaṇḍāṃstu tataḥ sarvān niḥśeṣaṃ kṛtavān prabhuḥ ।।
varṇavyatyāsajātāś ca ye ca tānanujīvinaḥ ।। adhṛṣyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ cacārātha vasuṃdharām ।। pūrvajanmani viṣṇostu pramitirnāma vīryavān ।। dvātriṃśe abhyudite varṣe prakrānto viṃśatiḥ samāḥ ।।
kṛtvā bījāvaśeṣāṃ tu pṛthivīṃ krūrakarmaṇaḥ ।। sa sādhayitvā vṛṣalān prāyaśas tān adhārmikān ।। tato vyatīte kāle tu sāmātyaḥ sahasainikaḥ ।। tatra saṃdhyāṃśake kāle samprāpte tu yugāntike ।।
apragrahāstatastā vai lobhāviṣṭāstu kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। arājake yugavaśāt saṃśaye samupasthite ।। vyākulāś ca paribhrāntās tyaktvā dārān gṛhāṇi ca ।। naṣṭe śraute smārtadharme parasparahatāstadā ।।
naṣṭe dharme pratihatāḥ hrasvakāḥ pañcaviṃśakāḥ ।। anāvṛṣṭihatāścaiva vārtāmutsṛjya dūrataḥ ।। saritsāgarakūpāṃste sevante parvatāṃs tathā ।। cīrapatrājinadharā niṣkriyā niṣparigrahāḥ ।।
evaṃ kaṣṭamanuprāptā alpaśeṣāḥ prajāstadā ।। vicāraṇā tu nirvedāt sāmyāvasthā vicāraṇā ।। arūpaśamayuktāstu kaliśiṣṭā hi vai svayam ।। cittasaṃmohanaṃ kṛtvā tāsāṃ vai suptamattavat ।।
pravṛtte tu tatastasmin punaḥ kṛtayuge tu vai ।। tiṣṭhanti ceha ye siddhā adṛṣṭā vicaranti ca ।। brahmakṣatraviśaḥ śūdrā bījārthaṃ ye smṛtā iha ।। teṣāṃ saptarṣayo dharmaṃ kathayantītare api ca ।।
tatasteṣu kriyāvatsu vardhante vai prajāḥ kṛte ।। keciddharmavyavasthārthaṃ tiṣṭhantīha yugakṣaye ।। yathā dāvapradagdheṣu tṛṇeṣviha tataḥ kṣitau ।। tathā kārtayugānāṃ tu kalijeṣviha saṃbhavaḥ ।।
vartate ha vyavacchedād yāvanmanvantarakṣayaḥ ।। yugeṣvetāni hīyante trīṃstrīn pādān krameṇa tu ।। ityeṣā pratisiddhirvai kīrtitaiṣā krameṇa tu ।। eṣā caturyugāvṛttir ā sahasrād guṇīkṛtā ।।
anārjavaṃ jaḍībhāvo bhūtānām ā yugakṣayāt ।। eṣāṃ caturyugāṇāṃ ca guṇitā hyekasaptatiḥ ।। caturyuge yathaikasmin bhavatīha yadā tu yat ।। sarge sarge yathā bhedā utpadyante tathaiva tu ।।
tathā kalpā yugaiḥ sārdhaṃ bhavanti saha lakṣaṇaiḥ ।। manvantarāṇāṃ sarveṣām etadeva tu lakṣaṇam ।। tathā tu saṃtiṣṭhati jīvalokaḥ kṣayodayābhyāṃ parivartamānaḥ ।। atītānāgatānāṃ hi sarvamanvantareṣu vai ।।
vyākhyātāni na saṃdehaḥ kalpaḥ kalpena caiva hi ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu atītānāgateṣviha ।। devā hyaṣṭavidhā ye ca ye ca manvantareśvarāḥ ।। evaṃ varṇāśramāṇāṃ tu pravibhāgo yuge yuge ।।
varṇāśramavibhāgāś ca yugāni yugasiddhayaḥ ।। vadāmi devīputratvaṃ padmayoneḥ samāsataḥ ।। sahasrayugaparyante prabhāte tu pitāmahaḥ ।। tadā dharāmbhasi vyāptā hy āpo vahnau samīraṇe ।।
indriyāṇi daśaikaṃ ca tanmātrāṇi dvijottama ।। abhimānastadā tatra mahāntaṃ vyāpya vai kṣaṇāt ।। avyaktaṃ svaguṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ pralīnamabhavadbhave ।। atha sṛṣṭāstadā tasya manasā tena mānasāḥ ।।
vṛddhyarthaṃ bhagavānbrahmā putrairvai mānasaiḥ saha ।। tuṣṭastu tapasā tasya bhavo jñātvā sa vāñchitam ।। putrasnehamiti procya strīpuṃrūpo abhavattadā ।। dadāha bhagavānsarvaṃ brahmāṇaṃ ca jagadgurum ।।
bubhuje yogamārgeṇa vṛddhyarthaṃ jagatāṃ śivaḥ ।। viśveśvarastu viśvātmā cāstraṃ pāśupataṃ tathā ।। aṇḍajaḥ padmajaścaiva bhavāṅgabhava eva ca ।। parārdhaṃ brahmaṇo yāvat tāvadbhūtiḥ samāsataḥ ।।
nārāyaṇo api bhagavān dvidhā kṛtvātmanastanum ।। tato brahmāṇamasṛjad brahmā rudraṃ pitāmahaḥ ।। tato brahmāṇamasṛjan mune kalpāntare hariḥ ।। tadā vicārya vai brahmā duḥkhaṃ saṃsāra ityajaḥ ।।
saṃhṛtya prāṇasañcāraṃ pāṣāṇa iva niścalaḥ ।। adhomukhaṃ tu yatpadmaṃ hṛdi saṃsthaṃ suśobhanam ।। tadūrdhvavaktram abhavat kumbhakena nirodhitam ।। tadomiti śivaṃ devam ardhamātrāparaṃ param ।।
yamī yamaviśuddhātmā niyamyaivaṃ hṛdīśvaram ।। tasya hṛtkamalasthasya niyogāccāṃśajo vibhuḥ ।। lohito abhūt svayaṃ nīlaḥ śivasya hṛdayodbhavaḥ ।। nīlaś ca lohitaścaiva yataḥ kālākṛtiḥ pumān ।।
brahmaṇā bhagavānkālaḥ prītātmā cābhavadvibhuḥ ।। nāmāṣṭakena viśvātmā viśvātmānaṃ mahāmune ।। namo bhavāya devāya rasāyāmbumayāya te ।। īśāya vāyave tubhyaṃ saṃsparśāya namo namaḥ ।।
bhīmāya vyomarūpāya śabdamātrāya te namaḥ ।। ugrāya yajamānāya namaste karmayogine ।। rudrāya kathitaṃ viprāñ śrāvayedvā samāhitaḥ ।। evaṃ stutvā mahādevam avaikṣata pitāmahaḥ ।।
tadā prakāśate bhānuḥ kṛṣṇavartmā niśākaraḥ ।। tadāprabhṛti taṃ prāhur aṣṭamūrtiritīśvaram ।। sṛṣṭvaitad akhilaṃ brahmā punaḥ kalpāntare prabhuḥ ।। prajāḥ sraṣṭumanās tepe tata ugraṃ tapo mahat ।।
tato dīrgheṇa kālena duḥkhātkrodho vyajāyata ।। tatastebhyo aśrubindubhyo bhūtāḥ pretāstadābhavan ।। anindata tadā devo brahmātmānam ajo vibhuḥ ।। tataḥ prāṇamayo rudraḥ prādurāsītprabhormukhāt ।।
tadaikādaśadhātmānaṃ pravibhajya vyavasthitaḥ ।। sā cāsṛjattadā lakṣmīṃ durgāṃ śreṣṭhāṃ sarasvatīm ।। kalāṃ vikiriṇīṃ caiva kālīṃ kamalavāsinīm ।। sarvabhūtasya damanīṃ sasṛje ca manonmanīm ।।
rudraiścaiva mahādevas tābhistribhuvaneśvaraḥ ।। mṛtasya tasya devasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। brahmaṇaḥ pradadau prāṇān ātmasthāṃstu tadā prabhuḥ ।। abhyabhāṣata deveśo brahmāṇaṃ paramaṃ vacaḥ ।।
mayeha sthāpitāḥ prāṇās tasmāduttiṣṭha vai prabho ।। pitāmahaḥ prasannātmā netraiḥ phullāmbujaprabhaiḥ ।। sa udvīkṣya ciraṃ kālaṃ snigdhagaṃbhīrayā girā ।। bho bho vada mahābhāga ānandayasi me manaḥ ।।
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā vyājahāra maheśvaraḥ ।। māṃ viddhi paramātmānam enāṃ māyāmajāmiti ।। tataḥ praṇamya taṃ brahmā devadevamuvāca ha ।। bhagavandevadeveśa duḥkhairākulito hyaham ।।
tataḥ prahasya bhagavān pitāmahamumāpatiḥ ।। tasmācchilāda lokeṣu durlabho vai tvayonijaḥ ।। kiṃtu deveśvaro rudraḥ prasīdati yadīśvaraḥ ।। mayā ca viṣṇunā caiva brahmaṇā ca mahātmanā ।।
evaṃ vyāhṛtya viprendram anugṛhya ca taṃ ghṛṇī ।। devairvṛto yayau devaḥ sitenebhena vai prabhuḥ ।। ārādhayanmahādevaṃ tapasātoṣayadbhavam ।। divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu gataṃ kṣaṇamivādbhutam ।।
vajrasūcīmukhaiścānyai raktakīṭaiś ca sarvataḥ ।। asthiśeṣo abhavatpaścāt tamamanyata śaṅkaraḥ ।। tadaiva muniśārdūlaś cotsasarja klamaṃ dvijaḥ ।। tuṣṭastavetyathovāca sagaṇaścomayā saha ।।
dadāmi putraṃ sarvajñaṃ sarvaśāstrārthapāragam ।। harṣagadgadayā vācā somaṃ somavibhūṣaṇam ।। ayonijaṃ mṛtyuhīnaṃ putramicchāmi sattama ।। śilādaṃ brahmaṇā rudraḥ prītyā paramayā punaḥ ।।
tapasā cāvatārārthaṃ munibhiś ca surottamaiḥ ।। pitā bhaviṣyasi mama piturvai jagatāṃ mune ।। somaḥ somopamaḥ prītas tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। yajñāṅgaṇaṃ mahatprāpya yajñārthaṃ yajñavittamaḥ ।।
saṃjātaḥ pūrvamevāhaṃ yugāntāgnisamaprabhaḥ ।। śilādātmajatvaṃ gate mayyupendraḥ sasarjātha vṛṣṭiṃ supuṣpaughamiśrām ।। tryakṣaṃ caturbhujaṃ bālaṃ śūlaṭaṅkagadādharam ।। vajrakuṇḍalinaṃ ghoraṃ nīradopamaniḥsvanam ।।
neduḥ samantataḥ sarve nanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ ।। mantrairmāheśvaraiḥ stutvā sampraṇemurmudānvitāḥ ।। jīvaścendurmahātejā bhāskaraḥ pavano analaḥ ।। viśvedevās tathā rudrā vasavaś ca mahābalāḥ ।।
aditiś ca ditiścaiva śraddhā lajjā dhṛtis tathā ।। vṛṣendraś ca mahātejā dharmo dharmātmajas tathā ।। śilādo api munirdṛṣṭvā pitā me tādṛśaṃ tadā ।। bhagavandevadeveśa triyaṃbaka mamāvyaya ।।
rakṣako jagatāṃ yasmāt pitā me putra sarvaga ।। pitā putra maheśāna jagatāṃ ca jagadguro ।। tvayāhaṃ nandito yasmān nandī nāmnā sureśvara ।। prasīda pitarau me adya rudralokaṃ gatau vibho ।।
mamaiva saphalaṃ loke janma vai jagatāṃ prabho ।। tubhyaṃ namaḥ sureśāna nandīśvara namo astu te ।। putratvameva nandīśa matvā yatkīrtitaṃ mayā ।। yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi mama putraprabhāṣitam ।।
evaṃ stutvā sutaṃ bālaṃ praṇamya bahumānataḥ ।। paśyadhvaṃ munayaḥ sarve mahābhāgyaṃ mamāvyayaḥ ।। matsamaḥ kaḥ pumāṃlloke devo vā dānavo api vā ।। eṣa nandī yato jāto yajñabhūmau hitāya me ।।
uṭajaṃ svaṃ jagāmāśu nidhiṃ labdhveva nirdhanaḥ ।। tadā vai daivikaṃ rūpaṃ tyaktvā mānuṣyam āsthitaḥ ।। mānuṣyamāsthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā pitā me lokapūjitaḥ ।। jātakarmādikāścaiva cakāra mama sarvavit ।।
upadiṣṭā hi tenaiva ṛkśākhā yajuṣas tathā ।। āyurvedaṃ dhanurvedaṃ gāndharvaṃ cāśvalakṣaṇam ।। sampūrṇe saptame varṣe tato atha munisattamau ।। tasyāśramaṃ gatau divyau draṣṭuṃ māṃ cājñayā vibhoḥ ।।
tāta nandyayamalpāyuḥ sarvaśāstrārthapāragaḥ ।। ityuktavati viprendraḥ śilādaḥ putravatsalaḥ ।। hā putra putra putreti papāta ca samantataḥ ।। tasya cārtasvaraṃ śrutvā tadāśramanivāsinaḥ ।।
tuṣṭuvuś ca mahādevaṃ triyaṃbakamumāpatim ।। dūrvāmayutasaṃkhyātāṃ sarvadravyasamanvitām ।। viceṣṭaś ca lalāpāsau mṛtavannipapāta ca ।। mṛtavatpatitaṃ sākṣāt pitaraṃ ca pitāmaham ।।
hṛtpuṇḍarīke suṣire dhyātvā devaṃ triyaṃbakam ।। saritaścāntare puṇye sthitaṃ māṃ parameśvaraḥ ।। vatsa nandinmahābāho mṛtyorbhītiḥ kutastava ।। vatsainattava dehaṃ ca laukikaṃ paramārthataḥ ।।
devaiś ca munibhiḥ siddhair gandharvairdānavottamaiḥ ।। saṃsārasya svabhāvo ayaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।। evamuktvā tu māṃ sākṣāt sarvadevamaheśvaraḥ ।। pasparśa bhagavān rudraḥ paramārtiharo haraḥ ।।
nirīkṣya gaṇapāṃścaiva devīṃ himavataḥ sutām ।। ajaro jarayā tyakto nityaṃ duḥkhavivarjitaḥ ।। mameṣṭo gaṇapaścaiva madvīryo matparākramaḥ ।। madbalaścaiva bhavitā mahāyogabalānvitaḥ ।।
kuśeśayamayīṃ mālāṃ samunmucyātmanastadā ।। tayāhaṃ mālayā jātaḥ śubhayā kaṇṭhasaktayā ।। tata eva samādāya hastena parameśvaraḥ ।। tato jaṭāśritaṃ vāri gṛhītvā cātinirmalam ।।
tataḥ sā divyatoyā ca pūrṇāsitajalā śubhā ।। tāmāha ca mahādevo nadīṃ paramaśobhanām ।। tasmājjaṭodakā puṇyā bhaviṣyasi saridvarā ।। tato devyā mahādevaḥ śilādatanayaṃ prabhuḥ ।।
sā māmāghrāya śirasi pāṇibhyāṃ parimārjatī ।। payasā śaṅkhagaureṇa devadevaṃ nirīkṣya sā ।। nadīṃ trisrotasaṃ devo bhagavānavadadbhavaḥ ।। nanāda nādāttasmācca saridanyā tato abhavat ।।
jāṃbūnadamayaṃ citraṃ sarvaratnamayaṃ śubham ।। mukuṭaṃ cābabandheśo mama mūrdhni vṛṣadhvajaḥ ।। ābabandha mahādevaḥ svayameva maheśvaraḥ ।। meghāṃbhasā cābhyaṣiñcac chilādanam atho mune ।।
yasmāt suvarṇānniḥsṛtya nadyeṣā sampravartate ।। jāmbūnadamayādyasmād dvitīyā mukuṭācchubhā ।। etatpañcanadaṃ nāma japyeśvarasamīpagam ।। pūjayecchivasāyujyaṃ prayātyeva na saṃśayaḥ ।।
devīmuvāca śarvāṇīm umāṃ girisutāmajām ।। gaṇendraṃ vyāhariṣyāmi kiṃ vā tvaṃ manyase avyaye ।। smayantī varadaṃ prāha bhavaṃ bhūtapatiṃ patim ।। dātumarhasi deveśa śailādistanayo mama ।।
sasmāra gaṇapān divyān devadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ ।। sarve sahasrahastāś ca sahasrāyudhapāṇayaḥ ।। koṭikālāgnisaṃkāśā jaṭāmukuṭadhāriṇaḥ ।। asaṃkhyātā mahātmānas tatrājagmurmudā yutāḥ ।।
mukhāḍambaravādyāni vādayantastathaiva ca ।। vimāneṣu tathārūḍhā hemacitreṣu vai gaṇāḥ ।। vāditrairvividhaiścānyaiḥ paṭahairekapuṣkaraiḥ ।। mardalairveṇuvīṇābhir vividhaistālaniḥsvanaiḥ ।।
vādyamānairmahāyogā ājagmurdevasaṃsadam ।। praṇamya devaṃ devīṃ ca idaṃ vacanam abruvan ।। kimarthaṃ ca smṛtā deva ājñāpaya mahādyute ।। hanmo mṛtyusutāṃ mṛtyuṃ paśuvaddhanma padmajam ।।
ānayāmaḥ susaṃkruddhā daityānvā saha dānavaiḥ ।। kasya vādyotsavo deva sarvakāmasamṛddhaye ।। uvāca devaḥ sampūjya koṭikoṭiśatānprabhuḥ ।। śrutvā ca prayatātmānaḥ kurudhvaṃ tadaśaṅkitāḥ ।।
vipro ayaṃ nāyakaścaiva senānīr vaḥ samṛddhimān ।। senānyam abhiṣiñcadhvaṃ mahāyogapatiṃ patim ।। evamastviti saṃmantrya saṃbhārānāharaṃstataḥ ।। āsanaṃ merusaṃkāśaṃ manoharam upāharan ।।
muktādāmāvalambaṃ ca maṇiratnāvabhāsitam ।। cāruratnakasaṃyuktaṃ maṇḍapaṃ viśvatomukham ।। tasyāgrataḥ pādapīṭhaṃ nīlavajrāvabhāsitam ।। sampūrṇau paramāmbhobhir aravindāvṛtānanau ।।
tāmrajaṃ mṛnmayaṃ caiva sarvatīrthāmbupūritam ।। keyūre kuṇḍale caiva mukuṭaṃ hārameva ca ।। dattaṃ mahātmanā tena brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā ।। vyajanaṃ candraśubhraṃ ca hemadaṇḍaṃ sucāmaram ।।
mukuṭaṃ kāñcanaṃ caiva nirmitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā ।। jāṃbūnadamayaṃ sūtraṃ keyūradvayameva ca ।। samantān ninyur avyagrā gaṇapā devasaṃmatāḥ ।। munayo bhagavānbrahmā navabrahmāṇa eva ca ।।
teṣvāgateṣu sarveṣu bhagavānparameśvaraḥ ।। pitāmaho api bhagavān niyogādeva tasya tu ।। arcayitvā tato brahmā svayamevābhyaṣecayat ।। abhyaṣiñcanta vidhivad gaṇendraṃ śivaśāsanāt ।।
stutavatsu tatasteṣu viṣṇuḥ sarvajagatpatiḥ ।। prāñjaliḥ praṇato bhūtvā jayaśabdaṃ cakāra ca ।। evaṃ stutaścābhiṣikto devaiḥ sabrahmakaistadā ।। marutāṃ ca sutā devī suyaśākhyā babhūva yā ।।
cāmare cāmarāsaktahastāgraiḥ strīgaṇairyutā ।। alaṃkṛtā mahālakṣmyā mukuṭādyaiḥ subhūṣaṇaiḥ ।। vṛṣendraś ca sito nāgaḥ siṃhaḥ siṃhadhvajas tathā ।। adyāpi sadṛśaḥ kaścin mayā nāsti vibhuḥ kvacit ।।
āruhya vṛṣamīśāno mayā devyā gataḥ śivaḥ ।। munidevarṣayaḥ siddhā ājñāṃ pāśupatīṃ dvijāḥ ।। nandiko nagajābhartus teṣāṃ pāśupatīṃ śubhām ।। bhavabhaktāstadā cāsaṃs tasmādevaṃ samarcayet ।।
brahmaghnadaśasaṃtulyaṃ tasya pāpaṃ garīyasam ।। ādau kuryānnamaskāraṃ tadante śivatāṃ vrajet ।। sarvātmabhāvaṃ rudrasya svarūpaṃ vaktumarhasi ।। satyalokaś ca pātālaṃ narakārṇavakoṭayaḥ ।।
vaimānikāstathānye ca tiṣṭhantyasya prasādataḥ ।। samaṣṭirūpaḥ sarvātmā saṃsthitaḥ sarvadā śivaḥ ।। na vijānanti saṃmūḍhā māyayā tasya mohitāḥ ।। tasmātpraṇamya taṃ vakṣye jagatāṃ nirṇayaṃ śubham ।।
bhuvanānāṃ svarūpaṃ ca brahmāṇḍe kathayāmyaham ।। tapaḥ satyaṃ ca saptaite lokāstvaṇḍodbhavāḥ śubhāḥ ।। mahātalādayasteṣāṃ adhastānnarakāḥ kramāt ।। prāsādaiś ca vicitraiś ca bhavasyāyatanais tathā ।।
nṛpeṇa balinā caiva pātālasvargavāsinā ।। pītaṃ sutalamityuktaṃ vitalaṃ vidrumaprabham ।। kṣmāyāstu yāvadvistāro hy adhasteṣāṃ ca suvratāḥ ।। sahasrayojanaṃ vyoma daśasāhasrameva ca ।।
vyomnaḥ pramāṇaṃ mūlaṃ tu triṃśatsāhasrakeṇa tu ।। rasātalamiti khyātaṃ tathānyaiś ca niṣevitam ।। talātalamiti khyātaṃ sarvaśobhāsamanvitam ।। pūrvadevaiḥ samākīrṇaṃ sutalaṃ ca tathāparaiḥ ।।
mahāntakādyair nāgaiś ca prahlādenāsureṇa ca ।। mahākumbhena vīreṇa hayagrīveṇa dhīmatā ।। tathānyair vividhair vīrais talaṃ caiva suśobhitam ।। skandena nandinā sārdhaṃ gaṇapaiḥ sarvato vṛtaḥ ।।
kṣmātalāni dharā cāpi saptadhā kathayāmi vaḥ ।। samudraiḥ saptabhiścaiva sarvataḥ samalaṃkṛtā ।। śākaḥ puṣkaranāmā ca dvīpāstvabhyantare kramāt ।। nānāveṣadharo bhūtvā sānnidhyaṃ kurute haraḥ ।।
dadhyarṇavaś ca kṣīrodaḥ svādūdaścāpyanukramāt ।। jalarūpī bhavaḥ śrīmān krīḍate cormibāhubhiḥ ।। śete śivajñānadhiyā sākṣādvai yoganidrayā ।। yadā suptastadā suptaṃ tanmayaṃ ca carācaram ।।
saṃhṛtaṃ devadevasya prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ ।। aniruddhaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharam ।। nārāyaṇasamāḥ sarve sarvasaṃpatsamanvitāḥ ।। vālakhilyāś ca siddhāś ca mitrāvaruṇakau tathā ।।
saptadvīpeṣu tiṣṭhanti nānāśṛṅgā mahodayāḥ ।। dharāyāḥ patayaścāsan bahavaḥ kālagauravāt ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu atītānāgateṣviha ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu atītānāgateṣu ca ।।
svāyaṃbhuvasya ca manoḥ pautrāstvāsanmahābalāḥ ।। āgnīdhraścāgnibāhuś ca medhā medhātithirvasuḥ ।। priyavrato abhyaṣiñcattān sapta saptasu pārthivān ।। plakṣadvīpeśvaraścāpi tena medhātithiḥ kṛtaḥ ।।
jyotiṣmantaṃ kuśadvīpe rājānaṃ kṛtavānnṛpaḥ ।। śākadvīpeśvaraṃ cāpi havyaṃ cakre priyavrataḥ ।। puṣkare savanasyāpi mahāvītaḥ suto abhavat ।। mahāvītaṃ smṛtaṃ varṣaṃ tasya nāmnā mahātmanaḥ ।।
havyo apyajanayat putrāñ chākadvīpeśvaraḥ prabhuḥ ।। kusumottaramodākī saptamastu mahādrumaḥ ।। kumārasya tu kaumāraṃ dvitīyaṃ parikīrtitam ।। maṇīcakaṃ caturthaṃ tu māṇīcakamihocyate ।।
modakaṃ cāpi modāker varṣaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ prakīrtitam ।। teṣāṃ tu nāmabhistāni sapta varṣāṇi tatra vai ।। kuśalo manugaścoṣṇaḥ pīvaraścāndhakārakaḥ ।। teṣāṃ svanāmabhir deśāḥ krauñcadvīpāśrayāḥ śubhāḥ ।।
uṣṇasyoṣṇaḥ smṛto deśaḥ pīvaraḥ pīvarasya ca ।। munerdeśo muniḥ prokto dundubher dundubhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। jyotiṣmantaḥ kuśadvīpe sapta cāsanmahaujasaḥ ।। ṣaṣṭhaḥ prabhākaraścāpi saptamaḥ kapilaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
tṛtīyaṃ dvairathaṃ caiva caturthaṃ lavaṇaṃ smṛtam ।। saptamaṃ kapilaṃ nāma kapilasya prakīrtitam ।। śvetaś ca haritaścaiva jīmūto rohitas tathā ।। śvetasya deśaḥ śvetastu haritasya ca hāritaḥ ।।
vaidyuto vaidyutasyāpi mānasasya ca mānasaḥ ।। plakṣadvīpe tu vakṣyāmi jambūdvīpādanantaram ।। jyeṣṭhaḥ śāntabhayasteṣāṃ saptavarṣāṇi tāni vai ।। ānandaś ca śivaścaiva kṣemakaś ca dhruvas tathā ।।
niveśitāni taistāni pūrvaṃ svāyaṃbhuve antare ।। varṇāśramācārayutāḥ prajāstatra niveśitāḥ ।। jñeyaḥ pañcasu dharmo vai varṇāśramavibhāgaśaḥ ।। pañcasveteṣu dvīpeṣu sarvasādhāraṇaṃ smṛtam ।।
anye ca puṣkaradvīpe prajātāś ca prajeśvarāḥ ।। prajāpateś ca rudrasya bhāvāmṛtasukhotkaṭāḥ ।। priyavrato abhyaṣiñcadvai jaṃbūdvīpeśvaraṃ nṛpaḥ ।। bhavārcanarataḥ śrīmān gomāndhīmāndvijarṣabhāḥ ।।
sarve māheśvarāścaiva mahādevaparāyaṇāḥ ।। harivarṣastṛtīyastu caturtho vai tvilāvṛtaḥ ।। kurustu saptamasteṣāṃ bhadrāśvastvaṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। nābhestu dakṣiṇaṃ varṣaṃ hemākhyaṃ tu pitā dadau ।।
naiṣadhaṃ yatsmṛtaṃ varṣaṃ haraye tatpitā dadau ।। nīlācalāśritaṃ varṣaṃ ramyāya pradadau pitā ।। yaduttaraṃ śṛṅgavarṣaṃ pitā tatkurave dadau ।। gandhamādanavarṣaṃ tu ketumālāya dattavān ।।
āgnīdhrasteṣu varṣeṣu putrāṃstānabhiṣicya vai ।। tapasā bhāvitaścaiva svādhyāyaniratastvabhūt ।। yāni kiṃpuruṣādyāni varṣāṇyaṣṭau śubhāni ca ।। viparyayo na teṣvasti jarāmṛtyubhayaṃ na ca ।।
na teṣvasti yugāvasthā kṣetreṣvaṣṭasu sarvataḥ ।। bhaktāḥ prāsaṃgikāścāpi teṣu kṣetreṣu yānti te ।। tatra teṣāṃ mahādevaḥ sānnidhyaṃ kurute sadā ।। sukhinaḥ sarvadā teṣāṃ sa eveha parā gatiḥ ।।
nābhistvajanayatputraṃ merudevyāṃ mahāmatiḥ ।। ṛṣabhādbharato jajñe vīraḥ putraśatāgrajaḥ ।। jñānavairāgyamāśritya jitvendriyamahoragān ।। nagno jaṭī nirāhāraś cīrī dhvāntagato hi saḥ ।।
himādrerdakṣiṇaṃ varṣaṃ bharatāya nyavedayat ।। bharatasyātmajo vidvān sumatirnāma dhārmikaḥ ।। putrasaṃkrāmitaśrīko vanaṃ rājā viveśa saḥ ।। nānāratnamayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ sthitaḥ sthitimatāṃ varaḥ ।।
praviṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśādhastād vistṛtaḥ ṣoḍaśaiva tu ।। vistārāt triguṇaś cāsya pariṇāho anumaṇḍalaḥ ।। dhattūrapuṣpasaṃkāśaḥ sarvadevaniketanaḥ ।। lakṣayojana āyāmas tasyaivaṃ tu mahāgireḥ ।।
śeṣaṃ copari viprendrā dharāyāstasya śṛṅgiṇaḥ ।। ūcurvistāramasyaiva dviguṇaṃ mūlato gireḥ ।। paścime nīlasaṃkāśa uttare vidrumaprabhaḥ ।। nānādevagaṇaiḥ kīrṇā maṇijālasamāvṛtā ।।
toraṇair hemacitraistu maṇikḷptaiḥ pathi sthitaiḥ ।। stanabhāravinamraiś ca madaghūrṇitalocanaiḥ ।। dīrghikābhirvicitrābhiḥ phullāmbhoruhasaṃkulaiḥ ।। nīlotpalaiścotpalaiś ca haimaiścāpi sugandhibhiḥ ।।
virājate purī śubhrā tayāsau parvataḥ śubhaḥ ।। amarāvatīsamā divyā sarvabhogasamanvitā ।। bhavanairāvṛtā divyair jāṃbūnadamayaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। tādṛśī gandhavantī ca vāyavyāṃ diśi śobhanā ।।
parvatasya diganteṣu śobhate divi sarvadā ।। sarvabhogayutaṃ puṇyaṃ dīrghikābhirnagottamam ।। tathānyairvividhākārair bhūtasaṃghaiś caturvidhaiḥ ।। sahasrabhaumaṃ vistīrṇaṃ vimānaṃ vāmataḥ sthitam ।।
siṃhāsane maṇimaye devyāste ṣaṇmukhena ca ।। padmarāgamayaṃ divyaṃ padmajasya ca dakṣiṇe ।। somasya varuṇasyātha nirṛteḥ pāvakasya ca ।। teṣāṃ teṣāṃ vimāneṣu divyeṣu vividheṣu ca ।।
siddheśvaraiś ca bhagavāñ chailādiḥ śiṣyasaṃmataḥ ।। sanakaś ca sanandaś ca sadṛśāś ca sahasraśaḥ ।। bālasūryapratīkāśaṃ vimānaṃ tatra śobhanam ।। ṣaṇmukhasya gaṇeśasya gaṇānāṃ tu sahasraśaḥ ।।
tasya jambūnadī nāma mūlamāveṣṭya saṃsthitā ।। atyucchritaḥ suvistīrṇaḥ sarvakālaphalapradaḥ ।। tatra jambūphalāhārāḥ keciccāmṛtabhojanāḥ ।। merupādāśrito viprā dvīpo ayaṃ madhyamaḥ śubhaḥ ।।
navavarṣaṃ tu vakṣyāmi jaṃbūdvīpaṃ yathātatham ।। vistārānmaṇḍalāccaiva yojanaiś ca nibodhata ।। anu dvīpaṃ sahasrāṇāṃ dviguṇaṃ dviguṇottaram ।। dvīpaiś ca saptabhir yuktā lokālokāvṛtā śubhā ।।
śṛṅgī tasyottare viprās trayaste varṣaparvatāḥ ।। hemakūṭa iti khyāto himavāṃstasya dakṣiṇe ।। mālyavāngandhamādaś ca dvāvetāvudagāyatau ।। teṣām antaraviṣkambho navasāhasramekaśaḥ ।।
hemakūṭaṃ paraṃ tasmān nāmnā kiṃpuruṣaṃ smṛtam ।। harivarṣātparaṃ caiva meroḥ śubhamilāvṛtam ।। ramyātparataraṃ śvetaṃ vikhyātaṃ taddhiraṇmayam ।। dhanuḥsaṃsthe tu vijñeye dve varṣe dakṣiṇottare ।।
meroḥ paścimapūrveṇa dve tu dīrghetare smṛte ।। vedyardhe dakṣiṇe trīṇi varṣāṇi trīṇi cottare ।। dakṣiṇena tu nīlasya niṣadhasyottareṇa tu ।। yojanānāṃ sahasre dve upariṣṭāttu vistṛtaḥ ।।
tasya pratīcyāṃ vijñeyaḥ parvato gandhamādanaḥ ।। jambūdvīpasya vistārāt samena tu samantataḥ ।। avagāḍhāścobhayataḥ samudrau pūrvapaścimau ।। taruṇādityasaṃkāśo hairaṇyo niṣadhaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
vṛttākṛtiparīṇāhaś caturasraḥ samutthitaḥ ।। mayūrabarhavarṇastu śātakuṃbhas triśṛṅgavān ।। mandaro devakūṭaś ca pūrvasyāṃ diśi parvatau ।। pūrvataś cāyatāvetāv arṇavāntarvyavasthitau ।।
yathā pūrvau tathā yāmyāv etau paścimataḥ śritau ।। pūrvataś cāyatāvetāv arṇavāntarvyavasthitau ।। yo asau merurdvijaśreṣṭhāḥ prāṃśuḥ kanakaparvataḥ ।। yairviṣṭabdhā na calati saptadvīpavatī mahī ।।
pūrve tu mandaro nāma dakṣiṇe gandhamādanaḥ ।। mahāvṛkṣāḥ samutpannāś catvāro dvīpaketavaḥ ।। pralambaśākhāśikharaḥ kadambaś caityapādapaḥ ।। jambūḥ sadā puṇyaphalā sadā mālyopaśobhitā ।।
vipulasyāpi śailasya paścime ca mahātmanaḥ ।। supārśvasyottarasyāpi śṛṅge jāto mahādrumaḥ ।। teṣāṃ caturṇāṃ vakṣyāmi śailendrāṇāṃ yathākramam ।। manoharāṇi catvāri devakrīḍanakāni ca ।।
pūrve caitrarathaṃ nāma dakṣiṇe gandhamādanam ।। mitreśvaraṃ tu pūrve tu ṣaṣṭheśvaram ataḥ param ।। mahāsarāṃsi ca tathā catvāri munipuṅgavāḥ ।। aruṇodaṃ saraḥ pūrvaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ mānasaṃ smṛtam ।।
śākhasya dakṣiṇe kṣetraṃ viśākhasya ca paścime ।। aruṇodasya pūrveṇa śailendrā nāmataḥ smṛtāḥ ।। sitāntaś ca kuraṇḍaś ca kuraraścācalottamaḥ ।। mahānīlo atha rucakaḥ sabindurdarduras tathā ।।
ityete parvatavarā hy anye ca girayas tathā ।। teṣu teṣu girīndreṣu guhāsu ca vaneṣu ca ।। saraso mānasasyeha dakṣiṇena mahācalāḥ ।। śailaś ca viśirāścaiva śikharaścācalottamaḥ ।।
pañcaśailo atha kailāso himavāṃścācalottamaḥ ।। teṣu teṣu ca sarveṣu parvateṣu vaneṣu ca ।। digbhāge dakṣiṇe proktāḥ paścime ca vadāmi vaḥ ।। kumudo madhumāṃścaiva hy añjano mukuṭas tathā ।।
pārijātaś ca śailendraḥ śrīśṛṅgaścācalottamaḥ ।। sarve paścimadigbhāge rudrakṣetrasamanvitāḥ ।। ye sthitāḥ kīrtyamānāṃstān saṃkṣipyeha nibodhata ।। nāgaś ca kapilaścaiva indraśailaś ca sānumān ।।
puṣpakośaḥ praśailaś ca virajaścācalottamaḥ ।। jārudhiścaiva śailendra eta uttarasaṃsthitāḥ ।। asaṃkhyātāni divyāni vimānāni sahasraśaḥ ।। santi caivāntaradroṇyaḥ sarāṃsyupavanāni ca ।।
kṛtavāsāḥ sapatnīkāḥ prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ ।। tathā tālavane proktam indropendroragātmanām ।। vidyādharāṇāṃ siddhānāṃ puṇye tvāmravane śubhe ।। sūryasya kiṃśukavane tathā rudragaṇasya ca ।।
kaumude tu vane viṣṇupramukhānāṃ mahātmanām ।। śeṣastvaśeṣajagatāṃ patirāste atigarvitaḥ ।। viṣṇorviśvagurormūrtir divyaḥ sākṣāddhalāyudhaḥ ।। vane panasavṛkṣāṇāṃ saśukrā dānavādayaḥ ।।
manoharavane vṛkṣāḥ sarvakoṭisamanvitāḥ ।। saṃtānakasthalīmadhye sākṣāddevī sarasvatī ।। asaṃkhyātā mayāpyatra vaktuṃ no vistareṇa tu ।। tasya prācyāṃ kumudādrikūṭo asau bahuvistaraḥ ।।
suvarṇakoṭare puṇye rākṣasānāṃ mahātmanām ।। mahānīle api śailendre purāṇi daśa pañca ca ।। veṇusaudhe mahāśaile vidyādharapuratrayam ।। vasudhāre vasūnāṃ tu nivāsaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।
saptasthānāni puṇyāni siddhāvāsayutāni ca ।। gajaśaile tu durgādyāḥ sumedhe vasavas tathā ।। aśītirdevapuryastu hemakakṣe nagottame ।। pañcakūṭe purāṇyāsan pañcakoṭipramāṇataḥ ।।
tāmrābhe kādraveyāṇāṃ viśākhe tu guhasya vai ।। piśācake kuberasya harikūṭe harergṛham ।। kṛṣṇe gandharvanilayaḥ pāṇḍure purasaptakam ।। sahasraśikhare śaile daityānāmugrakarmaṇām ।।
mukuṭe pannagāvāsaḥ puṣpaketau munīśvarāḥ ।। takṣake caiva śailendre catvāryāyatanāni ca ।। kuberasya ca somasya tathānyeṣāṃ mahātmanām ।। śrīkaṇṭhādriguhāvāsī sarvāvāsaḥ sahomayā ।।
aṇḍasyāsya pravṛttistu śrīkaṇṭhena na saṃśayaḥ ।। cakravartina ityuktās tato vidyeśvarāstviha ।। maryādāparvateṣvadya śṛṇvantu pravadāmy aham ।। kālāgniśivaparyantaṃ kathaṃ vakṣye savistaram ।।
hemavaiḍūryamāṇikyanīlagomedakāntibhiḥ ।। śākhāśatasahasrāḍhye sarvadrumavibhūṣite ।। pārijātakasampūrṇe nānāpakṣigaṇānvite ।। nitambapuṣpasālamben-aikasattvagaṇānvite ।।
nirjharaiḥ kusumākīrṇair anekaiś ca vibhūṣite ।। snigdhavarṇaṃ mahāmūlam anekaskandhapādapam ।। tatra bhūtavanaṃ nāma nānābhūtagaṇālayam ।। dīptamāyatanaṃ tatra mahāmaṇivibhūṣitam ।।
sphāṭikaiś ca vicitraiś ca gopuraiś ca samanvitam ।। kṣitāvitastataḥ samyak śarveṇādhiṣṭhitaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। maṇḍapaiḥ suvicitrais tu sphāṭikastambhasaṃyutaiḥ ।। varāhagajasiṃharkṣaśārdūlakarabhānanaiḥ ।।
pramathairvividhaiḥ sthūlair girikūṭopamaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। nānāvarṇākṛtidharair nānāsaṃsthānasaṃsthitaiḥ ।। brahmendraviṣṇusaṃkāśair aṇimādiguṇānvitaiḥ ।। tatra bhūtapaterdevāḥ pūjāṃ nityaṃ prayuñjate ।।
lalitāvasitodgītair vṛttavalgitagarjitaiḥ ।। siddharṣidevagandharvair brahmaṇā ca mahātmanā ।। vibhaktacāruśikharaṃ yatra tacchaṅkhavarcasam ।। nivāsaḥ koṭiyakṣāṇāṃ tathānyeṣāṃ mahātmanām ।।
tasminnāyatane somaḥ sadāste sagaṇo haraḥ ।। suvarṇamaṇisopānā kuberaśikhare śubhe ।। nīlavaiḍūryapatraiś ca gandhopetairmahotpalaiḥ ।। yakṣagandharvanārībhir apsarobhiś ca sevitā ।।
upaspṛṣṭajalā puṇyā nadī mandākinī śubhā ।। vaiḍūryamaṇisampannaṃ tatrāste śaṅkaro avyayaḥ ।। vanaṃ dvijasahasrāḍhyaṃ mṛgapakṣisamākulam ।। nandāyāḥ paścime tīre kiṃcid vai dakṣiṇāśrite ।।
tatrāpi śatadhā kṛtvā hy ātmānaṃ cāmbayā saha ।। evaṃ śatasahasrāṇi śarvasyāyatanāni tu ।। nadīnadataṭākānāṃ tīreṣvarṇavasaṃdhiṣu ।। sarovarebhyaḥ sambhūtās tv asaṃkhyātā dvijottamāḥ ।।
paścimāgrāḥ pavitrāś ca prativarṣaṃ prakīrtitāḥ ।। ādhāraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ devānāmamṛtākaraḥ ।। saptamenānilapathā pravṛttā cāmṛtodakā ।। tārākoṭisahasrāṇāṃ nabhasaś ca samāyutā ।।
catvāryaśītiś ca tathā sahasrāṇāṃ samucchritaḥ ।। tatrāsīno yataḥ śarvaḥ sāmbaḥ saha gaṇeśvaraiḥ ।। giriṃ meruṃ nadī puṇyā sā prayāti pradakṣiṇam ।। merorantarakūṭeṣu nipapāta caturṣvapi ।।
niyogāddevadevasya praviṣṭā sā mahārṇavam ।। sarvadvīpādrivarṣeṣu bahavaḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। ketumāle narāḥ kālāḥ sarve panasabhojanāḥ ।। bhadrāśve śuklavarṇāś ca striyaścandrāṃśusaṃnibhāḥ ।।
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi jīvanti śivabhāvitāḥ ।। tathā ramaṇake jīvā nyagrodhaphalabhojanāḥ ।। jīvanti śuklāste sarve śivadhyānaparāyaṇāḥ ।। ekādaśa sahasrāṇi śatāni daśapañca ca ।।
hairaṇmayā ivātyartham īśvarārpitamānasāḥ ।। sarve maithunajātāś ca kṣīriṇaḥ kṣīrabhojanāḥ ।। anāmayā hyaśokāś ca nityaṃ sukhaniṣeviṇaḥ ।। jīvanti te mahāvīryā na cānyastrīniṣeviṇaḥ ।।
hṛṣṭānāṃ supravṛddhānāṃ sarvānnāmṛtabhojinām ।। śyāmāṅgānāṃ sadā sarvabhūṣaṇāspadadehinām ।। tatra candraprabhaṃ śambhor vimānaṃ candramaulinaḥ ।। śatāyuṣaḥ samākhyātā nānāvarṇālpadehinaḥ ।।
nānājñānārthasampannā durbalāścālpabhoginaḥ ।। tāmradvīpaṃ gatāḥ kecit keciddeśaṃ gabhastimat ।। kecinmlecchāḥ pulindāś ca nānājātisamudbhavāḥ ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyā madhye śūdrāś ca sarvaśaḥ ।।
teṣāṃ saṃvyavahāro ayaṃ vartate atra parasparam ।। saṃkalpaścābhimānaś ca āśramāṇāṃ yathāvidhi ।। teṣāṃ ca yugakarmāṇi nānyatra munipuṅgavāḥ ।। suvarṇavarṇāś ca narāḥ striyaścāpsarasopamāḥ ।।
śuddhasattvāś ca hemābhāḥ sadārāḥ plakṣabhojanāḥ ।। devalokāccyutāḥ sarve devākārāś ca sarvaśaḥ ।। na jarā bādhate tena na ca jīryanti te narāḥ ।। madhyamaṃ yanmayā proktaṃ nāmnā varṣamilāvṛtam ।।
candrasūryau na nakṣatraṃ na prakāśam ilāvṛte ।। padmapattrasugandhāś ca jāyante bhavabhāvitāḥ ।। devalokāgatāstatra jāyante hyajarāmarāḥ ।। āyuḥpramāṇaṃ jīvanti varṣe divye tvilāvṛte ।।
na kṣudhā na klamaścāpi na jano mṛtyumāṃs tathā ।। indragopapratīkāśaṃ jāyate bhāsvaraṃ tu tat ।। varṇāyurbhojanādyāni saṃkṣipya na tu vistarāt ।। sarve nāgāś ca niṣadhe śeṣavāsukitakṣakāḥ ।।
nīle tu vaiḍūryamaye siddhā brahmarṣayo amalāḥ ।। śṛṅgavān parvataścaiva pitṝṇāṃ nilayaḥ sadā ।। sarvādriṣu mahādevo hariṇā brahmaṇāṃbayā ।। nīlaśvetatriśṛṅge ca bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ ।।
nīlaś ca vaiḍūryamayaḥ śvetaḥ śuklo hiraṇmayaḥ ।। ete parvatarājāno jaṃbūdvīpe vyavasthitāḥ ।। ṛjvāyatāḥ pratidiśaṃ niviṣṭā varṣaparvatāḥ ।। gomedako atra prathamo dvitīyaścāndra ucyate ।।
pañcamaḥ somako nāma sumanāḥ ṣaṣṭha ucyate ।। saptaite girayaḥ proktāḥ plakṣadvīpe viśeṣataḥ ।। kumudaścottamaścaiva parvataś ca balāhakaḥ ।। kuśadvīpe tu saptaiva dvīpāś ca kulaparvatāḥ ।।
vidrumaḥ prathamaḥ prokto dvitīyo hemaparvataḥ ।। kuśeśayaḥ pañcamastu ṣaṣṭho harigiriḥ smṛtaḥ ।। mandā iti hyapāṃ nāma mandaro dhāraṇād apām ।। somaḥ sanandī bhagavān āste hemagṛhottame ।।
avimukte mahākṣetre lebhe sa paramaṃ varam ।। avimuktādupāgamya cakre vāsaṃ sa mandare ।। krauñcadvīpe tu sapteha krauñcādyāḥ kulaparvatāḥ ।। andhakārātparaścāpi divāvṛnnāma parvataḥ ।।
vivindātparataścāpi puṇḍarīko mahāgiriḥ ।। ete ratnamayāḥ sapta krauñcadvīpasya parvatāḥ ।। udayo raivataścāpi śyāmako munisattamāḥ ।। āṃbikeyātparo ramyaḥ sarvauṣadhisamanvitaḥ ।।
puṣkare parvataḥ śrīmān eka eva mahāśilaḥ ।। dvīpasya tasya pūrvārdhe citrasānusthito mahān ।। adhaścaiva catustriṃśat sahasrāṇi mahācalaḥ ।। sthito velāsamīpe tu navacandra ivoditaḥ ।।
tāvadeva tu vistīrṇaḥ pārśvataḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ ।। eka eva mahāsānuḥ saṃniveśāddvidhā kṛtaḥ ।। rājatau mānasasyātha parvatasyānumaṇḍalau ।। tasyaivābhyantaro yastu dhātakīkhaṇḍa ucyate ।।
puṣkaradvīpavistāravistīrṇo asau samantataḥ ।। evaṃ dvīpāḥ samudraistu saptasaptabhir āvṛtāḥ ।। evaṃ dvīpasamudrāṇāṃ vṛddhirjñeyā parasparam ।। svādūdakasamudrastu samantātpariveṣṭya ca ।।
kāñcanī dviguṇā bhūmiḥ sarvā caikaśilopamā ।। prakāśaścāprakāśaś ca lokālokaḥ sa ucyate ।। yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi daśa tasyocchrayaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। arvācīne tu tasyārdhe caranti raviraśmayaḥ ।।
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ prokto bhūrlokasya ca vistaraḥ ।। āvahādyā niviṣṭāstu vāyorvai sapta nemayaḥ ।। saṃvaho vivahaścātha tataścordhvaṃ parāvahaḥ ।। balāhakās tathā bhānuś candro nakṣatrarāśayaḥ ।।
yojanānāṃ mahīpṛṣṭhād ūrdhvaṃ pañcadaśa ā dhruvāt ।। rathaḥ ṣoḍaśasāhasro bhāskarasya tathopari ।। koṭiyojanamākramya maharloko dhruvāddhruvaḥ ।। janalokāttapolokaś catasraḥ koṭayo mataḥ ।।
puṇyalokāstu saptaite hy aṇḍe asminkathitā dvijāḥ ।। māyāntāścaiva ghorādyā aṣṭāviṃśatireva tu ।। avīcyantāni sarvāṇi rauravādyāni teṣu ca ।। aṇḍamādau mayā proktam aṇḍasyāvaraṇāni ca ।।
aṇḍānāmīdṛśānāṃ tu koṭyo jñeyāḥ sahasraśaḥ ।। aṇḍeṣveteṣu sarveṣu bhuvanāni caturdaśa ।। aṇḍeṣu cāṇḍabāhyeṣu tathāṇḍāvaraṇeṣu ca ।। asyātmano maheśasya mahādevasya dhīmataḥ ।।
asyāṣṭamūrteḥ śarvasya śivasya gṛhamedhinaḥ ।। paśavaḥ kiṅkarāstasya sarve dehābhimāninaḥ ।। pradhānamūrtistvatha ṣoḍaśāṅgo maheśvaraścāṣṭatanuḥ sa eva ।। jyotirgaṇaḥ śakramukhāḥ surāś ca vaimānikāḥ sthāvarajaṅgamāś ca ।।
yakṣaṃ gatvā niścayātpāvakādyāḥ śaktikṣīṇāścābhavan yattato api ।। vāyustṛṇaṃ cālayituṃ tathānye svānsvānprabhāvān sakalāmarendrāḥ ।। sureśvaraṃ yakṣamuvāca ko vā bhavānitītthaṃ sa kutūhalātmā ।। umā śubhairābharaṇairanekaiḥ suśobhamānā tvanu cāvirāsīt ।।
tāṃ śakramukhyā bahuśobhamānām umāmajāṃ haimavatīmapṛcchan । kimetadīśe bahuśobhamāne vāṃbike yakṣavapuścakāsti ।। niśamya tadyakṣamumāmbikāha tvagocaraśceti surāḥ saśakrāḥ । praṇemurenāṃ mṛgarājagāminīmumāmajāṃ lohitaśuklakṛṣṇām ।।
ahaṃ purāsaṃ prakṛtiś ca puṃso yakṣasya cājñāvaśagetyathāha ।। ajaś ca aṇḍādakhilaṃ ca tasmāj jyotirgaṇairlokamajātmakaṃ tat ।। devakṣetrāṇi cālokya grahacāraprasiddhaye ।। dakṣiṇe bhānuputrasya varuṇasya ca vāruṇī ।।
amarāvatī saṃyamanī sukhā caiva vibhā kramāt ।। kāṣṭhāṃ gatasya sūryasya gatir yā tāṃ nibodhata ।। jyotiṣāṃ cakramādāya satataṃ parigacchati ।। sarvaiḥ sāyamanaiḥ sauro hy udayo dṛśyate dvijāḥ ।।
astameti punaḥ sūryo vibhāyāṃ viśvadṛg vibhuḥ ।। tathā saṃyamanīṃ prāpya sukhāṃ caiva vibhāṃ khagaḥ ।। tadā tvapararātraś ca vāyubhāge sudāruṇaḥ ।। evaṃ puṣkaramadhye tu yadā sarpati vāripaḥ ।।
yojanānāṃ muhūrtasya imāṃ saṃkhyāṃ nibodhata ।। pañcāśacca tathānyāni sahasrāṇyadhikāni tu ।। etena gatiyogena yadā kāṣṭhāṃ tu dakṣiṇām ।। madhye tu puṣkarasyātha bhramate dakṣiṇāyane ।।
maṇḍalānāṃ śataṃ pūrṇaṃ tadaśītyadhikaṃ vibhuḥ ।। pratyahaṃ carate tāni sūryo vai maṇḍalāni tu ।। dakṣiṇaprakrame devas tathā śīghraṃ pravartate ।। sūryo dvādaśabhiḥ śīghraṃ muhūrtairdakṣiṇāyane ।।
muhūrtaistāvadṛkṣāṇi naktamaṣṭādaśaiścaran ।। tathodagayane sūryaḥ sarpate mandavikramaḥ ।। sa ratho dhiṣṭhito bhānor ādityairmunibhis tathā ।। pradīpayan sahasrāṃśur agrataḥ pṛṣṭhato apyadhaḥ ।।
aṃbhobhir munibhistyaktaiḥ saṃdhyāyāṃ tu niśācarān ।। aṣṭādaśa muhūrtaṃ tu uttarāyaṇapaścimam ।। muhūrtais tāvad ṛkṣāṇi divāṣṭādaśabhiścaran ।। mṛtpiṇḍa iva madhyastho dhruvo bhramati vai tathā ।।
ubhayoḥ kāṣṭhayormadhye bhramato maṇḍalāni tu ।। auttānapādo bhramati grahaiḥ sārdhaṃ grahāgraṇīḥ ।। adhiṣṭhitaḥ punastena bhānustvādāya tiṣṭhati ।। auttānapādasya sadā dhruvatvaṃ vai prasādataḥ ।।
āpaḥ pītāstu sūryeṇa kramante śaśinaḥ kramāt ।। vṛndaṃ jalamucāṃ caiva śvasanenābhitāḍitam ।। toyasya nāsti vai nāśaḥ tadaiva parivartate ।। bhūrbhuvaḥ svas tathā hyāpo hy annaṃ cāmṛtameva ca ।।
bahunātra kimuktena carācaramidaṃ jagat ।। apāṃ tvadhipatirdevo bhava ityeva kīrtitaḥ ।। jagatāmālayo viṣṇus tv āpastasyālayāni tu ।। yā yā ūrdhvaṃ māruteneritā vai tāstāstvabhrāṇyagninā vāyunā ca ।।
vārīṇi varṣatītyabhram abhrasyeśaḥ sahasradṛk ।। dāvāgnidhūmasambhūtam abhraṃ vanahitaṃ smṛtam ।। abhicārāgnidhūmotthaṃ bhūtanāśāya vai dvijāḥ ।। tasmādācchādayeddhūmam abhicārakṛtaṃ naraḥ ।।
evamuddiśya lokasya kṣayakṛcca bhaviṣyati ।। varṣayantyeva jagatāṃ hitāya pavanājñayā ।। tridhā teṣāmihotpattir abhrāṇāṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।। kāṣṭhāvāhāś ca vairiñcyāḥ pakṣāścaiva pṛthagvidhāḥ ।।
dvitīyānāṃ ca saṃbhūtir viriñcocchvāsavāyunā ।। vāhneyāstvatha jīmūtās tv āvahasthānagāḥ śubhāḥ ।। pakṣajāḥ puṣkarādyāś ca varṣanti ca yadā jalam ।। kṣāmavṛṣṭipradā dīrghakālaṃ śītasamīriṇaḥ ।।
tiṣṭhantyākrośamātre tu dharāpṛṣṭhāditastataḥ ।। meghā yojanamātraṃ tu sādhyatvād bahutoyadāḥ ।। teṣāṃ teṣāṃ vṛṣṭisargaṃ tredhā kathitamatra tu ।। kalpānte te ca varṣanti rātrau nāśāya śāradāḥ ।।
tadārṇavamabhūtsarvaṃ tatra śete niśīśvaraḥ ।। jaladānāṃ sadā dhūmo hy āpyāyana iti smṛtaḥ ।। puṇḍradeśeṣu patitā nāgānāṃ śīkarā himāḥ ।। nagānāṃ ca nadīnāṃ ca diggajānāṃ samākulam ।।
parāvaho yaḥ śvasanaś cānayatyambikāgurum ।। abhyeti bhārate varṣe tv aparāntavivṛddhaye ।। sasyadvayasya saṃkṣepāt prabravīmi yathāmati ।। so api sākṣāddvijaśreṣṭhāś ceśānaḥ paramaḥ śivaḥ ।।
cakṣuḥ śrotraṃ mano mṛtyur ātmā manyur vidig diśaḥ ।। lokapālo harirbrahmā rudraḥ sākṣānmaheśvaraḥ ।। ardhanārivapuḥ sākṣāt trinetras tridaśādhipaḥ ।। sahasraguṇamutsraṣṭum ādatte kiraṇairjalam ।।
dhruveṇādhiṣṭhito vāyur vṛṣṭiṃ saṃharate punaḥ ।। cārasyānte viśatyarke dhruveṇa samadhiṣṭhitā ।। grahāṇām itareṣāṃ ca yathā gacchati cāmbupaḥ ।। saṃvatsarasyāvayavaiḥ kalpitaś ca dvijarṣabhāḥ ।।
sauvarṇaḥ sarvadevānām āvāso bhāskarasya tu ।। dviguṇo api rathopasthād īṣādaṇḍaḥ pramāṇataḥ ।। vājinastasya vai sapta chandobhir nirmitāstu te ।। sahāśvacakro bhramate sahākṣo bhramate dhruvaḥ ।।
prerako jyotiṣāṃ dhīmān dhruvo vai vātaraśmibhiḥ ।। dhruveṇa bhramate raśminibaddhaḥ sa yugākṣayoḥ ।। yugākṣakoṭī te tasya dakṣiṇe syandanasya hi ।। bhramantamanugacchanti dhruvaṃ raśmī ca tāvubhau ।।
kīle saktā yathā rajjur bhramate sarvatodiśam ।। vardhete dakṣiṇe caiva bhramatā maṇḍalāni tu ।। ābhyantarasthaḥ sūryo atha bhramate maṇḍalāni tu ।। dhruveṇa mucyamānābhyāṃ raśmibhyāṃ punareva tu ।।
udveṣṭayan sa vegena maṇḍalāni tu gacchati ।। yajanti satataṃ devaṃ bhāskaraṃ bhavamīśvaram ।। gandharvairapsarobhiś ca grāmaṇīsarparākṣasaiḥ ।। āpyāyayanti cādityaṃ tejobhir bhāskaraṃ śivam ।।
gandharvāpsarasaścaiva nṛtyageyairupāsate ।। sarpā vahanti vai sūryaṃ yātudhānā anuyānti ca ।। ityete vai vasantīha dvau dvau māsau divākare ।। nabhonabhasyau viprendrā iṣaścorjastathaiva ca ।।
ete dvādaśa māsāstu varṣaṃ vai mānuṣaṃ dvijāḥ ।। śāradaś ca himaścaiva śaiśira ṛtavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। vivasvāṃścaiva pūṣā ca parjanyo aṃśur bhagas tathā ।। vasiṣṭhaścāṅgirāścaiva bhṛgurbuddhimatāṃ varaḥ ।।
jamadagniḥ kauśikaś ca vāsukiḥ kaṅkaṇīkaraḥ ।। śaṅkhapālas tathā cānyas tv airāvata iti smṛtaḥ ।। kambalo aśvataraścaiva tumbururnāradas tathā ।। ugraseno atha surucir anyaścaiva parāvasuḥ ।।
dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ sūryavarcā devī sākṣāt kṛtasthalā ।। menakā sahajanyā ca pramlocātha śucismitā ।। pūrvacittiriti khyātā devī sākṣāttilottamā ।। rathaujā rathacitraś ca subāhurvai rathasvanaḥ ।।
tārkṣyaścāriṣṭanemiś ca kṣatajit satyajittathā ।। sarpo vyāghraḥ punaścāpo vāto vidyuddivākaraḥ ।। ete devādayaḥ sarve vasantyarke krameṇa tu ।। dhātrādiviṣṇuparyantā devā dvādaśa kīrtitāḥ ।।
pulastyādyāḥ kauśikāntā munayo munisattamāḥ ।। nāgāścāśvatarāntāstu vāsukipramukhāḥ śubhāḥ ।। krameṇa sūryavarcāntās tumburupramukhāmbupam ।। kṛtasthalādyā raṃbhāntā divyāścāpsaraso ravim ।।
divyāḥ satyajidantāś ca grāmaṇyo rathakṛnmukhāḥ ।। prayānti yajñopetāntā rakṣohetimukhāḥ saha ।। dhātāryamā pulastyaś ca pulahaś ca prajāpatiḥ ।। tumburur nāradaścaiva gandharvau gāyatāṃ varau ।।
grāmaṇī rathakṛccaiva rathaujāścaiva tāvubhau ।। madhumādhavayoreṣa gaṇo vasati bhāskare ।। ṛṣiratrirvasiṣṭhaś ca takṣako nāga eva ca ।। subāhunāmā grāmaṇyau rathacitraś ca tāvubhau ।।
ete vasanti vai sūrye māsayoḥ śuciśukrayoḥ ।। indraścaiva vivasvāṃś ca aṅgirā bhṛgureva ca ।। viśvāvasūgrasenau ca varuṇaś ca rathasvanaḥ ।। yātudhānās tathā sarpo vyāghraścaiva tu tāvubhau ।।
parjanyaścaiva pūṣā ca bharadvājo atha gautamaḥ ।। ghṛtācī cāpsaraḥśreṣṭhā viśvācī cātiśobhanā ।। āpo vātaś ca tāvetau yātudhānāvubhau smṛtau ।। haimantikau tu dvau māsau vasanti ca divākare ।।
bhujaṅgaś ca mahāpadmaḥ sarpaḥ karkoṭakas tathā ।। urvaśī pūrvacittiś ca tathaivāpsarasāvubhe ।। vidyuddivākaraścobhau yātudhānāvudāhṛtau ।। tataḥ śaiśirayoścāpi māsayor nivasanti vai ।।
kādraveyau tathā nāgau kambalāśvatarāvubhau ।। tilottamāpsarāścaiva devī raṃbhā manoharā ।। brahmopetas tathā rakṣo yajñopetaś ca yaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। sthānābhimānino hyete gaṇā dvādaśa saptakāḥ ।।
grathitaiḥ svairvacobhistu stuvanti munayo ravim ।। grāmaṇīyakṣabhūtāni kurvate abhīṣusaṃgraham ।। vālakhilyā nayantyastaṃ parivāryodayādravim ।। yathāyogaṃ yathāmantraṃ yathādharmaṃ yathābalam ।।
ityete vai vasantīha dvau dvau māsau divākare ।। grāmaṇyaś ca tathā yakṣā yātudhānāś ca mukhyataḥ ।। bhūtānāmaśubhaṃ karma vyapohantīha kīrtitāḥ ।। duritaṃ supracārāṇāṃ vyapohanti kvacit kvacit ।।
ete sahaiva sūryeṇa bhramanti divasānugāḥ ।। gopāyantīha bhūtāni sarvāṇi dyāmanukṣayāt ।। atītānāgatānāṃ vai vartante sāṃprataṃ ca ye ।। caturdaśasu sarveṣu gaṇā manvantareṣviha ।।
kathitaṃ muniśārdūlā devadevasya dhīmataḥ ।। sthānābhimānino hyete gaṇā dvādaśa saptakāḥ ।। haritairakṣarairaśvaiḥ sarpate asau divākaraḥ ।। saptadvīpasamudrāṅgāṃ saptabhiḥ sarpate divi ।।
tricakrobhayato aśvaś ca vijñeyastasya vai rathaḥ ।। daśabhistvakṛśair divyair asaṃgais tair manojavaiḥ ।। somo hyambumayair gobhiḥ śuklaiḥ śuklagabhastimān ।। āpūryate parasyāntaḥ satataṃ divasakramāt ।।
pītaṃ pañcadaśāhaṃ tu raśminaikena bhāskaraḥ ।। ityeṣā sūryavīryeṇa candrasyāpyāyitā tanuḥ ।। evamāpyāyitaṃ somaṃ śuklapakṣe dinakramāt ।। pibantyambumayaṃ devā madhu saumyaṃ sudhāmṛtam ।।
pānārthamamṛtaṃ somaṃ paurṇamāsyāmupāsate ।। somasya kṛṣṇapakṣādau bhāskarābhimukhasya ca ।। trayastriṃśacchatāścaiva trayastriṃśattathaiva ca ।। evaṃ dinakramātpīte vibudhaistu niśākare ।।
pitaraścopatiṣṭhanti amāvāsyāṃ niśākaram ।। aparāhṇe pitṛgaṇā jaghanyaṃ paryupāsate ।। nisṛtaṃ tadamāvāsyāṃ gabhastibhyaḥ svadhāmṛtam ।। pitṛbhiḥ pīyamānasya pañcadaśyāṃ kalā tu yā ।।
amāvāsyāṃ tatastasyā antarā pūryate punaḥ ।। evaṃ sūryanimittaiṣā pakṣavṛddhirniśākare ।। vāritejomayaścātha piśaṅgaiścaiva śobhanaiḥ ।। śukrasya kṣmāmayairyukto daityācāryasya dhīmataḥ ।।
jīvasya haimaścāṣṭāśvo mandasyāyasanirmitaḥ ।। svarbhānorbhāskarāreś ca tathā cāṣṭahayaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। etena bhrāmyamāṇāś ca yathāyogaṃ vrajanti vai ।। sarve dhruvanibaddhāś ca bhramanto bhrāmayanti tam ।।
yasmādvahati jyotīṃṣi pravahastena sa smṛtaḥ ।। unmukhābhimukhāḥ sarve cakrabhūtāḥ śritā divi ।। prayānti ceśvaraṃ draṣṭuṃ meḍhībhūtaṃ dhruvaṃ divi ।। triguṇastasya vistāro maṇḍalasya pramāṇataḥ ।।
tulyastayostu svarbhānur bhūtvādhastātprasarpati ।। svarbhānostu bṛhatsthānaṃ tṛtīyaṃ yat tamomayam ।। viṣkambhānmaṇḍalāccaiva yojanācca pramāṇataḥ ।। pādahīnau vakrasaurī tathāyāmapramāṇataḥ ।।
tārānakṣatrarūpāṇi vapuṣmantīha yāni vai ।। prāyaśaścandrayogīni vidyādṛkṣāṇi tattvavit ।। śatāni pañca catvāri trīṇi dve caiva yojane ।। yojanadvayamātrāṇi tebhyo hrasvaṃ na vidyate ।।
sauro aṅgirāś ca vakraś ca jñeyā mandavicāriṇaḥ ।। sūryaḥ somo budhaścaiva bhārgavaścaiva śīghragāḥ ।। dhruvāt tu niyamāccaiṣām ṛkṣamārge vyavasthitiḥ ।। uttarāyaṇamārgastho yadā parvasu candramāḥ ।।
tadā dakṣiṇamārgastho nīcāṃ vīthimupāśritaḥ ।। dadṛśe ca yathākālaṃ śīghramastamupaiti ca ।। dadṛśe dakṣiṇe mārge niyamāddṛśyate na ca ।। samānakālāstamayau viṣuvatsu samodayau ।।
paurṇimāvāsyayor jñeyau jyotiścakrānuvartinau ।। grahāṇāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ sūryo adhastāt prasarpati ।। nakṣatramaṇḍalaṃ kṛtsnaṃ somādūrdhvaṃ prasarpati ।। vakrastu bhārgavādūrdhvaṃ vakrād ūrdhvaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ ।।
ṛṣīṇāṃ caiva saptānāṃ dhruvasyordhvaṃ vyavasthitiḥ ।। dviguṇeṣu sahasreṣu yojanānāṃ śateṣu ca ।। grahāś ca candrasūryau ca yutau divyena tejasā ।। grahanakṣatrasūryās te nīcoccaṛjusaṃsthitāḥ ।।
ṛtavaḥ ṣaṭ smṛtāḥ sarve samāgacchanti pañcadhā ।। asaṃkareṇa vijñeyas teṣāṃ yogastu vai budhaiḥ ।। bhāskarapramukhānāṃ ca yathādṛṣṭaṃ yathāśrutam ।। abhiṣiktaḥ sahasrāṃśū rudreṇa tu yathā guhaḥ ।।
ādityagrahapīḍāyāṃ sadbhiḥ kāryārthasiddhaye ।। devadaityamukhān sarvān sarvātmā vada sāṃpratam ।। ṛkṣāṇāmoṣadhīnāṃ ca somaṃ brahmā prajāpatiḥ ।। ādityānāṃ tathā viṣṇuṃ vasūnāṃ pāvakaṃ tathā ।।
daityānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca prahlādaṃ daityapuṅgavam ।। rudraṃ paśūnāṃ bhūtānāṃ nandinaṃ gaṇanāyakam ।। mātṝṇāṃ caiva cāmuṇḍāṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtām ।। vighnānāṃ vyomajaṃ devaṃ gajāsyaṃ tu vināyakam ।।
viṣṇuṃ māyāvināṃ caiva svātmānaṃ jagatāṃ tathā ।। samudrāṇāṃ ca sarveṣām adhipaṃ payasāṃ nidhim ।। vṛkṣāṇāṃ caiva cāśvatthaṃ plakṣaṃ ca prapitāmahaḥ ।। nāgādhipaṃ vāsukimugravīryaṃ sarpādhipaṃ takṣakamugravīryam ।।
digvāraṇānāmadhipaṃ cakāra gajendram airāvatam ugravīryam । suparṇamīśaṃ patatāmathāśvarājānamuccaiḥśravasaṃ cakāra ।। senādhipānāṃ guhamaprameyaṃ śrutismṛtīnāṃ lakulīśamīśam ।। ketumantaṃ krameṇaiva hemaromāṇameva ca ।।
caturmūrtiṣu sarvajñaṃ śaṅkaraṃ vṛṣabhadhvajam ।। purābhiṣicya puṇyātmā rarāja bhuvaneśvaraḥ ।। abhiṣiktāstatastvete viśiṣṭā viśvayoninā ।। papracchuruttaraṃ bhūyas tadā te romaharṣaṇam ।।
etadvistarato brūhi jyotiṣāṃ ca vinirṇayam ।। uvāca paramaṃ vākyaṃ teṣāṃ saṃśayanirṇaye ।। etadvo ahaṃ pravakṣyāmi sūryacandramasorgatim ।। ataḥ paraṃ tu trividham agnervakṣye samudbhavam ।।
vyuṣṭāyāṃ tu rajanyāṃ ca brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।। caturbhāgāvaśiṣṭe asmin loke naṣṭe viśeṣataḥ ।। khadyotavatsa vyacarad āvirbhāvacikīrṣayā ।। saṃhṛtya tatprakāśārthaṃ tridhā vyabhajadīśvaraḥ ।।
yaścāsau lokādau sūrye śuciragnistu sa smṛtaḥ ।। vaidyuto jāṭharaḥ sauro vārigarbhāstrayo agnayaḥ ।। jale cābjaḥ samāviṣṭo nādbhir agniḥ praśāmyati ।। arciṣmānpavanaḥ so agnir niṣprabho jāṭharaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
prabhā saurī tu pādena hy astaṃ yāte divākare ।। udyantaṃ ca punaḥ sūryam auṣṇyam agneḥ samāviśet ।। prakāśoṣṇasvarūpe ca saurāgneye tu tejasī ।। uttare caiva bhūmyardhe tathā hyagniś ca dakṣiṇe ।।
tasmāttāmrā bhavantyāpo divārātripraveśanāt ।। tasmānnaktaṃ punaḥ śuklā āpo dṛśyanti bhāsvarāḥ ।। udayāstamane nityam ahorātraṃ viśaty apaḥ ।। pārthivāgnivimiśro asau divyaḥ śuciriti smṛtaḥ ।।
ādatte sa tu nāḍīnāṃ sahasreṇa samantataḥ ।। sthāvarā jaṅgamāścaiva vāpīkulyādikā apaḥ ।। tāsāṃ catuḥśatā nāḍyo varṣante citramūrtayaḥ ।। amṛtā nāmataḥ sarvā raśmayo vṛṣṭisarjanāḥ ।।
reśā meghāś ca vātsyāś ca hlādinyo himasarjanāḥ ।। śuklāś ca kakubhāścaiva gāvo viśvabhṛtas tathā ।। somo bibharti tābhistu manuṣyapitṛdevatāḥ ।। amṛtena surān sarvāṃs tisṛbhis tarpayatyasau ।।
varṣāsvatho śaradi ca caturbhiḥ saṃpravarṣati ।। indro dhātā bhagaḥ pūṣā mitro atha varuṇo aryamā ।। varuṇo māghamāse tu sūrya eva tu phālgune ।। jyeṣṭhe māsi bhavedindra āṣāḍhe cāryamā raviḥ ।।
parjanyo aśvayuje māsi tvaṣṭā vai kārtike raviḥ ।। pañcaraśmisahasrāṇi varuṇasyārkakarmaṇi ।। dhātāṣṭabhiḥ sahasraistu navabhistu śatakratuḥ ।। saptabhistapate mitras tvaṣṭā caivāṣṭabhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
ṣaḍbhī raśmisahasraistu viṣṇustapati medinīm ।। śveto varṣāsu varṇena pāṇḍuḥ śaradi bhāskaraḥ ।। iti varṇāḥ samākhyātā mayā sūryasamudbhavāḥ ।। sūryo amareṣvapyamṛtaṃ trayaṃ triṣu niyacchati ।।
bhidyate lokamāsādya jalaśītoṣṇaniḥsravam ।। nakṣatragrahasomānāṃ pratiṣṭhāyonireva ca ।। nakṣatrādhipatiḥ somo nayanaṃ vāmamīśituḥ ।। teṣāṃ janānāṃ loke asmin nayanaṃ nayate yataḥ ।।
paṭhyate cāgnirāditya udakaṃ candramāḥ smṛtaḥ ।। surasenāpatiḥ skandaḥ paṭhyate aṅgārako grahaḥ ।। sarvalokaprabhuḥ sākṣād yamo lokaprabhuḥ svayam ।। devāsuragurū dvau tu bhānumantau mahāgrahau ।।
ādityamūlamakhilaṃ trailokyaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। rudrendropendracandrāṇāṃ viprendrāgnidivaukasām ।। sarvātmā sarvalokeśo mahādevaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। tataḥ saṃjāyate sarvaṃ tatraiva pravilīyate ।।
avijñeyo graho viprā dīptimānsuprabho raviḥ ।। kṣaṇā muhūrtā divasā niśāḥ pakṣāś ca kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। tadādityādṛte hyeṣā kālasaṃkhyā na vidyate ।। ṛtūnāṃ ca vibhāgaś ca puṣpaṃ mūlaṃ phalaṃ kutaḥ ।।
abhāvo vyavahārāṇāṃ jantūnāṃ divi ceha ca ।। sa eṣa kālaścāgniś ca dvādaśātmā prajāpatiḥ ।। sa eṣa tejasāṃ rāśiḥ samastaḥ sārvalaukikaḥ ।। pārśvata ūrdhvam adhaś caiva tāpayatyeṣa sarvaśaḥ ।।
pārśvata ūrdhvam adhaścaiva tamo nāśayate samam ।। sūryo gobhir jagat sarvam ādīpayati sarvataḥ ।। teṣāṃ śreṣṭhāḥ punaḥ sapta raśmayo grahayonayaḥ ।। viśvavyacāḥ punaścādyaḥ saṃnaddhaś ca tataḥ paraḥ ।।
suṣumnaḥ sūryaraśmistu dakṣiṇāṃ rāśim aidhayat ।। harikeśaḥ purastād yo ṛkṣayoniḥ prakīrtyate ।। viśvavyacāstu yaḥ paścāc chukrayoniḥ smṛto budhaiḥ ।। ṣaṣṭhaḥ sarvāvasū raśmiḥ sa yonistu bṛhaspateḥ ।।
evaṃ sūryaprabhāvena nakṣatragrahatārakāḥ ।। na kṣīyante yatastāni tasmānnakṣatratā smṛtā ।। teṣāṃ kṣetrāṇyathādatte sūryo nakṣatratārakāḥ ।। tāraṇāttārakā hyetāḥ śuklatvāccaiva tārakāḥ ।।
ādānānnityamādityas tejasāṃ tamasāmapi ।। savanāttejaso apāṃ ca tenāsau savitā mataḥ ।। śuklatve cāmṛtatve ca śītatve ca vibhāvyate ।। jalatejomaye śukle vṛttakuṃbhanibhe śubhe ।।
ghanatejomayaṃ śuklaṃ maṇḍalaṃ bhāskarasya tu ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu ṛkṣasūryagrahāśrayāḥ ।। sauraṃ sūryo aviśatsthānaṃ saumyaṃ somastathaiva ca ।। bṛhad bṛhaspatiścaiva lohitaścaiva lohitam ।।
baudhaṃ budhastu svarbhānuḥ svarbhānusthānamāśritaḥ ।। gṛhāṇyetāni sarvāṇi jyotīṃṣi sukṛtātmanām ।। sthānānyetāni tiṣṭhanti yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam ।। abhimānino avatiṣṭhante devāḥ sthānaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।।
vartante vartamānaiś ca sthānibhistaiḥ suraiḥ saha ।। vivasvānaditeḥ putraḥ sūryo vaivasvate antare ।। śukro devastu vijñeyo bhārgavo asurayājakaḥ ।। budho manoharaścaiva ṛṣiputrastu sa smṛtaḥ ।।
agnirvikeśyāṃ jajñe tu yuvāsau lohitārciṣaḥ ।। svarbhānuḥ siṃhikāputro bhūtasaṃtāpano asuraḥ ।। sthānānyetānyathoktāni sthāninyaścaiva devatāḥ ।। himāṃśostu smṛtaṃ sthānam ammayaṃ śuklameva ca ।।
śuklasyāpyammayaṃ śuklaṃ padaṃ ṣoḍaśaraśmivat ।। haridrābhaṃ bṛhaccāpi ṣoḍaśārcirbṛhaspateḥ ।। svarbhānostāmasaṃ sthānaṃ bhūtasaṃtāpanālayam ।। āśrayāḥ puṇyakīrtīnāṃ śuklāścāpi svavarṇataḥ ।।
ādityaraśmisaṃyogāt saṃprakāśātmikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। triguṇastasya vistāro maṇḍalasya pramāṇataḥ ।। tulyastayostu svarbhānur bhūtvādhastātprasarpati ।। svarbhānostu bṛhatsthānaṃ tṛtīyaṃ yattamomayam ।।
ādityameti somācca punaḥ saureṣu parvasu ।। candrasya ṣoḍaśo bhāgo bhārgavasya vidhīyate ।। bhārgavātpādahīnastu vijñeyo vai bṛhaspatiḥ ।। vistārānmaṇḍalāccaiva pādahīnastayorbudhaḥ ।।
budhena tāni tulyāni vistārānmaṇḍalācca vai ।। tārānakṣatrarūpāṇi hīnāni tu parasparam ।। sarvopari nikṛṣṭāni tārakāmaṇḍalāni tu ।। upariṣṭāttrayasteṣāṃ grahāste dūrasarpiṇaḥ ।।
pūrvameva samākhyātā gatisteṣāṃ yathākramam ।। vivasvānaditeḥ putraḥ sūryo vai munisattamāḥ ।। tviṣimān dharmaputrastu somo devo vasustu saḥ ।। ṣoḍaśārcirbhṛgoḥ putraḥ śukraḥ sūryādanantaram ।।
grahaścāṅgirasaḥ putro dvādaśārcirbṛhaspatiḥ ।। navārcirlohitāṅgaś ca prajāpatisuto grahaḥ ।। revatīṣveva saptārciḥsthāne sauriḥ śanaiścaraḥ ।। tamomayo mṛtyusutaḥ prajākṣayakaraḥ śikhī ।।
tathā svanāmadheyeṣu dākṣāyaṇyaḥ samutthitāḥ ।। bharaṇīṣu samutpanno grahaścandrārkamardanaḥ ।। janmanakṣatrapīḍāsu yānti vaiguṇyatāṃ yataḥ ।। sarvagrahāṇāmeteṣām ādirāditya ucyate ।।
dhruvaḥ kila grahāṇāṃ tu vibhaktānāṃ caturdiśam ।। varṣāṇāṃ caiva pañcānām ādyaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ smṛtaḥ ।। pakṣāṇāṃ śuklapakṣastu tithīnāṃ pratipattathā ।। muhūrtānāṃ tathaivādir muhūrto rudradaivataḥ ।।
śravaṇāntaṃ dhaniṣṭhādi yugaṃ syātpañcavārṣikam ।। divākaraḥ smṛtastasmāt kālakṛdvibhurīśvaraḥ ।। tasyāpi bhagavān rudraḥ sākṣāddevaḥ pravartakaḥ ।। lokasaṃvyavahārārthaṃ mahādevena nirmitaḥ ।।
sa āśrayo abhimānī ca sarvasya jyotirātmakaḥ ।। naiṣa śakyaḥ prasaṃkhyātuṃ yāthātathyena kenacit ।। āgamādanumānācca pratyakṣādupapattitaḥ ।। cakṣuḥ śāstraṃ jalaṃ lekhyaṃ gaṇitaṃ munisattamāḥ ।।
pañcaite hetavo jñeyā jyotirmānavinirṇaye ।। meḍhībhūto grāhāṇāṃ vai vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam ।। mārkaṇḍeyaḥ purā prāha mahyaṃ śuśrūṣave dvijāḥ ।। uttānapādo rājā vai pālayāmāsa medinīm ।।
agrajāyāmabhūtputraḥ sunītyāṃ tu mahāyaśāḥ ।। kadācit saptavarṣe api pituraṅkam upāviśat ।। nyaveśayattaṃ viprendrā hy aṅkaṃ rūpeṇa mānitā ।। mātuḥ samīpamāgamya ruroda sa punaḥ punaḥ ।।
surucirdayitā bhartus tasyāḥ putro api tādṛśaḥ ।। kiṃ śocasi kimarthaṃ tvaṃ rodamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।। svasthasthānaṃ dhruvaṃ putra svaśaktyā tvaṃ samāpnuyāḥ ।। viśvāmitraṃ tato dṛṣṭvā praṇipatya yathāvidhi ।।
sarveṣāmuparisthānaṃ kena prāpsyāmi sattama ।। vyadhūnayatsa taṃ rājā pitā novāca kiṃcana ।। sunītirāha me mātā mā kṛthāḥ śokamuttamam ।। tasyā hi vacanaṃ śrutvā sthānaṃ tava mahāmune ।।
tava prasādāt prāpsye ahaṃ sthānamadbhutamuttamam ।। rājaputra śṛṇuṣvedaṃ sthānamuttamamāpsyasi ।। dakṣiṇāṅgabhavaṃ śaṃbhor mahādevasya dhīmataḥ ।। iṣṭadaṃ paramaṃ śuddhaṃ pavitramamalaṃ param ।।
namo astu vāsudevāya ityevaṃ niyatendriyaḥ ।। ityuktaḥ praṇipatyainaṃ viśvāmitraṃ mahāyaśāḥ ।। śākamūlaphalāhāraḥ saṃvatsaramatandritaḥ ।। vetālā rākṣasā ghorāḥ siṃhādyāś ca mahāmṛgāḥ ।।
japan sa vāsudeveti na kiṃcit pratyapadyata ।। piśāci samanuprāptā ruroda bhṛśaduḥkhitā ।। māmanāthāmapahāya tapa āsthitavānasi ।। anirīkṣyaiva hṛṣṭātmā harernāma jajāpa saḥ ।।
tato garuḍamāruhya kālameghasamadyutiḥ ।। āyayau bhagavānviṣṇuḥ dhruvāntikam arātihā ।। pibanniva hṛṣīkeśaṃ nayanābhyāṃ jagatpatim ।। śaṅkhaprāntena govindaḥ pasparśāsyaṃ hi tasya vai ।।
tuṣṭāva prāñjalirbhūtvā sarvalokeśvaraṃ harim ।। lokātman vedaguhyātman tvāṃ prapanno asmi keśava ।। tatkathaṃ tvāmahaṃ vidyāṃ namaste bhuvaneśvara ।। sthānaṃ dhruvaṃ samāsādya jyotiṣām agrabhug bhava ।।
matsthānametatparamaṃ dhruvaṃ nityaṃ suśobhanam ।। vāsudeveti yo nityaṃ praṇavena samanvitam ।। japedevaṃ hi yo vidvān dhruvaṃ sthānaṃ prapadyate ।। mātrā saha dhruvaṃ sarve tasmin sthāne nyaveśayan ।।
evaṃ dhruvo mahātejā dvādaśākṣaravidyayā ।। avāpa mahatīṃ siddhim etatte kathitaṃ mayā ।। sa yāti dhruvasālokyaṃ dhruvatvaṃ tasya tattathā ।। utpattiṃ brūhi sūtādya yathākramamanuttamam ।।
dakṣātprācetasādūrdhvaṃ sṛṣṭirmaithunasaṃbhavā ।। na vṛddhimagamallokas tadā maithunayogataḥ ।। tāṃstu dṛṣṭvā mahābhāgān sisṛkṣurvividhāḥ prajāḥ ।। bhuvaḥ pramāṇaṃ sarvaṃ tu jñātvordhvamadha eva ca ।।
te tu tadvacanaṃ śrutvā prayātāḥ sarvatodiśam ।। haryaśveṣu ca naṣṭeṣu punardakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। śabalā nāma te viprāḥ sametāḥ sṛṣṭihetavaḥ ।। bhuvaḥ pramāṇaṃ sarvaṃ tu jñātvā bhrātṝn punaḥ punaḥ ।।
te api tenaiva mārgeṇa jagmurbhrātṛgatiṃ tathā ।। vairiṇyāṃ janayāmāsa dakṣaḥ prācetasastadā ।। viṃśatsapta ca somāya catasro ariṣṭanemaye ।। dve caivāṅgirase tadvat tāsāṃ nāmāni vistarāt ।।
marutvatī vasūr yāmir lambā bhānurarundhatī ।। dharmapatnyaḥ samākhyātās tāsāṃ putrānvadāmi vaḥ ।। marutvatyāṃ marutvanto vasostu vasavas tathā ।। lambāyā ghoṣanāmāno nāgavīthistu yāmijaḥ ।।
jyotiṣmantastu ye devā vyāpakāḥ sarvatodiśam ।। āpo dhruvaś ca somaś ca dharaścaivānilo analaḥ ।। ajaikapād ahirbudhnyo virūpākṣaḥ sabhairavaḥ ।। sāvitraś ca jayantaś ca pinākī cāparājitaḥ ।।
kaśyapasya pravakṣyāmi patnībhyaḥ putrapautrakam ।। surabhir vinatā tāmrā tadvat krodhavaśā ilā ।। tuṣitā nāma ye devāś cākṣuṣasyāntare manoḥ ।। indro dhātā bhagastvaṣṭa mitro atha varuṇo aryamā ।।
ete sahasrakiraṇā ādityā dvādaśa smṛtāḥ ।। hiraṇyakaśipuṃ caiva hiraṇyākṣaṃ tathaiva ca ।। vipracittiḥ pradhāno abhūt teṣāṃ madhye dvijottamāḥ ।। śukīṃ śyenīṃ ca bhāsīṃ ca sugrīvīṃ gṛdhrikāṃ śucim ।।
śyenī śyenāṃs tathā bhāsī kuraṅgāṃś ca vyajījanat ।। haṃsasārasakāraṇḍaplavāñchucirajījanat ।। vinatā janayāmāsa garuḍaṃ cāruṇaṃ śubhā ।। surasāyāḥ sahasraṃ tu sarpāṇāmabhavatpurā ।।
pradhānāsteṣu vikhyātāḥ ṣaḍviṃśatiranuttamāḥ ।। dhanañjayamahānīlapadmāśvataratakṣakāḥ ।। śaṅkhapālamahāśaṅkhapuṣpadaṃṣṭraśubhānanāḥ ।। kapilo durmukhaścāpi patañjaliriti smṛtaḥ ।।
rudrāṇāṃ ca gaṇaṃ tadvad gomahiṣyau varāṅganā ।। munirmunīnāṃ ca gaṇaṃ gaṇamapsarasāṃ tathā ।। tṛṇavṛkṣalatāgulmam ilā sarvamajījanat ।। ete tu kāśyapeyāś ca saṃkṣepātparikīrtitāḥ ।।
evaṃ prajāsu sṛṣṭāsu kaśyapena mahātmanā ।। abhiṣicyādhipatyeṣu teṣāṃ mukhyānprajāpatiḥ ।। svāyaṃbhuve antare pūrvaṃ brahmaṇā ye abhiṣecitāḥ ।। yathopadeśamadyāpi dharmeṇa pratipālyate ।।
te hyete cābhiṣicyante manavaś ca bhavanti te ।। evamanye abhiṣicyante prāpte manvantare tataḥ ।। etānutpādya putrāṃstu prajāsaṃtānakāraṇāt ।। putro gotrakaro mahyaṃ bhavatād iti cintayan ।।
brahmayogātsutau paścāt prādurbhūtau mahaujasau ।। vatsarānnaidhruvo jajñe raibhyaś ca sumahāyaśāḥ ।। cyavanasya tu kanyāyāṃ sumedhāḥ samapadyata ।। asitasyaikaparṇāyāṃ brahmiṣṭhaḥ samapadyata ।।
śāṇḍilyā naidhruvā raibhyās trayaḥ pakṣāstu kāśyapāḥ ।। caturyuge hyatikrānte manorekādaśe prabhoḥ ।। mānavasya nariṣyantaḥ putra āsīd damaḥ kila ।। tretāyugamukhe rājā tṛtīye saṃbabhūva ha ।।
pulastyāya sa rājarṣis tāṃ kanyāṃ pratyapādayat ।। tasya patnyaścatasrastu paulastyakulavardhanāḥ ।। puṣpotkaṭā balākā ca sute mālyavataḥ smṛteḥ ।। jyeṣṭhaṃ vaiśravaṇaṃ tasmāt suṣuve devavarṇinī ।।
kumbhakarṇaṃ śūrpaṇakhāṃ dhīmantaṃ ca vibhīṣaṇam ।। mahodaraṃ prahastaṃ ca mahāpārśvaṃ kharaṃ tathā ।। triśirā dūṣaṇaścaiva vidyujjihvaś ca rākṣasaḥ ।। ityete krūrakarmāṇaḥ paulastyā rākṣasā nava ।।
pulastyasya mṛgāḥ putrāḥ sarve vyāghrāś ca daṃṣṭriṇaḥ ।। vānarāḥ kiṃnarāścaiva ye ca kiṃpuruṣās tathā ।। atreḥ patnyo daśaivāsan suṃdaryaś ca pativratāḥ ।। bhadrābhadrā ca jaladā mandā nandā tathaiva ca ।।
tathā tāmarasā caiva varakrīḍā ca vai daśa ।। svarbhānupihite sūrye patite asmindivo mahīm ।। svastyastu hi tavetyukte patanniha divākaraḥ ।। tataḥ prabhākaretyuktaḥ prabhuratrirmaharṣibhiḥ ।।
sa tāsu janayāmāsa punaḥ putrāṃstapodhanaḥ ।। teṣāṃ dvau khyātayaśasau brahmiṣṭhau ca mahaujasau ।। yavīyasī svasā teṣām amalā brahmavādinī ।। śyāvaś ca pratvasaścaiva vavalguścātha gahvaraḥ ।।
kāśyapo nāradaścaiva parvatānuddhatas tathā ।। nāradastu vasiṣṭhāyā-rundhatīṃ pratyapādayat ।। purā devāsure yuddhe ghore vai tārakāmaye ।। vasiṣṭhastapasā dhīmān dhārayāmāsa vai prajāḥ ।।
tānetāñjīvayāmāsa kāruṇyādauṣadhena ca ।। jyāyaso ajanayacchakter adṛśyantī parāśaram ।। kālī parāśarājjajñe kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ prabhum ।। upamanyuṃ ca pīvaryāṃ viddhīme śukasūnavaḥ ।।
kanyā kīrtimatī caiva yogamātā dhṛtavratā ।। śvetaḥ kṛṣṇaś ca gauraś ca śyāmo dhūmrastathāruṇaḥ ।। parāśarāṇāmaṣṭau te pakṣāḥ proktā mahātmanām ।। vasiṣṭhasya kapiñjalyo ghṛtācyāmudapadyata ।।
pṛthoḥ sutāyāṃ sambhūto bhadrastasyā bhavadvasuḥ ।। mitrāvaruṇayoścaiva kauṇḍinyā ye pariśrutāḥ ।। ete pakṣā vasiṣṭhānāṃ smṛtā daśa mahātmanām ।। bhartāraś ca mahābhāgā eṣāṃ vaṃśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।
teṣāṃ putrāś ca pautrāś ca śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।। yaistu vyāptāstrayo lokāḥ sūryasyeva gabhastibhiḥ ।। vāsiṣṭho vadatāṃ śreṣṭha sūta vaktumihārhasi ।। śaktiṃ sa bhakṣayāmāsa śakteḥ śāpātsahānujaiḥ ।।
kalmāṣapādaṃ rudhiro viśvāmitreṇa coditaḥ ।। śaktiḥ śaktimatāṃ śreṣṭho bhrātṛbhiḥ saha dharmavit ।। arundhatyā saha muniḥ papāta bhuvi duḥkhitaḥ ।। smaranputraśataṃ caiva śaktijyeṣṭhaṃ ca śaktimān ।।
na taṃ vināhaṃ jīviṣye iti niścitya duḥkhitaḥ ।। dharādharasyaiva tadā dharāyāṃ papāta patnyā saha sāśrudṛṣṭiḥ ।। karāṃbujābhyāṃ karikhelagāminī rudantamādāya ruroda sā ca ।। vasiṣṭhaṃ vadatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ rudantī bhayavihvalā ।।
pālayasva vibho draṣṭuṃ tava pautraṃ mamātmajam ।। garbhastho mama sarvārthasādhakaḥ śaktijo yataḥ ।। utthāpya śvaśuraṃ natvā netre saṃmṛjya vāriṇā ।। arundhatīṃ ca kalyāṇīṃ prārthayāmāsa duḥkhitām ।।
saṃjñāmavāpya cāliṅgya sā papāta suduḥkhitā ।। ruroda muniśārdūlo bhāryayā sutavatsalaḥ ।। āsīno garbhaśayyāyāṃ kumāra ṛcamāha saḥ ।। kenoktamiti saṃcintya tadātiṣṭhatsamāhitaḥ ।।
vasiṣṭhamāha viśvātmā ghṛṇayā sa ghṛṇānidhiḥ ।। tava pautramukhāmbhojād ṛg eṣādya viniḥsṛtā ।। tasmāduttiṣṭha saṃtyajya śokaṃ brahmasutottama ।। rudradevaprabhāveṇa kulaṃ te saṃtariṣyati ।।
vasiṣṭhaṃ muniśārdūlaṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। adṛśyantyā mahātejāḥ pasparśodaramādarāt ।। lalāpārundhatī prekṣya tadāsau rudatīṃ dvijāḥ ।। tava putramimaṃ dṛṣṭvā bho śakte kuladhāraṇam ।।
evamuktvā rudanvipra āliṅgyārundhatīṃ tadā ।। adṛśyantī jaghānātha śaktijasyālayaṃ śubhā ।। arundhati tadā bhītā vasiṣṭhaś ca mahāmatiḥ ।। samutthāpya snuṣāṃ bālām ūcaturbhayavihvalau ।।
kulaṃ vasiṣṭhasya samastamapyaho nihantumārye kathamudyatā vada ।। trātuṃ yato dehamimaṃ munīndraḥ suniścitaḥ pāhi tataḥ śarīram ।। arundhatī vasiṣṭhasya prāha cārteti vihvalā ।। jīvitaṃ rakṣa dehasya dhātrī ca kuru yaddhitam ।।
mamāśubhaṃ śubhaṃ dehaṃ kathaṃcit pālayāmyaham ।। mune duḥkhādahaṃ dagdhā yataḥ putrī mune tava ।। duḥkhatrātā bhava brahman brahmasūno jagadguro ।। pāhi māṃ tata āryendra paribhūtā bhaviṣyati ।।
ete na bāndhavāḥ strīṇāṃ bhartā bandhuḥ parā gatiḥ ।। tadapyatra mṛṣā hyāsīd gataḥ śaktirahaṃ sthitā ।। patiṃ prāṇasamaṃ tyaktvā sthitā yatra kṣaṇaṃ yataḥ ।। nirmūlāpyamṛtā bhartrā tyaktā dīnā sthitāpyaham ।।
tadā cakre matiṃ dhīmān yātuṃ svāśramamāśramī ।। adṛśyantyā ca puṇyātmā saṃviveśa sa cintayan ।। kulasaṃdhāraṇārthāya śaktipatnī pativratā ।। śaktipatnī yathā śaktiṃ śaktimantamarundhatī ।।
agniṃ yathāraṇiḥ patnī śakteḥ sākṣātparāśaram ।। śaktistyaktvā tadā duḥkhaṃ pitṝṇāṃ samatāṃ yayau ।। rarāja pitṛlokastho vāsiṣṭho munipuṅgavāḥ ।। prapitāmahāś ca viprendrā hy avatīrṇe parāśare ।।
puṣkarādyāś ca sasṛjuḥ puṣpavarṣaṃ ca khecarāḥ ।। āśramasthāś ca munayaḥ samūhurharṣasaṃtatim ।। adṛśyantyāścaturvaktro meghajālāddivākaraḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā putraṃ patiṃ smṛtvā arundhatyā munestathā ।।
lalāpa vihvalā bālā sannakaṇṭhī papāta ca ।। jātamātram anaghaṃ śucismitā budhya sāśrunayanā lalāpa ca ।। tyajya dīnavadanāṃ vanāntare putradarśanaparāmimāṃ prabho ।। yathā maheśvaro apaśyat sagaṇo hṛṣitānanaḥ ।।
śrutvā snuṣāmuvācedaṃ mā rodīr iti duḥkhitaḥ ।। tyaktvā hyapālayadbālaṃ bālā bālamṛgekṣaṇā ।। āsīnāmākulāṃ sādhvīṃ bāṣpaparyākulekṣaṇām ।। vaktumarhasi tavādya kāraṇaṃ candrabiṃbarahiteva śarvarī ।।
āsīnā bhartṛhīneva vaktumarhasi śobhane ।। na kiṃcid abravīt putraṃ śubhaṃ vā yadi vetarat ।। mātaḥ kutra mahātejāḥ pitā vada vadeti tām ।। bhakṣito rakṣasā tātas taveti nipapāta ca ।।
arundhatī cāśramavāsinastadā munervasiṣṭhasya munīśvarāś ca ।। śrutvā parāśaro dhīmān prāha cāsrāvilekṣaṇaḥ ।। kṣaṇena mātaḥ pitaraṃ darśayāmīti me matiḥ ।। tathyam etaditi taṃ nirīkṣya sā putra putra bhavamarcayeti ca ।।
vasiṣṭho bhagavānprāha pautraṃ dhīmān ghṛṇānidhiḥ ।। tathāpi śṛṇu lokasya kṣayaṃ kartuṃ na cārhasi ।। trailokyaṃ śṛṇu śākteya aparādhyati kiṃ tava ।। rākṣasānāmabhāvāya matiṃ cakre mahāmatiḥ ।।
kṛtvaikaliṅgaṃ kṣaṇikaṃ pāṃsunā munisannidhau ।। japtvā tvaritarudraṃ ca śivasaṃkalpameva ca ।। vāmīyaṃ pavamānaṃ ca pañcabrahma tathaiva ca ।। aṣṭāṅgamarghyaṃ rudrāya dattvābhyarcya yathāvidhi ।।
pitā mama mahātejā bhrātṛbhiḥ saha śaṅkara ।। evaṃ vijñāpayāṃlliṅgaṃ praṇipatya muhurmuhuḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagavānrudro devīmāha ca śaṅkaraḥ ।। mamānusmaraṇe yuktaṃ madārādhanatatparam ।।
duḥkhāt saṃklinnasarvāṅgam asrākulavilocanam ।। prāha bhartāramīśānaṃ śaṅkaraṃ jagatāmumā ।। niśamya vacanaṃ tasyāḥ śaṅkaraḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। rakṣāmyenaṃ dvijaṃ bālaṃ phullendīvaralocanam ।।
evamuktvā gaṇair divyair bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ ।। dadau ca darśanaṃ tasmai muniputrāya dhīmate ।। nipapāta ca hṛṣṭātmā pādayostasya sādaram ।। saphalaṃ jīvitaṃ me adya brahmādyāṃstāṃstadāha saḥ ।।
ko anyaḥ samo mayā loke devo vā dānavo api vā ।। pitaraṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ śākteyastu parāśaraḥ ।। bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaṃ dṛṣṭvā nanāma ca jaharṣa ca ।। vasiṣṭhaputraṃ prāhedaṃ putradarśanatatparam ।।
adṛśyantīṃ ca viprendra vasiṣṭhaṃ pitaraṃ tava ।। mātaraṃ pitaraṃ cobhau namaskuru mahāmate ।। vasiṣṭhaṃ ca tadā śreṣṭhaṃ śaktir vai śaṅkarājñayā ।। arundhatīṃ jagannāthaniyogātprāha śaktimān ।।
rakṣito ahaṃ tvayā tāta garbhasthena mahātmanā ।। labdhamadyānanaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tava bāla mamājñayā ।। arundhatīṃ ca pitaraṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ mama sarvadā ।। putreṇa lokāñjayatīty uktaṃ sadbhiḥ sadaiva hi ।।
gamiṣyāmyabhivandyeśaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha śaṅkaram ।। nirīkṣya bhāryāṃ sadasi jagāma pitaraṃ vaśī ।। tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhiḥ śākteyaḥ śaśibhūṣaṇam ।। anugṛhyātha śākteyaṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata ।।
dadāha rākṣasānāṃ tu kulaṃ mantreṇa mantravit ।। alam atyantakopena tāta manyumimaṃ jahi ।। mūḍhānāmeva bhavati krodho buddhimatāṃ na hi ।। saṃcitasyātimahatā vatsa kleśena mānavaiḥ ।।
alaṃ hi rākṣasair dagdhair dīnair anaparādhibhiḥ ।। evaṃ vasiṣṭhavākyena śākteyo munipuṅgavaḥ ।। tataḥ prītaś ca bhagavān vasiṣṭho munisattamaḥ ।। vasiṣṭhena tu dattārghyaḥ kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ ।।
vaire mahati yadvākyād guror adyāśritā kṣamā ।। saṃtatermama na chedaḥ kruddhenāpi yataḥ kṛtaḥ ।। purāṇasaṃhitākartā bhavānvatsa bhaviṣyati ।। pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā karmaṇas te amalā matiḥ ।।
tataś ca prāha bhagavān vasiṣṭho vadatāṃ varaḥ ।। atha tasya pulastyasya vasiṣṭhasya ca dhīmataḥ ।। ṣaṭprakāraṃ samastārthasādhakaṃ jñānasaṃcayam ।। caturthaṃ hi purāṇānāṃ saṃhitāsu suśobhanam ।।
prabhavaḥ śaktisūnoś ca prabhāvo munipuṅgavāḥ ।। vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ saṃkṣepād romaharṣaṇa ।। tasyādityasya caivāsīd bhāryā trayam athāparam ।। saṃjñā tvāṣṭrī ca suṣuve sūryānmanumanuttamam ।।
prabhā prabhātam ādityāc chāyāṃ saṃjñāpyakalpayat ।। tataḥ śaniṃ ca tapatīṃ viṣṭiṃ caiva yathākramam ।। pūrvo manurna cakṣāma yamastu krodhamūrchitaḥ ।। yamena tāḍitā sā tu chāyā vai duḥkhitābhavat ।।
pūyaśoṇitasampūrṇaṃ kṛmīṇāṃ nicayānvitam ।। ārādhayanmahādevaṃ yāvadvarṣāyutāyutam ।। pitṝṇāmādhipatyaṃ tu śāpamokṣaṃ tathaiva ca ।। asahantī purā bhānos tejomayam aninditā ।।
vaḍavārūpamāsthāya tapastepe tu suvratā ।। vaḍavāmagamatsaṃjñām aśvarūpeṇa bhāskaraḥ ।। suṣuve cāśvinau devau devānāṃ tu bhiṣagvarau ।। viṣṇoścakraṃ tu yadghoraṃ maṇḍalādbhāskarasya tu ।।
rudraprasādācca śubhaṃ sudarśanamiti smṛtam ।। manostu prathamasyāsan nava putrāstu tatsamāḥ ।। nariṣyantaś ca vai dhīmān nābhāgo ariṣṭa eva ca ।। ilā jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā ca puṃstvaṃ prāpa ca yā purā ।।
mitrāvaruṇayostvatra prasādānmunipuṅgavāḥ ।। sudyumno mānavaḥ śrīmān somavaṃśapravṛddhaye ।। ilā kiṃpuruṣatve ca sudyumna iti cocyate ।। ilā budhasya bhavanaṃ somaputrasya cāśritā ।।
somaputrādbudhāccāpi ailo jajñe purūravāḥ ।। ikṣvākorvaṃśavistāraṃ paścādvakṣye tapodhanāḥ ।। utkalaś ca gayaścaiva vinatāśvastathaiva ca ।। gayā gayasya cākhyātā purī paramaśobhanā ।।
ikṣvākujyeṣṭhadāyādo madhyadeśam avāptavān ।। vasiṣṭhavacanāt tvāsīt pratiṣṭhāne mahādyutiḥ ।। tatpurūravase prādād rājyaṃ prāpya mahāyaśāḥ ।। ikṣvākorabhavadvīro vikukṣirdharmavittamaḥ ।।
abhūjjyeṣṭhaḥ kakutsthaś ca kakutsthāttu suyodhanaḥ ।। viśvakasyārdrako dhīmān yuvanāśvastu tatsutaḥ ।। nirmitā yena śābastī gauḍadeśe dvijottamāḥ ।। dhundhumāratvamāpanno dhundhuṃ hatvā mahābalam ।।
dṛḍhāśvaścaiva caṇḍāśvaḥ kapilāśvaś ca te smṛtāḥ ।। haryaśvasya nikumbhastu saṃhatāśvastu tatsutaḥ ।। yuvanāśvo raṇāśvasya māndhātā tasya vai sutaḥ ।। mucukundaś ca puṇyātmā trayastrailokyaviśrutāḥ ।।
harito yuvanāśvasya haritāstu yataḥ smṛtāḥ ।। purukutsasya dāyādas trasaddasyur mahāyaśāḥ ।। viṣṇuvṛddhaḥ sutastasya viṣṇuvṛddhā yataḥ smṛtāḥ ।। sambhūtiraparaṃ putram anaraṇyamajījanat ।।
bṛhadaśvo anaraṇyasya haryaśvastasya cātmajaḥ ।। tasya putro abhavadrājā tridhanvā bhavabhāvitaḥ ।। aśvamedhasahasrasya phalaṃ prāpya tadājñayā ।। kathaṃ caivāśvamedhaṃ vai karomīti vicintayan ।।
taṇḍisaṃjñaṃ dvijaṃ tasmāl labdhavāndvijasattamāḥ ।। tena nāmnāṃ sahasreṇa stutvā taṇḍirmaheśvaram ।। tatastasmānnṛpo labdhvā taṇḍinā kathitaṃ purā ।। nāmnāṃ sahasraṃ rudrasya tāṇḍinā brahmayoninā ।।
nāmnāṃ sahasraṃ viprāṇāṃ vaktum arhasi śobhanam ।। aṣṭottarasahasraṃ tu nāmnāṃ śṛṇuta suvratāḥ ।। oṃ sthiraḥ sthāṇuḥ prabhurbhānuḥ pravaro varado varaḥ ।। jaṭī daṇḍī śikhaṇḍī ca sarvagaḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ ।।
pravṛttiś ca nivṛttiś ca śāntātmā śāśvato dhruvaḥ ।। abhivādyo mahākarmā tapasvī bhūtadhāraṇaḥ ।। mahārūpo mahākāyaḥ sarvarūpo mahāyaśāḥ ।। lokapālo antarhitātmā prasādo abhayado vibhuḥ ।।
svayaṃbhūḥ sarvakarmā ca ādirādikaro nidhiḥ ।। candraḥ sūryaḥ śaniḥ ketur graho grahapatirmataḥ ।। mahātapā dīrghatapā adṛśyo dhanasādhakaḥ ।। yogī yogo mahābījo mahārato mahābalaḥ ।।
daśabāhustvanimiṣo nīlakaṇṭha umāpatiḥ ।। gaṇakartā gaṇapatir digvāsāḥ kāmya eva ca ।। kamaṇḍaludharo dhanvī bāṇahastaḥ kapālavān ।। ajaś ca mṛgarūpaś ca tejastejaskaro vidhiḥ ।।
dīrghaś ca harikeśaś ca sutīrthaḥ kṛṣṇa eva ca ।। siṃhaśārdūlarūpaś ca gandhakārī kapardyapi ।। trijaṭī cīravāsāś ca rudraḥ senāpatir vibhuḥ ।। gajahā daityahā kālo lokadhātā guṇākaraḥ ।।
kālayogī mahānādaḥ sarvāvāsaścatuṣpathaḥ ।। bahubhūto bahudhanaḥ sarvasāro amṛteśvaraḥ ।। sakārmuko mahābāhur mahāghoro mahātapāḥ ।। sahasrahasto vijayo vyavasāyo hyaninditaḥ ।।
dakṣahā paricārī ca prahaso madhyamas tathā ।। gaṃbhīraghoṣo yogātmā yajñahā kāmanāśanaḥ ।। nyagrodharūpo nyagrodho viśvakarmā ca viśvabhuk ।। viṣṇuḥ prasādito yajñaḥ samudro vaḍavāmukhaḥ ।।
ugratejā mahātejā jayo vijayakālavit ।। khaḍgī śaṅkhī jaṭī jvālī khacaro dyucaro balī ।। nakṣatravigraho bhāvo nibhāvaḥ sarvatomukhaḥ ।। mekhalākṛtirūpaś ca jalācāraḥ stutas tathā ।।
sarvatūryaninādī ca sarvavyāpyaparigrahaḥ ।। vṛkṣaḥ śrīmālakarmā ca sarvabandhavimocanaḥ ।। sakhā pravāso durvāpaḥ sarvasādhuniṣevitaḥ ।। sarvavāsaḥ sarvacārī durvāsā vāsavo mataḥ ।।
ākāśo nirvirūpaś ca vivāsā uragaḥ khagaḥ ।। vasuretāḥ suvacasvī vasuvego mahābalaḥ ।। sarvāvāsī trayīvāsī upadeśakaro dharaḥ ।। pakṣī ca pakṣarūpaś ca atidīpto niśākaraḥ ।।
vāsudevaś ca devaś ca vāmadevaś ca vāmanaḥ ।। akṣuṇṇaḥ kṣuṇṇarūpaś ca vṛṣaṇo mṛdur avyayaḥ ।। cakrahastastu viṣṭambhī mūlastambhana eva ca ।। vānaspatyo vājasano nityamāśramapūjitaḥ ।।
īśāna īśvaraḥ kālo niśācārī hyanekadṛk ।। nandīśvaraḥ sunandī ca nandano viṣamardanaḥ ।। caturmukho mahāliṅgaś cāruliṅgastathaiva ca ।। bījādhyakṣo bījakartā adhyātmānugato balaḥ ।।
dambho dambhakaro dātā vaṃśo vaṃśakaraḥ kaliḥ ।। akṣaraṃ paramaṃ brahma balavāñchukta eva ca ।। prāsādastu balo darpo darpaṇo havya indrajit ।। mahāmeghanivāsī ca mahāghoro vaśīkaraḥ ।।
dhiṣaṇaḥ śaṅkaro nityo varcasvī dhūmralocanaḥ ।। svasti svastisvabhāvaś ca bhogī bhogakaro laghuḥ ।। kṛṣṇavarṇaḥ suvarṇaś ca indriyaḥ sarvavarṇikaḥ ।। mahāmūrdhā mahāmātro mahāmitro nagālayaḥ ।।
mahānāso mahākaṇṭho mahāgrīvaḥ śmaśānavān ।। lambitoṣṭhaś ca niṣṭhaś ca mahāmāyaḥ payonidhiḥ ।। mahānakho mahāromā mahākeśo mahājaṭaḥ ।। prasvedano asvedanaś ca ādikaś ca mahāmuniḥ ।।
maṇḍalī meruvāsaś ca devavāhana eva ca ।। yajuḥ pādabhujo guhyaḥ prakāśaujāstathaiva ca ।। upahāraḥ priyaḥ sarvaḥ kanakaḥ kāñcanasthitaḥ ।। sarvaśāstro dhanaścādyo yajño yajvā samāhitaḥ ।।
sagaṇo gaṇakāraś ca bhūtabhāvanasārathiḥ ।। āgamaś ca vilopaś ca mahātmā sarvapūjitaḥ ।। āśramasthaḥ kapotastho viśvakarmā patirvirāṭ ।। kapilaḥ kalaśaḥ sthūla āyudhaścaiva romaśaḥ ।।
paraśvadhāyudho devo hy arthakārī subāndhavaḥ ।। ugro vaṃśakaro vaṃśo vaṃśavādī hyaninditaḥ ।। bandhano bandhakartā ca subandhanavimocanaḥ ।। lambito lambitoṣṭhaś ca lambahasto varapradaḥ ।।
amareśo mahāghoro viśvadevaḥ surārihā ।। ajaikapācca kāpālī śaṃ kumāro mahāgiriḥ ।। dhātā viṣṇuś ca śakraś ca mitrastvaṣṭā dharo dhruvaḥ ।। dhṛtiścaiva vidhātā ca māndhātā bhūtabhāvanaḥ ।।
padmagarbho mahāgarbhaś candravaktro nabho anaghaḥ ।। krūrakartā krūravāsī tanurātmā mahauṣadhaḥ ।। devadevaḥ sukhotsiktaḥ sadasatsarvaratnavit ।। kulahārī kulākartā bahuvitto bahuprajaḥ ।।
hrasvagrīvo mahājānur alolaś ca mahauṣadhiḥ ।। siṃhanādaḥ siṃhadaṃṣṭraḥ siṃhāsyaḥ siṃhavāhanaḥ ।। sāraṅgo bhūtacakrāṅkaḥ ketumālī suvedhakaḥ ।। vasubhṛt sarvabhūtātmā niścalaḥ suvidur budhaḥ ।।
amoghaḥ saṃyamo hṛṣṭo bhojanaḥ prāṇadhāraṇaḥ ।। gopālo gopatirgrāmo gocarmavasano haraḥ ।। mahāmanā mahākāmaś cittakāmo jitendriyaḥ ।। mahābhūto bhūtavṛto hy apsarogaṇasevitaḥ ।।
avedanīya āvedyaḥ sarvagaś ca sukhāvahaḥ ।। saṃyogī vardhano vṛddho gaṇiko atha gaṇādhipaḥ ।। yuktaś ca yuktabāhuś ca sudevo api suparvaṇaḥ ।। vapurāvartamāno anyo vapuḥśreṣṭho mahāvapuḥ ।।
akṣayo rathagītaś ca sarvabhogī mahābalaḥ ।। nirjīvo jīvano mantraḥ subhago bahukarkaśaḥ ।। mūlaṃ viśālo hyamṛtaṃ vyaktāvyaktastaponidhiḥ ।। mahākaṇṭho mahāyogī yugo yugakaro hariḥ ।।
