nyāyo nirvāpaṇo apādaḥ paṇḍito hyacalopamaḥ ।। vistāro lavaṇaḥ kūpaḥ kusumāṅgaḥ phalodayaḥ ।। indurvisargaḥ sumukhaḥ śūraḥ sarvāyudhaḥ sahaḥ ।। girāvāso visargaś ca sarvalakṣaṇalakṣavit ।।
saṃtāno bahulo bāhuḥ sakalaḥ sarvapāvanaḥ ।। yantratantrasuvikhyāto lokaḥ sarvāśrayo mṛduḥ ।। vāryakṣaḥ kakubho vajrī dīptatejāḥ sahasrapāt ।। sahasrabāhuḥ sarvāṅgaḥ śaraṇyaḥ sarvalokakṛt ।।
brahmadaṇḍavinirmātā śataghnaḥ śatapāśadhṛk ।। viśvakṣetraprado bījaṃ liṅgamādyastu nirmukhaḥ ।। svargadvāraṃ mokṣadvāraṃ prajādvāraṃ triviṣṭapaḥ ।। devāsuravinirmātā devāsuraparāyaṇaḥ ।।
devāsuramahāmātro devāsuragaṇāśrayaḥ ।। devādhidevo devarṣir devāsuravarapradaḥ ।। sarvadevamayo acintyo devatātmā svayambhavaḥ ।। ijyo hastī tathā vyāghro devasiṃho maharṣabhaḥ ।।
saṃyuktaḥ śobhano vaktā āśānāṃ prabhavo avyayaḥ ।। śṛṅgī śṛṅgapriyo babhrū rājarājo nirāmayaḥ ।। lalāṭākṣo viśvadeho hariṇo brahmavarcasaḥ ।। siddhārthaḥ sarvabhūtārtho acintyaḥ satyaḥ śucivrataḥ ।।
vimukto muktakeśaś ca śrīmāñchrīvardhano jagat ।। bhaktimevaṃ puraskṛtya mayā yajñapatirvibhuḥ ।। tasmāllabdhvā stavaṃ śaṃbhor nṛpastrailokyaviśrutaḥ ।। gaṇādhipatyaṃ samprāptas taṇḍinastejasā prabhoḥ ।।
aśvamedhasahasrasya phalaṃ prāpnoti vai dvijāḥ ।। śaraṇāgataghātī ca mitraviśvāsaghātakaḥ ।। saṃvatsaraṃ kramājjaptvā trisaṃdhyaṃ śaṅkarāśrame ।। devam iṣṭvā trisaṃdhyaṃ ca sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।
aśvamedhasahasrasya phalaṃ prāpya prayatnataḥ ।। āsīttridhanvanaścāpi vidvāṃstrayyāruṇo nṛpaḥ ।। tena bhāryā vidarbhasya hṛtā hatvāmitaujasam ।। tenādharmeṇa saṃyuktaṃ rājā trayyāruṇo atyajat ।।
pitā tvenamathovāca śvapākaiḥ saha vartaya ।। sa tu satyavrato dhīmāñ chvapākāvasathāntike ।। sarvalokeṣu vikhyātas triśaṅkuriti vīryavān ।। viśvāmitro mahātejā varaṃ dattvā triśaṅkave ।।
miṣatāṃ devatānāṃ ca vasiṣṭhasya ca kauśikaḥ ।। tasya satyavratā nāma bhāryā kaikayavaṃśajā ।। hariścandrasya ca suto rohito nāma vīryavān ।। vijayaś ca sutejāś ca dhundhuputrau babhūvatuḥ ।।
rucakastasya tanayo rājā paramadhārmikaḥ ।। sagarastasya putro abhūd rājā paramadhārmikaḥ ।। tābhyāmārādhitaḥ pūrvam aurvo agniḥ putrakāmyayā ।। ekā ṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi sutamekaṃ parā tathā ।।
ekaṃ bhānumatiḥ putram agṛhṇād asamañjasam ।। khanantaḥ pṛthivīṃ dagdhā viṣṇuhuṅkāramārgaṇaiḥ ।। tasya putro dilīpastu dilīpāttu bhagīrathaḥ ।। bhagīrathasutaścāpi śruto nāma babhūva ha ।।
aṃbarīṣaḥ sutastasya sindhudvīpas tato abhavat ।। babhūva vasudhātyarthaṃ tāpatrayavivarjitā ।। putro ayutāyuṣo dhīmān ṛtuparṇo mahāyaśāḥ ।। nalau dvāveva vikhyātau purāṇeṣu dṛḍhavratau ।।
ṛtuparṇasya putro abhūt sārvabhaumaḥ prajeśvaraḥ ।। sudāsasya sutaḥ proktaḥ saudāso nāma pārthivaḥ ।। vasiṣṭhastu mahātejāḥ kṣetre kalmāṣapādake ।। aśmakasyottarāyāṃ tu mūlakastu suto abhavat ।।
bibharti trāṇamicchanvai nārīkavacamuttamam ।। tasmācchatarathājjajñe rājā tvilavilo balī ।। putro viśvasahastasya pitṛkanyā vyajījanat ।। yena svargād ihāgatya muhūrtaṃ prāpya jīvitam ।।
dīrghabāhuḥ sutastasya raghustasmādajāyata ।। rājā daśarathastasmāc chrīmānikṣvākuvaṃśakṛt ।। bharato lakṣmaṇaścaiva śatrughnaś ca mahābalaḥ ।। rāvaṇaṃ samare hatvā yajñairiṣṭvā ca dharmavit ।।
rāmasya tanayo jajñe kuśa ityabhiviśrutaḥ ।। atithistu kuśājjajñe niṣadhastasya cātmajaḥ ।। nabhasaḥ puṇḍarīkākhyaḥ kṣemadhanvā tataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। ahīnaraḥ sutas tasya sahasrāśvastataḥ paraḥ ।।
tasyātmajaścandragirir bhānucandras tato abhavat ।। bhārate yo mahātejāḥ saubhadreṇa nipātitaḥ ।। vaṃśe pradhānā etasmin prādhānyena prakīrtitāḥ ।। samabhyarcya yathājñānam iṣṭvā yajñairyathāvidhi ।।
nṛgo brāhmaṇaśāpena kṛkalāsatvam āgataḥ ।। raṇadhṛṣṭaś ca te putrās trayaḥ paramadhārmikāḥ ।। ānartasyābhavat putro rocamānaḥ pratāpavān ।। kakudmī cāparo jyeṣṭhaputraḥ putraśatasya tu ।।
nariṣyantasya putro abhūj jitātmā tu mahābalī ।। ṛtastasya sutaḥ śrīmān sarvadharmavidāṃvaraḥ ।। karūṣasya tu kārūṣāḥ sarve prakhyātakīrtayaḥ ।। śāpācchūdratvam āpannaś cyavanasyeti viśrutaḥ ।।
bhalandanasya vikrānto rājāsīd ajavāhanaḥ ।। ikṣvākoḥ putrapautrādyā elasyātha vadāmi vaḥ ।। cakre tvakaṇṭakaṃ rājyaṃ deśe puṇyatame dvijāḥ ।। pratiṣṭhānādhipaḥ śrīmān pratiṣṭhāne pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।।
gandharvalokaviditā bhavabhaktā mahābalāḥ ।। śrutāyuś ca śatāyuś ca divyāścaivorvaśīsutāḥ ।। svarbhānutanayāyāṃ te prabhāyāṃ jajñire nṛpāḥ ।। nahuṣasya tu dāyādāḥ ṣaḍindropamatejasaḥ ।।
yatiryayātiḥ saṃyātir āyātiḥ pañcamo andhakaḥ ।। yatirjyeṣṭhaś ca teṣāṃ vai yayātistu tato avaraḥ ।। teṣāṃ yayātiḥ pañcānāṃ mahābalaparākramaḥ ।। śarmiṣṭhāmāsurīṃ caiva tanayāṃ vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ ।।
tāvubhau śubhakarmāṇau stutau vidyāviśāradau ।। yayātaye rathaṃ tasmai dadau śukraḥ pratāpavān ।। susaṃgaṃ kāñcanaṃ divyam akṣaye ca maheṣudhī ।। sa tena rathamukhyena ṣaṇmāsenājayanmahīm ।।
bhavabhaktastu puṇyātmā dharmaniṣṭhaḥ samañjasaḥ ।। kauravāṇāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ sa bhavadratha uttamaḥ ।। pūrorvaṃśasya rājñastu rājñaḥ pārikṣitasya tu ।। gargasya hi sutaṃ bālaṃ sa rājā janamejayaḥ ।।
sa lohagandhī rājarṣiḥ paridhāvannitastataḥ ।। tataḥ sa duḥkhasaṃtapto na lebhe saṃvidaṃ kvacit ।। indretir nāma vikhyāto yo asau munirudāradhīḥ ।। aśvamedhena rājānaṃ pāvanārthaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।।
yajñasyāvabhṛthe madhye yāto divyo rathaḥ śubhaḥ ।। dattaḥ śakreṇa tuṣṭena lebhe tasmād bṛhadrathaḥ ।। pradadau vāsudevāya prītyā kauravanandanaḥ ।। kṛtopakārastenaiva puruṇā dvijasattamāḥ ।।
brāhmaṇapramukhā varṇā idaṃ vacanamabruvan ।। jyeṣṭhaṃ yadumatikramya kanīyānrājyamarhati ।। ete saṃbodhayāmastvāṃ dharmaṃ ca anupālaya ।। jyeṣṭhaṃ prati yathā rājyaṃ na deyaṃ me kathañcana ।।
pratikūlamatiścaiva na sa putraḥ satāṃ mataḥ ।। sa putraḥ putravad yas tu vartate mātṛpitṛṣu ।। druhyena cānunā caiva mayyavajñā kṛtā bhṛśam ।। kanīyānmama dāyādo jarā yena dhṛtā mama ।।
prārthitena punastena jarā saṃcāriṇī kṛtā ।। putro yastvanuvarteta sa te rājyadharastviti ।। yaḥ putro guṇasampanno mātāpitrorhitaḥ sadā ।। arhaḥ pūruridaṃ rājyaṃ yaḥ suto vākyakṛttava ।।
evaṃ jānapadaistuṣṭair ityukto nāhuṣastadā ।। diśi dakṣiṇapūrvasyāṃ turvasuṃ putramādiśat ।। pratīcyāmuttarasyāṃ tu druhyuṃ cānuṃ ca tāvubhau ।। vyabhajacca tridhā rājyaṃ putrebhyo nāhuṣastadā ।।
prītimānabhavadrājā bhāram āveśya bandhuṣu ।। yābhiḥ pratyāharet kāmān sarvato aṅgāni kūrmavat ।। na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyati ।। yatpṛthivyāṃ vrīhiyavaṃ hiraṇyaṃ paśavaḥ striyaḥ ।।
yadā na kurute bhāvaṃ sarvabhūteṣu pāpakam ।। yadā parānna bibheti pare cāsmānna bibhyati ।। yā dustyajā durmatibhir yānajīryati jīryataḥ ।। jīryanti jīryataḥ keśā dantā jīryanti jīryataḥ ।।
jīryanti dehinaḥ sarve svabhāvādeva nānyathā ।। yacca kāmasukhaṃ loke yacca divyaṃ mahatsukham ।। evamuktvā sa rājarṣiḥ sadāraḥ prāviśadvanam ।। sādhayitvā tvanaśanaṃ sadāraḥ svargamāptavān ।।
yairvyāptā pṛthivī kṛtsnā sūryasyeva marīcibhiḥ ।। yayāticaritaṃ puṇyaṃ paṭhañchṛṇvaṃś ca buddhimān ।। sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ śivaloke mahīyate ।। saṃkṣepeṇānupūrvyācca gadato me nibodhata ।।
sahasrajitsuto jyeṣṭhaḥ kroṣṭur nīlo ajako laghuḥ ।। sutāḥ śatajitaḥ khyātās trayaḥ paramakīrtayaḥ ।। haihayasya tu dāyādo dharma ityabhiviśrutaḥ ।। dharmanetrasya kīrtis tu saṃjayas tasya cātmajaḥ ।।
āsīn mahiṣmataḥ putro bhadraśreṇyaḥ pratāpavān ।। durdamasya suto dhīmān dhanako nāma viśrutaḥ ।। kṛtavīryaḥ kṛtāgniś ca kṛtavarmā tathaiva ca ।। jajñe bāhusahasreṇa saptadvīpeśvarottamaḥ ।।
tasya putraśatānyāsan pañca tatra mahārathāḥ ।। śūraś ca śūrasenaś ca dhṛṣṭaḥ kṛṣṇastathaiva ca ।। jayadhvajasya putro abhūt tālajaṅgho mahābalaḥ ।। teṣāṃ jyeṣṭho mahāvīryo vītihotro abhavannṛpaḥ ।।
vṛṣo vaṃśakarasteṣāṃ tasya putro abhavanmadhuḥ ।। yādavā yaduvaṃśena nirucyante tu haihayāḥ ।। teṣāṃ pañca gaṇā hyete haihayānāṃ mahātmanām ।। śūrasenāstu vikhyātās tālajaṅghāstathaiva ca ।।
jayadhvajaḥ pañcamastu vikhyātā haihayottamāḥ ।। śūrasenā iti khyātā deśāsteṣāṃ mahātmanām ।। durjayaḥ kṛṣṇaputrastu babhūvāmitrakarśanaḥ ।। yasyānvaye tu sambhūto viṣṇur vṛṣṇikulodvahaḥ ।।
tasya putro abhavat svātī kuśaṅkus tatsuto abhavat ।। mahākratubhir īje asau vividhairāptadakṣiṇaiḥ ।। atha caitraratho vīro yajvā vipuladakṣiṇaḥ ।। cakravartī mahāsattvo mahāvīryo bahuprajāḥ ।।
śaṃsanti tasya putrāṇām anantakam anuttamam ।। uśanāstasya tanayaḥ samprāpya tu mahīmimām ।। smṛtaścośanasaḥ putraḥ siteṣur nāma pārthivaḥ ।। vīraḥ kambalabarhistu marustasyātmajaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
nihatya rukmakavaco vīrān kavacino raṇe ।। aśvamedhe tu dharmātmā ṛtvigbhyaḥ pṛthivīṃ dadau ।। jajñire pañca putrāstu mahāsattvāḥ parāvṛtaḥ ।। parighaṃ ca hariṃ caiva videheṣu pitā nyasat ।।
taistu pravrājito rājā jyāmagho avasadāśrame ।। jagāma dhanurādāya deśamanyaṃ dhvajī rathī ।। ṛkṣavantaṃ giriṃ gatvā tyaktamanyairuvāsa saḥ ।। sā caiva tapasogreṇa śaibyā vai samprasūyata ।।
rājā putrasutāyāṃ tu vidvāṃsau krathakaiśikau ।। romapādastṛtīyaś ca babhrustasyātmajaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। kauśikastanayastasmāt tasmāccaidyānvayaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। kunter vṛtastato jajñe raṇadhṛṣṭaḥ pratāpavān ।।
daśārho naidhṛto nāmnā mahārigaṇasūdanaḥ ।। jīmūtaputro vikṛtis tasya bhīmarathaḥ sutaḥ ।। dānadharmarato nityaṃ satyaśīlaparāyaṇaḥ ।। tasmāt karambhaḥ sambhūto devarāto abhavattataḥ ।।
devagarbhopamo jajñe yo devakṣatranāmakaḥ ।। madhūnāṃ vaṃśakṛdrājā madhostu kuruvaṃśakaḥ ।। aṃśurjajñe ca vaidarbhyāṃ bhadravatyāṃ purutvataḥ ।। sattvāt sarvaguṇopetaḥ sātvataḥ kulavardhanaḥ ।।
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi nisṛṣṭiṃ jyāmaghasya tu ।। prajīvatyeti vai svargaṃ rājyaṃ saukhyaṃ ca vindati ।। bhajanaṃ bhrājamānaṃ ca divyaṃ devāvṛdhaṃ nṛpam ।। teṣāṃ nisargāṃścaturaḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ vistareṇa vai ।।
ayutāyuḥ śatāyuś ca balavān harṣakṛtsmṛtaḥ ।। putraḥ sarvaguṇopeto mama bhūyāditi smaran ।। anuvaṃśapurāṇajñā gāyantīti pariśrutam ।। yathaiva śṛṇumo dūrāt saṃpaśyāmastathāntikāt ।।
puruṣāḥ pañca ṣaṣṭistu ṣaṭ sahasrāṇi cāṣṭa ca ।। yajvā dānamatirvīro brahmaṇyastu dṛḍhavrataḥ ।। tasyānvavāye sambhūtā bhojā vai daivatopamāḥ ।। gāndhārī janayāmāsa sumitraṃ mitranandanam ।।
anamitraṃ śiniṃ caiva tāvubhau puruṣottamau ।। prasenaś ca mahābhāgaḥ satrājicca sutāvubhau ।। syamantako nāma maṇir dattastasmai vivasvatā ।। kadācinmṛgayāṃ yātaḥ prasenena sahaiva saḥ ।।
atha putraḥ śinerjajñe kaniṣṭhād vṛṣṇinandanāt ।। sātyakiryuyudhānastu śinernaptā pratāpavān ।। kuṇer yugaṃdharaḥ putraḥ śaineyā iti kīrtitāḥ ।। śvaphalka iti vikhyātas trailokyahitakārakaḥ ।।
nāsti vyādhibhayaṃ tatra nāvṛṣṭibhayamapyuta ।। gāndinīṃ nāma kāśyo hi dadau tasmai svakanyakām ।। vasantī na ca saṃjajñe garbhasthā tāṃ pitābravīt ।। provāca cainaṃ garbhasthā sā kanyā gāndinī tadā ।।
yadi dadyāstataḥ kukṣer nirgamiṣyāmyahaṃ pitaḥ ।। dātā śūraś ca yajvā ca śrutavānatithipriyaḥ ।। ratnā kanyā ca śaivasya hy akrūrastāmavāptavān ।। upamanyus tathā māṅgur vṛtastu janamejayaḥ ।।
dharmabhṛd vṛṣṭadharmā ca godhano atha varas tathā ।। akrūrasyograsenyāṃ tu putrau dvau kulanandanau ।। sumitrasya suto jajñe citrakaś ca mahāyaśāḥ ।। aśvagrīvaḥ subāhuś ca sudhāsūkagavekṣaṇau ।।
subhūmirbahubhūmiś ca śraviṣṭhāśravaṇe striyau ।। kukuraṃ bhajamānaṃ ca śuciṃ kambalabarhiṣam ।। kapotaromātibalas tasya putro vilomakaḥ ।। khyāyate sa sunāmnā tu candanānakadundubhiḥ ।।
aśvamedhaṃ sa putrārtham ājahāra narottamaḥ ।। tatastu vidvān sarvajño dātā yajvā punarvasuḥ ।। āhukaścāhukī caiva khyātau kīrtimatāṃ varau ।। devakaścograsenaś ca devagarbhasamāvubhau ।।
devavān upadevaś ca sudevo devarakṣitaḥ ।। vṛṣadevopadevā ca tathānyā devarakṣitā ।। devakī cāpi tāsāṃ ca variṣṭhābhūtsumadhyamā ।। teṣāṃ putrāśca pautrāś ca śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।।
babhūva vandyā pūjyā ca devairapi pativratā ।। pauravī bāhlikasutā saṃpūjyāsītsurairapi ।। āśritaṃ kaṃsabhītyā ca svātmānaṃ śāntatejasam ।। vasudevo hariṃ dhīmān devakyāmudapādayat ।।
halāyudhaś ca bhagavān ananto rajataprabhaḥ ।। babhūva tasyāṃ devakyāṃ vāsudevo janārdana ।। niyogāddevadevasya yaśodātanayā hyabhūt ।। puruṣo bhagavānkṛṣṇo dharmamokṣaphalapradaḥ ।।
caturbhujaṃ viśālākṣaṃ śrīvatsakṛtalāñchanam ।। yaśodāyai pradattvā tu vasudevaś ca buddhimān ।। rakṣakaṃ jagatāṃ viṣṇuṃ svecchayā dhṛtavigraham ।। rāmeṇa sārdhaṃ taṃ dattvā varadaṃ parameśvaram ।।
ato vai sarvakalyāṇaṃ yādavānāṃ bhaviṣyati ।। ugrasenātmajāyātha kaṃsāyānakadundubhiḥ ।। asyāstavāṣṭamo garbho devakyāḥ kaṃsa suvrata ।। tatastāṃ hantumārebhe kaṃsaḥ sollaṅghya cāṃbaram ।।
rakṣasva tatsvakaṃ deham āyāto mṛtyureva te ।। kiṃ kṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ mūrkha jātaḥ khalu tavāntakṛt ।। smaranti vihito mṛtyur devakyās tanayo aṣṭamaḥ ।। prabhāvānmuniśārdūlās tayā caiva jaḍīkṛtaḥ ।।
nihatā bahavaścānye devabrāhmaṇaghātinaḥ ।। bahavaḥ parisaṃkhyātāḥ sarve yuddhaviśāradāḥ ।। putreṣveteṣu sarveṣu cārudeṣṇādayo hareḥ ।। ṣoḍaśastrīsahasrāṇi śatamekaṃ tathādhikam ।।
tayā dvādaśavarṣāṇi kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā ।। cārudeṣṇaḥ sucāruś ca cāruveṣo yaśodharaḥ ।। ete labdhāstu kṛṣṇena śūlapāṇiprasādataḥ ।। jāmbavatyabravītkṛṣṇaṃ bhāryā kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ ।।
sureśasaṃmitaṃ putraṃ prasanno dātumarhasi ।। tapastaptuṃ samārebhe taponidhiraninditaḥ ।। vyāghrapādasya ca muner gatvā caivāśramottamam ।। divyaṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ labdhavāṃstasya cājñayā ।।
dīkṣito bhagavānkṛṣṇas tatāpa ca paraṃtapaḥ ।। phalāmbanilabhojī ca ṛtutrayam adhokṣajaḥ ।। sāmbaṃ jāṃbavatīputraṃ kṛṣṇāya ca mahātmane ।। praharṣamatulaṃ lebhe labdhvādityaṃ yathāditiḥ ।।
bhujānāṃ caiva sāhasraṃ śāpādrudrasya dhīmataḥ ।। tathā duṣṭakṣitīśānāṃ līlayaiva raṇājire ।। brāhmaṇasyordhvacakrasya varadānānmahātmanaḥ ।। śatādhikāni jagrāha sahasrāṇi mahābalaḥ ।।
saṃhṛtya tatkulaṃ caiva prabhāse atiṣṭhadacyutaḥ ।। kṛṣṇasya dvārakāyāṃ vai jarākleśāpahāriṇaḥ ।। śāpaṃ piṇḍārake arakṣad vaco durvāsasastadā ।। anugṛhya ca kṛṣṇo api lubdhakaṃ prayayau divam ।।
cauraiścāpahṛtāḥ sarvās tasya māyābalena ca ।। mahiṣyastasya kṛṣṇasya rukmiṇīpramukhāḥ śubhāḥ ।। revatī ca tathā devī balabhadreṇa dhīmatā ।। pretakāryaṃ hareḥ kṛtvā pārthaḥ paramavīryavān ।।
kandamūlaphalaistasya balikāryaṃ cakāra saḥ ।। evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥ kṛṣṇasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ ।। ityetatsomavaṃśānāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ caritaṃ dvijāḥ ।। sa yāti vaiṣṇavaṃ lokaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।।
sāṃprataṃ vistareṇaiva vaktumarhasi suvrata ।। paratve saṃsthito devaḥ paramātmā munīśvarāḥ ।। pradhānaṃ prakṛtiśceti yadāhustattvacintakāḥ ।। ajaraṃ dhruvamakṣayyaṃ nityaṃ svātmanyavasthitam ।।
vigrahaḥ sarvabhūtānām īśvarājñāpracoditam ।। aprakāśamavijñeyaṃ brahmāgre samavartata ।। guṇasāmye tadā tasminn avibhāge tamomaye ।। guṇabhāvādvyajyamāno mahān prādurbabhūva ha ।।
sattvodrikto mahānagre sattāmātraprakāśakaḥ ।। samutpannaṃ liṅgamātraṃ kṣetrajñādhiṣṭhitaṃ hi tat ।। mahān sṛṣṭiṃ vikurute codyamānaḥ sisṛkṣayā ।। prajñā citiḥ smṛtiḥ saṃvid viśveśaśceti sa smṛtaḥ ।।
saukṣmyāttena vibhaktaṃ tu yena tanmana ucyate ।। viśeṣebhyo guṇebhyo api mahāniti tataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। puruṣo bhogasaṃbandhāt tena cāsau matiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। yasmāddhārayate bhāvān brahma tena nirucyate ।।
nayate tattvabhāvaṃ ca tena pūriti cocyate ।। yasmādbodhayate caiva buddhistena nirucyate ।। bhogasya jñānaniṣṭhatvāt tena khyātiriti smṛtaḥ ।। tasmācca mahataḥ saṃjñā khyātirityabhidhīyate ।।
yasmājjñānānugaścaiva prajñā tena sa ucyate ।। cinoti yasmādbhogārthaṃ tenāsau citirucyate ।। smarate sarvakāryāṇi tenāsau smṛtirucyate ।। tasmād vinder videścaiva saṃvidityabhidhīyate ।।
tasmātsaṃviditi prokto mahadbhir munisattamāḥ ।। bandhanādiparībhāvād īśvaraḥ procyate budhaiḥ ।। vyākhyātaṃ tattvabhāvajñair devasadbhāvacetakaiḥ ।। saṃkalpo adhyavasāyaś ca tasya vṛttidvayaṃ smṛtam ।।
mahatā ca vṛtaḥ sargo bhūtādir bāhyatastu saḥ ।। bhūtatanmātrasargastu bhūtādistāmasastu saḥ ।। ākāśaṃ suṣiraṃ tasmād utpannaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam ।। vāyuścāpi vikurvāṇo rūpamātraṃ sasarja ha ।।
sparśamātrastu vai vāyū rūpamātraṃ samāvṛṇot ।। sambhavanti tato hyāpas tā vai sarvarasātmikāḥ ।। āpaścāpi vikurvatyo gandhamātraṃ sasarjire ।। tasmiṃstasmiṃś ca tanmātraṃ tena tanmātratā smṛtā ।।
praśāntaghoramūḍhatvād aviśeṣāstataḥ punaḥ ।। vaikārikādahaṅkārāt sattvodriktāttu sāttvikāt ।। buddhīndriyāṇi pañcaiva pañca karmendriyāṇi ca ।। ekādaśaṃ manastatra svaguṇenobhayātmakam ।।
śabdādīnāmavāptyarthaṃ buddhiyuktāni tāni vai ।। gatirvisargo hyānandaḥ śilpaṃ vākyaṃ ca karma tat ।। dviguṇastu tato vāyuḥ śabdasparśātmako abhavat ।। triguṇastu tatastvagniḥ saśabdasparśarūpavān ।।
tasmāccaturguṇā āpo vijñeyāstu rasātmikāḥ ।। saṃgatā gandhamātreṇa āviśanto mahīmimām ।। śāntā ghorāś ca mūḍhāś ca viśeṣāstena te smṛtāḥ ।। bhūmerantastvidaṃ sarvaṃ lokālokācalāvṛtam ।।
guṇaṃ pūrvasya sargasya prāpnuvantyuttarottarāḥ ।। upalabhyāpsu vai gandhaṃ kecid brūyur apāṃ guṇam ।। ete sapta mahātmāno hy anyonyasya samāśrayāt ।। mahādayo viśeṣāntā hy aṇḍamutpādayanti te ।।
viśeṣebhyo aṇḍam abhavan mahat tad udakeśayam ।। āpo daśaguṇenaitās tejasā bāhyato vṛtāḥ ।। vāyurdaśaguṇenaiva bāhyato nabhasā vṛtaḥ ।। bhūtādirmahatā cāpi avyaktenāvṛto mahān ।।
rudro agnimadhye bhagavān ugro vāyau punaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। buddhau ca bhagavānīśaḥ sarvataḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। etā āvṛtya cānyonyam aṣṭau prakṛtayaḥ sthitāḥ ।। evaṃ parasparotpannā dhārayanti parasparam ।।
maheśvaraḥ paro avyaktād aṇḍam avyaktasaṃbhavam ।। tasminkāryasya karaṇaṃ saṃsiddhaṃ svecchayaiva tu ।। tasya vāmāṅgajo viṣṇuḥ sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ ।। dakṣiṇāṅgabhavo brahmā sarasvatyā jagadguruḥ ।।
candrādityau sanakṣatrau sagrahau saha vāyunā ।। yattu sṛṣṭau prasaṃkhyātaṃ mayā kālāntaraṃ dvijāḥ ।। rātriścaitāvatī jñeyā parameśasya kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। nāhastu vidyate tasya na rātririti dhārayet ।।
indriyāṇīndriyārthāś ca mahābhūtāni pañca ca ।। ahastiṣṭhanti sarvāṇi parameśasya dhīmataḥ ।। svātmanyavasthite vyakte vikāre pratisaṃhṛte ।। tamaḥsattvarajopetau samatvena vyavasthitau ।।
guṇasāmye layo jñeyo vaiṣamye sṛṣṭirucyate ।। tathā tamasi sattve ca rajasyanusṛtaṃ jagat ।। arhamukhe pravṛttaś ca paraḥ prakṛtisaṃbhavaḥ ।। pradhānaṃ puruṣaṃ caiva praviśya sa maheśvaraḥ ।।
śāśvatāḥ paramā guhyaḥ sarvātmānaḥ śarīriṇaḥ ।। eta eva trayo lokā eta eva trayo agnayaḥ ।। paraspareṇa vartante dhārayanti parasparam ।। kṣaṇaṃ viyogo na hyeṣāṃ na tyajanti parasparam ।।
brahmā ca rajasā yuktaḥ sargādau hi pravartate ।। paraḥ sa puruṣo jñeyaḥ prakṛtiḥ sā parā smṛtā ।। anupravṛttastu mahāṃstadenāṃ cirasthiratvād viṣayaṃ śriyaḥ svayam ।। īśvarādhiṣṭhitātpūrvaṃ tasmātsadasadātmakāt ।।
tejasāpratimo dhīmān avyaktaḥ samprakāśakaḥ ।। brahmā ca bhagavāṃstasmāc caturvaktraḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। eka eva mahādevas tridhaivaṃ sa vyavasthitaḥ ।। dharmeṇa cāpratīpena vairāgyeṇa ca te anvitāḥ ।।
vaśīkṛtatvāttraiguṇyaṃ sāpekṣatvātsvabhāvataḥ ।। sahasramūrdhā puruṣas tisro avasthāḥ svayaṃbhuvaḥ ।। puruṣatve hyudāsīnas tisro avasthāḥ prajāpateḥ ।। puruṣaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣo rūpaṃ tatparamātmanaḥ ।।
maheśvaraḥ śarīrāṇi karoti vikaroti ca ।। maheśvaraḥ śarīrāṇi karoti vikaroti ca ।। caturdhā pravibhaktatvāc caturvyūhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। yaccāsya satataṃ bhāvas tasmādātmā nirucyate ।।
svāmitvamasya yatsarvaṃ viṣṇuḥ sarvapraveśanāt ।। paramaḥ samprakṛṣṭatvād avanād omiti smṛtaḥ ।। tridhā vibhajya cātmānaṃ trailokyaṃ sampravartate ।। āditvād ādidevo asāv ajātatvād ajaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
deveṣu ca mahāndevo mahādevastataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। bṛhattvācca smṛto brahmā bhūtatvādbhūta ucyate ।। yasmātpuryāṃ sa śete ca tasmātpūruṣa ucyate ।। yājyatvāducyate yajñaḥ kavir vikrāntadarśanāt ।।
ādityasaṃjñaḥ kapilo hy agrajo agniriti smṛtaḥ ।। tasmāddhiraṇyagarbhatvaṃ purāṇe asminnirucyate ।। na śakyaḥ parisaṃkhyātum api varṣaśatairapi ।। tāvaccheṣo asya kālo anyas tasyānte pratisṛjyate ।।
yastvayaṃ vartate kalpo vārāhastaṃ nibodhata ।। yasminsvāyaṃbhuvādyāstu manavaste caturdaśa ।। tairiyaṃ pṛthivī sarvā saptadvīpā saparvatā ।। prajābhistapasā caiva teṣāṃ śṛṇuta vistaram ।।
kathitāni bhaviṣyanti kalpaḥ kalpena caiva hi ।। anāgateṣu tadvacca tarkaḥ kāryo vijānatā ।। śāntatāraikanīre asmin na prājñāyata kiṃcana ।। tadā bhavati vai brahmā sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt ।।
brahmā nārāyaṇākhyastu suṣvāpa salile tadā ।। imaṃ codāharantyatra ślokaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prati ।। āpūrya tābhir ayanaṃ kṛtavānātmano yataḥ ।। caturyugasahasrasya naiśaṃ kālam upāsyataḥ ।।
brahmā tu salile tasmin vāyurbhūtvā samācarat ।। tatas tu salile tasmin vijñāyāntargatāṃ mahīm ।। akarotsa tanūmanyāṃ kalpādiṣu yathāpurā ।। salilenāplutāṃ bhūmiṃ dṛṣṭvā sa tu samantataḥ ।।
jalakrīḍānusadṛśaṃ vārāhaṃ rūpamāviśat ।। pṛthivyuddharaṇārthāya praviveśa rasātalam ।। upagamyojjahārainām āpaścāpi samāviśat ।। rasātalatale magnāṃ rasātalapuṭe gatām ।।
tataḥ svasthānamānīya pṛthivīṃ pṛthivīdharaḥ ।। tasyopari jalaughasya mahatī nauriva sthitā ।। tata utkṣipya tāṃ devo jagataḥ sthāpanecchayā ।। pṛthivīṃ ca samāṃ kṛtvā pṛthivyāṃ so acinod girīn ।।
tenāgninā viśīrṇāste parvatā bhūrivistarāḥ ।। niṣiktā yatra yatrāsaṃs tatra tatrācalābhavan ।। girayo hi nigīrṇatvāc chayānatvācchiloccayāḥ ।। viśvakarmā vibhajate kalpādiṣu punaḥ punaḥ ।।
bhūrādyāṃś caturo lokān punaḥ so atha vyakalpayat ।। brahmā svayaṃbhūrbhagavān sisṛkṣurvividhāḥ prajāḥ ।। tasyābhidhyāyataḥ sargaṃ tathā vai buddhipūrvakam ।। tamomoho mahāmohas tāmisraścāndhasaṃjñitaḥ ।।
pañcadhāvasthitaḥ sargo dhyāyataḥ so abhimāninaḥ ।। bahirantaścāprakāśas tabdho niḥsaṃjña eva ca ।। tasmātte saṃvṛtātmāno nagā mukhyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। aprasannamanāḥ so atha tato anyaṃ so hyamanyata ।।
tasmāt tiryakpravṛttaḥ sa tiryaksrotās tataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। tasyābhidhyāyato anyaṃ vai sāttvikaḥ samavartata ।। yasmātpravartate cordhvam ūrdhvasrotāstataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। prakāśā bahirantaś ca ūrdhvasrotobhavāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
ūrdhvasrotāstṛtīyo vai devasargastu sa smṛtaḥ ।। te ūrdhvasrotaso jñeyās tuṣṭātmāno budhaiḥ smṛtāḥ ।। prītimānabhavadbrahmā tato anyaṃ so abhyamanyata ।। tato abhidhyāyatastasya satyābhidhyāyinastadā ।।
yasmād arvāṅnyavartanta tato arvāksrotasas tu te ।। tasmātte duḥkhabahulā bhūyobhūyaś ca kāriṇaḥ ।। saṃvṛtā bahirantaś ca manuṣyāḥ sādhakāś ca te ।। lakṣaṇaistārakādyaiste hy aṣṭadhā tu vyavasthitāḥ ।।
ityeṣa taijasaḥ sargo hy arvāksrotaḥprakīrtitaḥ ।। viparyayeṇa śaktyā ca siddhyā tuṣṭyā tathaiva ca ।। siddhātmāno manuṣyāstu ṛṣideveṣu kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। bhūtādikānāṃ bhūtānāṃ ṣaṣṭhaḥ sargaḥ sa ucyate ।।
bhūtādikānāṃ bhūtānāṃ saptamaḥ sarga eva ca ।। svādanāś cāpyaśīlāś ca jñeyā bhūtādikāś ca te ।। prathamo mahataḥ sargo vijñeyo brahmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। vaikārikastṛtīyastu sarga aindriyakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
mukhyasargaścaturthaś ca mukhyā vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। aṣṭamo anugrahaḥ sargaḥ sāttvikastāmasaś ca saḥ ।। prākṛto vaikṛtaścaiva kaumāro navamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। buddhipūrvaṃ pravartante ṣaṭ punarbrahmaṇastu te ।।
caturdhāvasthitaḥ so atha sarvabhūteṣu kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। parasparānuraktāś ca kāraṇaiś ca budhaiḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ṛbhuḥ sanatkumāraś ca dvāvetāvūrdhvaretasau ।। vyatīte tvaṣṭame kalpe purāṇau lokasākṣiṇau ।।
tāvubhau mokṣakarmāṇāv āropyātmānamātmani ।। yathotpannastathaiveha kumāraḥ sa ihocyate ।। sanandaṃ sanakaṃ caiva vidvāṃsaṃ ca sanātanam ।। saṃbuddhāścaiva nānātve apravṛttāś ca yoginaḥ ।।
tatasteṣu vyatīteṣu tato anyān sādhakān sutān ।। ā bhūtasamplavāvasthā yairiyaṃ vidhṛtā mahī ।। samudrāṃś ca nadīścaiva tathā śailavanaspatīn ।। latāḥ kāṣṭhāḥ kalāścaiva muhūrtāḥ saṃdhirātryahān ।।
sthānābhimāninaḥ sarve sthānākhyāścaiva te smṛtāḥ ।। marīcibhṛgvaṅgirasaṃ pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum ।। nava brahmāṇa ityete purāṇe niścayaṃ gatāḥ ।। sthānāni kalpayāmāsa pūrvavatpadmasaṃbhavaḥ ।।
so asṛjad vyavasāyāttu dharmaṃ devo maheśvaraḥ ।। mānasaś ca rucirnāma vijajñe brahmaṇaḥ prabhoḥ ।। bhṛgustu hṛdayājjajñe ṛṣiḥ salilajanmanaḥ ।। pulastyaṃ ca tathodānād vyānācca pulahaṃ punaḥ ।।
ityete brahmaṇaḥ putrā divyā ekādaśā smṛtāḥ ।। bhṛgvādayastu te sṛṣṭā navaite brahmavādinaḥ ।। teṣāṃ dvādaśa te vaṃśā divyā devaguṇānvitāḥ ।। ṛbhuḥ sanatkumāraś ca dvāvetāvūrdhvaretasau ।।
vyatīte tvaṣṭame kalpe purāṇau lokasākṣiṇau ।। tāvubhau yogakarmāṇāv āropyātmānam ātmani ।। yathotpannaḥ sa eveha kumāraḥ sa ihocyate ।। tato abhidhyāyatastasya jajñire mānasāḥ prajāḥ ।।
kṣetrajñāḥ samavartanta gātrebhyastasya dhīmataḥ ।। sisṛkṣur ambhāṃsyetāni svam ātmānam ayūyujat ।। samabhidhyāyataḥ sargaṃ prayatnena prajāpateḥ ।। asuḥ prāṇaḥ smṛto viprās tajjanmānas tato asurāḥ ।।
sāpaviddhā tanus tena sadyo rātrir ajāyata ।। āvṛtāstamasā rātrau prajāstasmātsvapantyuta ।। avyaktāṃ sattvabahulāṃ tatastāṃ so abhyapūjayat ।। tato mukhātsamutpannā dīvyatastasya devatāḥ ।।
dhāturdiviti yaḥ proktaḥ krīḍāyāṃ sa vibhāvyate ।। devānsṛṣṭvātha deveśas tanumanyāmapadyata ।। tasmādaho dharmayuktaṃ devatāḥ samupāsate ।। pitṛvanmanyamānasya putrāṃstāndhyāyataḥ prabhoḥ ।।
tasmātte pitaro devāḥ pitṛtvaṃ tena teṣu tat ।। sāpaviddhā tanustena sadyaḥ saṃdhyā vyajāyata ।। tayormadhye tu paitrī yā tanuḥ sā tu garīyasī ।। upāsante mudāyuktā rātryahṇor madhyamāṃ tanum ।।
rajomātrātmikāyāṃ tu manasā so asṛjatprabhuḥ ।। manasvinastatastasya mānavā jajñire sutāḥ ।। sāpaviddhā tanustena jyotsnā sadyastvajāyata ।। ityetāstanavastena hy apaviddhā mahātmanā ।।
jyotsnā saṃdhyā ahaścaiva sattvamātrātmakaṃ trayam ।। tasmāddevā divātanvā tuṣṭyā sṛṣṭā mukhāttu vai ।। tanvā yayāsurān rātrau jaghanādasṛjatprabhuḥ ।। etānyeva bhaviṣyāṇāṃ devānāmasuraiḥ saha ।।
manvantareṣu sarveṣu nimittāni bhavanti hi ।। bhānti yasmāt tato aṃbhāṃsi śabdo ayaṃ sumanīṣibhiḥ ।। so ambhāṃsyetāni sṛṣṭvā tu devamānuṣadānavān ।। tāmutsṛjya tanuṃ jyotsnāṃ tato anyāṃ prāpya sa prabhuḥ ।।
andhakāre kṣudhāviṣṭāṃs tato anyān so asṛjat prabhuḥ ।। ambhāṃsyetāni rakṣāma uktavantastu teṣu ye ।। ye abruvan yakṣamo ambhāṃsi teṣāṃ hṛṣṭāḥ parasparam ।। rakṣeti pālane cāpi dhātureṣa vibhāṣyate ।।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā hyapriyeṇāsya keśāḥ śīrṇāstu dhīmataḥ ।। hīnāstacchiraso vālā yasmāccaivāvasarpiṇaḥ ।। patatvātpannagāścaiva sarpāścaivāvasarpaṇāt ।। sa tu sarpān sahotpannān āviveśa viṣātmakaḥ ।।
varṇena kapiśenogrās te bhūtāḥ piśitāśanāḥ ।। prasannaṃ gāyatastasya gandharvā jajñire yadā ।। dhayanto jajñire vācaṃ gandharvāstena te smṛtāḥ ।। tataḥ svacchandato anyāni vayāṃsi vayasāsṛjat ।।
paśūnsṛṣṭvā sa deveśo asṛjatpakṣigaṇānapi ।। gāścaivāthodarādbrahmā pārśvābhyāṃ ca vinirmame ।। uṣṭrānaśvatarāṃścaiva tathānyāścaiva jātayaḥ ।। evaṃ paśvoṣadhīḥ sṛṣṭvā yūyujat so adhvare prabhuḥ ।।
etāngrāmyānpaśūnāhur āraṇyānvai nibodhata ।। audakāḥ paśavaḥ ṣaṣṭhāḥ saptamāstu sarīsṛpāḥ ।। siṃhastu saptamasteṣām āraṇyāḥ paśavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। agniṣṭomaṃ ca yajñānāṃ nirmame prathamān mukhāt ।।
bṛhatsāma tathokthyaṃ ca dakṣiṇādasṛjanmukhāt ।। vairūpamatirātraṃ ca paścimādasṛjanmukhāt ।। anuṣṭubhaṃ savairājam uttarādasṛjanmukhāt ।। tejāṃsi ca sasarjādau kalpasya bhagavānprabhuḥ ।।
brahmaṇastu prajāsargaṃ sṛjato hi prajāpateḥ ।। tato asṛjat sa bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca ।। narakinnararakṣāṃsi vayaḥpaśumṛgoragān ।। teṣāṃ vai yāni karmāṇi prāksṛṣṭyāṃ pratipedire ।।
hiṃsrāhiṃsre mṛdukrūre dharmādharme nṛtānṛte ।। mahābhūteṣu sṛṣṭeṣu indriyārtheṣu mūrtiṣu ।। kecitpuruṣakāraṃ tu prāhuḥ karma sumānavāḥ ।। pauruṣaṃ karma daivaṃ ca phalavṛttisvabhāvataḥ ।।
etadevaṃ ca naikaṃ ca nāmabhedena nāpyubhe ।। nāma rūpaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ kṛtānāṃ ca prapañcanam ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ nāmadheyāni yāś ca vedeṣu vṛttayaḥ ।। evaṃvidhāḥ sṛṣṭayastu brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।।
evaṃbhūtāni sṛṣṭāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca ।। tamomātrāvṛto brahmā tadā śokena duḥkhitaḥ ।। athātmani samadrākṣīt tamomātrāṃ niyāmikām ।। tataḥ sa tena duḥkhena duḥkhaṃ cakre jagatpatiḥ ।।
tattamaḥ pratinunnaṃ vai mithunaṃ samajāyata ।। tatastasminsamudbhūte mithune dāruṇātmike ।। svāṃ tanuṃ sa tato brahmā tāmapohata bhāsvarām ।। ardhena nārī sā tasya śatarūpā vyajāyata ।।
sā divaṃ pṛthivīṃ caiva mahimnā vyāpyadhiṣṭhitā ।। yā tvardhātsṛjato nārī śatarūpā vyajāyata ।। bhartāraṃ dīptayaśasaṃ puruṣaṃ pratyapadyata ।। tasyaiva saptatiyugaṃ manvantaramihocyate ।।
tayā sārdhaṃ sa ramate tasmātsā ratirucyate ।। virājam asṛjad brahmā so abhavat puruṣo virāṭ ।। sa vairājaḥ prajāsargaṃ sasarja puruṣo manuḥ ।। priyavratottānapādau putrau dvau lokasaṃmatau ।।
devī nāma tathākūtiḥ prasūtiścaiva te ubhe ।। prāṇo dakṣa iti jñeyaḥ saṃkalpo manurucyate ।। ākūtyāṃ mithunaṃ jajñe mānasasya ruceḥ śubham ।। yajñasya dakṣiṇāyāṃ tu putrā dvādaśa jajñire ।।
etasya putrā yajñasya tasmādyāmāś ca te smṛtāḥ ।। yāmāḥ pūrvaṃ prajātā ye te abhavaṃstu divaukasaḥ ।। tasyāṃ kanyāścaturviṃśad dakṣas tvajanayat prabhuḥ ।। bhogavatyaś ca tāḥ sarvāḥ sarvāstā yogamātaraḥ ।।
śraddhā lakṣmīrdhṛtistuṣṭiḥ puṣṭirmedhā kriyā tathā ।। patnyarthaṃ pratijagrāha dharmo dākṣāyaṇīḥ prabhuḥ ।। tābhyaḥ śiṣṭāyavīyasya ekādaśa sulocanāḥ ।। saṃnatiścānasūyā ca ūrjā svāhā svadhā tathā ।।
rudro bhṛgur marīciś ca aṅgirāḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ ।। satīṃ bhavāya prāyacchat khyātiṃ ca bhṛgave tataḥ ।। prītiṃ caiva pulastyāya kṣamāṃ vai pulahāya ca ।। ūrjāṃ dadau vasiṣṭhāya svāhāmapyagnaye dadau ।।
etāḥ sarvā mahābhāgāḥ prajāsvanusṛtāḥ sthitāḥ ।। śraddhā kāmaṃ vijajñe vai darpo lakṣmīsutaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। puṣṭyā lobhaḥ sutaścāpi medhāputraḥ śrutas tathā ।। buddhyāṃ bodhaḥ sutas tadvat pramādo apyupajāyata ।।
kṣemaḥ śāntisutaścāpi sukhaṃ siddhervyajāyata ।। kāmasya harṣaḥ putro vai devyāṃ prītyāṃ vyajāyata ।। jajñe hiṃsā tvadharmādvai nikṛtiṃ cānṛtaṃ sutam ।। māyā ca vedanā cāpi mithunadvayametayoḥ ।।
vedanāyāḥ sutaścāpi duḥkhaṃ jajñe ca rauravaḥ ।। duḥkhottarāḥ sutā hyete sarve cādharmalakṣaṇāḥ ।। ityeṣa tāmasaḥ sargo jajñe dharmaniyāmakaḥ ।। so abhidhyāya satīṃ bhāryāṃ nirmame hyātmasaṃbhavān ।।
sahasraṃ hi sahasrāṇāṃ so asṛjat kṛttivāsasaḥ ।। piṅgalānsaniṣaṅgāṃś ca sakapardānsalohitān ।। mahārūpānvirūpāṃś ca viśvarūpān svarūpiṇaḥ ।। sahasraśatabāhūṃś ca divyān bhaumāntarikṣagān ।।
annādān piśitāśāṃś ca ājyapānsomapānapi ।। havyādāñchrutadharmāṃś ca dharmiṇo hyatha barhiṇaḥ ।। adhyāpino adhyāyinaś ca japato yuñjatas tathā ।। vṛddhānbuddhimataścaiva brahmiṣṭhāñśubhadarśanān ।।
adṛśyānsarvabhūtānāṃ mahāyogānmahaujasaḥ ।। ayātayāmān asṛjad rudrānetān surottamān ।। sraṣṭavyā nātmanastulyāḥ prajā deva namo astu te ।। nārapsyante hi karmāṇi prajāvagatamṛtyavaḥ ।।
prajāḥ srakṣyāmi bhadraṃ te sthito ahaṃ tvaṃ sṛja prajāḥ ।। sahasrāṇāṃ sahasraṃ tu ātmano niḥsṛtāḥ prajāḥ ।। pṛthivyāmantarikṣe ca dikṣu caiva pariśritāḥ ।। yajñabhājo bhaviṣyanti sarvadevagaṇaiḥ saha ।।
sārdhaṃ tair ījyamānās te sthāsyantīha ā yugakṣayāt ।। pratyuvāca namaskṛtya hṛṣyamāṇaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। brahmaṇā samanujñāte tathā sarvamabhūtkila ।। ūrdhvaretāḥ sthitaḥ sthāṇur yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ।।
eṣa devo mahādevaḥ puruṣo arkasamadyutiḥ ।। svecchayāsau dvidhābhūtaḥ pṛthak strī puruṣaḥ pṛthak ।। tatra yā sā mahābhāgā śaṅkarasyārdhakāyinī ।। hitāya jagatāṃ devī dakṣeṇārādhitā purā ।।
ātmānaṃ vibhajasveti proktā devena śaṃbhunā ।। tasyā nāmāni vakṣyāmi śṛṇvantu ca samāhitāḥ ।। satī dākṣāyaṇī vidyā icchāśaktiḥ kriyātmikā ।। umā haimavatī caiva kalyāṇī caikamātṛkā ।।
gaṇāṃbikā mahādevī nandinī jātavedasī ।। sāvitrī varadā puṇyā pāvanī lokaviśrutā ।। prakṛtirvikṛtā raudrī durgā bhadrā pramāthinī ।। dvāparāntavibhāge ca nāmānīmāni suvratāḥ ।।
kumārī yādavī devī varadā kṛṣṇapiṅgalā ।। mahendropendrabhaginī dṛṣadvaty ekaśūladhṛk ।। śumbhādidaityahantrī ca mahāmahiṣamardinī ।। devyā nāmavikārāṇi ityetāni yathākramam ।।
ye paṭhanti narāsteṣāṃ vidyate na ca pātakam ।। rakṣāmetāṃ prayuñjīta jale vātha sthale api vā ।। āpatsvapi ca sarvāsu devyā nāmāni kīrtayet ।। abhyarditānāṃ bālānāṃ rakṣāmetāṃ prayojayet ।।
ābhyāṃ devīsahasrāṇi yairvyāptamakhilaṃ jagat ।। ātiṣṭhatsarvalokānāṃ hitāya parameśvaraḥ ।। devāś ca paśavaḥ sarve babhūvustasya tejasā ।। sa yāti brahmaṇo lokaṃ śrāvayedvā dvijottamān ।।
kathaṃ paśupatiścāsīt puraṃ dagdhuṃ maheśvaraḥ ।। mayasya tapasā pūrvaṃ sudurgaṃ nirmitaṃ puram ।। sudurgaṃ devadevena dagdhamityeva naḥ śrutam ।। ekeneṣunipātena divyenāpi tadā katham ।।
purasya saṃbhavaḥ sarvo varalābhaḥ purā śrutaḥ ।। teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ ।। trailokyasyāsya śāpāddhi manovākkāyasaṃbhavāt ।। skandena vā prayatnena tasya putrā mahābalāḥ ।।
tapastepurmahātmāno mahābalaparākramāḥ ।। tapasā karśayāmāsur dehān svāndānavottamāḥ ।। avadhyatvaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ sarvabhūteṣu sarvadā ।। tān abravīt tadā devo lokānāṃ prabhur avyayaḥ ।।
anyaṃ varaṃ vṛṇīdhvaṃ vai yādṛśaṃ samprarocate ।। brahmāṇamabruvandaityāḥ praṇipatya jagadgurum ।। vicariṣyāma lokeśa tvatprasādājjagadguro ।। ekībhāvaṃ gamiṣyanti purāṇyetāni cānagha ।।
ekenaiveṣuṇā devaḥ sa no mṛtyurbhaviṣyati ।। tato mayaḥ svatapasā cakre vīraḥ purāṇyatha ।। āyasaṃ cābhavad bhūmau puraṃ teṣāṃ mahātmanām ।। kāñcanaṃ tārakākṣasya kamalākṣasya rājatam ।।
mayaś ca balavāṃstatra daityadānavapūjitaḥ ।। ālayaṃ cātmanaḥ kṛtvā tatrāste balavāṃstadā ।। purāṇi trīṇi viprendrās trailokyamiva cāparam ।। puratrayaṃ praviśyaiva babhūvuste balādhikāḥ ।।
nānāprasādasaṃkīrṇaṃ maṇijālaiḥ samāvṛtam ।। padmarāgamayaiḥ śubhraiḥ śobhitaṃ candrasaṃnibhaiḥ ।। śobhitaṃ tripuraṃ teṣāṃ pṛthakpṛthaganuttamaiḥ ।। rudrālayaiḥ pratigṛhaṃ sāgnihotrair dvijottamāḥ ।।
mattamātaṅgayūthaiś ca turaṅgaiś ca suśobhanaiḥ ।। sabhāprapādibhiś caiva krīḍāsthānaiḥ pṛthak pṛthak ।। adhṛṣyaṃ manasāpyanyair mayasyaiva ca māyayā ।। kṛtvāpi sumahat pāpam apāpaiḥ śaṅkarārcanāt ।।
śrautasmārtārthadharmajñais taddharmanirataiḥ sadā ।। vyūḍhoraskair vṛṣaskandhaiḥ sarvāyudhadharaiḥ sadā ।। praśāntaiḥ kupitaiścaiva kubjair vāmanakais tathā ।। mayena rakṣitaiḥ sarvaiḥ śikṣitairyuddhalālasaiḥ ।।
ravimarudamarendrasaṃnikāśaiḥ suramathanaiḥ sudṛḍhaiḥ susevitaṃ tat ।। puratrayāgninā dagdhā hy abhavan daityavaibhavāt ।। abhivandya tadā prāhus tamapratimavarcasam ।। kiṃ kāryaṃ devakāryeṣu bhagavāniti sa prabhuḥ ।।
yajvā yajñabhugīśāno yajvanāṃ phaladaḥ prabhuḥ ।। devaṃ te puruṣaṃ caiva praṇemustuṣṭuvustadā ।। sanātanastadā sendrān devān ālokya cācyutaḥ ।। puratrayavināśāya jagattrayavibhūtaye ।।
siṃhanādaṃ mahatkṛtvā yajñeśaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ surāḥ ।। punaḥ prāha sa sarvāṃstāṃs tridaśāṃstridaśeśvaraḥ ।। yajedyadi mahādevam apāpo nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। hantavyāḥ sarvayatnena kathaṃ vadhyāḥ surottamāḥ ।।
tasmānna vadhyā rudrasya prabhāvāt parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। munayaś ca mahātmānaḥ prasādena vinā prabhoḥ ।। viśvāmareśvaro vandyo viśvādhāro maheśvaraḥ ।। līlayā devadaityendravibhāgamakaroddharaḥ ।।
brahmā brahmatvam āpanno hy ahaṃ viṣṇutvameva ca ।। tasmāttenaiva hantavyā liṅgārcanavidher balāt ।। rudramiṣṭvā yathānyāyaṃ jeṣyāmo daityasattamān ।। ko nāma hantuṃ tripuraṃ samartho muktvā trinetraṃ bhagavantamekam ।।
upaviṣṭo dadarśātha bhūtasaṃghānsahasraśaḥ ।। nānāpraharaṇopetān nānāveṣadharāṃstadā ।। prāha devo hariḥ sākṣāt praṇipatya sthitān prabhuḥ ।। punaryathāgataṃ vīrā gantumarhatha bhūtaye ।।
praviśya naṣṭāste sarve śalabhā iva pāvakam ।। nanṛtur mumuduś caiva jagur daityāḥ sahasraśaḥ ।। tataḥ parājitā devā dhvastavīryāḥ kṣaṇena tu ।। tāndṛṣṭvā cintayāmāsa bhagavānpuruṣottamaḥ ।।
kathaṃ tu teṣāṃ daityānāṃ balaṃ hatvā prayatnataḥ ।। pāpaṃ vicārato nāsti dharmiṣṭhānāṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।। pāpaṃ nudati dharmeṇa dharme sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।। daityāścaite hi dharmiṣṭhāḥ sarve tripuravāsinaḥ ।।
kṛtvāpi sumahatpāpaṃ rudramabhyarcayanti ye ।। pūjayā bhogasaṃpattir avaśyaṃ jāyate dvijāḥ ।। tasmātkṛtvā dharmavighnam ahaṃ devāḥ svamāyayā ।। kartuṃ vyavasitaścābhūd dharmavighnaṃ surāriṇām ।।
māyī māyāmayaṃ teṣāṃ dharmavighnārthamacyutaḥ ।। sarvasaṃmohanaṃ māyī dṛṣṭapratyayasaṃyutam ।। māyī māyāmayaṃ śāstraṃ granthaṣoḍaśalakṣakam ।। ihaiva svarganarakaṃ pratyayaṃ nānyathā punaḥ ।।
puratrayavināśāya prāhainaṃ puruṣaṃ hariḥ ।। dharmās tathā praṇaśyantu śrautasmārtā na saṃśayaḥ ।। praviśya tatpuraṃ tūrṇaṃ munirmāyāṃ tadākarot ।। śrautaṃ smārtaṃ ca saṃtyajya tasya śiṣyāstadābhavan ।।
nārado api tadā māyī niyogānmāyinaḥ prabhoḥ ।। muniḥ śiṣyaiḥ praśiṣyaiś ca saṃvṛtaḥ sarvataḥ svayam ।। cakrustāḥ sarvadā labdhvā sadya eva phalaṃ striyaḥ ।। adyāpi gauravāttasya nāradasya kalau muneḥ ।।
strīṇāṃ mātā pitā bandhuḥ sakhā mitraṃ ca bāndhavaḥ ।। kṛtvāpi sumahatpāpaṃ yā bhartuḥ premasaṃyutā ।। puraikā muniśārdūlāḥ sarvadharmān sadā patim ।। tāḥ svargalokamāsādya modante vigatajvarāḥ ।।
tathāpi bhartṝn svāṃs tyaktvā babhūvuḥ svairavṛttayaḥ ।। alakṣmīś ca svayaṃ tasya niyogāttripuraṃ gatā ।। bahirgatā parityajya niyogādbrahmaṇaḥ prabhoḥ ।। teṣāṃ dattvā kṣaṇaṃ devas tāsāṃ māyī ca nāradaḥ ।।
evaṃ naṣṭe tadā dharme śrautasmārte suśobhane ।। tyakte maheśvare daityais tyakte liṅgārcane tathā ।। kṛtārtha iva deveśo devaiḥ sārdhamumāpatim ।। maheśvarāya devāya namaste paramātmane ।।
śāśvatāya hyanantāya avyaktāya ca te namaḥ ।। jajāpa rudraṃ bhagavān koṭivāraṃ jale sthitaḥ ।। sendrāḥ sasādhyāḥ sayamāḥ sarudrāḥ samarudgaṇāḥ ।। rudrāya nīlarudrāya kadrudrāya pracetase ।।
tvamādistvamanantaś ca anantaścākṣayaḥ prabhuḥ ।। trātā netā jagatyasmin dvijānāṃ dvijavatsala ।। yājyo muktyarthamīśāno yogibhir yogavibhramaiḥ ।। vadanti sūrayaḥ santaṃ paraṃ brahmasvarūpiṇam ।।
paramātmānamityāhur asmiñjagati tadvibho ।। aṇoralpataraṃ prāhur mahato api mahattaram ।। sarvataḥ śrutimalloke sarvamāvṛtya tiṣṭhasi ।। viśvarūpaṃ virūpākṣaṃ sadāśivam anāmayam ।।
koṭikālāgnisaṃkāśaṃ ṣaḍviṃśakamanīśvaram ।। vadanti varadaṃ devaṃ sarvāvāsaṃ svayaṃbhuvam ।। śrutayaḥ śrutisāraṃ tvāṃ śrutisāravido janāḥ ।। tvameva daityāsurabhūtasaṃghān devān narān sthāvarajaṅgamāṃś ca ।।
māyayā mohitāḥ sarve bhavataḥ parameśvara ।। jalāśrayādeva jaḍīkṛtāś ca surāsurāstadvadajasya sarvam ।। śṛṇuyādvā stavaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvakāmam avāpnuyāt ।। somaḥ somām athāliṅgya nandidattakaraḥ smayan ।।
jñātaṃ mayedamadhunā devakāryaṃ sureśvarāḥ ।। teṣāmadharmaniṣṭhānāṃ daityānāṃ devasattamāḥ ।। atha sabrahmakā devāḥ sendropendrāḥ samāgatāḥ ।। apyetadantare devī devamālokya vismitā ।।
krīḍamānaṃ vibho paśya ṣaṇmukhaṃ ravisannibham ।। mukuṭaiḥ kaṭakaiścaiva kuṇḍalairvalayaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। kiṅkiṇībhir anekābhir haimairaśvatthapatrakaiḥ ।। hārair vārijarāgādimaṇicitrais tathāṅgadaiḥ ।।
tilakaiś ca mahādeva paśya putraṃ suśobhanam ।। vaktravṛndaṃ ca paśyeśa vṛndaṃ kāmalakaṃ yathā ।। añjanāni vicitrāṇi maṅgalārthaṃ ca mātṛbhiḥ ।। ityevaṃ lokamātuś ca vāgbhiḥ saṃbodhitaḥ śivaḥ ।।
na sasmāra ca tāndevān daityaśastranipīḍitān ।। so api līlālaso bālo nanartārtiharaḥ prabhuḥ ।। trailokyamakhilaṃ tatra nanarteśājñayā kṣaṇam ।। tuṣṭuvurgaṇapāḥ skandaṃ mumodāṃbā ca mātaraḥ ।।
avāpatus tadā tṛptiṃ nandinā ca gaṇeśvarāḥ ।। viveśa divyaṃ bhavanaṃ bhavo api yathāmbudo anyāmbudam ambudābhaḥ ।। tuṣṭuvuś ca mahādevaṃ kiṃcid udvignacetasaḥ ।। pāpā vayam iti hyanye abhāgyāśceti cāpare ।।
pūjāphalamimaṃ teṣām ityanye neti cāpare ।। kumbhodaro mahātejā daṇḍenātāḍayatsurān ।। apatanmunayaścānye devāś ca dharaṇītale ।। dṛṣṭvāpi devadeveśaṃ devānāṃ cāsuradviṣām ।।
procurnamaḥ śivāyeti pūjya cālpataraṃ hṛdi ।। śūlī mālī tathā hālī kuṇḍalī valayī gadī ।। tato vai nandinaṃ dṛṣṭvā gaṇaḥ kumbhodaro api saḥ ।। nandī bhāti mahātejā vṛṣapṛṣṭhe vṛṣadhvajaḥ ।।
daśayojanavistīrṇaṃ muktājālair alaṃkṛtam ।। tatrāntarbaddhamālā sā muktāphalamayī śubhā ।। atha dṛṣṭvā gaṇādhyakṣaṃ devadundubhayaḥ śubhāḥ ।। tuṣṭuvuś ca gaṇeśānaṃ vāgbhir iṣṭapradaṃ śubham ।।
niyogādvajriṇo mūrdhni puṣpavarṣaṃ ca khecarāḥ ।। vṛṣṭyā tuṣṭastadā reje tuṣṭyā puṣṭyā yathārthayā ।। puṣpairnānāvidhaistatra bhāti pṛṣṭhaṃ vṛṣasya tat ।। kusumaiḥ saṃvṛto nandī vṛṣapṛṣṭhe rarāja saḥ ।।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā nandinaṃ devāḥ sendropendrās tathāvidham ।। namaste rudrabhaktāya rudrajāpyaratāya ca ।। kūṣmāṇḍagaṇanāthāya yogināṃ pataye namaḥ ।। vedānāṃ pataye caiva vedavedyāya te namaḥ ।।
vajrālaṃkṛtadehāya vajriṇārādhitāya te ।। raktānāṃ bhavapādābje rudralokapradāyine ।। bhūtānāṃ bhuvaneśānāṃ pataye pāpahāriṇe ।। namaḥ śivāya saumyāya rudrabhaktāya te namaḥ ।।
rathaṃ ca sārathiṃ śaṃbhoḥ kārmukaṃ śaramuttamam ।। atha te brahmaṇā sārdhaṃ tathā vai viśvakarmaṇā ।। rathaṃ cakruḥ susaṃrabdhā devadevasya dhīmataḥ ।। sarvalokamayo divyo ratho yatnena sādaram ।।
sarvadevamayaścaiva sauvarṇaḥ sarvasaṃmataḥ ।। dakṣiṇaṃ dvādaśāraṃ hi ṣoḍaśāraṃ tathottaram ।। śaśinaḥ ṣoḍaśāreṣu kalā vāmasya suvratāḥ ।। nemyaḥ ṣaḍṛtavaścaiva tayorvai viprapuṅgavāḥ ।।
astādrirudayādriś ca ubhau tau kūbarau smṛtau ।। vegaḥ saṃvatsarastasya ayane cakrasaṃgamau ।। tasya kāṣṭhāḥ smṛtā ghoṇā cākṣadaṇḍāḥ kṣaṇāś ca vai ।। dyaurvarūthaṃ rathasyāsya svargamokṣāvubhau dhvajau ।।
dakṣiṇāḥ saṃdhayastasya lohāḥ pañcāśadagnayaḥ ।। īṣādaṇḍastathāvyaktaṃ buddhistasyaiva naḍvalaḥ ।। indriyāṇi ca tasyaiva bhūṣaṇāni samantataḥ ।। padāni bhūṣaṇānyeva ṣaḍaṅgānyupabhūṣaṇam ।।
vālāśrayāḥ paṭāścaiva sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutāḥ ।। avacchedo hyanantastu sahasraphaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।। puṣkarādyāḥ patākāś ca sauvarṇā ratnabhūṣitāḥ ।। gaṅgādyāḥ saritaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ।।
tatratatra kṛtasthānāḥ śobhayāṃcakrire ratham ।। sārathirbhagavānbrahmā devābhīṣudharāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। lokālokācalastasya sasopānaḥ samantataḥ ।। nāsāḥ samantatastasya sarva evācalāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
merureva mahāchatraṃ mandaraḥ pārśvaḍiṇḍimaḥ ।। kālarātryā tathaiveha tathendradhanuṣā punaḥ ।। iṣurviṣṇurmahātejāḥ śalyaṃ somaḥ śarasya ca ।। anīkaṃ viṣasambhūtaṃ vāyavo vājakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
sārathiṃ jagatāṃ caiva brahmāṇaṃ prabhumīśvaram ।। sarvadevagaṇairyuktaṃ kampayanniva rodasī ।। upanṛttaścāpsarasāṃ gaṇairnṛtyaviśāradaiḥ ।। tasminnārohati rathaṃ kalpitaṃ lokasaṃbhṛtam ।।
athādhastādrathasyāsya bhagavān dharaṇīdharaḥ ।। kṣaṇāntare vṛṣendro api jānubhyāmagamaddharām ।। sthāpayāmāsa devasya vacanādvai rathaṃ śubham ।। purāṇyuddiśya khasthāni dānavānāṃ tarasvinām ।।
paśūnāmādhipatyaṃ me dattaṃ hanmi tato asurān ।। kalpayitvaiva vadhyāste nānyathā naiva sattamāḥ ।। viṣādamagaman sarve paśutvaṃ prati śaṅkitāḥ ।। mā vo astu paśubhāve asmin bhayaṃ vibudhasattamāḥ ।।
yo vai pāśupataṃ divyaṃ cariṣyati sa mokṣyati ।। ye cāpyanye cariṣyanti vrataṃ pāśupataṃ mama ।। naiṣṭhikaṃ dvādaśābdaṃ vā tadardhaṃ varṣakatrayam ।। tasmātparamidaṃ divyaṃ cariṣyatha surottamāḥ ।।
tasmādvai paśavaḥ sarve devāsuranarāḥ prabhoḥ ।। yaḥ paśustatpaśutvaṃ ca vratenānena saṃtyajet ।। tato vināyakaḥ sākṣād bālo abālaparākramaḥ ।। māmapūjya jagatyasmin bhakṣyabhojyādibhiḥ śubhaiḥ ।।
tatastasmin kṣaṇādeva devakārye sureśvarāḥ ।। tataḥ sendrāḥ surāḥ sarve bhītāḥ sampūjya taṃ prabhum ।। abruvaṃste gaṇeśānaṃ nirvighnaṃ cāstu naḥ sadā ।। bhavo apyanekaiḥ kusumair gaṇeśaṃ bhakṣyaiś ca bhojyaiḥ surasaiḥ sugandhaiḥ ।
āliṅgya cāghrāya sutaṃ tadānīmapūjayatsarvasurendramukhyaḥ ।। gaṇeśvaraireva nagendradhanvā puratrayaṃ dagdhumasau jagāma ।। gaṇeśvarā nandimukhāstadānīṃ svavāhanairanvayurīśamīśāḥ ।। vimānamāruhya puraṃ prahartuṃ jagāma mṛtyuṃ bhagavāniveśaḥ ।।
devāstadānīṃ gaṇapāś ca sarve gaṇā yayuḥ svāyudhacihnahastāḥ ।। khagendramāruhya nagendrakalpaṃ khagadhvajo vāmata eva śaṃbhoḥ । jagāma jagatāṃ hitāya puratrayaṃ dagdhumaluptaśaktiḥ ।। taṃ sarvadevāḥ suralokanāthaṃ samantataścānvayuraprameyam ।
surāsureśaṃ sahasraraśmir bhagavān sutīkṣṇaḥ ।। yathā sumeroḥ śikharādhirūḍhaḥ sahasraraśmir bhagavān sutīkṣṇaḥ ।। jagāma rudrasya puraṃ nihantuṃ yathoragāṃstatra tu vainateyaḥ ।। samantatastuṣṭuvuriṣṭadaṃ te jayeti śakraṃ varapuṣpavṛṣṭyā ।।
tadā hyahalyopapatiṃ sureśaṃ jagatpatiṃ diviṣṭhāḥ । praṇemurālokya sahasranetraṃ salīlamaṃbā tanayaṃ yathendram ।। apāmpatis tatheśāno bhavaṃ cānu samāgatāḥ ।। vṛṣabhendraṃ samāruhya romajaiś ca samāvṛtaḥ ।।
mahākālo mahātejā mahādeva ivāparaḥ ।। vāyavyāṃ sagaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ sevāṃ cakre rathasya tu ।। devanāthagaṇavṛndasaṃvṛto vāraṇena ca tathāgnisaṃbhavaḥ ।। vighneśvaro vighnagaṇaiś ca sārdhaṃ taṃ deśamīśānapadaṃ jagāma ।।
prakampayantī ca tadā surendrān mahāsurāsṛṅmadhupānamattā ।। mattebhacarmāṃbaraveṣṭitāṅgī yayau purastācca gaṇeśvarasya ।। praṇemuruccairabhituṣṭuvuś ca jayeti devīṃ himaśailaputrīm ।। mātaraṃ yayuratha svavāhanaiḥ svairgaṇairdhvajadharaiḥ samantataḥ ।।
prauḍhādityasahasrasadṛśairnetrairdahantī pathaṃ bālābālaparākramā bhagavatī daityānprahartuṃ yayau ।। gajairhayaiḥ siṃhavarai rathaiś ca vṛṣairyayuste gaṇarājamukhyāḥ ।। yayuḥ purastāddhi maheśvarasya sureśvarā bhūtagaṇeśvarāś ca ।। jayeti vāgbhir bhagavantamūcuḥ kirīṭadattāñjalayaḥ samantāt ।।
puratrayaṃ ca viprendrāḥ prāṇadatsarvatas tathā ।। jagāma yogī tripuraṃ nihantuṃ vimānamāruhya yathā mahendraḥ ।। somavallī savarṇaś ca somapaḥ senakas tathā ।। sūryākṣaḥ sūrināmā ca suraḥ sundara eva ca ।।
indraś cendrajayaścaiva mahābhīr bhīmakas tathā ।। yamajihvaḥ śatāśvaś ca kaṇṭhanaḥ kaṇṭhapūjanaḥ ।। muṇḍo ardhamuṇḍo dīrghaś ca piśācāsyaḥ pinākadhṛk ।। śithilaḥ śithilāsyaś ca akṣapādo hyajaḥ kujaḥ ।।
ityādyāḥ parivāryeśaṃ lakṣyalakṣaṇavarjitāḥ ।। sahasrāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi rudrāṇāmūrdhvaretasām ।। dagdhuṃ puratrayaṃ jagmuḥ koṭikoṭigaṇairvṛtāḥ ।। trayaś ca trisahasrāṇi jagmurdevāḥ samantataḥ ।।
bhūtānāṃ mātaraścaiva jagmurdevasya pṛṣṭhataḥ ।। nabhasyamalanakṣatre tārāmadhya ivoḍurāṭ ।। tadā prabhāvato gaurī bhavasyeva jaganmayī ।। cāmarāsaktahastāgrā sā hemāṃbujavarṇikā ।।
sitamivābhramaho saha vidyutā nabhasi devapateḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। hiraṇyadhanuṣā saumyaṃ vapuḥ śaṃbhoḥ śaśidyuti ।। yathodaye śaśāṅkasya bhātyakhaṇḍaṃ hi maṇḍalam ।। chatrāntā ratnajākāśāt patantīva saridvarā ।।
saha tadā ca jagāma tayāṃbayā sakalalokahitāya puratrayam ।। kimatra dagdhuṃ tripuraṃ pinākī svayaṃ gataścātra gaṇaiś ca sārdham ।। puratrayaṃ dagdhumaluptaśakteḥ kimetad ityāhur ajendramukhyāḥ ।। vyavasthitaśceti tathānyathā ced āḍambareṇāsya phalaṃ kimanyat ।।
gaṇairgaṇeśastu rarāja devyā jagadratho merurivāṣṭaśṛṅgaiḥ ।। tripuraraṅgatalopari saṃsthitaḥ suragaṇo anujagāma svayaṃ tathā ।। nareśvaraiścaiva gaṇaiś ca devaiḥ suretaraiś ca trividhairmunīndrāḥ ।। yuktvā pāśupatāstreṇa tripuraṃ samacintayat ।।
purāṇi tena kālena jagmurekatvamāśu vai ।। babhūva tumulo harṣo devatānāṃ mahātmanām ।। jayeti vāco mumucuḥ saṃstuvanto aṣṭamūrtikam ।। puṣyayoge api samprāpte līlāvaśamumāpatim ।।
pūrvadevāś ca devāś ca samāstava yataḥ prabho ।। yatastasmājjagannātha līlāṃ tyaktumihārhasi ।। iṣuṇā bhūtasaṃghaiś ca viṣṇunā ca mayā prabho ।। yāvanna yānti deveśa viyogaṃ tāvadeva tu ।।
atha devo mahādevaḥ sarvajñastadavaikṣata ।। somaś ca bhagavānviṣṇuḥ kālāgnirvāyureva ca ।। dagdhamapyatha deveśa vīkṣaṇena puratrayam ।। atha saṃmṛjya dhanuṣo jyāṃ hasan tripurārdanaḥ ।।
tatkṣaṇāttripuraṃ dagdhvā tripurāntakaraḥ śaraḥ ।। reje puratrayaṃ dagdhaṃ daityakoṭiśatairvṛtam ।। ye pūjayanti tatrāpi daityā rudraṃ sabāndhavāḥ ।। na kiṃcid abruvan devāḥ sendropendrā gaṇeśvarāḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvā bhītaṃ tadānīkaṃ devānāṃ devapuṅgavaḥ ।। kiṃ cetyāha tadā devān praṇemustaṃ samantataḥ ।। vavandire cādrisutāsutaṃ prabhuṃ vavandire devagaṇā maheśvaram ।। viṣṇunā ca bhavaṃ devaṃ tripurārātimīśvaram ।।
prasīda jagatāṃ nātha prasīdānandadāvyaya ।। ātmatrayopaviṣṭāya vidyātattvāya te namaḥ ।। aghorāṣṭakatattvāya dvādaśātmasvarūpiṇe ।। rūpamāsthāya loke asmin saṃsthitāya śivātmane ।।
dhavalaśyāmaraktānāṃ muktidāyāmarāya ca ।। trilokāya tridevāya vaṣaṭkārāya vai namaḥ ।। aṣṭakṣetrāṣṭarūpāya aṣṭatattvāya te namaḥ ।। pañcadhā pañcadhā caiva pañcamantraśarīriṇe ।।
dvātriṃśattattvarūpāya ukārāya namonamaḥ ।। aṣṭadhātmasvarūpāya ardhamātrātmane namaḥ ।। gaganeśāya devāya svargeśāya namo namaḥ ।। aṣṭakṣetrāṣṭarūpāya parātparatarāya ca ।।
sahasrapādayuktāya śarvāya parameṣṭhine ।। punaraṣṭaprakāśāya tathāṣṭāṣṭakamūrtaye ।। guṇāṣṭakavṛtāyaiva guṇine nirguṇāya te ।। nābhimaṇḍalasaṃsthāya hṛdi niḥsvanakāriṇe ।।
bhrūmadhye saṃsthitāyaiva nādamadhye sthitāya ca ।। vahnisomārkarūpāya ṣaṭtriṃśacchaktirūpiṇe ।। triprakāraṃ sthitāyaiva tretāgnimayarūpiṇe ।। sarvajñāya śaraṇyāya sadyojātāya vai namaḥ ।।
tatpuruṣāya namo astu īśānāya namonamaḥ ।। ananteśāya sūkṣmāya uttamāya namo astu te ।। namastrimūrtaye tubhyaṃ śrīkaṇṭhāya śikhaṇḍine ।। vimalāya viśālāya vimalāṅgāya te namaḥ ।।
yogapīṭhāntarasthāya yogine yogadāyine ।। pratyāhārāya te nityaṃ pratyāhāraratāya te ।। dhāraṇāyai namastubhyaṃ dhāraṇābhiratāya te ।। dhyānāya dhyānarūpāya dhyānagamyāya te namaḥ ।।
dhyeyānāmapi dhyeyāya namo dhyeyatamāya te ।। samādhānaratānāṃ tu nirvikalpārtharūpiṇe ।। kaḥ stotumicchet kathamīdṛśaṃ tvāṃ stoṣye hi tuṣṭāya śivāya tubhyam ।। ete gaṇāḥ siddhagaṇaiḥ praṇāmaṃ kurvanti deveśa gaṇeśa tubhyam ।।
līlālasenāṃbikayā kṣaṇena dagdhaṃ kileṣuś ca tadātha muktaḥ ।। anekayatnaiś ca mayātha tubhyaṃ phalaṃ na dṛṣṭaṃ surasiddhasaṃghaiḥ ।। tvameva sarve bhagavan kathaṃ tu stoṣye hy atoṣyaṃ praṇipatya mūrdhnā ।। anantamūrtiḥ katham īdṛśaṃ tvāṃ toṣye hy atoṣyaṃ kathamīdṛśaṃ tvām ।।
sthūlāya sūkṣmāya susūkṣmasūkṣmasūkṣmāya sūkṣmārthavide vidhātre ।। netre surāṇāmasureśvarāṇāṃ dātre praśāstre mama sarvaśāstre ।। vedātmarūpāya bhavāya tubhyam antāya madhyāya sumadhyamāya ।। aliṅgine liṅgamayāya tubhyaṃ liṅgāya vedādimayāya sākṣāt ।।
vidhvāntabhaṅgaṃ mama kartumīśa dṛṣṭvaiva bhūmau karajāgrakoṭyā ।। dehīva devaiḥ saha devakāryaṃ kariṣyase nirguṇarūpatattva ।। ekaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ vāṅmayaṃ caikamīśaṃ dhyeyaṃ caikaṃ tattvamatrādbhutaṃ te ।। mūrtirno vai daivakīśāna devair lakṣyā yatnairapyalakṣyaṃ kathaṃ tu ।।
tathāpi bhaktyā vilapantamīśa pitāmahaṃ māṃ bhagavankṣamasva ।। sa ca muñcati pāpabandhanaṃ bhavabhaktyā puraśāsituḥ stavam ।। stavaṃ tadā prāha mahānubhāvaṃ mahābhujo mandaraśṛṅgavāsī ।। varān varaya bhadraṃ te devānāṃ ca yathepsitān ।।
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā prāhedaṃ prītamānasaḥ ।। tvayi bhaktiṃ parāṃ me adya prasīda parameśvaram ।। prasīda bhaktiyogena sārathyena ca sarvadā ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā prāha sāṃbaṃ triyaṃbakam ।।
tvayi bhaktiṃ ca deveśa devadeva namo astu te ।। sarvajñatvaṃ ca varada sarvagatvaṃ ca śaṅkara ।। sārathye vāhanatve ca kalpayāmāsa vai bhavaḥ ।। sārdhaṃ devyā nandinā bhūtasaṃghair antardhānaṃ kārayāmāsa śarvaḥ ।।
sureśvarāḥ suvismitā bhavaṃ praṇamya pārvatīm ।। sureśvarā munīśvarā gaṇeśvarāś ca bhāskarāḥ ।। yaḥ paṭhecchrāddhakāle vā daive karmaṇi ca dvijāḥ ।। mānasairvācikaiḥ pāpais tathā vai kāyikaiḥ punaḥ ।।
pātakaiś ca dvijaśreṣṭhā upapātakasaṃbhavaiḥ ।। śatravo nāśamāyānti saṃgrāme vijayībhavet ।। dhanamāyuryaśo vidyāṃ prabhāvamatulaṃ labhet ।। sadasyāha surendrāṇāṃ bhagavānpadmasaṃbhavaḥ ।।
tārapautro mahātejās tārakasya suto balī ।। vidyunmālī ca daityeśaḥ anye cāpi sabāndhavāḥ ।। sarve vinaṣṭāḥ pradhvastāḥ svapuraiḥ purasaṃbhavaiḥ ।। yāvatpūjā sureśānāṃ tāvadeva sthitiryataḥ ।।
sarvaliṅgamayo lokaḥ sarvaṃ liṅge pratiṣṭhitam ।। sarve liṅgārcanādeva devā daityāś ca dānavāḥ ।। pitaro munayaścāpi piśācāḥ kinnarādayaḥ ।। tasmālliṅgaṃ yajennityaṃ yena kenāpi vā surāḥ ।।
paśutvaṃ ca parityajya kṛtvā pāśupataṃ tataḥ ।। viśodhya caiva bhūtāni pañcabhiḥ praṇavaiḥ samam ।। caturbhiḥ praṇavaiścaiva prāṇāyāmaparāyaṇaiḥ ।। dvidhā nyasya tathauṃkāraṃ prāṇāyāmaparāyaṇaḥ ।।
jñānāmṛtena sarvāṅgāny āpūrya praṇavena ca ।। tanmātrāṇi ca bhūtāni tathā buddhīndriyāṇi ca ।। cidātmānaṃ tanuṃ kṛtvā cāgnirbhasmeti saṃspṛśet ।। triyāyuṣaṃ trisaṃdhyaṃ ca dhūlayed bhasitena yaḥ ।।
bhavena pāśamokṣārthaṃ kathitaṃ devasattamāḥ ।। liṅge purā mayā dṛṣṭe viṣṇunā ca mahātmanā ।। asmābhiḥ sarvakāryāṇāṃ devamabhyarcya yatnataḥ ।। pratijñā mama viṣṇoś ca divyaiṣā surasattamāḥ ।।
sā hānistanmahacchidraṃ sa mohaḥ sā ca mūkatā ।। bhavabhaktiparā ye ca bhavapraṇatacetasaḥ ।। bhavanāni manojñāni divyamābharaṇaṃ striyaḥ ।। te arcayantu sadā kālaṃ liṅgamūrtiṃ maheśvaram ।।
hatvā bhittvā ca bhūtāni dagdhvā sarvamidaṃ jagat ।। śailaṃ liṅgaṃ madīyaṃ hi sarvadevanamaskṛtam ।। tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhir devadevaṃ triyaṃbakam ।। sākṣātpāśupataṃ kṛtvā bhasmoddhūlitavigrahāḥ ।।
viśvakarmā dadau teṣāṃ niyogādbrahmaṇaḥ prabhoḥ ।। padmarāgamayaṃ śakro haimaṃ viśravasaḥ sutaḥ ।। ārakūṭamayaṃ vāyur aśvinau pārthivaṃ sadā ।। mauktikaṃ somarāḍ dhīmāṃs tathā liṅgamanuttamam ।।
daityā hyayomayaṃ liṅgaṃ rākṣasāś ca mahātmanaḥ ।। cāmuṇḍā saikataṃ sākṣān mātaraś ca dvijottamāḥ ।। nīlādyāś ca tathā rudrāḥ śuddhaṃ bhasmamayaṃ śubham ।। munayo muniśārdūlāḥ kuśāgramayam uttamam ।।
sarasvatī ca ratnena kṛtaṃ rudrasya vāgbhavā ।। ugrā piṣṭamayaṃ sarve mantrā hyājyamayaṃ śubham ।। lebhire ca yathāyogyaṃ prasādādbrahmaṇaḥ padam ।। śivaliṅgaṃ samabhyarcya sthitamatra na saṃśayaḥ ।।
teṣāṃ bhedāścaturyuktacatvāriṃśaditi smṛtāḥ ।। dvitīyaṃ ratnajaṃ tacca saptadhā munisattamāḥ ।। turīyaṃ dārujaṃ liṅgaṃ tattu ṣoḍaśadhocyate ।। ṣaṣṭhaṃ tu kṣaṇikaṃ liṅgaṃ saptadhā parikīrtitam ।।
dhātujaṃ dhanadaṃ sākṣād dārujaṃ bhogasiddhidam ।। śailajaṃ cottamaṃ proktaṃ madhyamaṃ caiva dhātujam ।। mūle brahmā tathā madhye viṣṇustribhuvaneśvaraḥ ।। liṅgavedī mahādevī triguṇā trimayāṃbikā ।।
śailajaṃ ratnajaṃ vāpi dhātujaṃ vāpi dārujam ।। surendrāmbhojagarbhāgniyamāmbupadhaneśvaraiḥ ।। stūyamānaḥ supuṇyātmā devadundubhiniḥsvanaiḥ ।। tapaḥ satyaṃ parākramya bhāsayan svena tejasā ।।
āśu brahmāṇḍamudbhidya nirgacchannirviśaṅkayā ।। mṛnmayaṃ kṣaṇikaṃ tyaktvā sthāpayetsakalaṃ vapuḥ ।। kundagokṣīrasaṃkāśaṃ liṅgaṃ yaḥ sthāpayennaraḥ ।। darśanātsparśanāttasya labhante nirvṛtiṃ narāḥ ।।
śakyate naiva viprendrās tasmād vai sthāpayet tathā ।। sakalaṃ bhāvanāyogyaṃ yogināmeva niṣkalam ।। vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ yathā pūrvaṃ yathā śrutam ।। vijñānamiti viprendrāḥ śrutvā śrutiśirasyajam ।।
tajjñānaṃ bhrāntirahitam ityanye neti cāpare ।। guruprakāśakaṃ jñānam ityanye munayo dvijāḥ ।। ubhābhyāṃ mucyate yogī tatrānandamayo bhavet ।। kalpanākalpitaṃ rūpaṃ saṃhṛtya svecchayaiva hi ।।
somasūryāgnayo netre diśaḥ śrotraṃ mahātmanaḥ ।। devāstasya bhujāḥ sarve nakṣatrāṇi ca bhūṣaṇam ।। vaktrādvai brāhmaṇāḥ sarve brahmā ca bhagavānprabhuḥ ।। vaiśyāścorupradeśāttu śūdrāḥ pādātpinākinaḥ ।।
vāyavo ghrāṇajāstasya gatiḥ śrautaṃ smṛtis tathā ।। puṃsāṃ tu puruṣaḥ śrīmān jñānagamyo na cānyathā ।। tapoyajñasahasrebhyo japayajño viśiṣyate ।। dhyānayajñātparo nāsti dhyānaṃ jñānasya sādhanam ।।
dhyānayajñaratasyāsya tadā saṃnihitaḥ śivaḥ ।। viśuddhā vidyayā sarve brahmavidyāvido janāḥ ।। dharmādharmau japo homo dhyānināṃ saṃnidhiḥ sadā ।। niṣkalaṃ sarvagaṃ jñeyaṃ yogināṃ hṛdi saṃsthitam ।।
bāhyaṃ sthūlaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ sūkṣmamābhyantaraṃ dvijāḥ ।। asatāṃ bhāvanārthāya nānyathā sthūlavigrahaḥ ।। asau mūḍho bahiḥ sarvaṃ kalpayitvaiva nānyathā ।। yathā sthūlamayuktānāṃ mṛtkāṣṭhādyaiḥ prakalpitam ।।
niṣkalaḥ sakalaśceti sarvaṃ śivamayaṃ tataḥ ।। pṛthaktvaṃ cāpṛthaktvaṃ ca śaṅkarasyeti cāpare ।। eko api bahudhā dṛṣṭo jalādhāreṣu suvratāḥ ।। tathāpi bahulā dṛṣṭā jātivyaktivibhedataḥ ।।
bhedo janānāṃ loke asmin pratibhāso vicārataḥ ।। duḥkhī ca bhogaṃ duḥkhaṃ ca nānubhūtaṃ vicārataḥ ।। hṛdi saṃsāriṇāṃ sākṣāt sakalaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। trividhaṃ parameśasya vapurloke praśasyate ।।
tṛtīyaṃ sakalaṃ caiva nānyatheti dvijottamāḥ ।। sarvajñaṃ hṛdaye kecic chivaliṅge vibhāvasau ।। evamabhyarcayantyeva sadārāḥ sasutā narāḥ ।। tasmādabhedabuddhyaiva saptaviṃśatprabhedataḥ ।।
daśāre dvādaśāre ca ṣoḍaśāre trirasrake ।। saṃtāraṇārthaṃ ca śivaḥ sadasadvyaktivarjitaḥ ।। ūcus tathā taṃ ca śivaṃ tathānye saṃsāriṇaṃ vedavido vadanti ।। yajanti yogeśam aśeṣamūrtiṃ ṣaḍasramadhye bhagavantameva ।।
te yānti cainaṃ na ca yogino anye tayā ca devyā puruṣaṃ purāṇam ।। pratiṣṭhāyāḥ phalaṃ sarvaṃ sarvalokahitāya vai ।। kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya sarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt ।। yatphalaṃ labhate martyas tadvadāmi yathāśrutam ।।
rudrakanyāsamākīrṇair geyanāṭyasamanvitaiḥ ।। tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān vimānaiḥ sārvakāmikaiḥ ।। prājāpatyaṃ mahātejā janalokaṃ mahas tathā ।। bhuktvā caiva bhuvarloke bhogān divyān suśobhanān ।।
ekapādaṃ caturbāhuṃ trinetraṃ śūlasaṃyutam ।। aṣṭāviṃśatirudrāṇāṃ koṭiḥ sarvāṅgasuprabham ।। prakṛtiṃ vāmataścaiva buddhiṃ vai buddhideśataḥ ।। indriyāṇīndriyādeva līlayā parameśvaram ।।
nābhideśāt tathā vahniṃ hṛdayādbhāskaraṃ tathā ।। sṛṣṭaivaṃ saṃsthitaṃ sākṣāj jagatsarvaṃ carācaram ।। pratiṣṭhāpya yathānyāyaṃ śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt ।। kṛtvā yajñeśamīśānaṃ viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।।
kramādāgatya loke asmin sarvayajñāntago bhavet ।। hayamedhāyutaṃ kṛtvā yatpuṇyaṃ tad avāpya saḥ ।। gatvā śivapuraṃ divyaṃ tatraiva sa vimucyate ।। kṛtvā yatphalamāpnoti vakṣye tadvai yathāśrutam ।।
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇair devadānavadurlabhaiḥ ।। gatvā śivapuraṃ divyaṃ gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt ।। sahasrabāhuṃ sarvajñaṃ caturbāhum athāpi vā ।। śailajāsahitaṃ sākṣād vṛṣabhadhvajamīśvaram ।।
mātṛbhir munibhiścaiva saṃvṛtaṃ parameśvaram ।। sarvayajñatapodānatīrthadeveṣu yat phalam ।। tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam ।। nagnaṃ caturbhujaṃ śvetaṃ trinetraṃ sarpamekhalam ।।
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt ।। sudhūmravarṇaṃ raktākṣaṃ trinetraṃ candrabhūṣaṇam ।। siṃhājinottarīyaṃ ca mṛgacarmāṃbaraṃ prabhum ।। huṃphaṭkāre mahāśabdaśabditākhiladiṅmukham ।।
hasantaṃ ca nadantaṃ ca pibantaṃ kṛṣṇasāgaram ।। kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvibhavavistaram ।। tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ।। ardhanārīśvaraṃ devaṃ caturbhujamanuttamam ।।
strīpuṃbhāvena saṃsthānaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam ।। tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān aṇimādiguṇairyutaḥ ।। yaḥ kuryāddevadeveśaṃ sarvajñaṃ lakulīśvaram ।। kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śivalokaṃ sa gacchati ।।
jñānayogaṃ samāsādya tatraiva ca vimucyate ।। kṛtamudrasya devasya citābhasmānulepinaḥ ।। brahmaṇaḥ keśakenaikam upavītaṃ ca bibhrataḥ ।। viṣṇoḥ kalevaraṃ caiva bibhrataḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।।
oṃnamo nīlakaṇṭhāya iti puṇyākṣarāṣṭakam ।। mantreṇānena gandhādyair bhaktyā vittānusārataḥ ।। jālandharāntakaṃ devaṃ sudarśanadharaṃ prabhum ।। prayāti śivasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।।
arcamānena devena cārcitaṃ netrapūjayā ।। tiṣṭhato atha nikumbhasya pṛṣṭhataścaraṇāṃbujam ।। śūlāgre kūrparaṃ sthāpya kiṅkiṇīkṛtapannagam ।। rūpaṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt ।।
dhanurbāṇasamāyuktaṃ somaṃ somārdhabhūṣaṇam ।। tadākāratayā so api gatvā śivapuraṃ sukhī ।। tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān yāvad icchā dvijottamāḥ ।। jñānaṃ vicāritaṃ labdhvā tatraiva sa vimucyate ।।
gaṅgādharaṃ sukhāsīnaṃ candraśekharameva ca ।। vināyakaṃ tathā skandaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ durgāṃ suśobhanām ।। kaumārīṃ vaiṣṇavīṃ devīṃ vārāhīṃ varadāṃ tathā ।। vighneśena ca yo dhīmān śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt ।।
liṅgasya madhye vai kṛtvā candraśekharamīśvaram ।। viṣṇuṃ varāharūpeṇa liṅgasyādhastvadhomukham ।। madhye liṅgaṃ mahāghoraṃ mahāmbhasi ca saṃsthitam ।। kṣetrasaṃrakṣakaṃ devaṃ tathā pāśupataṃ prabhum ।।
kṛtvā bhaktyā yathānyāyaṃ śivaloke mahīyate ।। liṅgānāṃ caiva bhedāś ca śrutaṃ tava mukhādiha ।। yatphalaṃ labhate martyas tatphalaṃ vaktumarhasi ।। bādhyate jñānayuktaścen na ca tasya gṛhaistu kim ।।
prayānti divyaṃ hi vimānavaryaṃ surendrapadmodbhavavanditasya ।। bālyāttu loṣṭena ca kṛtvā mṛdāpi vā pāṃsubhir ādidevam । gṛhaṃ ca tādṛgvidhamasya śaṃbhoḥ sampūjya rudratvamavāpnuvanti ।। kartavyaṃ sarvayatnena dharmakāmārthasiddhaye ।।
kṛtvā rudrālayaṃ bhaktyā śivaloke mahīyate ।। kailāsaśikharākārair vimānair modate sukhī ।। bhaktyā vittānusāreṇa uttamādhamamadhyamam ।। apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇair devadānavadurlabhaiḥ ।।
jñānayogaṃ samāsādya gāṇapatyaṃ labhennaraḥ ।। sa yatphalamavāpnoti na tat sarvair mahāmakhaiḥ ।। tatphalaṃ sakalaṃ labdhvā śivavanmodate ciram ।। śivalokamanuprāpya śivavanmodate ciram ।।
himaśailopamair yānair gatvā śivapuraṃ śubham ।। nīlādriśikharākhyaṃ vā prāsādaṃ yaḥ suśobhanam ।। yatphalaṃ labhate martyas tatphalaṃ pravadāmyaham ।। tatphalaṃ sakalaṃ labdhvā sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ ।।
mahendraśailanāmānaṃ prāsādaṃ rudrasaṃmatam ।। mahendraparvatākārair vimānairvṛṣasaṃyutaiḥ ।। jñānaṃ vicāritaṃ rudraiḥ samprāpya munipuṅgavāḥ ।। hemnā yastu prakurvīta prāsādaṃ ratnaśobhitam ।।
kūṭaṃ vā maṇḍapaṃ vāpi samaṃ vā dīrgham eva ca ।। jīrṇaṃ vā patitaṃ vāpi khaṇḍitaṃ sphuṭitaṃ tathā ।। prāsādaṃ maṇḍapaṃ vāpi prākāraṃ gopuraṃ tu vā ।। vṛttyarthaṃ vā prakurvīta naraḥ karma śivālaye ।।
yaścātmabhogasiddhyartham api rudrālaye sakṛt ।। tasmād āyatanaṃ bhaktyā yaḥ kuryān munisattamāḥ ।। prasādārthaṃ maheśasya prāsāde munipuṅgavāḥ ।। aśaktaścenmuniśreṣṭhāḥ prāsādaṃ kartumuttamam ।।
saṃmārjanaṃ tu yaḥ kuryān mārjanyā mṛdusūkṣmayā ।। yaḥ kuryādvastrapūtena gandhagomayavāriṇā ।। ardhakrośaṃ śivakṣetraṃ śivaliṅgātsamantataḥ ।। svāyaṃbhuvasya mānaṃ hi tathā bāṇasya suvratāḥ ।।
mānuṣe ca tadardhaṃ syāt kṣetramānaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। rudrāvatāre cādyaṃ yac chiṣye caiva praśiṣyake ।। śrīparvate mahāpuṇye tasya prānte ca vā dvijāḥ ।। vārāṇasyāṃ tathāpyevam avimukte viśeṣataḥ ।।
kurukṣetre ca yaḥ prāṇān saṃtyajedyāti nirvṛtim ।। vaṇīśailākule caiva mṛto yāti śivātmatām ।। triviṣṭape vimukte ca kedāre saṃgameśvare ।। śukreśvare vā gokarṇe bhāskareśe guheśvare ।।
niyamaiḥ śoṣya yo dehaṃ tyajetkṣetre śivasya tu ।। ārṣe vāpi muniśreṣṭhās tathā svāyaṃbhuve api vā ।। ādhāyāgniṃ śivakṣetre sampūjya parameśvaram ।। yāvattāvannirāhāro bhūtvā prāṇān parityajet ।।
chittvā pādadvayaṃ cāpi śivakṣetre vasettu yaḥ ।। kṣetrasya darśanaṃ puṇyaṃ praveśastacchatādhikaḥ ।। tasmācchataguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ jalasnānamataḥ param ।। dadhnā sahasramākhyātaṃ madhunā tacchatādhikam ।।
śivakṣetrasamīpasthāṃ nadīṃ prāpyāvagāhya ca ।। śivakṣetrasamīpasthā nadyaḥ sarvāḥ suśobhanāḥ ।। snātvā teṣu naro bhaktyā tīrtheṣu dvijasattamāḥ ।। prātaḥ snātvā muniśreṣṭhāḥ śivatīrtheṣu mānavaḥ ।।
madhyāhne śivatīrtheṣu snātvā bhaktyā sakṛnnaraḥ ।। astaṃ gate tathā cārke snātvā gacchecchivaṃ padam ।। dvijās triṣavaṇaṃ snātvā śivatīrthe sakṛnnaraḥ ।। purātha sūkaraḥ kaścit śvānaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhayātpathi ।।
mṛtaḥ svayaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhā gāṇapatyamavāptavān ।। paśyetsa yāti sarvasmād adhikāṃ gatimeva ca ।। sāyāhne sarvayajñānāṃ phalaṃ prāpya vimucyate ।। tathopapātakaiścaiva pāpaiścaivānupātakaiḥ ।।
māsena yatkṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tyaktvā yāti śivaṃ padam ।। viṣuve caiva sampūjya prayāti paramāṃ gatim ।। savyāpasavyanyāyena mṛdugatyā śucirnaraḥ ।। vācā yastu śivaṃ nityaṃ saṃrauti parameśvaram ।।
kṛtvā maṇḍalakaṃ kṣetraṃ gandhagomayavāriṇā ।। padmarāgamayaiścaiva sphāṭikaiś ca suśobhanaiḥ ।। tadvarṇair laukikaiścaiva cūrṇairvittavivarjitaiḥ ।। sakarṇikaṃ mahābhāgā mahādevasamīpataḥ ।।
pañcabhiśca tathā ṣaḍbhir aṣṭābhiśceṣṭadaṃ param ।। punarbāhye ca daśabhiḥ sampūjya praṇipatya ca ।। śālipiṣṭādibhir vāpi padmamālikhya nirdhanaḥ ।। dvādaśāraṃ tathālikhya maṇḍalaṃ padam uttamam ।।
maṇḍalasya ca madhye tu bhāskaraṃ sthāpya pūjayet ।। evaṃ prākṛtam apyārthyāṃ ṣaḍasraṃ parikalpya ca ।। dakṣiṇe sattvamūrtiṃ ca vāmataś ca rajoguṇam ।। pañcabhūtāni tanmātrāpañcakaṃ caiva dakṣiṇe ।।
uttare vidhivatpūjya ṣaḍasre caiva pūjayet ।। ahaṅkāraṃ ca mahatā sarvayajñaphalaṃ labhet ।। ato vakṣyāmi viprendrāḥ sarvakāmārthasādhanam ।। caturaśraṃ vidhānena cādbhir abhyukṣya mantravit ।।
budbudairardhacandraiś ca haimairaśvatthapatrakaiḥ ।। muktādāmair vitānānte lambitastu sitairdhvajaiḥ ।। phalapallavamālābhir vaijayantībhir aṃśukaiḥ ।। pañcāśaddalasaṃyuktam ālikhetpadmamuttamam ।।
ekahastapramāṇena kṛtvā padmaṃ vidhānataḥ ।। varṇāni ca nyasetpatre rudraiḥ prāgādyanukramāt ।। sampūjyaivaṃ muniśreṣṭhā gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ kramāt ।। akṣamālopavītaṃ ca kuṇḍalaṃ ca kamaṇḍalum ।।
dattvā teṣāṃ munīndrāṇāṃ devadevāya śaṃbhave ।। ante ca devadevāya dāpayeccūrṇamaṇḍalam ।। oṅkārādyaṃ japeddhīmān prativarṇam anukramāt ।। yatphalaṃ labhate martyas tadvadāmi samāsataḥ ।।
iṣṭvā yajñairyathānyāyaṃ jyotiṣṭomādibhiḥ kramāt ।। vānaprasthāśramaṃ gatvā sadāraḥ sāgnireva ca ।। brahmavidyāmadhītyaiva jñānamāsādya yatnataḥ ।। tatphalaṃ labhate sarvaṃ varṇamaṇḍaladarśanāt ।।
uttare dakṣiṇe vāpi pṛṣṭhato vā dvijottamāḥ ।। puṣpākṣatādibhiḥ pūjya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। candanādyaiḥ sakarpūrair gandhadravyaiḥ samantataḥ ।। prārthayeddevamīśānaṃ śivalokaṃ sa gacchati ।।
svadehagandhakusumaiḥ pūrayañchivamandiram ।। kramādāgatya loke asmin rājā bhavati vīryavān ।। śivabrahmāmṛtaṃ grāhyaṃ mokṣasādhanam uttamam ।। vyaktāvyaktaṃ sadā nityam acintyam arcayet prabhum ।।
śivakṣetre muniśreṣṭhā nānyathā siddhiriṣyate ।। aphenā muniśārdūlā nādeyāś ca viśeṣataḥ ।। adbhiḥ kāryāṇi pūtābhiḥ sarvakāryaprasiddhaye ।। yatpāpaṃ sakalaṃ cādbhir apūtābhiściraṃ labhet ।।
agnau kaṇḍanake caiva peṣaṇe toyasaṃgrahe ।। ahiṃseyaṃ paro dharmaḥ sarveṣāṃ prāṇināṃ dvijāḥ ।। taddānamabhayaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvadānottamottamam ।। manasā karmaṇā vācā sarvadāhiṃsakaṃ naram ।।
trailokyamakhilaṃ dattvā yatphalaṃ vedapārage ।। manasā karmaṇā vācā sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ ।। svāmivatparirakṣanti bahūni vividhāni ca ।। tasmātsarvaprayatnena vastrapūtena vāriṇā ।।
trailokyamakhilaṃ hatvā yatphalaṃ parikīrtyate ।। śivārthaṃ sarvadā kāryā puṣpahiṃsā dvijottamāḥ ।। vihitāvihitaṃ nāsti yogināṃ brahmavādinām ।। sarvakarmāṇi vinyasya saṃnyastā brahmavādinaḥ ।।
pavitrāstu striyaḥ sarvā atreś ca kulasaṃbhavāḥ ।। striyaḥ sarvā na hantavyāḥ pāpakarmaratā api ।। sarvavarṇeṣu viprendrāḥ pāpakarmaratā api ।। na hantavyāḥ sadā martyaiḥ śivavacchaṅkayā tathā ।।
pāṣaṇḍina iti khyātā na saṃbhāṣyā dvijātibhiḥ ।। tathāpi tena vadhyāś ca nṛpairanyaiś ca jantubhiḥ ।। rudralokamavāpnoti samabhyarcya maheśvaram ।। bhaktihīnā narāḥ sarve bhave paramakāraṇe ।।
bhāgyavanto vimucyante bhuktvā bhogānihaiva te ।। sakṛtprasaṃgādyatitāpasānāṃ teṣāṃ na dūraḥ parameśalokaḥ ।। kalpāyuṣair alpavīryair alpasattvaiḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। na paśyanti surāścāpi kathaṃ devaṃ yajanti te ।।
tathāpi śraddhayā dṛśyaḥ pūjyaḥ saṃbhāṣya eva ca ।। bhāvānurūpaphalado bhagavāniti kīrtitaḥ ।। saṃkruddho rākṣasaṃ sthānaṃ prāpnuyān mūḍhadhīr dvijāḥ ।। gānaśīlaś ca gāndharvaṃ nṛtyaśīlastathaiva ca ।।
madārtaḥ pūjayan rudraṃ somasthānamavāpnuyāt ।। brāhmaṃ hi praṇavenaiva vaiṣṇavaṃ cābhinandya ca ।। rudralokamanuprāpya rudraiḥ sārdhaṃ pramodate ।। jalaiḥ pūtaistathā pīṭhe devamāvāhya bhaktitaḥ ।।
kalpite cāsane sthāpya dharmajñānamaye śubhe ।। oṅkārapadmamadhye tu somasūryāgnisaṃbhave ।। snāpayeddivyatoyaiś ca ghṛtena payasā tathā ।। tataḥ śuddhāṃbunā snāpya candanādyaiś ca pūjayet ।।
bilvapatrairakhaṇḍaiś ca padmairnānāvidhais tathā ।। campakair jātipuṣpaiśca bakulaiḥ karavīrakaiḥ ।। apāmārgakadambaiś ca bhūṣaṇairapi śobhanaiḥ ।। dadhibhaktaṃ ca madhvājyapariplutamataḥ param ।।
atha pañcavidhaṃ vāpi saghṛtaṃ vinivedayet ।। kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ cānte namaskṛtya muhurmuhuḥ ।। īśānaṃ puruṣaṃ caiva aghoraṃ vāmameva ca ।। anena vidhinā devaḥ prasīdati maheśvaraḥ ।।
gāvaścaiva dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ prayānti paramāṃ gatim ।। sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ punarāvṛttivarjitam ।। sakṛtprasaṃgādvā dṛṣṭvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। dṛṣṭvā prayāti vai martyo brahmalokaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।।
yo dadyād ghṛtadīpaṃ ca sakṛlliṅgasya cāgrataḥ ।। dīpavṛkṣaṃ pārthivaṃ vā dāravaṃ vā śivālaye ।। āyasaṃ tāmrajaṃ vāpi raupyaṃ sauvarṇikaṃ tathā ।। sūryāyutasamaiḥ ślakṣṇair yānaiḥ śivapuraṃ vrajet ।।
sampūjyamānaṃ vā paśyed vidhinā parameśvaram ।। āvāhanaṃ susānnidhyaṃ sthāpanaṃ pūjanaṃ tathā ।। pañcabhiḥ snapanaṃ proktaṃ rudrādyaiś ca viśeṣataḥ ।। brahmāṇaṃ dakṣiṇe tasya praṇavena samarcayet ।।
vahnau hutvā yathānyāyaṃ pañcabhiḥ praṇavena ca ।। iti saṃkṣepataḥ prokto liṅgārcanavidhikramaḥ ।। vyāsena kathitaḥ pūrvaṃ śrutvā rudramukhātsvayam ।। paśutvaṃ tatyajurdevās tanno vaktumihārhasi ।।
sametya devāḥ sarvajñam ājagmustatprasādataḥ ।। garuḍasya tathā skandham āruhya puruṣottamaḥ ।। sarve samprāpya devasya sārdhaṃ girivaraṃ śubham ।। avatīrya giriṃ merum āruroha surottamaiḥ ।।
madhuraraṇitagītaṃ sānukūlāndhakāraṃ padaracitavanāntaṃ kāntavātāntatoyam ।। dhavakhadirapalāśaiś candanādyaiś ca vṛkṣair dvijavaragaṇavṛndaiḥ kokilādyairdvirephaiḥ ।। bahukadambatamālalatāvṛtaṃ girivaraṃ śikharairvividhais tathā ।। krīḍārthaṃ devadevasya bhavasya parameṣṭhinaḥ ।।
praṇemurdūrataścaiva prabhāvādeva śūlinaḥ ।। jagāma kailāsagiriṃ mahātmā meruprabhāge puramādidevaḥ ।। gaṇairgaṇeśaiś ca girīndrasaṃnibhaṃ mahāpuradvāramajo hariś ca ।। vimānairvividhākāraiḥ prākāraiś ca samāvṛtam ।।
prahṛṣṭavadano bhūtvā praviveśa tataḥ puram ।। dvitīyaṃ devadevasya caturdvāraṃ suśobhanam ।। dolāvikṣepasaṃyuktaṃ ghaṇṭācāmarabhūṣitam ।। devendrabhavanākārair bhavanair dṛṣṭimohanaiḥ ।।
sthitāḥ karaistasya hareḥ samantāt pracikṣipurmūrdhni yathā bhavasya ।। dṛṣṭvā nāryastadā viṣṇuṃ madāghūrṇitalocanāḥ ।। kāściddṛṣṭvā hariṃ nāryaḥ kiṃcit prahasitānanāḥ ।। caturthaṃ pañcamaṃ caiva ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca saptamaṃ tathā ।।
atītyāsādya devasya puraṃ śaṃbhoḥ suśobhanam ।। sūryamaṇḍalasaṃkāśair vimānaiś ca vibhūṣitam ।। nānāratnamayaiścaiva digvidikṣu vibhūṣitam ।। anekaiḥ sarvatobhadraiḥ sarvaratnamayais tathā ।।
upadvārairmahādvārair vidikṣu vividhairdṛḍhaiḥ ।। grāmyair anyair mahābhāgā mauktikair dṛṣṭimohanaiḥ ।। candanairvividhākāraiḥ puṣpodyānaiś ca śobhanaiḥ ।। strīṇāṃ gatijitair haṃsaiḥ sevitābhiḥ samantataḥ ।।
śobhitābhiś ca vāpībhir divyāmṛtajalais tathā ।। stanabhārāvanamraiś ca madāghūrṇitalocanaiḥ ।। nṛtyadbhir apsaraḥsaṃghair amarairapi durlabhaiḥ ।। rudrastrīgaṇasaṃkīrṇair jalakrīḍāratais tathā ।।
grāmarāgānuraktaiś ca padmarāgasamaprabhaiḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā vismayamāpannās tasthurdevāḥ samantataḥ ।। gaṇeśvarāṇāṃ vīrāṇām api vṛndaṃ sahasraśaḥ ।। sphāṭikān devadevasya dadṛśuste vimānakān ।।
viśālajaghanā yakṣā gandharvāpsarasas tathā ।। nānāveṣadharāścānyā nānābhūṣaṇabhūṣitāḥ ।। nīlotpaladalaprakhyāḥ padmapatrāyatekṣaṇāḥ ।। valayairnūpurairhāraiś chatraiścitraistathāṃśukaiḥ ।।
jagmurgaṇeśasya puraṃ sureśāḥ puradviṣaḥ śakrapurogamāś ca ।। bhavasya bālārkasahasravarṇaṃ vimānamādyaṃ parameśvarasya ।। nandinaṃ dadṛśuḥ sarve devāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ ।। jayeti devāstaṃ dṛṣṭvā so apyāha ca gaṇeśvaraḥ ।।
samprāptāḥ sarvalokeśā vaktumarhatha suvratāḥ ।। paśupāśavimokṣārthaṃ darśayāsmān maheśvaram ।। śaṅkitāś ca vayaṃ tatra paśutvaṃ prati suvrata ।। vratenānena bhūteśa paśutvaṃ naiva vidyate ।।
dinadvādaśakaṃ vāpi kṛtvā tad vratam uttamam ।। darśayāmāsa tāndevān nārāyaṇapurogamān ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā devamīśānaṃ sāṃbaṃ sagaṇam avyayam ।। vijñāpya śitikaṇṭhāya paśupāśavimokṣaṇam ।।
tataḥ samprekṣya tān sarvān devadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ ।। vrataṃ pāśupataṃ caiva svayaṃ devo maheśvaraḥ ।। tadāprabhṛti te devāḥ sarve pāśupatāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। tasmātpāśupatāḥ proktās tapastepuś ca te punaḥ ।।
yayuryathāgataṃ sarve brahmaṇā saha viṣṇunā ।। purā sanatkumāreṇa tasmādvyāsena dhīmatā ।। sa dehabhedamāsādya paśupāśaiḥ pramucyate ।। vrataṃ pāśupataṃ laiṅgaṃ purā devair anuṣṭhitam ।।
purā sanatkumāreṇa pṛṣṭaḥ śailādirādarāt ।। devairdaityais tathā siddhair gandharvaiḥ siddhacāraṇaiḥ ।। vrataṃ dvādaśaliṅgākhyaṃ paśupāśavimokṣaṇam ।। aviyogakaraṃ puṇyaṃ bhaktānāṃ bhayanāśanam ।।
sarvadānottamaṃ puṇyam aśvamedhāyutādhikam ।। saṃsārārṇavamagnānāṃ jantūnāmapi mokṣadam ।। devairanuṣṭhitaṃ pūrvaṃ brahmaṇā viṣṇunā tathā ।। caitramāsādi viprendrāḥ śivaliṅgavrataṃ caret ।।
navaratnaiś ca khacitam aṣṭapatraṃ yathāvidhi ।। tatra bhaktyā yathānyāyam arcayed bilvapatrakaiḥ ।। śvetārkakarṇikāraiś ca karavīrairbakairapi ।। sampūjya caiva gandhādyair dhūpairdīpaiś ca maṅgalaiḥ ।।
agaruṃ dakṣiṇe dadyād aghoreṇa dvijottamāḥ ।। uttare vāmadevena candanaṃ vāpi dāpayet ।। sitāgarūdbhavaṃ viprās tathā kṛṣṇāgarūdbhavam ।। sitāraṃ nāma dhūpaṃ ca dadyād īśāya bhaktitaḥ ।।
etad vaḥ kathitaṃ puṇyaṃ śivaliṅgamahāvratam ।। vaiśākhe vajraliṅgaṃ ca jyeṣṭhe mārakataṃ tathā ।। māsi bhādrapade liṅgaṃ padmarāgamayaṃ śubham ।। pravālenaiva kārtikyāṃ tathā vai mārgaśīrṣake ।।
māghe ca sūryakāntena phālgune sphāṭikena ca ।। alābhe rājataṃ vāpi kevalaṃ kamalaṃ tu vā ।। rajatasyāpyalābhe tu tāmralohena kārayet ।। sarvagandhamayaṃ vāpi kṣaṇikaṃ parikalpayet ।।
sarvamāseṣu kamalaṃ haimamekamathāpi vā ।। rājatasyāpyabhāve tu bilvapatraiḥ samarcayet ।। tadardhārdhena vā rudram aṣṭottaraśatena vā ।। nīlotpale aṃbikā sākṣād utpale ṣaṇmukhaḥ svayam ।।
tasmātsarvaprayatnena śrīpattraṃ na tyajedbudhaḥ ।। sarvavaśyakaraṃ padmaṃ śilā sarvārthasiddhidā ।। gugguluprabhṛtīnāṃ caiva dīpānāṃ ca nivedanam ।। saugandhikaṃ tathā dhūpaṃ sarvakāmārthasādhakam ।।
saumyaṃ sītāridhūpaṃ ca sākṣānnirvāṇasiddhidam ।। karṇikārasya kusume medhā sākṣādvyavasthitā ।। sugandhiṣu ca sarveṣu kusumeṣu nagātmajā ।। pūjayeddevadeveśaṃ bhaktyā vittānusārataḥ ।।
saghṛtaṃ sopadaṃśaṃ ca sarvadravyasamanvitam ।। cāmaraṃ tālavṛntaṃ ca tasmai bhaktyā nivedayet ।। nānāvidhāni cārhāṇi prokṣitānyaṃbhasā punaḥ ।। kṣīrādvai sarvadevānāṃ sthityarthamamṛtaṃ dhruvam ।।
bhūtānām annadānena prītir bhavati śaṅkare ।। upahāre tathā tuṣṭir vyañjane pavanaḥ svayam ।। pīṭhe vai prakṛtiḥ sākṣān mahadādyairvyavasthitā ।। paurṇamāsyāṃ vrataṃ kāryaṃ sarvakāmārthasiddhaye ।।
paurṇamāsyāmamāvāsyām upavāsaṃ ca kārayet ।। bhojayedbrāhmaṇānbhaktyā śrotriyān vedapāragān ।। sthāpayed vā śivakṣetre dāpayed brāhmaṇāya vā ।। kuryādbhaktyā muniśreṣṭhāḥ sa eva tapatāṃ varaḥ ।।
gatvā śivapuraṃ divyaṃ nehāyāti kadācana ।। śivalokamavāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। varṣamekaṃ caredevaṃ tāṃstānprāpya śivaṃ vrajet ।। gāṇapatyapadaṃ vāpi sakto api labhate naraḥ ।।
dravyārthī ca nidhiṃ paśyed āyuḥkāmaś cirāyuṣam ।। ekamāsavratādeva so ante rudratvamāpnuyāt ।। hitāya devāsurasiddhamartyavidyādharāṇāṃ paramaṃ śivena ।। vyapohanaṃ nāma japetstavaṃ ca pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtya śivaṃ prayatnāt ।।
pitāmahenaiva suraiśca sārdhaṃ mahānubhāvena mahārghyam etat ।। nandinaś ca mukhācchrutvā kumāreṇa mahātmanā ।। namaḥ śivāya śuddhāya nirmalāya yaśasvine ।। pañcavaktro daśabhujo hy akṣapañcadaśairyutaḥ ।।
sarvajñaḥ sarvagaḥ śāntaḥ sarvopari susaṃsthitaḥ ।। īśānaḥ puruṣaścaiva aghoraḥ sadya eva ca ।। anantaḥ sarvavidyeśaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvadaḥ prabhuḥ ।। sūkṣmaḥ surāsureśāno viśveśo gaṇapūjitaḥ ।।
śivottamo mahāpūjyaḥ śivadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ ।। ekākṣo bhagavānīśaḥ śivārcanaparāyaṇaḥ ।। trimūrtir bhagavān īśaḥ śivabhaktiprabodhakaḥ ।। śrīkaṇṭhaḥ śrīpatiḥ śrīmāñ śivadhyānarataḥ sadā ।।
trailokyanamitā devī solkākārā purātanī ।। trailokyanamitā devī solkākārā purātanī ।। ekaparṇāgrajā saumyā tathā vai caikapāṭalā ।। umā suraharā sākṣāt kauśikī vā kapardinī ।।
naigameyādibhir divyaiś caturbhiḥ putrakairvṛtā ।। aṃbāyā vītaśokasya nandinaś ca mahātmanaḥ ।। sṛṣṭyarthaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ prakṛtitvaṃ gatāvyayā ।। lakṣmyādiśaktibhir nityaṃ namitā nandanandinī ।।
māyayā yā jagatsarvaṃ brahmādyaṃ sacarācaram ।। ekānekasthitā loke indīvaranibhekṣaṇā ।। gaṇendrāmbhojagarbhendrayamavitteśapūrvakaiḥ ।। bhaktānāmārtihā bhavyā bhavabhāvavināśanī ।।
sā me sākṣānmahādevī pāpam āśu vyapohatu ।। śivārcanarataḥ śrīmān sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।। jāmātā marutāṃ devaḥ sarvabhūtamaheśvaraḥ ।। sanārāyaṇakair devaiḥ sendracandradivākaraiḥ ।।
uragairṛṣibhiścaiva brahmaṇā ca mahātmanā ।। sarvadā pūjitaḥ sarvair nandī pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।। śivārcanarataḥ śrīmān sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।। airāvatādibhir divyair diggajaiś ca supūjitaḥ ।।
saptārṇavāṅkuśaścaiva sarvatīrthodaraḥ śivaḥ ।। hatāsuramahāvṛkṣo brahmavidyāmahotkaṭaḥ ।। baddho hṛtpuṇḍarīkākhye staṃbhe vṛttiṃ nirudhya ca ।। śivadhyānaikasampannaḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।।
śivārcanarataḥ śrīmān sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।। skandaḥ śaktidharaḥ śāntaḥ senānīḥ śikhivāhanaḥ ।। bhavaḥ śarvastatheśāno rudraḥ paśupatis tathā ।। etāḥ pāpaṃ vyapohantu mūrtayaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।।
īśāno vijayo bhīmo devadevo bhavodbhavaḥ ।। śivapraṇāmasampannā vyapohantu malaṃ mama ।। lokaprakāśakaścaiva lokasākṣītrivikramaḥ ।। ete vai dvādaśādityā vyapohantu malaṃ mama ।।
candraḥ sūryastathātmā ca tanavaḥ śivabhāṣitāḥ ।। vāsavaḥ pāvakaścaiva yamo nirṛtireva ca ।। pitāmahaś ca bhagavān śivadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ ।। nabhasvānsparśano vāyur anilo mārutas tathā ।।
śivārcanaratāḥ sarve vyapohantu malaṃ mama ।। suṣeṇaḥ śāśvataḥ pṛṣṭaḥ supuṣṭaś ca mahābalaḥ ।। vyapohantu malaṃ sarvaṃ pāpaṃ caiva mayā kṛtam ।। siddhavatparamaḥ siddhaḥ sarvasiddhipradāyinaḥ ।।
yakṣo yakṣeśadhanado jṛmbhako maṇibhadrakaḥ ।। narendraścaiva yakṣeśā vyapohantu malaṃ mama ।। karkoṭako mahāpadmaḥ śaṅkhapālo mahābalaḥ ।। mama pāpaṃ vyapohantu viṣaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam ।।
atīśayaḥ sa prayogī gītajñaścaiva kinnarāḥ ।। vidyādharaś ca vibudho vidyārāśirvidāṃ varaḥ ।। ete vidyādharāḥ sarve śivadhyānaparāyaṇāḥ ।। vāmadevī mahājambhaḥ kālanemirmahābalaḥ ।।
prahrādaścāpyanuhrādaḥ saṃhrādaḥ kila bāṣkalau ।। ete asurā mahātmāno mahādevaparāyaṇāḥ ।। garutmān khagatiścaiva pakṣirāṭ nāgamardanaḥ ।। nāgāśīrviṣanāśaś ca viṣṇuvāhana eva ca ।।
nānābharaṇasampannā vyapohantu malaṃ mama ।। kāśyapo nāradaścaiva dadhīcaścyavanas tathā ।। śivārcanaratāḥ sarve vyapohantu malaṃ mama ।। agniṣvāttā barhiṣadas tathā mātāmahādayaḥ ।।
lakṣmīś ca dharaṇī caiva gāyatrī ca sarasvatī ।। devānāṃ mātaraś caiva gaṇānāṃ mātaras tathā ।। prasādāddevadevasya vyapohantu malaṃ mama ।। sumukhī durmukhī caiva kāmukī kāmavardhanī ।।
śivāya tāṇḍavaṃ nityaṃ kurvantyo atīva bhāvitāḥ ।। arkaḥ somo aṅgārakaś ca budhaścaiva bṛhaspatiḥ ।। vyapohantu bhayaṃ ghoraṃ grahapīḍāṃ śivārcakāḥ ।। siṃhaś ca kanyā vipulā tulā vai vṛścikas tathā ।।
rāśayo dvādaśa hyete śivapūjāparāyaṇāḥ ।। aśvinī bharaṇī caiva kṛttikā rohiṇī tathā ।। maghā vai pūrvaphālgunya uttarāphālgunī tathā ।। jyeṣṭhā mūlaṃ mahābhāgā pūrvāṣāḍhā tathaiva ca ।।
śatabhiṣak pūrvabhadrā tathā proṣṭhapadā tathā ।। jvaraḥ kumbhodaraścaiva śaṅkukarṇo mahābalaḥ ।। śyenajicchivadūtaś ca pramathāḥ prītivardhanāḥ ।। vyapohantu bhayaṃ pāpaṃ mahādevaprasādataḥ ।।
kundendusadṛśākāraḥ kuṃbhakundendubhūṣaṇaḥ ।। catuṣpādasamāyuktaḥ kṣīroda iva pāṇḍuraḥ ।। vṛṣendro viśvadhṛg devo viśvasya jagataḥ pitā ।। śivārcanarato nityaṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।।
śivabhaktā tu yā nandā sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।। mātā gavāṃ mahābhāgā sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।। rudrapūjāratā nityaṃ sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।। śivaloke sthitā nityaṃ sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।।
samastaguṇasampannaḥ sarvadeveśvarātmajaḥ ।। āryaḥ senāpatiḥ sākṣād gahano makhamardanaḥ ।। kṛṣṇāṅgo raktanayanaḥ śaśipannagabhūṣaṇaḥ ।। śivārcanarataḥ sākṣāt sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।।
vārāhī caiva māhendrī cāmuṇḍāgneyikā tathā ।। yoginībhir mahāpāpaṃ vyapohantu samāhitāḥ ।। rudrasya tanayo raudraḥ śūlāsaktamahākaraḥ ।। tretāgninayano devas trailokyābhayadaḥ prabhuḥ ।।
trailokyanamitaḥ śrīmān śivapādārcane rataḥ ।। vahnerhastaharaḥ sākṣād bhaganetranipātanaḥ ।। upendrendrayamādīnāṃ devānāmaṅgarakṣakaḥ ।। gaṇeśvaro yaḥ senānīḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।।
mahālakṣmīrjaganmātā sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।। śivārcanaratā nityaṃ sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।। sarvadā sarvagā devī sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।। viṣṇornidrā mahāmāyā vaiṣṇavī surapūjitā ।।
śivārcanaratā durgā sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।। satyāś ca mānasāḥ sarve vyapohantu bhayaṃ mama ।। kūṣmāṇḍakāś ca te pāpaṃ vyapohantu samāhitāḥ ।। praṇamya śirasā bhūmau pratimāse dvijottamāḥ ।।
vidhūya sarvapāpāni rudraloke mahīyate ।। arthakāmo labhedarthaṃ putrakāmo bahūn sutān ।। yānyānprārthayate kāmān mānavaḥ śravaṇādiha ।। paṭhyamānamidaṃ puṇyaṃ yamuddiśya tu paṭhyate ।।
nākāle maraṇaṃ tasya na sarpairapi daśyate ।। dānānāṃ caiva yatpuṇyaṃ vratānāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।। goghnaścaiva kṛtaghnaś ca vīrahā brahmahā bhavet ।। duṣṭaḥ pāpasamācāro mātṛhā pitṛhā tathā ।।
vyapohya sarvapāpāni śivaloke mahīyate ।। prasaṃgālliṅgadānasya vratānyapi vadasva naḥ ।। nandinā kathitānīha brahmaputrāya dhīmate ।। aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ pakṣayorubhayorapi ।।
sarvayajñaphalaṃ prāpya sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। ahorātreṇa caikena trirātraphalamaśnute ।। kṣīradhārāvrataṃ kuryāt so aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ।। bhuñjanbhogānavāpnoti brahmalokaṃ ca gacchati ।।
brahmacārī jitakrodhaḥ śivadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ ।। sa yāti śāṅkaraṃ lokaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। ayācitāt paraṃ naktaṃ tasmān naktena vartayet ।। aparāhṇe ca pitṛbhiḥ saṃdhyāyāṃ guhyakādibhiḥ ।।
haviṣyabhojanaṃ snānaṃ satyamāhāralāghavam ।। pratimāsaṃ pravakṣyāmi śivavratamanuttamam ।। puṣyamāse ca sampūjya yaḥ kuryānnaktabhojanam ।। pakṣayoraṣṭamīṃ yatnād upavāsena vartayet ।।
snāpya rudraṃ mahādevaṃ sampūjya vidhipūrvakam ।। bhojayed brāhmaṇāñśiṣṭāñ japecchāntiṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। bhavāya devadevāya śivāya parameṣṭhine ।। bhuktvā sa vipulān lokān tatraiva sa vimucyate ।।
kṛśaraṃ ghṛtasaṃyuktaṃ bhuñjānaḥ saṃyatendriyaḥ ।। rudrāya paurṇamāsyāṃ tu dadyādvai ghṛtakambalam ।। bhojayedbrāhmaṇāṃścaiva yathāvibhavavistaram ।। phālgune caiva samprāpte kuryādvai naktabhojanam ।।
caturdaśyāmathāṣṭamyām upavāsaṃ ca kārayet ।। dadyādgomithunaṃ vāpi tāmrābhaṃ śūlapāṇaye ।। sa yāti candrasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। śālyannaṃ payasā yuktaṃ ghṛtena ca yathāsukham ।।
paurṇamāsyāṃ śivaṃ snāpya dadyādgomithunaṃ sitam ।। vaiśākhe ca tathā māse kṛtvā vai naktabhojanam ।। śvetaṃ gomithunaṃ dattvā so aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ।। sampūjya śraddhayā bhaktyā kṛtvā vai naktabhojanam ।।
vīrāsano niśārdhaṃ ca gavāṃ śuśrūṣaṇe rataḥ ।। snāpya śaktyā yathānyāyaṃ caruṃ dadyāc ca śūline ।। dhūmraṃ gomithunaṃ dattvā vāyuloke mahīyate ।। bhūrikhaṇḍājyasaṃmiśraṃ saktubhiścaiva gorasam ।।
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca śrotriyān vedapāragān ।। śrāvaṇe ca dvijā māse kṛtvā vai naktabhojanam ।। paurṇamāsyāṃ ghṛtādyaistu snāpya pūjya yathāvidhi ।। śvetāgrapādaṃ pauṇḍraṃ ca dadyādgomithunaṃ punaḥ ।।
prāpte bhādrapade māse kṛtvaivaṃ naktabhojanam ।। paurṇamāsyāṃ tu deveśaṃ snāpya sampūjya śaṅkaram ।। brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca vedavedāṅgapāragān ।। tataścāśvayuje māsi kṛtvaivaṃ naktabhojanam ।।
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca śivabhaktān sadā śucīn ।। gāṃ ca dattvā yathānyāyam aiśānaṃ lokamāpnuyāt ।। kṣīraudanena sājyena sampūjya ca bhavaṃ prabhum ।। brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca yathāvibhavavistaram ।।
sūryasāyujyamāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। yavānnena yathānyāyam ājyakṣīrādibhiḥ samam ।। brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca daridrānvedapāragān ।। somalokamanuprāpya somena saha modate ।।
triḥsnānaṃ cāgnihotraṃ ca bhūśayyā naktabhojanam ।। pakṣayorupavāsaṃ ca caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu ca ।। ityetadakhilaṃ proktaṃ pratimāsaṃ śivavratam ।। sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ jñānayogamavāpnuyāt ।।
naranāryādijantūnāṃ hitāya munisattamāḥ ।। naktamabdaṃ prakurvīta haviṣyaṃ pūjayedbhavam ।। rājatīṃ vātha varṣānte pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi ।। rathādyairvāpi deveśaṃ nītvā rudrālayaṃ prati ।।
nivedayedvrataṃ caiva śivāya parameṣṭhine ।। aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ niyatā brahmacāriṇī ।। varṣānte pratimāṃ kṛtvā pūrvoktavidhinā tataḥ ।। brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca bhavānyā saha modate ।।
varṣānte pratimāṃ kṛtvā yena kenāpi vā dvijāḥ ।। amāvāsyāṃ nirāhārā bhavedabdaṃ suyantritā ।। snāpyeśānaṃ yajedbhaktyā sahasraiḥ kamalaiḥ sitaiḥ ।। dattvā bhavāya viprebhyaḥ pradadyād dakṣiṇām api ।।
tatsarvaṃ śūladānena bhindyānnārī na saṃśayaḥ ।। kuryādyadvā naraḥ so api rudrasāyujyamāpnuyāt ।। upavāsaratā nārī naro api dvijasattamāḥ ।। japaṃ dānaṃ tapaḥ sarvam asvatantrā yataḥ striyaḥ ।।
sā bhavānyāś ca sāyujyaṃ sārūpyaṃ cāpi suvratā ।। kārtikyāṃ vā tu yā nārī ekabhaktena vartate ।। dadyātkṛṣṇatilānāṃ ca bhāramekam atandritā ।। dattvā ca brāhmaṇebhyaś ca yathā vibhavavistaram ।।
bhavānyā modate sārdhaṃ sārūpyaṃ prāpya suvratā ।। sarvavrateṣvayaṃ dharmaḥ sāmānyo rudrapūjanam ।। mārgaśīrṣakamāsādikārttikāntaṃ yathākramam ।। mārgaśīrṣakamāse atha vṛṣaṃ pūrṇāṅgamuttamam ।।
