sā ca sārdhaṃ bhavānyā vai modate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। pūrvoktamakhilaṃ kṛtvā bhavānyā saha modate ।। dadyāt sampūjya deveśaṃ brāhmaṇāṃścaiva bhojayet ।। phālgune pratimāṃ kṛtvā hiraṇyena yathāvidhi ।।
pratiṣṭhāpya samabhyarcya sthāpayecchaṅkarālaye ।। caitre bhavaṃ kumāraṃ ca bhavānīṃ ca yathāvidhi ।। bhavānyā modate sārdhaṃ dattvā rudrāya śaṃbhave ।। īśvaromāsamāyuktaṃ gaṇeśaiś ca samantataḥ ।।
sthāpayetparameśasya bhavasyāyatane śubhe ।। kailāsaparvataṃ prāpya bhavānyā saha modate ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭenaiva brahmaṇā viṣṇunā tathā ।। haṃsena ca varāheṇa kṛtvā tāmrādibhiḥ śubhām ।।
śivāya śivamāsādya śivasthāne yathāvidhi ।। āṣāḍhe ca śubhe māse gṛhaṃ kṛtvā suśobhanam ।। sarvabījarasaiścāpi sampūrṇaṃ sarvaśobhanaiḥ ।। dāsīdāsādibhiścaiva śayanairaśanādibhiḥ ।।
devaṃ ghṛtādibhiḥ snāpya mahādevamumāpatim ।। vidyāvinayasampannaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragam ।। kanyāṃ sumadhyamāṃ yāvat kālajīvanasaṃyutām ।। sāyanair vividhair divyair meruparvatasannibhaiḥ ।।
bhavānyā sadṛśībhūtvā sarvakalpeṣu sāvyayā ।। sarvadhātusamākīrṇaṃ vicitradhvajaśobhitam ।। vitānadhvajavastrādyair dhātubhiś ca nivedayet ।। kṛtvā bhādrapade māsi śobhanaṃ śāliparvatam ।।
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca dāpayecca yathāvidhi ।। kṛtvā cāśvayuje māsi vipulaṃ dhānyaparvatam ।। brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca pūrvoktamakhilaṃ bhavet ।। sarvadhātusamāyuktaṃ sarvaratnopaśobhitam ।।
gandhamālyais tathā dhūpaiś citraiścāpi suśobhitam ।। brahmaghoṣairmahāpuṇyaṃ maṅgalaiś ca viśeṣataḥ ।। nagendraṃ merunāmānaṃ trailokyādhāramuttamam ।। dakṣiṇe ca yathānyāyaṃ brahmāṇaṃ ca caturmukham ।।
indrādilokapālāṃś ca kṛtvā bhaktyā yathāvidhi ।। devasya dakṣiṇe haste śūlaṃ tridaśapūjitam ।। viṣṇoś ca śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ ca gadāmabjaṃ prayatnataḥ ।। indrasya vajram agneś ca śaktyākhyaṃ paramāyudham ।।
varuṇasya mahāpāśaṃ nāgākhyaṃ rudramadbhutam ।। ṭaṅkaṃ ceśānadevasya nivedyaivaṃ krameṇa ca ।। pūjayetsarvadevāṃś ca yathāvibhavavistaram ।। mahāmeruvrataṃ kṛtvā mahādevāya dāpayet ।।
ciraṃ sāyujyam āpnoti mahādevyā na saṃśayaḥ ।। sarvābharaṇasampūrṇāṃ sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitām ।। devaṃ ca kṛtvā deveśaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam ।। nārāyaṇaṃ ca dātāraṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam ।।
rudrālaye vrataṃ tasmai dāpayedbhaktipūrvakam ।। ekabhaktavrataṃ puṇyaṃ pratimāsamanukramāt ।। naranāryādijantūnāṃ hitāya munisattamāḥ ।। nārī devyā na saṃdehaḥ śivena paribhāṣitam ।।
japetpañcākṣarīṃ vidyāṃ vidhinaiva dvijottamāḥ ।। samāptirnānyathā tasmāj japetpañcākṣarīṃ śubhām ।। kramopāyaṃ mahābhāga śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। pārvatyāḥ kathitaṃ puṇyaṃ pravadāmi samāsataḥ ।।
pañcākṣarasya māhātmyaṃ śrotumicchāmi tattvataḥ ।। na śakyaṃ kathituṃ devi tasmāt saṃkṣepataḥ śṛṇu ।। naṣṭe devāsure caiva naṣṭe coragarākṣase ।। eko ahaṃ saṃsthito devi na dvitīyo asti kutracit ।।
te nāśaṃ naiva samprāptā macchaktyā hyanupālitāḥ ।। sa tu nārāyaṇaḥ śete devo māyāmayīṃ tanum ।। tannābhipaṅkajājjātaḥ pañcavaktraḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। daśa brahmā sasarjādau mānasānamitaujasaḥ ।।
matputrāṇāṃ mahādeva śaktiṃ dehi maheśvara ।। pañcākṣarānpañcamukhaiḥ proktavān padmayonaye ।। vācyavācakabhāvena jñātavānparameśvaram ।। vācakaḥ paramo mantras tasya pañcākṣaraḥ sthitaḥ ।।
provāca putreṣu jagaddhitāya mantraṃ mahārthaṃ kila pañcavarṇam ।। tamārādhayituṃ devaṃ parātparataraṃ śivam ।। dattavānakhilaṃ jñānam aṇimādiguṇāṣṭakam ।। merostu śikhare ramye muñjavānnāma parvataḥ ।।
tasyābhyāśe tapastīvraṃ lokasṛṣṭisamutsukāḥ ।। tiṣṭhanto anugrahārthāya devi te ṛṣayaḥ purā ।। pañcākṣaram ṛṣicchando daivataṃ śaktibījavat ।। proktavānahamāryāṇāṃ lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।।
mantrasya viniyogaṃ ca kṛtvā sarvamanuṣṭhitāḥ ।। varṇānvarṇavibhāgāṃś ca sarvadharmāṃś ca śobhanān ।। pañcākṣaraprabhāvācca lokā vedā maharṣayaḥ ।। tad idānīṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu cāvahitākhilam ।।
ājñāsiddhamasaṃdigdhaṃ vākyametacchivātmakam ।। suniścitārthaṃ gaṃbhīraṃ vākyaṃ me pārameśvaram ।। tadbījaṃ sarvavidyānāṃ mantramādyaṃ suśobhanam ।। vedaḥ sa triguṇātītaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvakṛtprabhuḥ ।।
mantre ṣaḍakṣare sūkṣme pañcākṣaratanuḥ śivaḥ ।। vācyaḥ śivaḥ prameyatvān mantrastadvācakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। vede śivāgame vāpi yatra yatra ṣaḍakṣaraḥ ।। kiṃ tasya bahubhir mantraiḥ śāstrairvā bahuvistṛtaiḥ ।।
tenādhītaṃ śrutaṃ tena tena sarvamanuṣṭhitam ।। etāvaddhi śivajñānam etāvatparamaṃ padam ।। pañcākṣaraiḥ sapraṇavo mantro ayaṃ hṛdayaṃ mama ।। asya mantrasya vakṣyāmi ṛṣicchando adhidaivatam ।।
vāmadevo nāma ṛṣiḥ paṅktiśchanda udāhṛtaḥ ।। nakārādīni bījāni pañcabhūtātmakāni ca ।। śaktistvameva deveśi sarvadevanamaskṛte ।। tvadīyaṃ devi mantrāṇāṃ śaktibhūtaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।।
ukāraṃ ca makāraṃ ca akāraṃ ca krameṇa vai ।। oṅkārasya svarodātta ṛṣirbrahma sitaṃ vapuḥ ।। udāttaḥ prathamastadvac caturthaś ca dvitīyakaḥ ।। nakāraḥ pītavarṇaś ca sthānaṃ pūrvamukhaṃ smṛtam ।।
makāraḥ kṛṣṇavarṇo asya sthānaṃ vai dakṣiṇāmukham ।। śikāro dhūmravarṇo asya sthānaṃ vai paścimaṃ mukham ।। vākāro hemavarṇo asya sthānaṃ caivottaraṃ mukham ।। yakāro raktavarṇaś ca sthānam ūrdhvaṃ mukhaṃ virāṭ ।।
nyāsamasya pravakṣyāmi sarvasiddhikaraṃ śubham ।। utpattisthitisaṃhārabhedatastrividhaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। utpattirbrahmacāriṇāṃ gṛhasthānāṃ sthitiḥ sadā ।। aṅganyāsaḥ karanyāso dehanyāsa iti tridhā ।।
nyasetpūrvaṃ karanyāsaṃ dehanyāsam anantaram ।। mūrdhādipādaparyantam utpattinyāsa ucyate ।। hṛdayāsyagalanyāsaḥ sthitinyāsa udāhṛtaḥ ।। saśiraskaṃ tato dehaṃ sarvamantreṇa saṃspṛśet ।।
dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhamārabhya vāmāṅguṣṭhānta eva hi ।। aṅguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhāntaṃ nyasyate hastayor dvayoḥ ।। karanyāsaṃ purā kṛtvā dehanyāsam anantaram ।। oṅkāraṃ saṃpuṭīkṛtya sarvāṅgeṣu ca vinyaset ।।
prakṣālya pādāvācamya śucirbhūtvā samāhitaḥ ।। smaret pūrvam ṛṣiṃ chando daivataṃ bījameva ca ।। mantreṇa pāṇī saṃmṛjya talayoḥ praṇavaṃ nyaset ।। sabindukāni bījāni pañca madhyamaparvasu ।।
ubhābhyāmeva pāṇibhyām āpādatalamastakam ।। mūrdhni vaktre ca kaṇṭhe ca hṛdaye guhyake tathā ।। kaṇṭhe ca mukhamadhye ca mūrdhni ca praṇavādikam ।। kaṇṭhe caiva nyasedeva praṇavāditribhedataḥ ।।
pūrvādi cordhvaparyantaṃ nakārādi yathākramam ।। namaḥ svāhā vaṣaḍḍhuṃ ca vauṣaṭphaṭkārakaiḥ saha ।। śikhā makāra ākhyātaḥ śikāraḥ kavacaṃ tathā ।। itthamaṅgāni vinyasya tato vai bandhayeddiśaḥ ।।
āgneyādiṣu koṇeṣu caturṣvapi yathākramam ।। rakṣadhvamiti coktvā tu namaskuryātpṛthakpṛthak ।। aṅguṣṭhena karanyāsaṃ kuryādeva vicakṣaṇaḥ ।। sarvasiddhikaraṃ puṇyaṃ sarvarakṣākaraṃ śivam ।।
janmāntarakṛtaṃ pāpam api naśyati tatkṣaṇāt ।। japetpañcākṣaraṃ mantraṃ labdhvācāryaprasādataḥ ।। yaṃ vinā niṣphalaṃ nityaṃ yena vā saphalaṃ bhavet ।। ājñaptaṃ dakṣiṇāhīnaṃ sadā japtaṃ ca niṣphalam ।।
evaṃ ca dakṣiṇāsiddhaṃ mantraṃ siddhaṃ yatastataḥ ।। jñāninaṃ sadguṇopetaṃ dhyānayogaparāyaṇam ।। vācā ca manasā caiva kāyena draviṇena ca ।। hastyaśvaratharatnāni kṣetrāṇi ca gṛhāṇi ca ।।
etāni gurave dadyād bhaktyā ca vibhave sati ।। paścānnivedayeddevi ātmānaṃ saparicchadam ।। ādadīta gurormantraṃ jñānaṃ caiva krameṇa tu ।। śuśrūṣum anahaṅkāram upavāsakṛśaṃ śucim ।।
samudratīre nadyāṃ ca goṣṭhe devālaye api vā ।। nakṣatre śubhayoge ca sarvadā doṣavarjite ।। svareṇoccārayet samyag ekānte api prasannadhīḥ ।। śivaṃ cāstu śubhaṃ cāstu śobhano astu priyo astviti ।।
japennityaṃ sasaṃkalpaṃ puraścaraṇameva ca ।। anaśnaṃstatparo bhūtvā sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। naktāśī saṃyamī yaś ca pauraścaraṇikaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। acirātsiddhikāṅkṣī tu tayoranyataro bhavet ।।
tasya nāsti samo loke sa siddhaḥ siddhido vaśī ।। prāṅmukhodaṅmukho vāpi japenmantramanuttamam ।। tathā cānte japedbījaṃ śatamaṣṭottaraṃ śubham ।। pañcākṣarasya mantrasya prāṇāyāma udāhṛtaḥ ।।
indriyāṇāṃ vaśitvaṃ ca tasmātprāṇāṃś ca saṃyamet ।। nadyāṃ śatasahasraṃ tu anantaḥ śivasannidhau ।। puṇyāśrameṣu sarveṣu japaḥ koṭiguṇo bhavet ।। dīpasya gorjalasyāpi japakarma praśasyate ।।
rekhairaṣṭaguṇaṃ proktaṃ putrajīvaphalair daśa ।। sphāṭikair daśasāhasraṃ mauktikairlakṣamucyate ।। kuśagranthyā ca rudrākṣair anantaguṇamucyate ।। triṃśacca dhanasaṃpattyai pañcāśaccābhicārikam ।।
paścimaṃ dhanadaṃ vidyād uttaraṃ śāntikaṃ bhavet ।। madhyamā dhanadā śāntiṃ karotyeṣā hy anāmikā ।। aṅguṣṭhena japejjapyam anyairaṅgulibhiḥ saha ।। śṛṇuṣva sarvayajñebhyo japayajño viśiṣyate ।।
yāvantaḥ karmayajñāḥ syuḥ pradānāni tapāṃsi ca ।। māhātmyaṃ vācikasyaiva japayajñasya kīrtitam ।। yad uccanīcasvaritaiḥ śabdaiḥ spaṣṭapadākṣaraiḥ ।। śanairuccārayenmantram īṣad oṣṭhau tu cālayet ।।
dhiyā yadakṣaraśreṇyā varṇādvarṇaṃ padātpadam ।। trayāṇāṃ japayajñānāṃ śreyān syāduttarottaraḥ ।। japena devatā nityaṃ stūyamānā prasīdati ।। jāpinaṃ nopasarpanti bhayabhītāḥ samantataḥ ।।
japena pāpaṃ śamayedaśeṣaṃ yattatkṛtaṃ janmaparaṃparāsu । japena bhogān jayate ca mṛtyuṃ japena siddhiṃ labhate ca muktim ।। evaṃ labdhvā śivaṃ jñānaṃ jñātvā japavidhikramam ।। sadācāraṃ pravakṣyāmi samyagdharmasya sādhanam ।।
ācāraḥ paramo dharma ācāraḥ paramaṃ tapaḥ ।। sadācāravatāṃ puṃsāṃ sarvatrāpyabhayaṃ bhavet ।। sadācāreṇa devatvam ṛṣitvaṃ ca varānane ।। ācārahīnaḥ puruṣo loke bhavati ninditaḥ ।।
durvṛttaḥ śuddhibhūyiṣṭhaḥ pāpīyān jñānadūṣakaḥ ।। varṇāśramavidhānoktaṃ dharmaṃ kurvīta yatnataḥ ।। saṃdhyopāsanaśīlaḥ syāt sāyaṃ prātaḥ prasannadhīḥ ।। kāmānmohādbhayāllobhāt saṃdhyāṃ nātikrameddvijaḥ ।।
asatyaṃ na vadet kiṃcin na satyaṃ ca parityajet ।। anṛtaṃ paruṣaṃ śāṭhyaṃ paiśunyaṃ pāpahetukam ।। kvaciccāpi na kurvīta vācā ca manasā tathā ।। gaṇānnaṃ samudāyānnaṃ rājānnaṃ ca vivarjayet ।।
sattvaśuddhau bhavetsiddhis tato annaṃ pariśodhayet ।। svinnānāmapi bījānāṃ punarjanma na vidyate ।। budhena parihartavyaḥ śvamāṃsaṃ cāpi varjayet ।। parṇapṛṣṭhe na bhuñjīyād rātrau dīpaṃ vinā tathā ।।
śūdraśeṣaṃ na bhuñjīyāt sahānnaṃ śiśukairapi ।। bhoktā śiva iti smṛtvā maunī caikāgramānasaḥ ।। vāmahastena śayyāyāṃ tathaivānyaṃkareṇa vā ।। staṃbhadīpamanuṣyāṇām anyeṣāṃ prāṇināṃ tathā ।।
nāvaroheta kūpādiṃ nāroheduccapādapān ।। na kuryādiha kāryāṇi japakarma śubhāni vā ।। agnernocchrayam āsīta nāgnau kiṃcin malaṃ tyajet ।। malaṃ prakṣālayet tīre prakṣālya snānamācaret ।।
aśrīkaraṃ manuṣyāṇām aśuddhaṃ saṃspṛśedyadi ।। saṃspṛśed yadi mūḍhātmā śriyaṃ hanti harerapi ।। bhojayedyastu viprendrān mārjārasaṃnidhau yadi ।। sphigvātaṃ śūrpavātaṃ ca vātaṃ prāṇamukhānilam ।।
uṣṇīṣī kañcukī nagno muktakeśo malāvṛtaḥ ।। krodho madaḥ kṣudhā tandrā niṣṭhīvanavijṛmbhaṇe ।। eteṣāṃ saṃbhave vāpi kuryātsūryādidarśanam ।। sūryo agniścandramāścaiva grahanakṣatratārakāḥ ।।
prasārya pādau na japet kukkuṭāsana eva ca ।। raktabhūmyāṃ ca khaṭvāyāṃ na japejjāpakas tathā ।। kauśeyaṃ vyāghracarmaṃ vā cailaṃ taulamathāpi vā ।। trisaṃdhyaṃ tu guroḥ pūjā kartavyā hitamicchatā ।।
yathā śivas tathā vidyā yathā vidyā tathā guruḥ ।। sarvadevamayo devi sarvaśaktimayo hi saḥ ।। śreyo arthī yastu gurvājñāṃ manasāpi na laṅghayet ।। gacchaṃstiṣṭhansvapan bhuñjan yadyatkarma samācaret ।।
gurordevasamakṣaṃ vā na yatheṣṭāsano bhavet ।। pāpinā ca yathāsaṃgāt tatpāpaiḥ patanaṃ bhavet ।। yathaiva vahnisaṃparkān malaṃ tyajati kāñcanam ।। yathā vahnisamīpastho ghṛtakuṃbho vilīyate ।।
yathā prajvalito vahnir viṣṭhāṃ kāṣṭhaṃ ca nirdahet ।। brahmā haris tathā rudro devāś ca munayas tathā ।। karmaṇā manasā vācā guroḥ krodhaṃ na kārayet ।। tatkrodhaṃ ye kariṣyanti teṣāṃ yajñāś ca niṣphalāḥ ।।
gurorviruddhaṃ yadvākyaṃ na vadetsarvayatnataḥ ।। cittenaiva ca vittena tathā vācā ca suvratāḥ ।। durguṇe khyāpite tasya nairguṇyaśatabhāgbhavet ।। gurorhitaṃ priyaṃ kuryād ādiṣṭo vā na vā sadā ।।
gurorhitaṃ priyaṃ kuryān manovākkāyakarmabhiḥ ।। tasmātsa sarvadopāsyo vandanīyaś ca sarvadā ।। evamācāravān bhakto nityaṃ japaparāyaṇaḥ ।। viniyogaṃ pravakṣyāmi siddhamantraprayojanam ।।
yasya yena viyuñjīta kāryeṇa tu viśeṣataḥ ।। viniyogajamāyuṣyam ārogyaṃ tanunityatā ।। prokṣaṇaṃ cābhiṣekaṃ ca aghamarṣaṇameva ca ।। śuciḥ parvatamāruhya japellakṣamatandritaḥ ।।
dūrvāṅkurāstilā vāṇī guḍūcī ghuṭikā tathā ।। aśvatthavṛkṣamāśritya japellakṣadvayaṃ sudhīḥ ।। śanaiścaradine aśvatthaṃ pāṇibhyāṃ saṃspṛśetsudhīḥ ।। ādityābhimukho bhūtvā japellakṣamananyadhīḥ ।।
samastavyādhiśāntyarthaṃ palāśasamidhair naraḥ ।। nityamaṣṭaśataṃ japtvā pibed ambho arkasannidhau ।। ekādaśena bhuñjīyād annaṃ caivābhimantritam ।। japel lakṣaṃ tu pūrvāhṇe hutvā cāṣṭaśatena vai ।।
nadītoyena sampūrṇaṃ ghaṭaṃ saṃspṛśya śobhanam ।। aṣṭāviṃśajjapitvānnam aśnīyād anvahaṃ śuciḥ ।। candrasūryagrahe pūrvam upoṣya vidhinā śuciḥ ।। japetsamudragāminyāṃ vimokṣe grahaṇasya tu ।।
aihikāṃ labhate medhāṃ sarvaśāstradharāṃ śubhām ।। grahanakṣatrapīḍāsu japedbhaktyāyutaṃ naraḥ ।। duḥsvapnadarśane snātvā japedvai cāyutaṃ naraḥ ।। candrasūryagrahe liṅgaṃ samabhyarcya yathāvidhi ।।
saṃnidhāvasya devasya śuciḥ saṃyatamānasaḥ ।। gajānāṃ turagāṇāṃ tu gojātīnāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। māsamabhyarcya vidhinā-yutaṃ bhaktisamanvitaḥ ।। utpāte śatrubādhāyāṃ juhuyādayutaṃ śuciḥ ।।
ābhicārikabādhāyām etaddevi samācaret ।। vidveṣaṇārthaṃ juhuyād vaibhītasamidhāṣṭakam ।। viṣeṇa rudhirābhyakto vidveṣaṇakaraṃ nṛṇām ।। pāpaśuddhiryathā samyak kartumabhyudyato naraḥ ।।
pāpaśuddhirna cetpuṃsaḥ kriyāḥ sarvāścaniṣphalāḥ ।। vidyālakṣmīviśuddhyarthaṃ māṃ dhyātvāñjalinā śubhe ।। aṣṭottaraśatenaiva snāyātpāpaviśuddhaye ।। saṃdhyopāsanavicchede japedaṣṭaśataṃ naraḥ ।।
spṛṣṭamannaṃ na bhuñjīta bhuktvā cāṣṭaśataṃ japet ।। pātakānāṃ tadardhaṃ syān nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। śeṣāṇāmapi pāpānāṃ japetpañcasahasrakam ।। śivaḥ syātsa japenmantraṃ pañcalakṣam anākulaḥ ।।
japecca pañcalakṣaṃ tu vigṛhītendriyaḥ śuciḥ ।। dhyānayukto japedyastu pañcalakṣamanākulaḥ ।। caturthaṃ pañcalakṣaṃ tu yo japedbhaktisaṃyutaḥ ।। caturlakṣaṃ japedyastu manaḥ saṃyamya yatnataḥ ।।
pañcaviṃśatilakṣāṇāṃ japena kamalānane ।। madhyarātre atinirvāte japedayutamādarāt ।। japellakṣamanālasyo nirvāte dhvanivarjite ।। andhakāravināśaś ca dīpasyeva prakāśanam ।।
sarvasaṃpatsamṛddhyarthaṃ japedayutamātmavān ।। matsāyujyamavāpnoti bhaktimān kimataḥ param ।। yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। daive karmaṇi pitrye vā śivaloke mahīyate ।।
viraktānāṃ prabuddhānāṃ dhyānayajñaṃ suśobhanam ।। vistārātsarvayatnena viraktānāṃ mahātmanām ।। rudreṇa kathitaṃ prāha guhāṃ prāpya mahātmanām ।। guhāṃ prāpya sukhāsīnaṃ bhavānyā saha śaṅkaram ।।
astuvaṃś ca tataḥ sarve nīlakaṇṭhamumāpatim ।। ataḥ pratiṣṭhitaṃ sarvaṃ tvayā deva vṛṣadhvaja ।। prahasanprāha viśvātmā sanandanapurogamān ।। saṃharettadviṣaṃ yastu sa samartho hyanena kim ।।
tasmātsarvaprayatnena saṃhareta sudāruṇam ।। puṃsāṃ saṃmūḍhacittānām asaṃkṣīṇaḥ sudāruṇaḥ ।। tadvaśādeva sarveṣāṃ dharmādharmau na saṃśayaḥ ।। buddhimutpādayatyeva saṃsāre viduṣāṃ dvijāḥ ।।
saṃtyajetsarvayatnena viraktaḥ so abhidhīyate ।। mūrdhānaṃ brahmaṇaḥ sāram ṛṣīṇāṃ karmaṇaḥ phalam ।। śrutiḥ pravartikā teṣām iti karmaṇyatadvidaḥ ।। tasmādajñānamūlo hi saṃsāraḥ sarvadehinām ।।
sakalastrividho jīvo jñānahīnastvavidyayā ।। vyatimiśreṇa vai jīvaś caturdhā saṃvyavasthitaḥ ।। evaṃ vyavasthito dehī karmaṇājño hyanirvṛtaḥ ।। tyāgenaikena muktiḥ syāt tadabhāvādbhramatyasau ।।
ṣaṭkauśikaṃ samudbhūtaṃ bhajatyeṣa kalevaram ।। kaumāre yauvane caiva vārddhake maraṇe api vā ।। duḥkhenaikena vai duḥkhaṃ praśāmyatīha duḥkhinaḥ ।। haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmeva bhūya evābhivardhate ।।
arthānām arjane apyevaṃ pālane ca vyaye tathā ।। gāndharve ca tathā cāndre saumyaloke dvijottamāḥ ।। kṣayasātiśayādyaistu duḥkhairduḥkhāni suvratāḥ ।। tasmādaṣṭaguṇaṃ bhogaṃ tathā ṣoḍaśadhā sthitam ।।
dvātriṃśadbhedamanaghāś catvāriṃśadguṇaṃ punaḥ ।। catuḥṣaṣṭividhaṃ caiva duḥkhameva vivekinaḥ ।। vāyavyaṃ ca tathā vyauma[ṃ] mānasaṃ ca yathākramam ।। duḥkhameva na saṃdeho yogināṃ brahmavādinām ।।
ādau madhye tathā cānte sarvalokeṣu sarvadā ।। doṣaduṣṭeṣu deśeṣu duḥkhāni vividhāni ca ।। kṣudvyādheḥ parihārārthaṃ na sukhāyānnamucyate ।। śītoṣṇavātavarṣādyais tattatkāleṣu dehinām ।।
svarge apyevaṃ muniśreṣṭhā hy aviśuddhakṣayādibhiḥ ।। chinnamūlataruryadvad avaśaḥ patati kṣitau ।। duḥkhābhilāṣaniṣṭhānāṃ duḥkhabhogādisaṃpadām ।। narake duḥkhamevātra narakāṇāṃ niṣevaṇāt ।।
vihitākaraṇāccaiva varṇināṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।। evaṃ yatirdhyānaparo mahātmā saṃsārabhīto na labheta nidrām ।। dṛṣṭam evāsukhaṃ tasmāt tyajataḥ sukhamuttamam ।। sthānābhimānināṃ caiva manvādīnāṃ ca suvratāḥ ।।
duḥkhameva nṛpāṇāṃ ca rākṣasānāṃ jagattraye ।। āśramairna ca devaiś ca yajñaiḥ sāṃkhyairvratais tathā ।। na labhante tathātmānaṃ labhante jñāninaḥ svayam ।। bhasmaśāyī bhavennityaṃ vrate pāśupate budhaḥ ।।
kaivalyakaraṇaṃ yogavidhikarmacchidaṃ budhaḥ ।। parayā vidyayā vedyaṃ vidantyaparayā na hi ।। aparā tatra ṛgvedo yajurvedo dvijottamāḥ ।। śikṣā kalpo vyākaraṇaṃ niruktaṃ chanda eva ca ।।
tadadṛśyaṃ tadagrāhyam agotraṃ tadavarṇakam ।। tadajātamabhūtaṃ ca tadaśabdaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। avyayaṃ cāpratiṣṭhaṃ ca tannityaṃ sarvagaṃ vibhum ।। aprāṇamamanaskaṃ ca tadasnigdhamalohitam ।।
ahrasvaṃ tadapāraṃ ca tadānandaṃ tadacyutam ।। asaṃvṛtaṃ tadātmaikaṃ parā vidyā na cānyathā ।। ahameva jagatsarvaṃ mayyeva sakalaṃ jagat ।। matto nānyaditīkṣeta manovākpāṇibhis tathā ।।
sarvaṃ hyātmani saṃpaśyan na bāhye kurute manaḥ ।। hṛdayaṃ tadvijānīyād viśvasyāyatanaṃ mahat ।। dharmakandasamudbhūtaṃ jñānanālaṃ suśobhanam ।। chidrāṇi ca diśo yasya prāṇādyāś ca pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।।
daśaprāṇavahā nāḍyaḥ pratyekaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।। netrasthaṃ jāgrataṃ vidyāt kaṇṭhe svapnaṃ samādiśet ।। jāgre brahmā ca viṣṇuś ca svapne caiva yathākramāt ।। vadanty evam athānye api samastakaraṇaiḥ pumān ।।
manobuddhir ahaṅkāraṃ cittaṃ ceti catuṣṭayam ।। karaṇāni vilīnāni yadā svātmani suvratāḥ ।। parasturīyātīto asau śivaḥ paramakāraṇam ।। ādhyātmikaṃ ca viprendrāś cādhidaivikamucyate ।।
buddhīndriyāṇi viprendrās tathā karmendriyāṇi ca ।। adhyātmaṃ pṛthagevedaṃ caturdaśavidhaṃ smṛtam ।। rasitavyaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ sparśitavyaṃ tathaiva ca ।। tathā cetayitavyaṃ ca vaktavyaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।।
ānanditavyamityete hy adhibhūtamanukramāt ।। vāyuścandras tathā brahmā rudraḥ kṣetrajña eva ca ।। ādhidaivikamevaṃ hi caturdaśavidhaṃ kramāt ।। moghā rudrāmṛtā satyā madhyamā ca dvijottamāḥ ।।
bhāsvatī nāḍayaścaitāś caturdaśanibandhanāḥ ।। prāṇo vyānastvapānaś ca udānaś ca samānakaḥ ।। kūrmakaś ca tathā śyenaḥ śvetaḥ kṛṣṇas tathānilaḥ ।। yaścakṣuḥṣvatha draṣṭavye tathāditye ca suvratāḥ ।।
hṛdyākāśe ya etasmin sarvasminnantare paraḥ ।। ajaraṃ tamanantaṃ ca aśokamamṛtaṃ dhruvam ।। līyante tāni tatraiva yadanyaṃ nāsti vai dvijāḥ ।। eṣa sarvādhipo devas tv antaryāmī mahādyutiḥ ।।
upāsyati na caiveha sarvasaukhyaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। na vaiṣa vedaśāstrāṇi sarvajño yāsyati prabhuḥ ।। svātmanā rakṣitaṃ cādyād annabhūtaṃ na kutracit ।। praśāstā nayanaścaiva pañcātmā sa vibhāgaśaḥ ।।
prāṇamayaścendriyātmā saṃkalpātmā manomayaḥ ।। sadānandamayo bhūtvā maheśaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। paratantraṃ svatantre api tadabhāvādvicārataḥ ।। evaṃ nāstyatha martyaṃ ca kuto amṛtamajodbhavaḥ ।।
na prajñānaghanastvevaṃ na prājño jñānapūrvakaḥ ।। nirvāṇaṃ caiva kaivalyaṃ niḥśreyasamanāmayam ।। nirvikalpaṃ nirābhāsaṃ jñānaṃ paryāyavācakam ।। ajñānamitaratsarvaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।।
rāgadveṣānṛtakrodhaṃ kāmatṛṣṇādibhiḥ sadā ।। ajñānamalapūrvatvāt puruṣo malinaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। jñānamekaṃ vinā nāsti puṇyapāpaparikṣayaḥ ।। jñānābhyāsāddhi vai puṃsāṃ buddhirbhavati nirmalā ।।
jñānenaikena tṛptasya tyaktasaṃgasya yoginaḥ ।। iha loke pare cāpi kartavyaṃ nāsti tasya vai ।। jñānābhyāsarato nityaṃ jñānatattvārthavit svayam ।। varṇāśramābhimānī yas tyaktakrodho dvijottamāḥ ।।
saṃsāraheturajñānaṃ saṃsārastanusaṃgrahaḥ ।। ajñāne sati viprendrāḥ krodhādyā nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। dharmādharmau hi teṣāṃ ca tadvaśāttanusaṃgrahaḥ ।। avidyāṃ vidyayā hitvā sthitasyaiva ca yoginaḥ ।।
tatkṣayācca śarīreṇa na punaḥ samprayujyate ।। evaṃ jñānaṃ vinā nāsti dhyānaṃ dhyātur dvijarṣabhāḥ ।। caturvyūhamiti jñātvā dhyātā dhyānaṃ samabhyaset ।। jñānāgnirdahate kṣipraṃ śuṣkendhanam ivānalaḥ ।।
abhyasecca sadā jñānaṃ sarvasaṃgavivarjitaḥ ।। krīḍannapi na lipyeta pāpairnānāvidhairapi ।। dhyānaṃ nirviṣayaṃ proktam ādau saviṣayaṃ tathā ।। tathā dvādaśadhā caiva punaḥ ṣoḍaśadhā kramāt ।।
śuddhajāṃbūnadākāraṃ vidhūmāṅgārasannibham ।। athavā brahmarandhrasthaṃ cittaṃ kṛtvā prayatnataḥ ।। ahiṃsakaḥ satyavādī asteyī sarvayatnataḥ ।। saṃtuṣṭaḥ śaucasampannaḥ svādhyāyanirataḥ sadā ।।
na budhyati tathā dhyātā sthāpya cittaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। na ghrāti na śṛṇotyeva līnaḥ svātmani yaḥ svayam ।। pārthive paṭale brahmā vāritattve hariḥ svayam ।। suṣire sa śivaḥ sākṣāt kramādevaṃ vicintayet ।।
rudra eva tathā vahnau ugro vāyau vyavasthitaḥ ।। īśānaḥ somabimbe ca mahādeva iti smṛtaḥ ।। kāṭhinyaṃ yattanau sarvaṃ pārthivaṃ parigīyate ।। yatsaṃcarati tadvāyuḥ suṣiraṃ yaddvijottamāḥ ।।
tathaiva viprā vijñānaṃ sparśākhyaṃ vāyusaṃbhavam ।। gandhākhyaṃ pārthivaṃ bhūyaś cintayedbhāskaraṃ kramāt ।। ājānu pṛthivītattvam ānābher vārimaṇḍalam ।। vāyavyaṃ vai lalāṭādyaṃ vyomākhyaṃ vā śikhāgrakam ।।
vyomākhyo vyomamadhyastho hy ayaṃ prāthamikaḥ smaret ।। mahāṃstathābhimānaś ca tanmātrāṇīndriyāṇi ca ।। vyāpya tiṣṭhadyato viśvaṃ sthāṇurityabhidhīyate ।। dyotate candramā vahnir jvalatyāpo vahanti ca ।।
tadājñayā tataṃ sarvaṃ tasmādvai cintayeddvijāḥ ।। sarvarūpamayaḥ śarva iti matvā smaredbhavam ।। pratīkāraḥ samākhyāto nānyathā dvijasattamāḥ ।। vairāgyātparamaṃ jñānaṃ paramārthaprakāśakam ।।
yogasiddhyā vimuktiḥ syāt sattvaniṣṭhasya nānyathā ।। sattvaśaktiṃ samāsthāya śivamabhyarcayeddvijāḥ ।। sarvato dharmaniṣṭhaś ca sadotsāhī samāhitaḥ ।। ṛjusvabhāvaḥ satataṃ svasthacitto mṛduḥ sadā ।।
sadā mumukṣurdharmajñaḥ svātmalakṣaṇalakṣaṇaḥ ।। jarāyukto dvijo bhūtvā śraddhayā ca guroḥ kramāt ।। svargalokamanuprāpya bhuktvā bhogānanukramāt ।। saṃparkājjñānamāsādya jñānino yogavidbhavet ।।
tasmādanena mārgeṇa tyaktasaṃgo dṛḍhavrataḥ ।। evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ mayā yuṣmākamacyutam ।। evaṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ kathitaṃ tvīśvareṇa tu ।। dātavyaṃ yogine nityaṃ bhasmaniṣṭhāya supriyam ।।
sa yāti brahmasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। procuḥ praṇamya vai bhītāḥ prasannaṃ parameśvaram ।। krīḍase vividhairbhogaiḥ kathaṃ vaktumihārhasi ।। prāha tām aṃbikāṃ prekṣya praṇipatya sthitān dvijān ।।
akartajñaḥ paśurjīvo vibhurbhoktā hyaṇuḥ pumān ।। jñānaṃ dhyānaṃ ca bandhaś ca mokṣo nāstyātmano dvijāḥ ।। eṣā vidyā hyahaṃ vedyaḥ prajñaiṣā ca śrutiḥ smṛtiḥ ।। icchākhyā ca tathā hyājñā dve vidye na ca saṃśayaḥ ।।
vikāro naiva māyaiṣā sadasadvyaktivarjitā ।। pañcavaktrā mahābhāgā jagatāmabhayapradā ।। saptaviṃśatprakāreṇa sarvaṃ vyāpyānayā śivaḥ ।। evamuktvā tadāpaśyad bhavānīṃ parameśvaraḥ ।।
te māyāmalanirmuktā munayaḥ prekṣya pārvatīm ।। umāśaṅkarayorbhedo nāstyeva paramārthataḥ ।। yadā vidvānasaṃgaḥ syād ājñayā parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। kramo avivakṣito bhūtavivṛddhaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।।
garbhastho jāyamāno vā bālo vā taruṇo api vā ।। aṇḍajaś codbhijjo vāpi svedajo vāpi mucyate ।। eṣa eva jagannātho bandhamokṣakaraḥ śivaḥ ।। satyalokas tathāṇḍānāṃ koṭikoṭiśatāni ca ।।
saptadvīpeṣu sarveṣu parvateṣu vaneṣu ca ।। tathānyeṣu ca lokeṣu vasanti ca carācarāḥ ।। sarvo rudro namastasmai puruṣāya mahātmane ।। rudrājñaiṣā sthitā devī hy anayā muktiraṃbikā ।।
yadāvalokya tān sarvān prasādādanayāṃbikā ।। tadā tiṣṭhanti sāyujyaṃ prāptāste khecarāḥ prabhoḥ ।। tatsarvaṃ vistarātsūta vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam ।। pañcadhā saṃsmaredādau sthāpya citte sanātanam ।।
ṣaḍviṃśacchaktisaṃyuktam aṣṭadhā ca dvijottamāḥ ।। smarec ca tat tathā madhye devyā devam umāpatim ।। tābhiścāṣṭavidhā rudrāś catuḥṣaṣṭividhāḥ punaḥ ।। evaṃ smaretkrameṇaiva labdhvā jñānamanuttamam ।।
tasyāṇimādayo viprā nānyathā karmakoṭibhiḥ ।। tatsarvaṃ kramayogena hy ucyamānaṃ nibodhata ।। prākāmyaṃ caiva sarvatra īśitvaṃ caiva sarvataḥ ।। taccāpi trividhaṃ jñeyam aiśvaryaṃ sārvakāmikam ।।
sāvadyaṃ nāma yattatra pañcabhūtātmakaṃ smṛtam ।। tatra sūkṣmapravṛttistu pañcabhūtātmikā punaḥ ।। tathā sarvamayaṃ caiva ātmasthā khyātireva ca ।। punaraṣṭaguṇaścāpi sūkṣmeṣveva vidhīyate ।।
trailokye sarvabhūteṣu yathāsya niyamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। trailokye sarvabhūtānāṃ duṣprāpyaṃ samudāhṛtam ।। laṅghanaṃ plavanaṃ loke rūpamasya sadā bhavet ।। trailokye sarvabhūtānāṃ mahimnā caiva vanditam ।।
trailokye sarvabhūteṣu yatheṣṭagamanaṃ smṛtam ।। trailokye sarvabhūtānāṃ sukhaduḥkhaṃ pravartate ।। vaśyāni cāsya bhūtāni trailokye sacarācare ।। yatra kāmāvasāyitvaṃ trailokye sacarācare ।।
pravartante asya cecchāto na bhavanti yathecchayā ।। na dahyate na muhyeta līyate na ca lipyate ।। kriyate vā na sarvatra tathā vikriyate na ca ।। avarṇo hyasvaraś caiva asavarṇastu karhicit ।।
aṇutvāttu paraḥ sūkṣmaḥ sūkṣmatvād apavargikaḥ ।। puruṣaḥ sūkṣmabhāvāttu aiśvarye parame sthitaḥ ।। aiśvaryaṃ cāpratīghātaṃ prāpya yogamanuttamam ।। evaṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ jñātavyaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।।
athavā gatavijñāno rāgātkarma samācaret ।। tathā sukṛtakarmā tu phalaṃ svarge samaśnute ।। tasmādbrahma paraṃ saukhyaṃ brahma śāśvatam uttamam ।। pariśramo hi yajñānāṃ mahatārthena vartate ।।
athavā dhyānasaṃyukto brahmatattvaparāyaṇaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā tu puruṣaṃ divyaṃ viśvākhyaṃ viśvatomukham ।। viśvagandhaṃ viśvamālyaṃ viśvāṃbaradharaṃ prabhum ।। kaviṃ purāṇam anuśāsitāraṃ sūkṣmācca sūkṣmaṃ mahato mahāntam ।।
aliṅginaṃ nirguṇaṃ cetanaṃ ca nityaṃ sadā sarvagaṃ sarvasāram ।। paśyanti yuktyā hyacalaprakāśaṃ tadbhāvitāstejasā dīpyamānam । apāṇipādodarapārśvajihvo hyatīndriyo vāpi susūkṣma ekaḥ ।। paśyatyacakṣuḥ sa śṛṇotyakarṇo na cāstyabuddhaṃ na ca buddhir asti ।
sa veda sarvaṃ na ca sarvavedyaṃ tamāhuragryaṃ puruṣaṃ mahāntam ।। prakṛtiṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ yuktāḥ paśyanti yoginaḥ ।। sarvataḥ śrutimal loke sarvamāvṛtya tiṣṭhati ।। puruṣaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ taṃ vidvānna vimuhyati ।।
sarvātmānaṃ paraṃ brahma tadvai dhyātā na muhyati ।। puri śete sudurgrāhyas tasmātpuruṣa ucyate ।। tatastu brahmagarbhe vai śukraśoṇitasaṃyute ।। tatastu garbhakālena kalalaṃ nāma jāyate ।।
mṛtpiṇḍastu yathā cakre cakrāvartena pīḍitaḥ ।। evamādhyātmikairyuktā vāyunā saṃprapūritaḥ ।। yāvaddhi vaiṣṇavo vāyur jātamātraṃ na saṃspṛśet ।। jāyate mānuṣastatra yathārūpaṃ yathāvayaḥ ।।
jalāt sambhavati prāṇaḥ prāṇācchukraṃ vivardhate ।। bhāgato ardhaphalaṃ kṛtvā tato garbho niṣicyate ।। pituḥ śarīrātpratyaṅgaṃ rūpamasyopajāyate ।। nābhideśena vai prāṇās te hy ādhārā hi dehinām ।।
veṣṭitaḥ sarvagātraiś ca aparyāptapraveśanaḥ ।। tataḥ svakarmabhiḥ pāpair nirayaṃ samprapadyate ।। tāḍanaṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ caiva pūyaśoṇitabhakṣaṇam ।। tathā chinnāś ca bhinnāśca yātanāsthānam āgatāḥ ।।
prāpnuyuḥ karmabhiḥ śeṣair duḥkhaṃ vā yadi vetarat ।। ekenaiva tu bhoktavyaṃ tasmātsukṛtamācaret ।। yadanena kṛtaṃ karma tadenamanugacchati ।। śuṣyante parigatavedanāḥ śarīrā bahvībhiḥ subhṛśamanantayātanābhiḥ ।।
tadabhyāso haratyenaṃ tasmātkalyāṇamācaret ।। saṃsāraṃ tāmasaṃ ghoraṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ pratipadyate ।। mṛgatvātpakṣibhāvaś ca tasmāccaiva sarīsṛpaḥ ।। sthāvaratve punaḥ prāpte yāvad unmilate janaḥ ।।
ityevaṃ hi manuṣyādiḥ saṃsāraḥ sthāvarāntikaḥ ।। sāttvikaścāpi saṃsāro brahmādiḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। brāhme tu kevalaṃ sattvaṃ sthāvare kevalaṃ tamaḥ ।। marmasu chidyamāneṣu vedanārtasya dehinaḥ ।।
saṃsāraḥ pūrvadharmasya bhāvanābhiḥ praṇoditaḥ ।। caturdaśavidhaṃ hyetad buddhvā saṃsāramaṇḍalam ।। tatastarati saṃsāraṃ krameṇa parivartitaḥ ।। tathā samārabhedyogaṃ yathātmānaṃ sa paśyati ।।
vivṛtyā hyeṣa saṃbhedād bhūtānāṃ caiva śāśvataḥ ।। hṛdisthaṃ sarvabhūtānām upāsīta maheśvaram ।। aṣṭadhā cāṣṭadhā caiva tathā cāṣṭavidhena ca ।। dhyātvā yathāvaddeveśaṃ rudraṃ bhuvananāyakam ।।
vaiśvānaraṃ hṛdisthaṃ tu yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।। prāṇāyeti tatastasya prathamā hyāhutiḥ smṛtā ।। udānāya caturthī syāt samānāyeti pañcamī ।। apaḥ punaḥ sakṛtprāśya ācamya hṛdayaṃ spṛśet ।।
rudro vai hyātmanaḥ prāṇa evamāpyāyayetsvayam ।। prāṇāya caiva rudrāya juhotyamṛtamuttamam ।। evaṃ pañcāhutīścaiva prabhuḥ prīṇātu śāśvataḥ ।। āśritaścaiva cāṅguṣṭham īśaḥ paramakāraṇam ।।
tvaṃ devānāmasi jyeṣṭho rudrastvaṃ ca puro vṛṣā ।। ityevaṃ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ guṇaprāptiviśeṣataḥ ।। evaṃ pāśupataṃ jñānaṃ jñātavyaṃ ca prayatnataḥ ।। yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā dvijottamān ।।
daive karmaṇi pitrye vā sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। yadanuṣṭhāya śuddhātmā paretya gatimāpnuyāt ।। saṃkṣepātsarvavedārthaṃ saṃcayaṃ brahmavādinām ।। yastatrāthāpramattaḥ syāt sa munirnāvasīdati ।।
avamāno amṛtaṃ tatra sanmāno viṣamucyate ।। niyameṣvapramattastu yameṣu ca sadā bhavet ।। avirodhena dharmasya careta pṛthivīmimām ।। satyapūtaṃ vadedvākyaṃ manaḥpūtaṃ samācaret ।।
ekāhaṃ tatsamaṃ jñeyam apūtaṃ yajjalaṃ bhavet ।। aghoralakṣaṇaṃ mantraṃ tataḥ śuddhimavāpnuyāt ।। tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya śudhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। evaṃ hyahiṃsako yogī bhavediti vicāritam ।।
carettu matimān bhaikṣyaṃ na tu teṣveva nityaśaḥ ।। tathā yuktaṃ caredbhaikṣyaṃ satāṃ dharmamadūṣayan ।। śreṣṭhā tu prathamā hīyaṃ vṛttirasyopajāyate ।। śraddadhāneṣu dānteṣu śrotriyeṣu mahātmasu ।।
bhaikṣyacaryā hi varṇeṣu jaghanyā vṛttirucyate ।। phalamūlādi pakvaṃ vā kaṇapiṇyākasaktavaḥ ।। āhārāsteṣu siddheṣu śreṣṭhaṃ bhaikṣyamiti smṛtam ।। nyāyato yaścaredbhaikṣyaṃ pūrvoktātsa viśiṣyate ।।
evaṃ dāyayate tasmāt tadbhaikṣyamiti saṃsmṛtam ।। sarve te bhaikṣyabhakṣasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ।। ya icchet paramaṃ sthānaṃ vrataṃ pāśupataṃ caret ।। ekaṃ dve trīṇi catvāri śaktito vā samācaret ।।
vratāni pañca bhikṣūṇām ahiṃsā paramā tviha ।। nityaṃ svādhyāya ityete niyamāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। yathā dvipa ivāraṇye manuṣyāṇāṃ vidhīyate ।। jñānād dhyānaṃ saṃgarāgādapetaṃ tasminprāpte śāśvatasyopalambhaḥ ।।
atīndriyaṃ jñānamidaṃ tathā śivaṃ prāhus tathā jñānaviśuddhabuddhayaḥ ।। samāhito brahmaparo apramādī śucis tathaikāntaratir jitendriyaḥ । samāpnuyādyogamimaṃ mahātmā maharṣayaścaivam aninditāmalāḥ ।। etanmārgeṇa śuddhena dagdhabījo hyakalmaṣaḥ ।।
sarvāṃllokān vinirjitya brahmalokaṃ vrajanti te ।। sarvalokopakārārthaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ pravadāmi vaḥ ।। abhyutthānādikaṃ sarvaṃ praṇāmaṃ caiva kārayet ।। triḥpradakṣiṇayogena vandyo vai brahmaṇo guruḥ ।।
ājñābhaṅgaṃ na kurvīta yadīcchet siddhim uttamām ।। viṣagrahaviḍambādīn varjayet sarvayatnataḥ ।। atihāsam avaṣṭambhaṃ līlāsvecchāpravartanam ।। tadvākyapratikūlaṃ ca ayuktaṃ vai gurorvacaḥ ।।
yatīnāmāsanaṃ vastraṃ daṇḍādyaṃ pāduke tathā ।। yajñopakaraṇāṅgaṃ ca na spṛśed vai padena ca ।। kṛtvā pramādato viprāḥ praṇavasyāyutaṃ japet ।। mahāpātakaśuddhyarthaṃ tathaiva ca yathāvidhi ।।
upapātakinaḥ sarve tadardhenaiva suvratāḥ ।। āhnikacchedane jāte śatamekamudāhṛtam ।। avācyavācane caiva sahasrācchuddhirucyate ।। śatamaṣṭottaraṃ japtvā mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
smaraṇācchuddhimāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। viśvasyaiva hi te śuddhā brahmavidyāvido janāḥ ।। śuddhānāṃ śodhanaṃ nāsti viśuddhā brahmavidyayā ।। adbhiḥ samācaretsarvaṃ varjayetkaluṣodakam ।।
paṅkāśmadūṣitaṃ caiva sāmudraṃ palvalodakam ।। vastraśaucānvitaḥ kuryāt sarvakāryāṇi vai dvijāḥ ।। vastraśaucavihīnātmā hy aśucirnātra saṃśayaḥ ।। itareṣāṃ hi vastrāṇāṃ śaucaṃ kāryaṃ malāgame ।।
kauśeyāvikayo rūkṣaiḥ kṣaumāṇāṃ gaurasarṣapaiḥ ।। carmaṇāṃ vidalānāṃ ca vetrāṇāṃ vastravanmatam ।। cailavacchaucamākhyātaṃ brahmavidbhir munīśvaraiḥ ।। tāmramamlena vai viprās trapusīsakayorapi ।।
maṇyaśmaśaṅkhamuktānāṃ śaucaṃ taijasavatsmṛtam ।। rasānāmiha sarveṣāṃ śuddhirutplavanaṃ smṛtam ।। uṣṇena vāriṇā śuddhis tathā sruksruvayorapi ।। śṛṅgāsthidārudantānāṃ takṣaṇenaiva śodhanam ।।
asaṃhatānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ pratyekaṃ śaucamucyate ।। tāvanmātraṃ samuddhṛtya prokṣayedvai kuśāṃbhasā ।। mārjanonmārjanair veśma punaḥpākena mṛnmayam ।। gonivāsena vai śuddhā secanena dharā smṛtā ।।
avyāptaṃ yadamedhyena gandhavarṇarasānvitam ।। svadārāsyaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ ratau bhāryābhikāṅkṣayā ।। kuśāṃbunā susaṃprokṣya gṛhṇīyāddharmavittamaḥ ।। śucirākarajaṃ teṣāṃ śvā mṛgagrahaṇe śuciḥ ।।
rajo bhūr vāyur agniś ca medhyāni sparśane sadā ।। ṣṭhīvitvādhyayanādau ca śucirapyācametpunaḥ ।। te pārthivaiḥ samā jñeyā na tairaprayato bhavet ।। sūkaraṃ caiva kākādi śvānamuṣṭraṃ kharaṃ tathā ।।
rajasvalāṃ sūtikāṃ ca na spṛśedantyajāmapi ।। saṃspṛśenna rajastāsāṃ spṛṣṭvā snātvaiva śudhyati ।। naiṣṭhikānāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ ca maṇḍalīnāṃ ca suvratāḥ ।। vaikhānasānāṃ viprāṇāṃ patitānāmasaṃbhavāt ।।
tathā saṃnihitānāṃ ca yajñārthaṃ dīkṣitasya ca ।। tatastvadhītaśākhānāṃ caturbhiḥ sarvadehinām ।। arvāg ekādaśāhāntaṃ bāndhavānāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। tata ṛtutrayādarvāg ekāhaḥ parigīyate ।।
daśāhaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ vai prathame ahani vā pituḥ ।। arvāk trivarṣātsnānena bāndhavānāṃ pituḥ sadā ।। dvādaśābdāttataścārvāk trirātraṃ strīṣu suvratāḥ ।। atikrānte daśāhe tu trirātramaśucirbhavet ।।
saṃvatsare vyatīte tu snānamātreṇa śudhyati ।। dāhakānāṃ ca netṝṇāṃ snānamātramabāndhave ।। ācāryamaraṇe caiva trirātraṃ śrotriye mṛte ।। bhūpānāṃ maṇḍalīnāṃ ca sadyo nīrāṣṭravāsinām ।।
nābhiṣiktasya cāśaucaṃ saṃpramādeṣu vai raṇe ।। iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktā dravyaśuddhiranuttamā ।। tretāprabhṛti nārīṇāṃ māsi māsyārtavaṃ dvijāḥ ।। prayānti ca mahābhāgā bhāryābhiḥ kuravo yathā ।।
bhārate dakṣiṇe varṣe vyavasthā netareṣvatha ।। śākadvīpādiṣu prokto dharmo vai bhārate yathā ।। saivārtavakṛtād doṣād rāgadveṣādibhir nṛṇām ।। yavādyāḥ samprajāyante grāmyāraṇyāścaturdaśa ।।
akālakṛṣṭā vidhvastāḥ punarutpāditās tathā ।। prathame ahani cāṇḍālī yathā varjyā tathāṅganā ।। tṛtīye ahni tadardhena caturthe ahani suvratāḥ ।। ā ṣoḍaśāt tataḥ strīṇāṃ mūtravacchaucamiṣyate ।।
sā viṃśaddivasādūrdhvaṃ rajasā pūrvavattathā ।। yānamabhyañjanaṃ nārī dyūtaṃ caivānulepanam ।। maithunaṃ mānasaṃ vāpi vācikaṃ devatārcanam ।। rajasvalāṅganāsparśasaṃbhāṣe ca rajasvalā ।।
snātvānyapuruṣaṃ nārī na spṛśettu rajasvalā ।। kevalaṃ pañcagavyaṃ vā kṣīraṃ vā cātmaśuddhaye ।। vidyāhīnaṃ vratabhraṣṭaṃ patitaṃ pāradārikam ।। kanyārthinaiva gantavyā pañcamyāṃ vidhivatpunaḥ ।।
same napuṃsakaṃ caiva pañcamyāṃ kanyakā bhavet ।। putratvaṃ vyañjayettasya jātaputro mahādyutiḥ ।। puṃsastrāṇānvitaṃ putraṃ tathābhūtaṃ prasūyate ।। aṣṭamyāṃ sarvasampannaṃ tanayaṃ samprasūyate ।।
ekādaśyāṃ tathā nārīṃ janayetsaiva pūrvavat ।। trayodaśyāṃ jaḍāṃ nārīṃ sarvasaṃkarakāriṇīm ।। caturdaśyāṃ yadā gacchet sā putrajananī bhavet ।। strīṇāṃ vai maithune kāle vāmapārśve prabhañjanaḥ ।।
strīṇāṃ maithunakāle tu pāpagrahavivarjite ।। ityevaṃ saṃprasaṃgena yatīnāṃ dharmasaṃgrahe ।। yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyād vāpi sadācāraṃ śucirnaraḥ ।। brahmalokamanuprāpya brahmaṇā saha modate ।।
prāyaścittaṃ śivaproktaṃ yatīnāṃ pāpaśodhanam ।। satataṃ hi divā rātrau yenedaṃ veṣṭyate jagat ।। kṣaṇamevaṃ prayojyaṃ tu āyuṣyaṃ tu vidhāraṇam ।। na hi yogātparaṃ kiṃcin narāṇāṃ dṛśyate śubham ।।
avidyāṃ vidyayā jitvā prāpyaiśvaryamanuttamam ।। vratāni yāni bhikṣūṇāṃ tathaivopavratāni ca ।। upetya tu striyaṃ kāmāt prāyaścittaṃ vinirdiśet ।। tataścarati nirdeśāt kṛcchraṃ cānte samāhitaḥ ।।
na dharmayuktamanṛtaṃ hinastīti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। ahorātropavāsaś ca prāṇāyāmaśataṃ tathā ।। paramāpadgatenāpi na kāryaṃ steyamapyuta ।। hiṃsā hyeṣā parā sṛṣṭā stainyaṃ vai kathitaṃ tathā ।।
sa tasya harate prāṇān yo yasya harate dhanam ।। bhūyo nirvedamāpannaś careccāndrāyaṇaṃ vratam ।। punarnirvedamāpannaś caredbhikṣuratandritaḥ ।। akāmādapi hiṃseta yadi bhikṣuḥ paśūn kṛmīn ।।
skandedindriyadaurbalyāt striyaṃ dṛṣṭvā yatiryadi ।। divā skannasya viprasya prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate ।। rātrau skannaḥ śuciḥ snātvā dvādaśaiva tu dhāraṇā ।। ekānnaṃ madhumāṃsaṃ vā aśṛtānnaṃ tathaiva ca ।।
ekaikātikramātteṣāṃ prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate ।। vyatikramāś ca ye kecid vāṅmanaḥkāyasaṃbhavāḥ ।। sadbhiḥ saha viniścitya yadbrūyustatsamācaret ।। sthānaṃ dhruvaṃ śāśvatamavyayaṃ tu paraṃ hi gatvā na punarhi jāyate ।।
yena jñānaviśeṣeṇa mṛtyuṃ paśyanti yoginaḥ ।। yo na paśyenna jīvetsa naraḥ saṃvatsarātparam ।। yaḥ paśyati na jīvedvai māsādekādaśātparam ।। pratyakṣamathavā svapne daśamāsānna jīvati ।।
paśyet pretapiśācāṃś ca navamāsān sa jīvati ।। prakṛteś ca nivarteta cāṣṭau māsāṃś ca jīvati ।। pāṃsuke kardame vāpi saptamāsānsa jīvati ।। kravyādo vā khago yasya ṣaṇmāsān nātivartate ।।
svacchāyāṃ vikṛtāṃ paśyec catuḥpañca sa jīvati ।। udake dhanur aindraṃ vā trīṇi dvau vā sa jīvati ।। aśiraskaṃ tathā paśyen māsād ūrdhvaṃ na jīvati ।। mṛtyurhyupāgatastasya ardhamāsānna jīvati ।।
dhūmaṃ vā mastakātpaśyed daśāhānna sa jīvati ।। adbhiḥ spṛṣṭo na hṛṣyeta tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ ।। gāyannṛtyan vrajet svapne vidyānmṛtyurupasthitaḥ ।। yaṃ nayeddakṣiṇāmāśāṃ svapne so api na jīvati ।।
nagnaṃ vā śramaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā vidyānmṛtyumupasthitam ।। dṛṣṭvā tu tādṛśaṃ svapnaṃ sadya eva na jīvati ।। paśyedyo daśarātraṃ tu na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ ।। pāṣāṇaistāḍyate svapne yaḥ sadyo na sa jīvati ।।
krośantyabhimukhaṃ pretya sa gatāyurbhavennaraḥ ।। jāyate dantaharṣaś ca taṃ gatāyuṣamādiśet ।। dīpagandhaṃ ca nāghrāti vidyānmṛtyum upasthitam ।। paranetreṣu cātmānaṃ na paśyenna sa jīvati ।।
vakrā ca nāsā bhavati vijñeyo gatajīvitaḥ ।। gaṇḍe vā piṇḍikārakte tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ ।। yāmyāmabhimukhaṃ gacchet tadantaṃ tasya jīvitam ।। śvetā ca mūrtirhyasakṛt tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ ।।
yasya so api na jīvettu dakṣiṇābhimukho gataḥ ।। ghoṣaṃ na śṛṇuyātkarṇe jyotir netre na paśyati ।। na cottiṣṭhati yaḥ śvabhrāt tadantaṃ tasya jīvitam ।। ūrdhvā ca dṛṣṭirna ca sampratiṣṭhā raktā punaḥ samparivartamānā ।
mukhasya śoṣaḥ suṣirā ca nābhiratyuṣṇamūtro viṣamastha eva ।। hantāraṃ na ca paśyecca sa gatāyurna jīvati ।। smṛtiṃ nopalabheccāpi tadantaṃ tasya jīvitam ।। kṛṣṇaṃ raktamapi svapne tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ ।।
tyaktvā khedaṃ viṣādaṃ ca upekṣed buddhimān naraḥ ।। same atisthāvare deśe vivikte jantuvarjite ।। svastikenopaviṣṭastu namaskṛtvā maheśvaram ।। yathā dīpo nivātastho neṅgate sopamā smṛtā ।।
kāmaṃ vitarkaṃ prītiṃ ca sukhaduḥkhe ubhe tathā ।। ghrāṇe ca rasane nityaṃ cakṣuṣī sparśane tathā ।। kālakarmāṇi vijñāya samūheṣveva nityaśaḥ ।। śatamardhaśataṃ vāpi dhāraṇāṃ mūrdhni dhārayet ।।
tataścāpūrayed deham oṅkāreṇa samanvitaḥ ।। ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi oṅkāraprāptilakṣaṇam ।। prathamā vidyutī mātrā dvitīyā tāmasī smṛtā ।। gāndhārī caiva vijñeyā gāndhārasvarasaṃbhavā ।।
yathā prayukta oṅkāraḥ pratiniryāti mūrdhani ।। praṇavo dhanuḥ śaro hyātmā brahmalakṣaṇamucyate ।। omityekākṣaraṃ hyetad guhāyāṃ nihitaṃ padam ।। viṣṇukramāstrayastvete ṛksāmāni yajūṃṣi ca ।।
tatprayuktastu yo yogī tasya sālokyamāpnuyāt ।। makārasahitauṃkāras trimātra iti saṃjñitaḥ ।। savyañjano makārastu svarloka iti gīyate ।। bhuvanāṅgaṃ ca tatsarvaṃ brāhmaṃ tatpadamucyate ।।
evaṃ jñānaviśeṣeṇa tatpadaṃ samupāsyate ।। upāsyaṃ hi prayatnena śāśvataṃ sukhamicchatā ।। tataḥ plutavatī caiva tṛtīyā copadiśyate ।। yāvadeva tu śakyante dhāryante tāvadeva hi ।।
ardhaṃ tanmātram api cec chṛṇu yat phalamāpnuyāt ।। tena yatprāpyate puṇyaṃ mātrayā tadavāpnuyāt ।। yatphalaṃ prāpyate samyaṅ mātrayā tadavāpnuyāt ।। eṣā eva bhavetkāryā gṛhasthānāṃ tu yoginām ।।
aṇimādye tu vijñeyā tasmādyuñjīta tāṃ dvijāḥ ।। ātmānaṃ vidyate yastu sa sarvaṃ vindate dvijāḥ ।। ātmānaṃ jānate ye tu śucayaste na saṃśayaḥ ।। yogajñānādavāpnoti brāhmaṇo adhyātmacintakaḥ ।।
yonisaṃkramaṇaṃ tyaktvā yāti vai śāśvataṃ padam ।। namaskāreṇa rudrasya tathā pāpaṃ praṇaśyati ।। anyadevanamaskārān na tatphalamavāpnuyāt ।। daśavistārakaṃ brahma tathā ca brahmavistaraiḥ ।।
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ samuddhṛtya kulatrayam ।। avimukteśvaraṃ gatvā vārāṇasyāṃ tu śodhanam ।। śrīparvate vā viprendrāḥ saṃtyajetsvatanuṃ naraḥ ।। avimuktaṃ paraṃ kṣetraṃ jantūnāṃ muktidaṃ sadā ।।
seveta satataṃ dhīmān viśeṣānmaraṇāntike ।। vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ tatprabhāvaṃ hi sāṃpratam ।। vistareṇa yathānyāyaṃ śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। avimuktasya māhātmyaṃ yathāha bhagavān bhavaḥ ।।
śakyate naiva viprendrā varṣakoṭiśatairapi ।। himavacchikharāddevyā haimavatyā gaṇeśvaraiḥ ।। avimukteśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ vāsaṃ tatra cakāra saḥ ।। tuṅgeśvare ca kedāre tatsthāne yo yatirbhavet ।।
tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya caret pāśupataṃ vratam ।। manasā nirmame rudro vimānaṃ ca suśobhanam ।। haimavatyāḥ svayaṃ devaḥ sanandī parameśvaraḥ ।। uktavānparameśānaḥ pārvatyāḥ prītaye bhavaḥ ।।
virūḍhapuṣpaiḥ paritaḥ priyaṅgubhiḥ supuṣpitaiḥ kaṇṭakitaiś ca ketakaiḥ ।। aśokapunnāgaśataiḥ supuṣpitair dvirephamālākulapuṣpasaṃcayaiḥ ।। vināditaṃ sārasacakravākaiḥ pramattadātyūhavaraiś ca sarvataḥ ।। kvacicca mattālikulākulīkṛtaṃ madākulābhir bhramarāṅganādibhiḥ ।।
latopagūḍhaistilakaiś ca gūḍhaṃ pragītavidyādharasiddhacāraṇam ।। pranṛttahārītakulopanāditaṃ mṛgendranādākulamattamānasaiḥ ।। praphullanānāvidhacārupaṅkajaiḥ sarastaḍāgairupaśobhitaṃ kvacit ।। kusumitataruśākhālīnamattadvirephaṃ navakisalayaśobhāśobhitaṃ prāṃśuśākham ।।
kvacicca dantakṣatacāruvīrudhaṃ kvacillatāliṅgitacāruvṛkṣakam । kvacidvilāsālasagāminībhir niṣevitaṃ kiṃpuruṣāṅganābhiḥ ।। ākīrṇapuṣpanikarapravibhaktahaṃsair vibhrājitaṃ tridaśadivyakulairanekaiḥ ।। mārgāntarākalitapuṣpavicitrapaṅktisambaddhagulmaviṭapair vividhairupetam ।।
rātrau candrasya bhāsā kusumitatilakairekatāṃ samprayātaṃ chāyāsuptaprabuddhasthitahariṇakulāluptadūrvāṅkurāgram ।। māyūraiḥ pakṣacandraiḥ kvacidavanigatai rañjitakṣmāpradeśaṃ deśe deśe vilīnapramuditavilasanmattahārītavṛndam ।। hṛṣṭābhiḥ kvacidapi kinnarāṅganābhir vīṇābhiḥ sumadhuragītanṛttakaṇṭham ।। ā mūlāt phalanicitaiḥ kvacidviśālair uttuṅgaiḥ panasamahīruhairupetam ।।
phullātimuktakalatāgṛhanītasiddhasiddhāṅganākanakanūpurarāvaramyam । ramyaṃ priyaṅgutarumañjarisaktabhṛṅgaṃ bhṛṅgāvalīkavalitāmrakadambapuṣpam ।। gulmāntaraprasabhabhītamṛgīsamūhaṃ vāteritaṃ tanubhṛtāmapavargadātṛ ।। cāmīkaradyutisamairatha karṇikāraiḥ puṣpotkarairupacitaṃ suviśālaśākhaiḥ ।।
kvacitkāñcanasaṃkāśaiḥ puṣpair ācitabhūtalam ।। ramyopāntaklamahārabhavanaṃ phullābjeṣu bhramaravilasitam ।। vividhataruviśālaṃ mattahṛṣṭānnapuṣṭair upavanam atiramyaṃ darśayāmāsa devyāḥ ।। sā cāpyenaṃ tuhinagirisutā śaṅkaraṃ devadevaṃ puṣpairdivyaiḥ śubhataratamair bhūṣayāmāsa bhaktyā ।।
gaṇeśvarair nandimukhaiś ca sārdham uvāca devaṃ praṇipatya devī ।। kṣetrasya ca guṇānsarvān punarme vaktumarhasi ।। vaktumarhasi deveśa devadeva vṛṣadhvaja ।। āghrāya vadanāmbhojaṃ tadāha girijāṃ hasan ।।
sarveṣāmeva jantūnāṃ heturmokṣasya sarvadā ।। nānāliṅgadharā nityaṃ mama lokābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।। nānāvṛkṣasamākīrṇe nānāvihagaśobhite ।। apsarogaṇagandharvaiḥ sadā saṃsevite śubhe ।।
manmanā mama bhaktaś ca mayi nityārpitakriyaḥ ।। kāmaṃ hyatra mṛto devi janturmokṣāya kalpate ।। brahmādayo vijānanti ye ca siddhā mumukṣavaḥ ।। vimuktaṃ na mayā yasmān mokṣyate vā kadācana ।।
naimiṣe ca kurukṣetre gaṅgādvāre ca puṣkare ।। iha samprāpyate yena tata etadviśiṣyate ।। prayāgādapi tīrthāgryād avimuktamidaṃ śubham ।। kṣetratīrthopaniṣadaṃ na vidurbudhasattamāḥ ।।
avimukte tyajetprāṇān janturmokṣāya kalpate ।। na tu śakrasahasratvaṃ svarge kāśīpurīṃ vinā ।। jaigīṣavyaḥ parāṃ siddhiṃ gato yatra mahātapāḥ ।। jaigīṣavyaguhā śreṣṭhā yogināṃ sthānamiṣyate ।।
kaivalyaṃ paramaṃ yāti devānāmapi durlabham ।। iha samprāpyate mokṣo durlabho anyatra karhicit ।। ātmanaścaiva sāyujyam īpsitaṃ sthānameva ca ।। kṣetrasaṃsevanādeva gaṇeśatvamavāpa ha ।।
ihaivārādhya māṃ devi siddhiṃ yāsyatyanuttamām ।। mama bhakto bhaviṣyaś ca vedasaṃsthāpravartakaḥ ।। brahmā devarṣibhiḥ sārddhaṃ viṣṇurvāpi divākaraḥ ।। upāsate mahātmānaḥ sarve māmiha suvrate ।।
ananyamanaso bhūtvā māmihopāsate sadā ।। iha kṣetre mṛtaḥ so api saṃsāre na punarbhavet ।। vratinaś ca nirārambhāḥ sarve te mayi bhāvitāḥ ।। gatā iha paraṃ mokṣaṃ prasādānmama suvrate ।।
tamihaiva paraṃ mokṣaṃ prasādānmama suvrate ।। kailāsabhavanaṃ cātra paśya divyaṃ varānane ।। na durgatimavāpnoti kalmaṣaiś ca vimucyate ।। gavāṃ stanyajatoyena tīrthaṃ puṇyatamaṃ mahat ।।
sānnidhyaṃ kṛtavān devi sadāhaṃ dṛśyate tvayā ।। sarvairdevairahaṃ devi asmindeśe prasāditaḥ ।। atrāhaṃ brahmaṇānīya sthāpitaḥ parameṣṭhinā ।। brahmaṇāpi tato viṣṇuḥ proktaḥ saṃvignacetasā ।।
tamuvāca punar viṣṇur brahmāṇaṃ kupitānanam ।। mayaiva sthāpitaṃ liṅgaṃ tava nāmnā bhaviṣyati ।। dṛṣṭvainamapi deveśaṃ mama lokaṃ vrajennaraḥ ।। sthāpayāmāsa vidhivad bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ ।।
prāṇān iha narastyaktvā na punarjāyate kvacit ।। asminnapi mayā deśe daityo daivatakaṇṭakaḥ ।। vyāghreśvara iti khyāto nityamatrāhamāsthitaḥ ।। utpalo vidalaścaiva yau daityau brahmaṇā purā ।।
sāvajñaṃ kandukenātra tasyedaṃ dehamāsthitam ।। jyeṣṭhasthānamidaṃ tasmād etanme puṇyadarśanam ।। dṛṣṭvāpi niyato martyo dehabhede gaṇo bhavet ।। mama priyahitaṃ sthānaṃ jñātvā liṅgaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।।
dṛṣṭvaitanmanujo devi na durgatimato vrajet ।। kṣetrametad alaṃkṛtya jāhnavyā saha saṃgatā ।। saṃgameśvaram ityevaṃ khyātaṃ jagati dṛśyatām ।। arcayet saṃgameśvaraṃ tasya janmabhayaṃ kutaḥ ।।
kṣetramadhye ca yatrāhaṃ svayaṃ bhūtvāgramāsthitaḥ ।। siddhānāṃ sthānametaddhi madīyavratadhāriṇām ।। dṛṣṭvainaṃ madhyameśānaṃ janma prati na śocati ।। nāmnā śukreśvaraṃ nāma sarvasiddhāmarārcitam ।।
mṛtaś ca na punarjantuḥ saṃsārī tu bhavennaraḥ ।। brahmaṇo hi varaṃ labdhvā gomāyurbandhaśaṅkitaḥ ।। adyāpi jagati khyātaṃ surāsuranamaskṛtam ।। grahaiḥ śukrapurogaiś ca etāni sthāpitāni ha ।।
evametāni puṇyāni mannivāsāni pārvati ।। catuḥkrośaṃ caturdikṣu kṣetrametatprakīrtitam ।। mahālayagiristhaṃ māṃ kedāre ca vyavasthitam ।। gāṇapatyaṃ labhedyasmād yataḥ sā muktiruttamā ।।
smṛtaṃ puṇyatamaṃ kṣetram avimuktaṃ varānane ।। mama puṇyāni bhūrloke tebhyaḥ śreṣṭhatamaṃ tvidam ।। kadācinna mayā muktam avimuktaṃ tato abhavat ।। sadyaḥ pāpavinirmuktaḥ paśupāśairvimucyate ।।
hiraṇyagarbham īśānaṃ goprekṣaṃ vṛṣabhadhvajam ।। śukreśvaraṃ ca vikhyātaṃ vyāghreśaṃ jambukeśvaram ।। evam uktvā mahādevo diśaḥ sarvā vyalokayat ।। akasmādabhavatsarvaḥ sa deśojjvalito yathā ।।
māheśvarā mahātmānas tathā vai niyatavratāḥ ।। punarnirīkṣya yogeśaṃ dhyānayogaṃ ca kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। sthitānāṃ sa tadā teṣāṃ devadeva umāpatiḥ ।। kṛtsnaṃ jagadihaikasthaṃ kartum anta iva sthitaḥ ।।
na śaśāka punardraṣṭuṃ hṛṣṭaromā girīndrajā ।। prakṛtermūrtimāsthāya yogena parameśvarī ।। tataste layamādhāya yoginaḥ puruṣasya tu ।। pañcākṣarasya vai bījaṃ saṃsmarantaḥ suśobhanam ।।
nīlalohitamūrtisthaṃ punaścakre vapuḥ śubham ।। stuvatī caraṇau natvā ka ime bhagavanniti ।। madīyaṃ vratamāśritya bhaktimadbhir dvijottamaiḥ ।। kṣetrasyāsya prabhāvena bhaktyā ca mama bhāmini ।।
tasmād etan mahat kṣetraṃ brahmādyaiḥ sevitaṃ tathā ।। pratimāsaṃ tathāṣṭamyāṃ pratimāsaṃ caturdaśīm ।। śaśibhānūparāge ca kārtikyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।। pṛthivyāṃ sarvatīrthāni vārāṇasyāṃ tu jāhnavīm ।।
pituste girirājasya śubhāṃ himavataḥ sutām ।। bhajante sarvato abhyetya ye tāñchṛṇu varānane ।। puṣkaraṃ nimiṣaṃ caiva prayāgaṃ ca pṛthūdakam ।। kṣetrāṇi sarvato devi devatā ṛṣayas tathā ।।
samudrāḥ sapta caivātra devatīrthāni kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। avimukteśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā caiva triviṣṭapam ।। bhavanti hi sureśāni sarvaparvasu parvasu ।। avimuktaṃ kṣetravaraṃ mahāpāpanibarhaṇam ।।
kedāre caiva yalliṅgaṃ yacca liṅgaṃ mahālaye ।। śaṅkukarṇeśvaraṃ caiva gokarṇau ca tathā hyubhau ।। sthāneśvaraṃ tathaikāgraṃ kāleśvaram ajeśvaram ।। amareśaṃ mahākālaṃ jyotiṣaṃ bhasmagātrakam ।।
aṣṭaṣaṣṭisamākhyāni rūḍhānyanyāni kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। sarvaparvasu puṇyeṣu guhyaṃ caitadudāhṛtam ।। snātasya caiva gaṅgāyāṃ dṛṣṭena ca mayā śubhe ।। sadya eva samāpnoti kiṃ tataḥ paramādbhutam ।।
parātparataraṃ devī budhyasveti mayoditam ।। tena muktaṃ mayā juṣṭam avimuktam ata ucyate ।। sudṛṣṭaṃ kuru deveśi avimuktaṃ gṛhaṃ mama ।। darśayāmāsa bhagavān śrīparvatamanuttamam ।।
sarvagatvācca sarvatvāt sarvātmā sadasanmayaḥ ।। kṣetrāṇi darśayāmāsa sarvabhūtapatirbhavaḥ ।। āśāliṅgaṃ ca deveśaṃ divyaṃ yacca bileśvaram ।। dakṣiṇadvārapārśve tu kuṇḍaleśvaramīśvaram ।।
vivṛddhaṃ giriṇā sārdhaṃ devadevanamaskṛtam ।। amareśvaraṃ ca varadaṃ devaiḥ pūrvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।। karmeśvaraṃ ca vipulaṃ kāryārthaṃ brahmaṇā kṛtam ।। ajena nirmitaṃ divyaṃ sākṣādajabilaṃ śubham ।।
tatra śṛṅgāṭakākāraṃ śṛṅgāṭācalamadhyame ।। mallikārjunakaṃ caiva mama vāsamidaṃ śubham ।। gajeśvaraṃ ca vaiśākhaṃ kapoteśvaramavyayam ।। sevitaṃ devi paśyādya sarvasmādadhikaṃ śubham ।।
uttare sthāpitaṃ caiva viṣṇunā caiva śailajam ।। paścime parvate paśya brahmeśvaramaleśvaram ।। ityuktvā tadgṛhe tiṣṭhad alaṃgṛhamiti smṛtam ।। kadambeśvaram etaddhi skandenaiva pratiṣṭhitam ।।
devaiḥ sarvaistu śakrādyaiḥ sthāpitāni varānane ।। tathā hārapure devi tava hāre nipātite ।। śivarudrapure caiva tatkāyopari suvrate ।। alaṃkṛtaṃ mayā brahma purastān munibhiḥ saha ।।
caṇḍikānirmitaṃ sthānam aṃbikātīrtham uttamam ।। eteṣu devi sthāneṣu tīrtheṣu vividheṣu ca ।। śrīśaile saṃtyajed dehaṃ brāhmaṇo dagdhakilbiṣaḥ ।। mahāsnānaṃ ca yaḥ kuryād ghṛtena vidhinaiva tu ।।
snānaṃ palaśataṃ jñeyam abhyaṅgaṃ pañcaviṃśati ।। snāpya liṅgaṃ madīyaṃ tu gavyenaiva ghṛtena ca ।। saṃmārjya śatayajñānāṃ snānena prayutaṃ tathā ।। mahāsnāne prasaktaṃ tu snānamaṣṭaguṇaṃ smṛtam ।।
anulepanaṃ tu tat sarvaṃ pañcaviṃśatpalena vai ।। anyānyapi ca puṣpāṇi bilvapatraṃ na saṃtyajet ।। daśadroṇais tu naivedyam aṣṭadroṇairathāpi vā ।। vittahīnasya viprasya nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।।
vāditrairvividhaiścānyair ninādairvividhairapi ।। sa bhṛtyaputradāraiś ca tathā saṃbandhibāndhavaiḥ ।। dravyahīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ śraddhāhīnaṃ sureśvara ।। ityuktvā vai japedrudraṃ tvaritaṃ śāntimeva ca ।।
sa evaṃ sarvatīrtheṣu sarvayajñeṣu yatphalam ।। tathaiva mama sāyujyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। ye na kurvanti te bhaktā na bhavanti na saṃśayaḥ ।। avimukteśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ payasā ca ghṛtena ca ।।
avimukte ca tapasā mandarasya mahātmanaḥ ।। tatrāndhakaṃ mahādaityaṃ hiraṇyākṣasutaṃ prabhuḥ ।। etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ kathāsarvasvamādarāt ।। sarvakṣetreṣu yatpuṇyaṃ tatsarvaṃ sahasā labhet ।।
sa eva sarvayajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।। damitastu kathaṃ lebhe gāṇapatyaṃ maheśvarāt ।। andhakānugrahaṃ caiva mandare śoṣaṇaṃ tathā ।। hiraṇyākṣasya tanayo hiraṇyanayanopamaḥ ।।
prasādādbrahmaṇaḥ sākṣād avadhyatvamavāpya ca ।। līlayā cāprayatnena trāsayāmāsa vāsavam ।। viviśurmandaraṃ bhītā nārāyaṇapurogamāḥ ।। yadṛcchayā giriṃ prāpto mandaraṃ cārukandaram ।।
drutaṃ cālpavīryaprabhinnāṅgabhinnā vayaṃ daityarājasya śastrairnikṛttāḥ ।। gaṇeśvaraiś ca bhagavān andhakābhimukhaṃ yayau ।। tatrendrapadmodbhavaviṣṇumukhyāḥ sureśvarā vipravarāś ca sarve । jayeti vācā bhagavantam ūcuḥ kirīṭabaddhāñjalayaḥ samantāt ।।
bhasmīkṛtya mahādevo nirbibhedāndhakaṃ tadā ।। dṛṣṭvāndhakaṃ nanādeśaṃ praṇamya sa pitāmahaḥ ।। nanṛturmunayaḥ sarve mumudurgaṇapuṅgavāḥ ।। trailokyamakhilaṃ harṣān nananda ca nanāda ca ।।
sāttvikaṃ bhāvamāsthāya cintayāmāsa cetasā ।। ārādhito mayā śaṃbhuḥ purā sākṣānmaheśvaraḥ ।। yaḥ smarenmanasā rudraṃ prāṇānte sakṛdeva vā ।। brahmā ca bhagavānviṣṇuḥ sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ ।।
evaṃ saṃcintya tuṣṭātmā so andhakaś cāndhakārdanam ।। prārthitastena bhagavān paramārtiharo haraḥ ।। provāca dānavaṃ prekṣya ghṛṇayā nīlalohitaḥ ।। varānvaraya daityendra varado ahaṃ tavāndhaka ।।
harṣagadgadayā vācā provācedaṃ maheśvaram ।। tvayi bhaktiḥ prasīdeśa yadi deyo varaś ca me ।। pradadau durlabhāṃ śraddhāṃ daityendrāya mahādyutiḥ ।। praṇemustaṃ surendrādyā gāṇapatye pratiṣṭhitam ।।
viṣṇunā sūdito viṣṇur vārāhatvaṃ kathaṃ gataḥ ।। etatsarvaṃ viśeṣeṇa sūta vaktumihārhasi ।। purāndhakāsureśasya pitā kālāntakopamaḥ ।। nītvā rasātalaṃ cakre vandīm indīvaraprabhām ।।
bādhitāstāḍitā baddhvā hiraṇyākṣeṇa tena vai ।। praṇamya śirasā viṣṇuṃ daityakoṭivimardanam ।। śrutvaitadbhagavān viṣṇur dharaṇībandhanaṃ hariḥ ।। daityaiś ca sārdhaṃ daityendraṃ hiraṇyākṣaṃ mahābalam ।।
kalpādiṣu yathāpūrvaṃ praviśya ca rasātalam ।। tatas tuṣṭāva deveśaṃ devadevaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। śāśvatāya varāhāya daṃṣṭriṇe daṇḍine namaḥ ।। kartre netre surendrāṇāṃ śāstre ca sakalasya ca ।।
tvayā kṛtaṃ sarvamidaṃ prasīda sureśa lokeśa varāha viṣṇo ।। hatāḥ kṣaṇāt kāmada daityamukhyāḥ svadaṃṣṭrakoṭyā saha putrabhṛtyaiḥ ।। dharādharaiḥ sarvajanaiḥ samudraiḥ surāsuraiḥ sevitacandravaktra ।। aho pradattastu varaḥ prasīda vāgdevatā vārijasaṃbhavāya ।।
tava romṇi sakalāmareśvarānayanadvaye śaśiravī padadvaye । nihitā rasātalagatā vasuṃdharā tava pṛṣṭhataḥ sakalatārakādayaḥ ।। abaloddhṛtā ca bhagavaṃstavaiva sakalaṃ tvayaiva hi dhṛtaṃ jagadguro ।। vividhānvarān harimukhāttu labdhavān harinābhivārijadehabhṛt svayam ।।
mūrdhnyāropya namaścakruś cakriṇaḥ saṃnidhau tadā ।। kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakāryeṇa śatahastena viṣṇunā ।। lokānāṃ dhāriṇī tvaṃ hi mṛttike hara pātakam ।। tvayā hatena pāpena jīvāmastvatprasādataḥ ।।
varāhadaṃṣṭrābhinnāyāṃ dharāyāṃ mṛttikāṃ dvijāḥ ।। āyuṣmān balavān dhanyaḥ putrapautrasamanvitaḥ ।। atha deve gate tyaktvā varāhe kṣīrasāgaram ।। tasya daṃṣṭrābharākrāntā devadevasya dhīmataḥ ।।
daṃṣṭrāṃ jagrāha dṛṣṭvā tāṃ bhūṣaṇārthamathātmanaḥ ।। devāś ca tuṣṭuvuḥ sendrā devadevasya vaibhavam ।। bhūtānāṃ saṃplave cāpi viṣṇoścaiva kalevaram ।। vibhuraṅgavibhāgena bhūṣito na yadi prabhuḥ ।।
kathaṃ vimuktirviprāṇāṃ tasmāddaṃṣṭrī maheśvaraḥ ।। kathaṃ niṣūditastena hiraṇyakaśipurvada ।। dharmajñaḥ satyasampannas tapasvī cābhavatsudhīḥ ।। sarvajñaṃ sarvagaṃ viṣṇuṃ sarvadevabhavodbhavam ।।
brahmaṇo adhipatiṃ sṛṣṭisthitisaṃhārakāraṇam ।। namo nārāyaṇāyeti govindeti muhurmuhuḥ ।। na māṃ jānāsi durbuddhe sarvadaityāmareśvaram ।। ko viṣṇuḥ padmajo vāpi śakraś ca varuṇo athavā ।।
māmevārcaya bhaktyā ca svalpaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ sadā ।। śrutvāpi tasya vacanaṃ hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sudhīḥ ।। namo nārāyaṇāyeti sarvadaityakumārakān ।। durlaṅghyāṃ cātmano dṛṣṭvā śakrādibhir api svayam ।।
etaṃ nānāvidhairvadhyaṃ duṣputraṃ hantumarhatha ।। nijaghnurdevadevasya bhṛtyaṃ prahrādamavyayam ।। kṣīravārinidhiśāyinaḥ prabhor niṣphalaṃ tvatha babhūva tejasā ।। tatraivāvirabhūddhantuṃ nṛsiṃhākṛtimāsthitaḥ ।।
bibheda tatkṣaṇādeva karajair niśitaiḥ śataiḥ ।। pīḍayāmāsa daityendraṃ yugāntāgnirivāparaḥ ।। ā brahmabhuvanād viprāḥ pracacāla ca suvratāḥ ।। dhairyaṃ balaṃ ca samavāpya yayurvisṛjya ā diṅmukhāntam asurakṣaṇatatparāś ca ।।
sahasrekṣaṇaḥ somasūryāgninetras tadā saṃsthitaḥ sarvamāvṛtya māyī ।। sabrahmakāḥ sasādhyāś ca sayamāḥ samarudgaṇāḥ ।। jyotiṣāṃ tu paraṃ jyotiḥ paramātmā jaganmayaḥ ।। vāgatīto nirālaṃbo nirdvandvo nirupaplavaḥ ।।
bhavānmatsyākṛtiḥ kaurmam āsthāya jagati sthitaḥ ।। devānāṃ devarakṣārthaṃ nihatya ditijeśvaram ।। na dṛṣṭaṃ yattvadanyaṃ hi bhavān sarvaṃ carācaram ।। bhavānādirbhavānanto bhavāneva vayaṃ vibho ।।
māyayā bahudhā saṃstham advitīyamayaṃ prabho ।। stuto api vividhaiḥ stutyair bhāvairnānāvidhaiḥ prabhuḥ ।। yo nṛsiṃhastavaṃ bhaktyā paṭhedvārthaṃ vicārayet ।। tadantare śivaṃ devāḥ sendrāḥ sabrahmakāḥ prabhum ।।
tato brahmādayastūrṇaṃ saṃstūya parameśvaram ।। mandarasthaṃ mahādevaṃ krīḍamānaṃ sahomayā ।। praṇamya daṇḍavadbhūmau tuṣṭāva parameśvaram ।। namaḥ śivāya rudrāya śaṅkarāya śivāya te ।।
namaḥ śivāya śarvāya śaṅkarāyārttihāriṇe ।। antakāya namastubhyam umāyāḥ pataye namaḥ ।। śarvāya sarvarūpāya puruṣāya namonamaḥ ।। nityāya viśvarūpāya jāyamānāya te namaḥ ।।
rudrāya nīlarudrāya kadrudrāya pracetase ।। mīḍhuṣṭamāya devāya śitikaṇṭhāya te namaḥ ।। tārāya ca sutārāya tāraṇāya namonamaḥ ।। devānāṃ śaṃbhave tubhyaṃ bhūtānāṃ śaṃbhave namaḥ ।।
kapardine namastubhyaṃ kālakaṇṭhāya te namaḥ ।। bhasmadigdhaśarīrāya daṇḍamuṇḍīśvarāya ca ।। nama ugratriśūlāya ugrāya ca namo namaḥ ।। agrevadhāya vai bhūtvā namo dūrevadhāya ca ।।
cakriṇe varmiṇe nityaṃ daityānāṃ karmabhedine ।। vāmāya vāmarūpāya vāmanetrāya te namaḥ ।। aghorarūpāya vikaṭāya vikaṭaśarīrāya te namaḥ । puruṣarūpāya puruṣaikatatpuruṣāya vai namaḥ ।।
īśānāya namastubhyam īśvarāya namonamaḥ ।। sarvaviṣṇurnṛsiṃhasya rūpamāsthāya viśvakṛt ।। daityendrairbahubhiḥ sārdhaṃ hitārthaṃ jagatāṃ prabhuḥ ।। yatkṛtyamatra deveśa tatkuruṣva bhavāniha ।।
kālakūṭādivapuṣā trāhi naḥ śaraṇāgatān ।। tavonmeṣanimeṣābhyām asmākaṃ pralayodayau ।। saṃtaptāsmo vayaṃ deva hariṇāmitatejasā ।। vijñāpitas tathā devaḥ prahasanprāha tān surān ।।
so api śakraḥ suraiḥ sārdhaṃ praṇipatya yathāgatam ।। athotthāya mahādevaḥ śārabhaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ ।। apahṛtya tadā prāṇān śarabhaḥ surapūjitaḥ ।। evaṃ stutastadā devair jagāma sa yathākramam ।।
rudralokamanuprāpya rudreṇa saha modate ।। śarabhākhyaṃ mahāghoraṃ vikṛtaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ ।। evamabhyarthito devair matiṃ cakre kṛpālayaḥ ।। tadarthaṃ smṛtavān rudro vīrabhadraṃ mahābalam ।।
ājagāma purā sadyo gaṇānāmagrato hasan ।। nṛsiṃharūpairatyugraiḥ koṭibhiḥ parivāritaḥ ।। krīḍadbhiś ca mahādhīrair brahmādyaiḥ kandukairiva ।। kalpāntajvalanajvālo vilasallocanatrayaḥ ।।
bālendudvitayākāratīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrāṅkuradvayaḥ ।। mahāpracaṇḍahuṅkārabadhirīkṛtadiṅmukhaḥ ।। vādakhaṇḍam akhaṇḍābhyāṃ bhrāmayaṃstriśikhaṃ muhuḥ ।। svayaṃ vijñāpayāmāsa kimatra smṛtikāraṇam ।।
akāle bhayamutpannaṃ devānāmapi bhairava ।। sāntvayan bodhayādau taṃ tena kiṃ nopaśāmyati ।। sūkṣmaṃ sūkṣmeṇa saṃhṛtya sthūlaṃ sthūlena tejasā ।। ityādiṣṭo gaṇādhyakṣaḥ praśāntavapurāsthitaḥ ।।
tatastaṃ bodhayāmāsa vīrabhadro haro harim ।। jagatsukhāya bhagavann avatīrṇo asi mādhava ।। jantucakraṃ bhagavatā rakṣitaṃ matsyarūpiṇā ।। bibharṣi kūrmarūpeṇa vārāheṇoddhṛtā mahī ।।
vāmanena balirbaddhas tvayā vikramatā punaḥ ।। yadā yadā hi lokasya duḥkhaṃ kiṃcit prajāyate ।। nādhikastvatsamo apyasti hare śivaparāyaṇa ।। yadartham avatāro ayaṃ nihataḥ so api keśava ।।
upasaṃhara viśvātmaṃs tvameva mama saṃnidhau ।। tato adhikaṃ mahāghoraṃ kopaṃ prajvālayaddhariḥ ।। idānīṃ saṃhariṣyāmi jagadetaccarācaram ।। śāsitaṃ mama sarvatra śāstā ko api na vidyate ।।
ahaṃ hi sarvaśaktīnāṃ pravartakanivartakaḥ ।। tattadviddhi gaṇādhyakṣa mama tejovijṛmbhitam ।। madaṃśāḥ śaktisampannā brahmaśakrādayaḥ surāḥ ।। tallalāṭasamutpanno bhagavānvṛṣabhadhvajaḥ ।।
ahaṃ niyantā sarvasya matparaṃ nāsti daivatam ।। idaṃ tu matparaṃ tejaḥ kaḥ punaḥ śrotumicchati ।। avehi paramaṃ bhāvam idaṃ bhūtamaheśvaraḥ ।। mṛtyormṛtyuṃ viddhi māṃ vīrabhadra jīvantyete matprasādena devāḥ ।।
vihasyovāca sāvajñaṃ tato visphuritādharaḥ ।। asadvādo vivādaś ca vināśastvayi kevalaḥ ।। kṛtāni yena kenāpi kathāśeṣo bhaviṣyati ।। tena saṃhāradakṣeṇa kṣaṇātsaṃkṣayameṣyasi ।।
tvannābhipaṅkajājjātaḥ pañcavaktraḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। lalāṭe cintayāmāsa tapasyugre vyavasthitaḥ ।। aṃśo ahaṃ devadevasya mahābhairavarūpiṇaḥ ।। evaṃ rakṣo vidāryaiva tvaṃ śaktikalayā yutaḥ ।।
upakāro hyasādhūnām apakārāya kevalam ।। na tvaṃ sraṣṭā na saṃhartā na svatantro hi kutracit ।। adyāpi tava nikṣiptaṃ kapālaṃ kūrmarūpiṇaḥ ।। vismṛtaṃ kiṃ tadaṃśena daṃṣṭrotpātanapīḍitaḥ ।।
dagdho asi yasya śūlāgre viṣvaksenacchalādbhavān ।। adyāpi tava putrasya brahmaṇaḥ pañcamaṃ śiraḥ ।। nirjitastvaṃ dadhīcena saṃgrāme samarudgaṇaḥ ।। cakraṃ vikramato yasya cakrapāṇe tava priyam ।।
te mayā sakalā lokā gṛhītāstvaṃ payonidhau ।। tvadādistambaparyantaṃ rudraśaktivijṛmbhitam ।। tattejaso api māhātmyaṃ yuvāṃ draṣṭuṃ na hi kṣamau ।। dyāvāpṛthivyā indrāgniyamasya varuṇasya ca ।।
kālo asi tvaṃ mahākālaḥ kālakālo maheśvaraḥ ।। sthiradhanvā kṣayo vīro vīro viśvādhikaḥ prabhuḥ ।। śāstāśeṣasya jagato na tvaṃ naivacaturmukhaḥ ।। no cedidānīṃ krodhasya mahābhairavarūpiṇaḥ ।।
ityukto vīrabhadreṇa nṛsiṃhaḥ krodhavihvalaḥ ।। atrāntare mahāghoraṃ vipakṣabhayakāraṇam ।। vīrabhadrasya tadrūpaṃ tatkṣaṇādeva dṛśyate ।। na taḍiccandrasadṛśam anaupamyaṃ maheśvaram ।।
tato vyakto mahātejā vyakte saṃbhavatastataḥ ।। tataḥ saṃhārarūpeṇa suvyaktaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। sahasrabāhur jaṭilaś candrārdhakṛtaśekharaḥ ।। atitīkṣṇamahādaṃṣṭro vajratulyanakhāyudhaḥ ।।
yugāntodyatajīmūtabhīmagaṃbhīraniḥsvanaḥ ।। spaṣṭadaṃṣṭro adharoṣṭhaś ca huṅkāreṇa yuto haraḥ ।। bibhrad aurmyaṃ sahasrāṃśor adhaḥ khadyotavibhramam ।। pādāvābadhya pucchena bāhubhyāṃ bāhumaṇḍalam ।।
tato jagāma gaganaṃ devaiḥ saha maharṣibhiḥ ।। utkṣipyotkṣipya saṃgṛhya nipātya ca nipātya ca ।। hariṃ harantaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ viśveśānaṃ tamīśvaram ।। nīyamānaḥ paravaśo dīnavaktraḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ ।।
namo rudrāya śarvāya mahāgrāsāya viṣṇave ।। namo bhavāya śarvāya śaṅkarāya śivāya te ।। vīrāya vīrabhadrāya kṣayadvīrāya śūline ।। ekāya nīlakaṇṭhāya śrīkaṇṭhāya pinākine ।।
parāya parameśāya parātparatarāya te ।। namo viṣṇukalatrāya viṣṇukṣetrāya bhānave ।। bhairavāya śaraṇyāya mahābhairavarūpiṇe ।। mahāpāśaughasaṃhartre viṣṇumāyāntakāriṇe ।।
mṛtyuñjayāya śarvāya sarvajñāya makhāraye ।। mahāghrāṇāya jihvāya prāṇāpānapravartine ।। saṃsārāya pravāhāya mahāyantrapravartine ।। varadāyāvatārāya sarvakāraṇahetave ।।
amoghāyāgninetrāya lakulīśāya śaṃbhave ।। meghavāhāya devāya pārvatīpataye namaḥ ।। sthāṇave kṛttivāsāya namaḥ pañcārthahetave ।। namaste adhvararājāya vayasāṃ pataye namaḥ ।।
sarvātmane namastubhyaṃ namaḥ sarveśvarāya te ।। daśakṛtvastu sāhasrakṛtvaste ca namonamaḥ ।। namonamo namo bhūyaḥ punarbhūyo namonamaḥ ।। punastu prārthayāmāsa nṛsiṃhaḥ śarabheśvaram ।।
tadā tadāpanetavyaṃ tvayaiva parameśvara ।। nanvaśakto bhavān viṣṇo jīvitāntaṃ parājitaḥ ।। śuktiśityaṃ tadā maṅgaṃ vīrabhadraḥ kṣaṇāttataḥ ।। jīvitāḥ smo vayaṃ devāḥ parjanyeneva pādapāḥ ।।
vāto vāti ca so asi tvaṃ mṛtyurdhāvati pañcamaḥ ।। bhagavaṃstvāmeva bhavaṃ vadanti brahmavādinaḥ ।। na viddhi paramaṃ dhāma rūpalāvaṇyavarṇane ।। ekādaśātman bhagavān vartate rūpavān haraḥ ।।
kadācit saṃdihen nāsmāṃs tvaccintāstamayā tathā ।। abhyasaṃhara gamyaṃ te na nītavyaṃ parāparā ।। ghorāpyanyā śivāpyanyā te pratyekamanekadhā ।। bhavatā hi jagatsarvaṃ vyāptaṃ svenaiva tejasā ।।
surāsurāḥ samprasūtās tvattaḥ sarve maheśvara ।। tato nigṛhya ca hariṃ siṃha ity upacetasam ।। ato asmān pāhi bhagavan surān dānair abhīpsitaiḥ ।। yathā jale jalaṃ kṣiptaṃ kṣīraṃ kṣīre ghṛtaṃ ghṛte ।।
eṣa eva nṛsiṃhātmā sadarpaś ca mahābalaḥ ।। yājanīyo namastasmai madbhaktisiddhikāṅkṣibhiḥ ।। apaśyan sarvabhūtānāṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। vaktraṃ tanmuṇḍamālāyāṃ nāyakatvena kalpitam ।।
vismayotphullanayanā jagmuḥ sarve yathāgatam ।। paṭhitvā śṛṇute caiva sarvaduḥkhavināśanam ।। sarvavighnapraśamanaṃ sarvavyādhivināśanam ।। aricakrapraśamanaṃ sarvādhipravināśanam ।।
viṣagrahakṣayakaraṃ putrapautrādivardhanam ।। śeṣalokasya sopānaṃ vāñchitārthaikasādhanam ।। vāñchāsiddhipradaṃ caiva ṛddhiprajñādisādhanam ।। prakāśitavyaṃ bhakteṣu cireṣūdyamiteṣu ca ।।
śivotsaveṣu sarveṣu caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu ca ।। coravyāghrāhisiṃhāntakṛto rājabhayeṣu ca ।। ulkāpāte mahāvāte vinā vṛṣṭyātivṛṣṭiṣu ।। yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi stavaṃ sarvamanuttamam ।।
sa rudratvaṃ samāsādya rudrasyānucaro bhavet ।। kathaṃ jaghāna bhagavān bhaganetraharo haraḥ ।। jalandhara iti khyāto jalamaṇḍalasaṃbhavaḥ ।। tena devāḥ sagandharvāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ ।।
jitvaiva devasaṃghātaṃ brahmāṇaṃ vai jalandharaḥ ।। tayoḥ samabhavadyuddhaṃ divārātram aviśramam ।। jalandharo api taṃ jitvā devadevaṃ janārdanam ।। sarve jitā mayā yuddhe śaṅkaro hyajito raṇe ।।
ahameva bhavatvaṃ ca brahmatvaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tathā ।। jalandharavacaḥ śrutvā sarve te dānavādhamāḥ ।। daityairetaistathānyaiś ca rathanāgaturaṅgamaiḥ ।। bhavo api dṛṣṭvā daityendraṃ merukūṭamiva sthitam ।।
brahmaṇo vacanaṃ rakṣan rakṣako jagatāṃ prabhuḥ ।। kiṃ kṛtyamasureśāna yuddhenānena sāṃpratam ।। jalandharo api tadvākyaṃ śrutvā śrotravidāraṇam ।। vākyenālaṃ mahābāho devadeva vṛṣadhvaja ।।
mahāṃbhasi cakārāśu rathāṅgaṃ raudramāyudham ।। dakṣāndhakāntakapuratrayayajñahartā lokatrayāntakakaraḥ prahasaṃtadāha ।। balavān yadi coddhartuṃ tiṣṭha yoddhuṃ na cānyathā ।। pradahanniva netrābhyāṃ prāhālokya jagattrayam ।।
hatvā lokānsuraiḥ sārdhaṃ ḍuṇḍubhān garuḍo yathā ।। ko maheśvara madbāṇair acchedyo bhuvanatraye ।। brahmā balī yauvane vai munayaḥ surapuṅgavaiḥ ।। tapasā kiṃ tvayā rudra nirjito bhagavānapi ।।
na sehire yathā nāgā gandhaṃ pakṣipateriva ।। samastānparvatānprāpya gharṣitāś ca gaṇeśvara ।। gharṣito bāhudaṇḍena kaṇḍūnodārtham āpatat ।। nārīṇāṃ mama bhṛtyaiś ca vajro baddho divaukasām ।।
tatkṣaṇādeva sakalaṃ caikārṇavamabhūdidam ।। saratho bhagavānindraḥ kṣiptaś ca śatayojanam ।। urvaśyādyā mayā nītā nāryaḥ kārāgṛhāntaram ।। māṃ na jānāsi daityendraṃ jalandharamumāpate ।।
tasya netrāgnibhāgaikakalārdhārdhena cākulam ।। nāgād vaiśasam anusaṃvṛtaś ca nāgair deveśaṃ vacanamuvāca cālpabuddhiḥ ।। yattasmādbhayamihanāsti yoddhum īśa vāñchaiṣā vipulatarā na saṃśayo atra ।। bhūtendrairharivadanena devasaṃghair yoddhuṃ te balamiha cāsti ceddhi tiṣṭha ।।
na cacāla na sasmāra nihatānbāndhavānyudhi ।। sudarśanākhyaṃ yaccakraṃ tena hantuṃ samudyataḥ ।। sthāpayāmāsa vai skandhe dvidhābhūtaś ca tena vai ।। papāta daityo balavān añjanādririvāparaḥ ।।
tadraktamakhilaṃ rudraniyogānmāṃsameva ca ।। jalandharaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā devagandharvapārṣadāḥ ।। yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi jalandharavimardanam ।। śrāvayedvā yathānyāyaṃ gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt ।।
sudarśanākhyaṃ vai labdhaṃ vaktumarhasi viṣṇunā ।। sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ vināśakaraṇo mahān ।। prabhidyamānāḥ kuntaiś ca dudruvurbhayavihvalāḥ ।। praṇemustaṃ sureśānaṃ śokasaṃvignamānasāḥ ।।
praṇipatya sthitāndevān idaṃ vacanamabravīt ।। samāgatāḥ sasaṃtāpā vaktumarhatha suvratāḥ ।। praṇamyāhuryathāvṛttaṃ devadevāya viṣṇave ।। dānavaiḥ pīḍitāḥ sarve vayaṃ śaraṇamāgatāḥ ।।
tvameva paramātmā hi tvaṃ pitā jagatāmapi ।। hantumarhasi tasmāttvaṃ dānavāndānavārdana ।। kauberaiścaiva saumyaiś ca nairṛtyairvāruṇairdṛḍhaiḥ ।। saurai raudrais tathā bhīmaiḥ kampanair jṛmbhaṇair dṛḍhaiḥ ।।
sūryamaṇḍalasambhūtaṃ tvadīyaṃ cakram udyatam ।। daṇḍaṃ śārṅgaṃ tavāstraṃ ca labdhaṃ daityaiḥ prasādataḥ ।। rathāṅgaṃ suśitaṃ ghoraṃ tena tān hantum arhasi ।। tato niśamya teṣāṃ vai vacanaṃ vārijekṣaṇaḥ ।।
bhobho devā mahādevaṃ sarvair devaiḥ sanātanaiḥ ।। devā jalandharaṃ hantuṃ nirmitaṃ hi purāriṇā ।। sarvāndhundhumukhāndaityān aṣṭaṣaṣṭiśatān surān ।। evam uktvā suraśreṣṭhān suraśreṣṭhamanusmaran ।।
liṅgaṃ sthāpya yathānyāyaṃ himavacchikhare śubhe ।। tvaritākhyena rudreṇa raudreṇa ca janārdanaḥ ।। tuṣṭāva ca tadā rudraṃ sampūjyāgnau praṇamya ca ।। pūjayāmāsa ca śivaṃ praṇavādyaṃ namo antakam ।।
pratināma sa padmena pūjayāmāsa śaṅkaram ।। svāhāntairvidhivaddhutvā pratyekamayutaṃ prabhum ।। bhavaḥ śivo haro rudraḥ puruṣaḥ padmalocanaḥ ।। īśvaraḥ sthāṇurīśānaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt ।।
gaṅgādharaḥ śūladharaḥ parārthaikaprayojanaḥ ।। candrāpīḍaścandramaulir vidvānviśvāmareśvaraḥ ।। dhyānādhāroparicchedyo gaurībhartā gaṇeśvaraḥ ।। jñānagamyo dṛḍhaprajño devadevastrilocanaḥ ।।
viśvarūpo virūpākṣo vāgīśaḥ śucirantaraḥ ।। īśaḥ pinākī khaṭvāṅgī citraveṣaścirantanaḥ ।। kālakālaḥ kṛttivāsāḥ subhagaḥ praṇavātmakaḥ ।। dṛḍhāyudhaḥ skandaguruḥ parameṣṭhī parāyaṇaḥ ।।
kuberabandhuḥ śrīkaṇṭho lokavarṇottamottamaḥ ।। viśālākṣo mṛgavyādhaḥ sureśaḥ sūryatāpanaḥ ।। ugraḥ paśupatis tārkṣyaḥ priyabhaktaḥ priyaṃvadaḥ ।। śmaśānanilayaḥ sūkṣmaḥ śmaśānastho maheśvaraḥ ।।
uttaro gopatirgoptā jñānagamyaḥ purātanaḥ ।। somapo amṛtapaḥ somo mahānītirmahāmatiḥ ।। lokakāro vedakāraḥ sūtrakāraḥ sanātanaḥ ।। pinākapāṇir bhūdevaḥ svastidaḥ svastikṛtsadā ।।
brahmadhṛg viśvasṛk svargaḥ karṇikāraḥ priyaḥ kaviḥ ।। gaṅgāplavodako bhāvaḥ sakalaḥ sthapatiḥ sthiraḥ ।। sagaṇo gaṇakāryaś ca sukīrtiś chinnasaṃśayaḥ ।। bhasmapriyo bhasmaśāyī kāmī kāntaḥ kṛtāgamaḥ ।।
caturmukhaścaturbāhur durāvāso durāsadaḥ ।। adhyātmayoganilayaḥ sutantustantuvardhanaḥ ।। bhasmaśuddhikaro merur ojasvī śuddhavigrahaḥ ।। mahāhrado mahāgarbhaḥ siddhavṛndāravanditaḥ ।।
amṛtāṅgo amṛtavapuḥ pañcayajñaḥ prabhañjanaḥ ।। sulabhaḥ suvrataḥ śūro vāṅmayaikanidhirnidhiḥ ।। āśramaḥ kṣapaṇaḥ kṣāmo jñānavānacalācalaḥ ।। dhanurdharo dhanurvedo guṇarāśirguṇākaraḥ ।।
abhivādyo mahācāryo viśvakarmā viśāradaḥ ।। unmattaveṣaḥ pracchanno jitakāmo jitapriyaḥ ।। tapasvī tārako dhīmān pradhānaprabhur avyayaḥ ।। vedaśāstrārthatattvajño niyamo niyamāśrayaḥ ।।
bhaktigamyaḥ paraṃ brahma mṛgabāṇārpaṇo anaghaḥ ।। sarvakarmācalastvaṣṭā maṅgalyo maṅgalāvṛtaḥ ।। ahaḥ saṃvatsaro vyāptiḥ pramāṇaṃ paramaṃ tapaḥ ।। ajaḥ sarveśvaraḥ snigdho mahāretā mahābalaḥ ।।
vasurvasumanāḥ satyaḥ sarvapāpaharo haraḥ ।। kamaṇḍaludharo dhanvī vedāṅgo vedavinmuniḥ ।। atīndriyo mahāmāyaḥ sarvāvāsaścatuṣpathaḥ ।। mahābuddhir mahāvīryo bhūtacārī purandaraḥ ।।
anirdeśyavapuḥ śrīmān sarvahāryamito gatiḥ ।। ojastejo dyutikaro nartakaḥ sarvakāmakaḥ ।। buddhaspaṣṭākṣaro mantraḥ sanmānaḥ sārasaṃplavaḥ ।। iṣṭo viśiṣṭaḥ śiṣṭeṣṭaḥ śarabhaḥ śarabho dhanuḥ ।।
pratiṣṭhitaḥ pramāṇajño hiraṇyakavaco hariḥ ।। bālarūpo balonmāthī vivarto gahano guruḥ ।। vidvattamo vītabhayo viśvabhartā niśākaraḥ ।। dundubho lalito viśvo bhavātmātmani saṃsthitaḥ ।।
vīracūḍāmaṇirvettā tīvranādo nadīdharaḥ ।। vālakhilyo mahācāpas tigmāṃśur nidhir avyayaḥ ।। maghavānkauśiko gomān viśrāmaḥ sarvaśāsanaḥ ।। amoghadaṇḍī madhyastho hiraṇyo brahmavarcasī ।।
rucir vararucir vandyo vācaspatiraharpatiḥ ।। yuktirunnatakīrtiś ca śāntarāgaḥ parājayaḥ ।। vidvattamo vītabhayo viśvahartā nivāritaḥ ।। dūraśravā viśvasaho dhyeyo duḥsvapnanāśanaḥ ।।
anādirbhūrbhuvolakṣmīḥ kirīṭī tridaśādhipaḥ ।। janano janajanmādiḥ prītimānnītimānnayaḥ ।। praṇavaḥ saptadhācāro mahākāyo mahādhanuḥ ।। tattvātattvavivekātmā vibhūṣṇur bhūtibhūṣaṇaḥ ।।
yajño yajñapatiryajvā yajñānto amoghavikramaḥ ।। pañcabrahmasamutpattir viśveśo vimalodayaḥ ।। gāyatrīvallabhaḥ prāṃśur viśvāvāsaḥ prabhākaraḥ ।। amogho ariṣṭamathano mukundo vigatajvaraḥ ।।
piṅgalaḥ kapilaśmaśruḥ śāstranetras trayītanuḥ ।। bhago vivasvānādityo yogācāryo bṛhaspatiḥ ।। nakṣatramālī rākeśaḥ sādhiṣṭhānaḥ ṣaḍāśrayaḥ ।। hṛtpuṇḍarīkamāsīnaḥ śuklaḥ śānto vṛṣākapiḥ ।।
adharmaśatrurakṣayyaḥ puruhūtaḥ puruṣṭutaḥ ।। jagaddhitaiṣī sugataḥ kumāraḥ kuśalāgamaḥ ।। arogo niyamādhyakṣo viśvāmitro dvijottamaḥ ।। mātāmaho mātariśvā nabhasvān nāgahāradhṛk ।।
nirāvaraṇadharmajño viriñco viṣṭaraśravāḥ ।। lokacūḍāmaṇirvīraḥ caṇḍasatyaparākramaḥ ।। alaṃkariṣṇus tvacalo rociṣṇurvikramottamaḥ ।। asaṃsṛṣṭo atithiḥ śakraḥ pramāthī pāpanāśanaḥ ।।
jaryo jarādhiśamano lohitaś ca tanūnapāt ।। nidāghastapano meghaḥ pakṣaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ ।। vasaṃto mādhavo grīṣmo nabhasyo bījavāhanaḥ ।। pāvanaḥ purujicchakras trividyo naravāhanaḥ ।।
tejonidhir jñānanidhir vipāko vighnakārakaḥ ।। śailo nagastanurdeho dānavārirarindamaḥ ।। caturvedaścaturbhāvaś caturaścaturapriyaḥ ।। bahurūpo mahārūpaḥ sarvarūpaś carācaraḥ ।।
sahasramūrdhā devendraḥ sarvaśastraprabhañjanaḥ ।। piṅgalākṣo atha haryakṣo nīlagrīvo nirāmayaḥ ।। padmāsanaḥ paraṃ jyotiḥ parāvaraṃ paraṃ phalam ।। parāvarajño bījeśaḥ sumukhaḥ sumahāsvanaḥ ।।
devāsuramahāmātro devāsuramahāśrayaḥ ।। devāsureśvaro divyo devāsuramaheśvaraḥ ।। īḍyo anīśaḥ suravyāghro devasiṃho divākaraḥ ।। śivajñānarataḥ śrīmān śikhiśrīparvatapriyaḥ ।।
brahmacārī lokacārī dharmacārī dhanādhipaḥ ।। liṅgādhyakṣaḥ surādhyakṣo yugādhyakṣo yugāvahaḥ ।। bījādhyakṣo bījakartā dhanakṛd dharmavardhanaḥ ।। śmaśānanilayastiṣyaḥ seturapratimākṛtiḥ ।।
andhakārirmakhadveṣī viṣṇukandharapātanaḥ ।। dhūrjaṭiḥ khaṇḍaparaśuḥ sakalo niṣkalo anaghaḥ ।। pūrṇaḥ pūrayitā puṇyaḥ sukumāraḥ sulocanaḥ ।। manojavastīrthakaro jaṭilo jīviteśvaraḥ ।।
sadgatiḥ satkṛtiḥ saktaḥ kālakaṇṭhaḥ kalādharaḥ ।। candrasaṃjīvanaḥ śāstā lokagūḍho amarādhipaḥ ।। anapāyyakṣaraḥ kāntaḥ sarvaśāstrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ ।। śucismitaḥ prasannātmā durjayo duratikramaḥ ।।
tumbavīṇī mahākāyo viśokaḥ śokanāśanaḥ ।। avyaktalakṣaṇo vyakto vyaktāvyakto viśāṃpatiḥ ।। brahmā viṣṇuḥ prajāpālo haṃso haṃsagatiryamaḥ ।। kailāsaśikharāvāsī sarvāvāsī satāṃ gatiḥ ।।
bhūtālayo bhūtapatir bhūtido bhuvaneśvaraḥ ।। devapriyo devanātho devajño devacintakaḥ ।। nirmado nirahaṅkāro nirmoho nirupadravaḥ ।। saptajihvaḥ sahasrārciḥ snigdhaḥ prakṛtidakṣiṇaḥ ।।
artho anartho mahākośaḥ parakāryaikapaṇḍitaḥ ।। sattvavān sāttvikaḥ satyakīrtistambhakṛtāgamaḥ ।। suprītaḥ sumukhaḥ sūkṣmaḥ sukaro dakṣiṇo analaḥ ।। aparājitaḥ sarvasaho vidagdhaḥ sarvavāhanaḥ ।।
varāhaśṛṅgadhṛg vāyur balavān ekanāyakaḥ ।। śrīvallabhaśivārambhaḥ śāntabhadraḥ samañjasaḥ ।। akāyo bhaktakāyasthaḥ kālajñānī kalāvapuḥ ।। parārthavṛttir varado viviktaḥ śrutisāgaraḥ ।।
svabhāvarudro madhyasthaḥ śatrughno madhyanāśakaḥ ।। mekhalī kavacī khaḍgī māyī saṃsārasārathiḥ ।। asaṃkhyeyo aprameyātmā vīryavān kāryakovidaḥ ।। anuttamo durādharṣo madhuraḥ priyadarśanaḥ ।।
kālabhakṣaḥ kalaṅkāriḥ kaṅkaṇīkṛtavāsukiḥ ।। dyumaṇis taraṇir dhanyaḥ siddhidaḥ siddhisādhanaḥ ।। ekajyotir nirātaṅko naro nārāyaṇapriyaḥ ।। stavyastavapriyaḥ stotā vyāsamūrtiranākulaḥ ।।
praśāntabuddhirakṣudraḥ kṣudrahā nityasundaraḥ ।। paramārthagurur dṛṣṭir gurur āśritavatsalaḥ ।। evaṃ nāmnāṃ sahasreṇa tuṣṭāva vṛṣabhadhvajam ।। parīkṣārthaṃ hareḥ pūjākamaleṣu maheśvaraḥ ।।
hṛtapuṣpo haristatra kimidaṃ tvabhyacintayat ।। pūjayāmāsa bhāvena nāmnā tena jagadgurum ।। tasmādavatatārāśu maṇḍalātpāvakasya ca ।। jvālāmālāvṛtaṃ divyaṃ tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭraṃ bhayaṅkaram ।।
varādabhayahastaṃ ca dvīpicarmottarīyakam ।। hṛṣṭo namaścakārāśu devadevaṃ janārdanaḥ ।। cacāla brahmabhuvanaṃ cakampe ca vasuṃdharā ।। adhastāccordhvataścaiva hāhetyakṛta bhūtale ।।
samprekṣya praṇayādviṣṇuṃ kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ sthitam ।। sudarśanākhyaṃ cakraṃ ca dadāmi tava śobhanam ।। hitāya tava yatnena tava bhāvāya suvrata ।। śāntasya cāstraṃ śāntaḥ syāc chāntenāstreṇa kiṃ phalam ।।
yoddhuḥ śāntyā balacchedaḥ parasya balavṛddhidaḥ ।। kimāyudhena kāryaṃ vai yoddhuṃ devārisūdana ।। anāgate vyatīte ca daurbalye svajanotkare ।। evamuktvā dadau cakraṃ sūryāyutasamaprabham ।।
tadāprabhṛti taṃ prāhuḥ padmākṣamiti suvratam ।। pasparśa ca karābhyāṃ vai suśubhābhyāmuvāca ha ।। bhaktyā vaśīkṛto nūnaṃ tvayāhaṃ puruṣottama ।। tvayi bhaktirmahādeva prasīda varamuttamam ।।
tacchrutvā vacanaṃ tasya dayāvān sutarāṃ bhavaḥ ।। prāha caivaṃ mahādevaḥ paramātmānamacyutam ।। bhaviṣyasi na saṃdeho matprasādātsurottama ।। mātaraṃ pitaraṃ dakṣaṃ bhaviṣyati sureśvarī ।।
bhaginīṃ tava kalyāṇīṃ devīṃ haimavatīmumām ।। matsaṃbandhī ca lokānāṃ madhye pūjyo bhaviṣyasi ।। drakṣyase ca prasannena mitrabhūtamivātmanā ।। janārdano api bhagavān devānāmapi saṃnidhau ।।
mayā proktaṃ stavaṃ divyaṃ padmayone suśobhanam ।। pratināmni hiraṇyasya tat tasya phalam āpnuyāt ।। ghṛtādyaiḥ snāpayedrudraṃ sthālyā vai kalaśaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। so api yajñasahasrasya phalaṃ labdhvāsureśvaraiḥ ।।
tathāstviti tathā prāha padmayonerjanārdanam ।। tasmānnāmnāṃ sahasreṇa pūjayed anagho dvijāḥ ।। japennāmnāṃ sahasraṃ ca sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। savistaraṃ vadasvādya satītve ca yathātatham ।।
viṣṇunā ca kathaṃ dattā devadevāya śaṃbhave ।। teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ ।। brahmaṇā kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ daṇḍine tat suvistaram ।। tasmādahamupaśrutya pravadāmi suvistaram ।।
sā bhagākhyā jagaddhātrī liṅgamūrtestrivedikā ।। liṅgamūrtiḥ śivo jyotis tamasaścopari sthitaḥ ।। brahmāṇaṃ vidadhe devam agre putraṃ caturmukham ।। viśvādhiko asau bhagavān ardhanārīśvaro vibhuḥ ।।
so api rudraṃ mahādevaṃ brahmāpaśyata śaṅkaram ।। tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhir varadaṃ vārijodbhavaḥ ।। sasarja devīṃ vāmāṅgāt patnīṃ caivātmanaḥ samām ।। saivājñayā vibhordevī dakṣaputrī babhūva ha ।।
dakṣaṃ vinindya kālena devī mainā hyabhūtpunaḥ ।। avajñādurmado dakṣo devadevamumāpatim ।। bhasmīkṛtvātmano dehaṃ yogamārgeṇa sā punaḥ ।। jñātvaitadbhagavān bhargo dadāha ruṣitaḥ prabhuḥ ।।
cyavanasya suto dhīmān dadhīca iti viśrutaḥ ।। viṣṇunā lokapālāṃś ca śaśāpa ca munīśvaraḥ ।। vināśo vai kṣaṇādeva māyayā śaṅkarasya vai ।। sarvāndadhīcavacanāt kathaṃ bheje maheśvaraḥ ।।
dadāha bhagavān rudraḥ sarvān munigaṇān api ।। viprayogena devyā vai duḥsahenaiva suvratāḥ ।। gaṇeśvaraiḥ samāruhya rathaṃ bhadraḥ pratāpavān ।। gaṇeśvarāś ca te sarve vividhāyudhapāṇayaḥ ।।
himavacchikhare ramye hemaśṛṅge suśobhane ।। taddeśe caiva vikhyātaṃ śubhaṃ kanakhalaṃ dvijāḥ ।। tadotpāto babhūvātha lokānāṃ bhayaśaṃsanaḥ ।। marutaś cāpy aghūrṇanta cukṣubhe makarālayaḥ ।।
grahāś ca na prakāśyante na devā na ca dānavāḥ ।। romajaiḥ sahito bhadraḥ kālāgnirivacāparaḥ ।। saṃparkādeva dakṣādya munīndevān pinākinā ।। ityuktvā yajñaśālāṃ tāṃ dadāha gaṇapuṅgavaḥ ।।
prastotrā saha hotrā ca dagdhaṃ caiva gaṇeśvaraiḥ ।। vīrabhadro mahātejāḥ śakrasyodyacchataḥ karam ।। bhagasya netre cotpāṭya karajāgreṇa līlayā ।। tathā candramasaṃ devaṃ pādāṅguṣṭhena līlayā ।।
cicheda ca śirastasya śakrasya bhagavānprabhoḥ ।। jaghāna mūrdhni pādena vīrabhadro mahābalaḥ ।। jaghāna devamīśānaṃ triśūlena mahābalam ।। trayaś ca triśataṃ teṣāṃ trisāhasraṃ ca līlayā ।।
anyāṃś ca devān devo asau sarvānyuddhāya saṃsthitān ।। atha viṣṇurmahātejāś cakram udyamya mūrchitaḥ ।। tayoḥ samabhavadyuddhaṃ sughoraṃ romaharṣaṇam ।। viṣṇoryogabalāttasya divyadehāḥ sudāruṇāḥ ।।
tānsarvānapi devo asau nārāyaṇasamaprabhān ।। tataścorasi taṃ devaṃ līlayaiva raṇājire ।। punarutthāya taṃ hantuṃ cakramudyamya sa prabhuḥ ।। tasya cakraṃ ca yadraudraṃ kālādityasamaprabham ।।
atiṣṭhat stambhitastena śṛṅgavāniva niścalaḥ ।। śārṅgakoṭiprasaṅgād vai cicheda ca śiraḥ prabhoḥ ।। vāyunā preritaṃ caiva prāṇajena pinākinā ।। tat pratidhvastakalaśaṃ bhagnayūpaṃ satoraṇam ।।
taṃ tadā mṛgarūpeṇa dhāvantaṃ gaganaṃ prati ।। tataḥ prajāpatiṃ dharmaṃ kaśyapaṃ ca jagadgurum ।। munim aṅgirasaṃ caiva kṛṣṇāśvaṃ ca mahābalaḥ ।। cicheda ca śirastasya dadāhāgnau dvijottamāḥ ।।
nikṛtya karajāgreṇa vīrabhadraḥ pratāpavān ।। etasminneva kāle tu bhagavānpadmasaṃbhavaḥ ।। alaṃ krodhena vai bhadra naṣṭāścaiva divaukasaḥ ।। so api bhadraḥ prabhāveṇa brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।।
devo api tatra bhagavān antarikṣe vṛṣadhvajaḥ ।। prārthitaścaiva devena brahmaṇā bhagavān bhavaḥ ।। indrasya ca śirastasya viṣṇoścaiva mahātmanaḥ ।। vāgīśyāścaiva nāsāgraṃ devamātustathaiva ca ।।
dakṣasya dhvastavaktrasya śirasā bhagavānprabhuḥ ।। dakṣo api labdhasaṃjñaś ca samutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। stutastena mahātejāḥ pradāya vividhānvarān ।। devāś ca sarve deveśaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ parameśvaram ।।
brahmā ca munayaḥ sarve pṛthakpṛthagajodbhavam ।। tān devān anugṛhyaiva bhavo apyantaradhīyata ।। kathaṃ vā devadeveśam avāpa patimīśvaram ।। tadā haimavatī jajñe tapasā ca dvijottamāḥ ।।
dvādaśe ca tadā varṣe pūrṇe haimavatī śubhā ।। anyā ca devī hyanujā sarvaloke namaskṛtā ।। tuṣṭuvus tapasā devīṃ samāvṛtya samantataḥ ।। tṛtīyā ca varārohā tathā caivaikapāṭalā ।।
vaśīkṛto mahādevaḥ sarvabhūtapatirbhavaḥ ।। tārātmajo mahātejā babhūva ditinandanaḥ ।। vidyunmālī ca bhagavān kamalākṣaś ca vīryavān ।। tapasā labdhavīryaś ca prasādādbrahmaṇaḥ prabhoḥ ।।
vijitya samare pūrvaṃ viṣṇuṃ ca jitavān asau ।। divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu divārātram aviśramam ।। tāreṇa vijitaḥ saṃkhye dudrāva garuḍadhvajaḥ ।। pitāmahājjagatsarvam avāpa ditinandanaḥ ।।
vārayāmāsa tair devān sarvalokeṣu māyayā ।। na śāntiṃ lebhire śūrāḥ śaraṇaṃ vā bhayārditāḥ ।। uvācāṅgirasaṃ devo devānāmapi saṃnidhau ।। tena saṃnihatā yuddhe vatsā gopatinā yathā ।।
aniketā bhramantyete śakuntā iva pañjare ।। tāni moghāni jāyante prabhāvādamaradviṣaḥ ।। viṣṇunā yodhito yuddhe tenāpi na ca sūditaḥ ।। kathamasmadvidhastasya sthāsyate samare agrataḥ ।।
sahasrākṣeṇa ca vibhuṃ samprāpyāha kuśadhvajam ।। devairaśeṣaiḥ sendraistu jīvamāha pitāmahaḥ ।। vinindya dakṣaṃ yā devī satī rudrāṅgasaṃbhavā ।। tasyāścaiveha rūpeṇa yūyaṃ devāḥ surottamāḥ ।।
tayoryogena sambhūtaḥ skandaḥ śaktidharaḥ prabhuḥ ।। svāheyaḥ kārtikeyaś ca gāṅgeyaḥ śaradhāmajaḥ ।। senāpatiḥ kumārākhyaḥ sarvalokanamaskṛtaḥ ।। bālo api vinihatyaiko devān saṃtārayiṣyati ।।
bṛhaspatis tathā sendrair devair devaṃ praṇamya tam ।। smaraṇāddevadevasya smaro api saha bhāryayā ।। saśakramāha taṃ jīvaṃ jagajjīvo dvijottamāḥ ।। brūhi yanme vidhātavyaṃ tamāha surapūjitaḥ ।।
śaṅkareṇāṃbikāmadya saṃyojaya yathāsukham ।। tena mārgeṇa mārgasva patnyā ratyānayā saha ।। viprayuktastayā pūrvaṃ labdhvā tāṃ girijāmumām ।। devadevāśramaṃ gantuṃ matiṃ cakre tayā saha ।।
vasaṃtena sahāyena devaṃ yoktumanā bhavat ।। nayanena tṛtīyena sāvajñaṃ tam avaikṣata ।। adahattatkṣaṇādeva lalāpa karuṇaṃ ratiḥ ।। kṛpayā parayā prāha kāmapatnīṃ nirīkṣya ca ।।
ratikāle dhruve bhadre kariṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।। śāpādbhṛgormahātejāḥ sarvalokahitāya vai ।। sā praṇamya tadā rudraṃ kāmapatnī śucismitā ।। jagāma madanaṃ labdhvā vasaṃtena samanvitā ।।
prītiś ca bhagavāñcharvo vacanādbrahmaṇastadā ।। tadā haimavatīṃ devīm upayeme yathāvidhi ।। tapovanaṃ mahādevyāḥ pārvatyāḥ padmasaṃbhavaḥ ।। kim arthaṃ tapasā lokān saṃtāpayasi śailaje ।।
tvaṃ hi saṃdhārayellokān imān sarvān svatejasā ।। yasya vai devadevasya vayaṃ kiṅkaravādinaḥ ।। varade yena sṛṣṭāsi na vinā yastvayāṃbike ।। ityuktvā tāṃ namaskṛtya muhuḥ samprekṣya pārvatīm ।।
jagāmānugrahaṃ kartuṃ dvijarūpeṇa cāśramam ।। pratibhādyaiḥ prabhuṃ jñātvā nanāma vṛṣabhadhvajam ।। tuṣṭāva parameśānaṃ pārvatī parameśvaram ।। kuladharmāśrayaṃ rakṣan bhūdharasya mahātmanaḥ ।।
svayaṃvare mahādevī tava divyasuśobhane ।। ityuktvā tāṃ samālokya devo divyena cakṣuṣā ।। dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭastadā devīṃ menayā tuhinācalaḥ ।। duhiturdevadevena na jānannabhimantritam ।।
atha brahmā ca bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sākṣājjanārdanaḥ ।। tvaṣṭāryamā vivasvāṃś ca yamo varuṇa eva ca ।। aśvinau dvādaśādityā gandharvā garuḍas tathā ।। samudrāś ca nadā vedā mantrāḥ stotrādayaḥ kṣaṇāḥ ।।
trayastriṃśacca devānāṃ trayaś ca triśataṃ tathā ।। jagmur girīndraputryāstu svayaṃvaramanuttamam ।। vimānaṃ sarvatobhadraṃ sarvaratnair alaṃkṛtam ।। gandharvasiddhairvividhaiḥ kinnaraiś ca suśobhanaiḥ ।।
sitātapatraṃ ratnāṃśumiśritaṃ cāvahattathā ।। cāmarāsaktahastābhir divyastrībhiś ca saṃvṛtā ।। vijayā vyajanaṃ gṛhya sthitā devyāḥ samīpagā ।। śiśurbhūtvā mahādevaḥ krīḍārthaṃ vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ ।।
atha dṛṣṭvā śiśuṃ devās tasyā utsaṃgavarttinam ।। vajramāhārayattasya bāhum udyamya vṛtrahā ।। stambhitaḥ śiśurūpeṇa devadevena līlayā ।। vahniḥ śaktiṃ tathā kṣeptuṃ na śaśāka tathā sthitaḥ ।।
varuṇo nāgapāśaṃ ca dhvajayaṣṭiṃ samīraṇaḥ ।। īśānaś ca tathā śūlaṃ tīvramudyamya saṃsthitaḥ ।। mudgaraṃ stambhitāḥ sarve devenāśu divaukasaḥ ।। śiraḥ prakampayan viṣṇuś cakram udyamya saṃsthitaḥ ।।
cakraṃ kṣeptuṃ na śaśāka bāhūṃścālayituṃ na ca ।। tasyāpi daśanāḥ petur dṛṣṭamātrasya śaṃbhunā ।। atha teṣu sthiteṣveva manyumatsu sureṣvapi ।। bubudhe devamīśānam umotsaṃge tamāsthitam ।।
vavande caraṇau śaṃbhor astuvacca pitāmahaḥ ।। bhūtānāmindriyāṇāṃ ca tvameveśa pravarttakaḥ ।। vāmahastān mahābāho devo nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।। patnīrūpaṃ samāsthāya jagatkāraṇamāgatā ।।
prasādāttava deveśa niyogācca mayā prajāḥ ।। kuru prasādameteṣāṃ yathāpūrvaṃ bhavantvime ।। saṃstambhitāṃstadā tena bhagavān āha padmajaḥ ।। devadevam ihāyāntaṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam ।।
sanārāyaṇakāḥ sarve munibhiḥ śaṅkaraṃ prabhum ।। anayā haimavatyā ca prakṛtyā saha sattamam ।। praṇemur manasā sarve sanārāyaṇakāḥ prabhum ।। yathāpūrvaṃ cakārāśu vacanādbrahmaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।।
vapuścakāra deveśo divyaṃ paramamadbhutam ।। sabrahmakāḥ sasādhyāś ca sanārāyaṇakās tathā ।। tebhyaś ca paramaṃ cakṣuḥ sarvadṛṣṭau ca śaktimat ।। labdhvā cakṣustadā devā indraviṣṇupurogamāḥ ।।
