brahmādyā nemire tūrṇaṃ bhavānī ca girīśvaraḥ ।। sasarjuḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiṃ ca khecarāḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ ।। jagurgandharvamukhyāś ca nanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ ।। tasya devī tadā hṛṣṭā samakṣaṃ tridivaukasām ।।
sādhu sādhviti samprocya tayā tatraiva cārcitam ।। sarve sabrahmakā devāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ ।। udvāhaḥ kriyatāṃ deva ityuvāca maheśvaram ।। yatheṣṭamiti lokeśaṃ prāha bhūtapatiḥ prabhuḥ ।।
brahmaṇā kalpitaṃ divyaṃ puraṃ ratnamayaṃ śubham ।। pulomā surasā caiva siṃhikā vinatā tathā ।। sāvitrī vedamātā ca rajanī dakṣiṇā dyutiḥ ।। rākā kuhūḥ sinīvālī devī anumatī tathā ।।
etāścānyāś ca devānāṃ mātaraḥ patnayas tathā ।। uragā garuḍā yakṣā gandharvāḥ kinnarā gaṇāḥ ।। vedā mantrās tathā yajñāḥ stomā dharmāś ca sarvaśaḥ ।। koṭirapsaraso divyās tāsāṃ ca paricārikāḥ ।।
tāś ca strīvigrahāḥ sarvāḥ saṃjagmurhṛṣṭamānasāḥ ।। udvāhaḥ śaṅkarasyeti tatrājagmurmudānvitāḥ ।। daśabhiḥ kekarākṣaś ca vidyuto aṣṭābhir eva ca ।। ṣaḍbhiḥ sarvāntakaḥ śrīmān tathaiva vikṛtānanaḥ ।।
saptabhiḥ samadaḥ śrīmān dundubho aṣṭābhir eva ca ।। koṭikoṭibhir eveha gaṇḍakaḥ kuṃbhakas tathā ।। pippalaś ca sahasreṇa saṃnādaś ca tathā dvijāḥ ।। mahākeśaḥ sahasreṇa koṭīnāṃ gaṇapo vṛtaḥ ।।
kālaś ca kālakaścaiva mahākālaḥ śatena vai ।। ādityamūrdhā koṭyā ca tathā caiva dhanāvahaḥ ।। amoghaḥ kokilaścaiva koṭikoṭyā sumantrakaḥ ।। mahābalaś ca navabhir madhupiṅgaś ca piṅgalaḥ ।।
koṭīnāṃ caiva saptatyā caturvaktro mahābalaḥ ।। tatrājagmus tathā devās te sarve śaṅkaraṃ bhavam ।। vīrabhadraścatuḥṣaṣṭyā romajāścaiva koṭibhiḥ ।। pañcākṣaḥ śatamanyuś ca meghamanyus tathaiva ca ।।
virūpākṣaś ca bhagavān catuḥṣaṣṭyā sanātanaḥ ।। saṃvartakas tathā caitro lakulīśaḥ svayaṃ prabhuḥ ।। mṛtyuhṛt kālahā kālo mṛtyuñjayakaras tathā ।। devo bhṛṅgī riṭiḥ śrīmān devadevapriyas tathā ।।
ete cānye ca gaṇapā asaṃkhyātā mahābalāḥ ।। candrarekhāvataṃsāś ca nīlakaṇṭhās trilocanāḥ ।। brahmendraviṣṇusaṃkāśā aṇimādiguṇairvṛtāḥ ।। pātālacāriṇaścaiva sarvalokanivāsinaḥ ।।
ratnānyādāya vādyāṃś ca tatrājagmustadā puram ।। puṇyān vaivāhikān mantrān ajapur hṛṣṭamānasāḥ ।। girijāṃ tām alaṃkṛtya svayameva śucismitām ।। sadasyāha ca deveśaṃ nārāyaṇamajo harim ।।
vāmāṅgādasya rudrasya dakṣiṇāṅgādahaṃ prabho ।। eṣā haimavatī jajñe māyayā parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। ato asau jagatāṃ dhātrī dhātā tava mamāpi ca ।। kṣmābagnikhendusūryātmapavanātmā yato bhavaḥ ।।
eṣā hy ajā śuklakṛṣṇā lohitā prakṛtirbhavān ।। tava pādme samudbhūtaḥ kalpe nābhyaṃbujādaham ।। bāḍham ityajam āhāsau devadevo janārdanaḥ ।। tataścotthāya vidvānsaḥ padmanābhaḥ praṇamya tām ।।
abhyukṣad ātmano mūrdhni brahmaṇaś ca gires tathā ।। ityuktvā sodakaṃ dattvā devīṃ deveśvarāya tām ।। atha sarve muniśreṣṭhāḥ sarvavedārthapāragāḥ ।। eṣa devo haro nūnaṃ māyayā hi tato jagat ।।
sasṛjuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi khecarāḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ ।। vedāś ca mūrtimantaste praṇemustaṃ maheśvaram ।। devo api devīmālokya salajjāṃ himaśailajām ।। varado asmīti taṃ prāha hariṃ so apyāha śaṅkaram ।।
tatastu punarevāha brahmā vijñāpayanprabhum ।। dadāsi mama yadyājñāṃ kartavyo hyakṛto vidhiḥ ।। yadyadiṣṭaṃ suraśreṣṭha tatkuruṣva yathepsitam ।। tataḥ praṇamya hṛṣṭātmā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।।
jvalanaś ca svayaṃ tatra kṛtāñjalirupasthitaḥ ।। yathoktavidhinā hutvā lājānapi yathākramam ।। triś ca taṃ jvalanaṃ devaṃ kārayitvā pradakṣiṇam ।। suraiś ca mānavaiḥ sarvaiḥ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā ।।
tataḥ pādyaṃ tayor dattvā śaṃbhorācamanaṃ tathā ।। atiṣṭhadbhagavānbrahmā devairindrapurogamaiḥ ।। sūryādayaḥ samabhyarcya tuṣṭuvurvṛṣabhadhvajam ।। tayā samāgato rudraḥ sarvalokahitāya vai ।।
śrāvayedvā dvijāñchuddhān vedavedāṅgapāragān ।। yatrāyaṃ kīrtyate viprais tāvadāste tadā bhavaḥ ।। udvāhe ca dvijendrāṇāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। kṛtodvāhastadā devyā haimavatyā vṛṣadhvajaḥ ।।
purīṃ vārāṇasīṃ divyām ājagāma mahādyutiḥ ।। apṛcchatkṣetramāhātmyaṃ bhavānī harṣitānanā ।। avimuktasya māhātmyaṃ vistarācchakyate nahi ।। kiṃ mayā varṇyate devī hy avimuktaphalodayaḥ ।।
anyatra tu kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ vārāṇasyāṃ vyapohati ।। kṛtvā pāpasahasrāṇi piśācatvaṃ varaṃ nṛṇām ।। yatra triviṣṭapo devo yatra viśveśvaro vibhuḥ ।। uktvā kṣetrasya māhātmyaṃ saṃkṣepācchaśiśekharaḥ ।।
tatraiva bhagavān jāto gajavaktro vināyakaḥ ।। etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ kathāsarvasvamuttamam ।। yathāśrutaṃ mayā sarvaṃ prasādādvaḥ suśobhanam ।। kathaṃ prabhāvastasyaivaṃ sūta vaktumihārhasi ।।
dharmavighnaṃ tadā kartuṃ daityānāmabhavandvijāḥ ।। tāmasāś ca tathā cānye rājasāś ca tathā bhuvi ।। brahmāṇaṃ ca hariṃ viprā labdhepsitavarā yataḥ ।। teṣāṃ tatastu vighnārtham avighnāya divaukasām ।।
vighneśaṃ śaṅkaraṃ sraṣṭuṃ gaṇapaṃ stotumarhatha ।। namaḥ sarvātmane tubhyaṃ sarvajñāya pinākine ।। akāyāyārthakāyāya hareḥ kāyāpahāriṇe ।। kṛtādibhedakālāya kālavegāya te namaḥ ।।
kālīviśuddhadehāya kālikākāraṇāya te ।। aṃbikāpataye tubhyaṃ hiraṇyapataye namaḥ ।। kapāladaṇḍapāśāsicarmāṅkuśadharāya ca ।। pītaśuklāya rakṣārthaṃ surāṇāṃ kṛṣṇavartmane ।।
pañcāsyaphaṇihārāya pañcākṣaramayāya te ।। pañcākṣaradṛśe tubhyaṃ parātparatarāya te ।। kādipañcakahastāya cādihastāya te namaḥ ।। pādimeṇḍhrāya yadyaṅgadhātusaptakadhāriṇe ।।
lavarephahalāṅgāya niraṅgāya ca te namaḥ ।। bhruvor ante sadā sadbhir dṛṣṭāyātyantabhānave ।। guṇatrayoparisthāya tīrthapādāya te namaḥ ।। ṛgyajuḥsāmavedāya oṃkārāya namo namaḥ ।।
pītāya kṛṣṇavarṇāya raktāyātyantatejase ।। brahmaṇe viṣṇave tubhyaṃ kumārāya namonamaḥ ।। mūlasūkṣmasvarūpāya sthūlasūkṣmāya te namaḥ ।। ādimadhyāntaśūnyāya citsaṃsthāya namonamaḥ ।।
diṅmukhe diṅmukhe nityaṃ sagaṇaiḥ pūjitāya te ।। maheśvarāya dhīrāya namaḥ sākṣācchivāya te ।। atha śṛṇu bhagavan stavacchalena kathitamajendramukhaiḥ surāsureśaiḥ । makhamadanayamāgnidakṣayajñakṣapaṇavicitraviceṣṭitaṃ kṣamasva ।।
kīrtitaṃ śrāvayedvidvān sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। tadāṃbikāpatir bhavaḥ pinākadhṛṅ maheśvaraḥ ।। praṇemurādarāddharaṃ surā mudārdralocanāḥ ।। tadāha bhadramastu vaḥ sureśvarān maheśvaraḥ ।।
praṇamya cāha vākpatiḥ patiṃ nirīkṣya nirbhayaḥ ।। samastakarmasiddhaye surāpakārakāribhiḥ ।। surāpakārakāriṇām ihaiṣa eva no varaḥ ।। gaṇeśvaraṃ sureśvaraṃ vapurdadhāra saḥ śivaḥ ।।
samastalokasaṃbhavaṃ bhavārttihāriṇaṃ śubham ।। samastalokasaṃbhavaṃ gajānanaṃ tadāṃbikā ।। tadā tuṣṭuvuścaikadantaṃ sureśāḥ praṇemurgaṇeśaṃ maheśaṃ vitandrāḥ ।। sthito nanarta bālakaḥ samastamaṅgalālayaḥ ।।
maheśvarasya putrako abhivandya tātam ambikām ।। gajānanāya kṛtyāṃstu sarvānsarveśvaraḥ svayam ।। āliṅgyāghrāya mūrdhānaṃ mahādevo jagadguruḥ ।। devānāmupakārārthaṃ dvijānāṃ brahmavādinām ।।
tasya dharmasya vighnaṃ ca kuru svargapathe sthitaḥ ।। yo anyāyataḥ karotyasmin tasya prāṇānsadā hara ।। svadharmarahitānāṃ ca prāṇānapahara prabho ।। yajanti tāsāṃ teṣāṃ ca tvatsāmyaṃ dātumarhasi ।।
yauvanasthāṃś ca vṛddhāṃś ca ihāmutra ca pūjitaḥ ।। saṃpūjyo vandanīyaś ca bhaviṣyasi na saṃśayaḥ ।। yajanti yajñairvā viprair agre pūjyo bhaviṣyasi ।। kurute tasya kalyāṇam akalyāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।
sampūjya sarvasiddhyarthaṃ bhakṣyabhojyādibhiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। devairapi tathānyaiś ca labdhavyaṃ nāsti kutracit ।। te cārcanīyāḥ śakrādyair bhaviṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ ।। vighnair bādhayasi tvāṃ cen nārcayanti phalārthinaḥ ।।
gaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ namaskṛtvāpy atiṣṭhattasya cāgrataḥ ।। daityānāṃ dharmavighnaṃ ca cakārāsau gaṇeśvaraḥ ।। yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā sukhībhavet ।। vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ śrutaḥ skandāgrajodbhavaḥ ।।
sūdayāmāsa kālāgnir iva devāndvijottamān ।। brahmāṇaṃ ca tatheśānaṃ kumāraṃ viṣṇumeva ca ।। strīrūpadhāribhiḥ stutyair brahmādyairyudhi saṃsthitaiḥ ।। vijñāpya tasmai tatsarvaṃ tena sārdhamumāpatim ।।
brahmā prāpya ca deveśaṃ praṇamya bahudhā nataḥ ।। nihatya dārukaṃ daityaṃ strīvadhyaṃ trātumarhasi ।। devīmuvāca deveśo girijāṃ prahasanniva ।। vadhārthaṃ dārukasyāsya strīvadhyasya varānane ।।
viveśa dehe devasya deveśī janmatatparā ।। na viveda tadā brahmā devāścendrapurogamāḥ ।। māyayā mohitastasyāḥ sarvajño api caturmukhaḥ ।। kaṇṭhasthena viṣeṇāsya tanuṃ cakre tadātmanaḥ ।।
sasarja kālīṃ kāmāriḥ kālakaṇṭhīṃ kapardinīm ।। devetarāṇāmajayastvasiddhyā tuṣṭirbhavānyāḥ parameśvarasya ।। kālīṃ garālaṃkṛtakālakaṇṭhīm upendrapadmodbhavaśakramukhyāḥ ।। kaṇṭhe karālaṃ niśitaṃ triśūlaṃ kare karālaṃ ca vibhūṣaṇāni ।।
siddhendrasiddhāś ca tathā piśācā jajñire punaḥ ।। dānavaṃ sūdayāmāsa sūdayantaṃ surādhipān ।। krodhāgninā ca viprendrāḥ saṃbabhūva tadāturam ।। ruroda māyayā tasyāḥ krodhāgniṃ pātum īśvaraḥ ।।
utthāpyāghrāya vakṣojaṃ stanaṃ sā pradadau dvijāḥ ।। krodhenānena vai bālaḥ kṣetrāṇāṃ rakṣako abhavat ।। evaṃ vai tena bālena kṛtā sā krodhamūrchitā ।। saṃdhyāyāṃ sarvabhūtendraiḥ pretaiḥ prītena śūlinā ।।
nanarta sā ca yoginyaḥ pretasthāne yathāsukham ।। praṇemustuṣṭuvuḥ kālīṃ punardevīṃ ca pārvatīm ।। yogānandena ca vibhos tāṇḍavaṃ ceti cāpare ।। kṣīrārṇavaḥ kathaṃ labdho vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam ।।
upamanyuḥ samabhyarcya tapasā labdhavānphalam ।। kumāra iva tejasvī krīḍamāno yadṛcchayā ।। īrṣyayā mātulasuto hy apibat kṣīram uttamam ।। mātarmātarmahābhāge mama dehi tapasvini ।।
upalālitaivaṃ putreṇa putram āliṅgya sādaram ।। dehi dehīti tāmāha rodamāno mahādyutiḥ ।। bījapiṣṭaṃ tadāloḍya toyena kalabhāṣiṇī ।। āliṅgyādāya duḥkhārtā pradadau kṛtrimaṃ payaḥ ।।
naitatkṣīramiti prāha mātaraṃ cātivihvalaḥ ।। saṃmārjya netre putrasya karābhyāṃ kamalāyate ।। bhāgyahīnā na paśyanti bhaktihīnāś ca ye śive ।। na labhante priyāṇyeṣāṃ no tuṣyati sadā bhavaḥ ।।
anyadeveṣu niratā duḥkhārtā vibhramanti ca ।। pūrvajanmani yaddattaṃ śivamudyamya vai suta ।। niśamya vacanaṃ mātur upamanyurmahādyutiḥ ।। tyaja śokaṃ mahābhāge mahādevo asti cetkvacit ।।
tāṃ praṇamyaivamuktvā sa tapaḥ kartuṃ pracakrame ।। anujñātastayā tatra tapastepe sudustaram ।। tapasā tasya viprasya vidhūpitamabhūjjagat ।। śrutvā teṣāṃ tadā vākyaṃ bhagavānpuruṣottamaḥ ।।
jagāma mandaraṃ tūrṇaṃ maheśvaradidṛkṣayā ।। bhagavan brāhmaṇaḥ kaścid upamanyuritiśrutaḥ ।। śakrarūpaṃ samāsthāya gantuṃ cakre matiṃ tadā ।। saha surāsurasiddhamahoragair amararājatanuṃ svayamāsthitaḥ ।।
sahaiva cāruhya tadā dvipaṃ taṃ pragṛhya vālavyajanaṃ vivasvān । vāmena śacyā sahitaṃ surendraṃ kareṇa cānyena sitātapatram ।। sitātapatreṇa yathā candrabiṃbena mandaraḥ ।। jagāmānugrahaṃ kartum upamanyos tadāśramam ।।
praṇamya śirasā prāha munirmunivarāḥ svayam ।। prāptaḥ śakro jagannātho bhagavānbhānunā prabhuḥ ।। prāha gaṃbhīrayā vācā śakrarūpadharo haraḥ ।। dadāmi cepsitān sarvān dhaumyāgraja mahāmate ।।
varayāmi śive bhaktim ityuvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। prāha savyagramīśānaḥ śakrarūpadharaḥ svayam ।। trailokyādhipatiṃ śakraṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam ।। dadāmi sarvaṃ bhadraṃ te tyaja rudraṃ ca nirguṇam ।।
upamanyuridaṃ prāha japan pañcākṣaraṃ śubham ।। kartuṃ daityādhamaḥ kaścid dharmavighnaṃ ca nānyathā ।। prasaṃgāddevadevasya nirguṇatvaṃ mahātmanaḥ ।। bhavāntarakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ śrutā nindā bhavasya tu ।।
svadehaṃ taṃ nihatyāśu śivalokaṃ sa gacchati ।। triḥ saptakulamuddhṛtya śivalokaṃ sa gacchati ।। nihatya tvāṃ śivāstreṇa tyajāmyetatkalevaram ।। pūrvajanmani cāsmābhir apūjita iti prabhuḥ ।।
śakraṃ cakre matiṃ hantum atharvāstreṇa mantravit ।। atharvāstraṃ tatastasmai sasarja ca nanāda ca ।। atiṣṭhacca mahātejāḥ śuṣkendhanamivāvyayaḥ ।। vārayāmāsa saumyena dhāraṇāṃ tasya yoginaḥ ।।
kālāgnisadṛśaṃ cedaṃ niyogānnandinas tathā ।। darśayāmāsa viprāya bālendukṛtaśekharam ।। dadhyāderarṇavaṃ caiva ghṛtodārṇavameva ca ।। apūpagirayaścaiva tathātiṣṭhan samantataḥ ।।
girijām avalokya sasmitāṃ saghṛṇaṃ prekṣyatu taṃ tadā ghṛṇī ।। bhuṅkṣva bhogānyathākāmaṃ bāndhavaiḥ paśya vatsa me । upamanyo mahābhāga tavāṃbaiṣā hi pārvatī ।। madhunaścārṇavaścaiva dadhnaścārṇava eva ca ।।
apūpagirayaścaiva bhakṣyabhojyārṇavaḥ punaḥ ।। mātā tava mahābhāgā jaganmātā na saṃśayaḥ ।। varānvaraya dāsyāmi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। āghrāya mūrdhani vibhur dadau devyāstadā bhavaḥ ।।
yogaiśvaryaṃ tadā tuṣṭā brahmavidyāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। tuṣṭāva ca mahādevaṃ harṣagadgadayā girā ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā praṇipatya punaḥ punaḥ ।। śraddhā caiva mahādeva sānnidhyaṃ caiva sarvadā ।।
dattvepsitaṃ hi viprāya tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। dhaumyāgrajastato labdhaṃ divyaṃ pāśupataṃ vratam ।। vaktumarhasi tāṃ sūta kathāṃ pātakanāśinīm ।। nindayanneva mānuṣyaṃ dehaśuddhiṃ cakāra saḥ ।।
āśramaṃ copamanyorvai dṛṣṭavāṃstatra taṃ munim ।। bahumānena vai kṛṣṇas triḥ kṛtvā vai pradakṣiṇam ।। naṣṭameva malaṃ sarvaṃ kāyajaṃ karmmajaṃ tathā ।। tamagniriti viprendrā vāyurityādibhiḥ kramāt ।।
muneḥ prasādānmānyo asau kṛṣṇaḥ pāśupate dvijāḥ ।। sāṃbaṃ sagaṇamavyagraṃ labdhavānputramātmanaḥ ।। divyāḥ pāśupatāḥ sarve tasthuḥ saṃvṛtya sarvadā ।। sauvarṇīṃ mekhalāṃ kṛtvā ādhāraṃ daṇḍadhāraṇam ।।
naraiḥ striyātha vā kāryaṃ maṣībhājanalekhanīm ।। pāśupatāya dātavyaṃ bhasmoddhūlitavigrahaiḥ ।। ātmavittānusāreṇa yoginaṃ pūjayedbudhaḥ ।। yānti rudrapadaṃ divyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।।
yogināṃ saṃpradānena śivaḥ kṣipraṃ prasīdati ।। sarvasvaṃ vāpi dātavyaṃ yadīcchenmokṣamuttamam ।। bhavyaṃ pāśupataṃ nityaṃ saṃsārārṇavatārakam ।। yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।।
